010101 The book of the genealogy of Jesus Christ, the son of David, the son of Abraham.
010102 Abraham fathered Isaac, and Isaac fathered Jacob, and Jacob fathered Judah and his brothers.
010103 And Judah fathered Pharez and Zarah of Tamar. And Pharez fathered Hezron, and Hezron fathered Ram,
010104 and Ram fathered Amminadab, and Amminadab fathered Nahshon, and Nahshon fathered Salmon.
010105 And Salmon fathered Boaz of Rahab, and Boaz fathered Obed of Ruth, and Obed fathered Jesse,
010106 and Jesse fathered David the king. And David the king fathered Solomon of her who had been wife of Uriah.
010107 And Solomon fathered Rehoboam, and Rehoboam fathered Abijah, and Abijah fathered Asa.
010108 And Asa fathered Jehoshaphat, and Jehoshaphat fathered Jehoram, and Jehoram fathered Uzziah.
010109 And Uzziah fathered Jotham, and Jotham fathered Ahaz, and Ahaz fathered Hezekiah.
010110 And Hezekiah fathered Manasseh, and Manasseh fathered Amon, and Amon fathered Josiah.
010111 And Josiah fathered Jehoiachin and his brothers, at the time they were carried away to Babylon.
010112 And after the carrying away to Babylon, Jehoiachin fathered Shealtiel, and Shealtiel fathered Zerubbabel.
010113 And Zerubbabel fathered Abiud, and Abiud fathered Eliakim, and Eliakim fathered Azor.
010114 And Azor fathered Sadoc, and Sadoc fathered Achim, and Achim fathered Eliud.
010115 And Eliud fathered Eleazar, and Eleazar fathered Matthan, and Matthan fathered Jacob.
010116 And Jacob fathered Joseph, the husband to be of Mary, of whom Jesus was born, who is called Christ.
010117 So all the generations from Abraham to David are fourteen generations. And from David until the carrying away into Babylon, fourteen generations. And from the carrying away into Babylon until Christ, fourteen generations.
010118 Now the birth of Jesus Christ was this way (for His mother Mary was betrothed to Joseph) before they came together, she was found to be with child by the Holy Spirit.
010119 But Joseph, her husband to be , being just, and not willing to make her a public example, he purposed to put her away secretly.
010120 And as he thought upon these things, behold, the angel of the Lord appeared to him in a dream, saying, Joseph, son of David, do not fear to take to you Mary as your wife. For that in her is fathered of the Holy Spirit.
010121 And she shall bear a son, and you shall call His name JESUS: for He shall save His people from their sins.
010122 Now all this happened so that might be fulfilled that which was spoken of the LORD by the prophet, saying,
010123 "Behold, the virgin shall conceive in her womb, and will bear a son. And they will call His name Emmanuel," which being interpreted is, God with us.
010124 And Joseph, being roused from sleep, did as the angel of the Lord commanded him and took his wife,
010125 and did not know her until she bore her son, the First-born. And he called His name JESUS.
010201 Now when Jesus was born in Bethlehem of Judea in the days of Herod the king, behold, wise men came from the east to Jerusalem,
010202 saying, Where is He who is born king of the Jews? For we have seen His star in the east and have come to worship Him.
010203 But when Herod the king heard these things , he was troubled, and all Jerusalem with him.
010204 And when he had gathered all the chief priests and scribes of the people together, he demanded of them where Christ should be born.
010205 And they said to him, In Bethlehem of Judea. For so it is written by the prophet,
010206 "And you, Bethlehem, in the land of Judah, are not the least among the governors of Judah. For out of you shall come a Governor who shall rule My people Israel."
010207 Then Herod, when he had secretly called the wise men, inquired of them exactly what time the star appeared.
010208 And he sent them to Bethlehem, and said, Go and search diligently for the young child. And when you have found him , bring me word again so that I may come and worship him also.
010209 When they had heard the king, they departed. And lo, the star which they saw in the east went before them until it came and stood over where the child was.
010210 And seeing the star, they rejoiced with exceedingly great joy.
010211 And coming into the house, they saw the child with Mary His mother. And they fell down and worshiped Him. And opening their treasures, they presented gifts to Him, gold and frankincense and myrrh.
010212 And being warned of God in a dream that they should not return to Herod, they departed into their own country another way.
010213 And when they had departed, behold, the angel of the Lord appeared to Joseph in a dream, saying, Arise and take the young child and His mother and flee into Egypt. And be there until I bring you word, for Herod is about to seek the child to destroy Him.
010214 And he arose and took the young child and his mother by night and departed into Egypt.
010215 And he was there until the death of Herod; so that it might be fulfilled which was spoken by the LORD through the prophet, "Out of Egypt I have called My Son."
010216 Then Herod, when he saw that he was mocked by the wise men, was greatly enraged. And he sent and killed all the boys in Bethlehem, and in all its districts, from two years old and under, according to the time which he had carefully inquired of the wise men.
010217 Then was fulfilled that which was spoken by Jeremiah the prophet, saying,
010218 "A voice was heard in Ramah, wailing and weeping and great mourning, Rachel weeping for her children, and would not be comforted, because they are not ."
010219 But Herod having expired, behold, an angel of the Lord appeared in a dream to Joseph in Egypt,
010220 saying, Arise, and take the child and His mother. And go into the land of Israel. For the ones who sought the child's life are dead.
010221 And he arose and took the child and His mother and came into the land of Israel.
010222 But when he heard that Archelaus reigned in Judea in his father Herod's place, he was afraid to go there. And being warned by God in a dream, he turned aside into the parts of Galilee.
010223 And he came and lived in a city called Nazareth, so that it might be fulfilled which was spoken by the prophets, "He shall be called a Nazarene."
010301 In those days John the Baptist came preaching in the wilderness of Judea,
010302 and saying, Repent, for the kingdom of Heaven is at hand.
010303 For this is he who was spoken of by the prophet Isaiah, saying, "The voice of one crying in the wilderness: Prepare the way of the Lord, make His paths straight."
010304 And the same John had his clothing of camel's hair and a leather girdle about his loins. And his food was locusts and wild honey.
010305 Then Jerusalem and all Judea went out to him, and all the region round about Jordan.
010306 And they were baptized by him in the Jordan, confessing their sins.
010307 But seeing many of the Pharisees and Sadducees come to his baptism, he said to them, O generation of vipers, who has warned you to flee from the wrath to come?
010308 Bring forth therefore fruits worthy of repentance;
010309 and do not think to say within yourselves, We have Abraham as our father. For I say to you that God is able to raise up children to Abraham from these stones.
010310 And now also, the axe is laid to the root of the trees. Therefore every tree which does not bring forth good fruit is cut down and cast into the fire.
010311 I indeed baptize you with water to repentance. But He who comes after me is mightier than I, whose sandals I am not worthy to carry. He shall baptize you with the Holy Spirit and with fire;
010312 whose fan is in His hand, and He will cleanse His floor and gather His wheat into the storehouse; but He will burn up the chaff with unquenchable fire.
010313 Then Jesus came from Galilee to Jordan, to John, to be baptized by him.
010314 But John restrained Him, saying, I have need to be baptized by You, and do You come to me?
010315 And answering Jesus said to him, Allow it now, for it is becoming to us to fulfill all righteousness. Then he allowed Him.
010316 And Jesus, when He had been baptized, went up immediately out of the water. And lo, the heavens were opened to Him, and He saw the Spirit of God descending like a dove and lighting upon Him.
010317 And lo, a voice from Heaven, saying, This is My beloved Son, in whom I am well pleased.
010401 Then Jesus was led by the Spirit up into the wilderness, to be tempted by the Devil.
010402 And when He had fasted forty days and forty nights, He was afterwards hungry.
010403 And when the tempter came to Him, he said, If You are the Son of God, command that these stones be made bread.
010404 But He answered and said, It is written, "Man shall not live by bread alone, but by every word that proceeds out of the mouth of God."
010405 Then the Devil took Him up into the holy city and set Him upon a pinnacle of the Temple.
010406 And he said to Him, If you are the Son of God, cast yourself down. For it is written, "He shall give His angels charge concerning You, and in their hands they shall bear You up, lest at any time You dash Your foot against a stone."
010407 Jesus said to him, It is written again, "You shall not tempt the Lord your God."
010408 Again, the Devil took Him up into a very high mountain and showed Him all the kingdoms of the world and their glory.
010409 And he said to Him, All these things I will give You if You will fall down and worship me.
010410 Then Jesus said to him, Go, Satan! For it is written, "You shall worship the Lord your God, and Him only you shall serve."
010411 Then the Devil left him. And behold, angels came and ministered to Him.
010412 But when Jesus heard that John was thrown into prison, He went back into Galilee.
010413 And leaving Nazareth, He came and lived in Capernaum, which is on the seacoast, in the borders of Zebulun and Naphtali,
010414 so that it might be fulfilled which was spoken by Isaiah the prophet, saying,
010415 "The land of Zebulun and the land of Naphtali, by way of the sea, beyond Jordan, Galilee of the nations!
010416 The people who sat in darkness saw a great Light; and Light has sprung up to those who sat in the region and shadow of death."
010417 From that time Jesus began to preach and to say, Repent! For the kingdom of Heaven is at hand.
010418 And walking by the Sea of Galilee, Jesus saw two brothers, Simon called Peter, and Andrew his brother, casting a net into the sea. For they were fishermen.
010419 And He said to them, Follow Me, and I will make you fishers of men.
010420 And they immediately left their nets and followed him.
010421 And going on from there, he saw another two brothers, James the son of Zebedee, and John his brother, in a boat with Zebedee their father, mending their nets. And He called them;
010422 and they immediately left the boat and their father and followed Him.
010423 And Jesus went about all Galilee, teaching in their synagogues and preaching the gospel of the kingdom, and healing all kinds of sickness and all kinds of disease among the people.
010424 And His fame went throughout all Syria. And they brought to Him all those being badly ill suffering various diseases and torments, and those who had been possessed with demons, and those who had been moonstruck, and paralytics. And He healed them.
010425 And great multitudes of people followed Him, from Galilee and Decapolis and Jerusalem and Judea and beyond Jordan.
010501 And seeing the multitudes, He went up into a mountain. And when He had sat down, His disciples came to Him.
010502 And He opened His mouth and taught them, saying,
010503 Blessed are the poor in spirit! For theirs is the kingdom of Heaven.
010504 Blessed are they that mourn! For they shall be comforted.
010505 Blessed are the meek! For they shall inherit the earth.
010506 Blessed are they who hunger and thirst after righteousness! For they shall be filled.
010507 Blessed are the merciful! For they shall obtain mercy.
010508 Blessed are the pure in heart! For they shall see God.
010509 Blessed are the peacemakers! For they shall be called the sons of God.
010510 Blessed are they who have been persecuted for righteousness sake! For theirs is the kingdom of Heaven.
010511 Blessed are you when men shall revile you and persecute you , and shall say all kinds of evil against you falsely, for My sake.
010512 Rejoice and be exceedingly glad, for your reward in Heaven is great. For so they persecuted the prophets who were before you.
010513 You are the salt of the earth, but if the salt loses its savor, with what shall it be salted? It is no longer good for anything, but to be thrown out and to be trodden underfoot by men.
010514 You are the light of the world. A city that is set on a hill cannot be hidden.
010515 Nor do men light a lamp and put it under the grain-measure, but on a lampstand. And it gives light to all who are in the house.
010516 Let your light so shine before men that they may see your good works and glorify your Father who is in Heaven.
010517 Do not think that I have come to destroy the Law or the Prophets. I have not come to destroy but to fulfill.
010518 For truly I say to you, Till the heaven and the earth pass away, not one jot or one tittle shall in any way pass from the law until all is fulfilled.
010519 Therefore whoever shall break one of these commandments, the least, and shall teach men so, he shall be called the least in the kingdom of Heaven. But whoever shall do and teach them , the same shall be called great in the kingdom of Heaven.
010520 For I say to you that unless your righteousness shall exceed that of the scribes and Pharisees, you shall in no case enter into the kingdom of Heaven.
010521 You have heard that it was said to the ancients, "You shall not kill" --and, "Whoever shall kill shall be liable to the judgment."
010522 But I say to you that whoever is angry with his brother without a cause shall be liable to the judgment. And whoever shall say to his brother, Raca, shall be liable to the sanhedrin; but whoever shall say, Fool! shall be liable to be thrown into the fire of hell.
010523 Therefore if you offer your gift on the altar, and there remember that your brother has anything against you,
010524 leave your gift there before the altar and go. First be reconciled to your brother, and then come and offer your gift.
010525 Agree with your adversary quickly, while you are in the way with him; that the opponent not deliver you to the judge, and the judge deliver you to the officer, and you be thrown into prison.
010526 Truly I say to you, You shall by no means come out from there until you have paid the last kodrantes.
010527 You have heard that it was said to the ancients, "You shall not commit adultery."
010528 But I say to you that whoever looks on a woman to lust after her has already committed adultery with her in his heart.
010529 And if your right eye offends you, pluck it out and throw it from you. For it is profitable for you that one of your members should perish, and not that your whole body should be thrown into hell.
010530 And if your right hand offends you, cut it off and throw it from you. For it is profitable for you that one of your members should perish, and not that your whole body should be thrown into hell.
010531 It was also said, Whoever shall put away his wife, let him give her a bill of divorce.
010532 But I say to you that whoever shall put away his wife, except for the cause of fornication, causes her to commit adultery. And whoever shall marry her who is put away commits adultery.
010533 Again, you have heard that it has been said to the ancients, "You shall not swear falsely, but you shall perform your oaths to the Lord."
010534 But I say to you, Do not swear at all! Not by Heaven, because it is God's throne;
010535 not by the earth, for it is the footstool of His feet; not by Jerusalem, because it is the city of the great King;
010536 nor shall you swear by your head, because you cannot make one hair white or black.
010537 But let your word be, Yes, yes; No, no. For whatever is more than these comes from evil.
010538 You have heard that it was said, "An eye for an eye, and a tooth for a tooth."
010539 But I say to you, Do not resist evil. But whoever shall strike you on your right cheek, turn the other to him also.
010540 And to him desiring to sue you, and to take away your tunic, let him have your coat also.
010541 And whoever shall compel you to go a mile, go with him two.
010542 Give to him who asks of you, and you shall not turn away from him who would borrow from you.
010543 You have heard that it was said, "You shall love your neighbor and hate your enemy."
010544 But I say to you, Love your enemies, bless those who curse you, do good to those who hate you, and pray for those who despitefully use you and persecute you,
010545 so that you may become sons of your Father in Heaven. For He makes His sun to rise on the evil and on the good, and sends rain on the just and on the unjust.
010546 For if you love those who love you, what reward do you have? Do not even the tax-collectors do the same?
010547 And if you greet your brothers only, what do you do more than others? Do not even the tax-collectors do so?
010548 Therefore be perfect, even as your Father in Heaven is perfect.
010601 Take heed that you do not do your merciful deeds before men, to be seen by them. Otherwise you have no reward with your Father in Heaven.
010602 Therefore when you do your merciful deeds, do not sound a trumpet before you, as the hypocrites do in the synagogues and in the streets, so that they may have glory from men. Truly I say to you, They have their reward.
010603 But when you do merciful deeds, do not let your left hand know what your right hand does,
010604 so that your merciful deeds may be in secret. And your Father who sees in secret Himself shall reward you openly.
010605 And when you pray, you shall not be like the hypocrites. For they love to pray standing in the synagogues and in the corners of the streets, so that they may be seen by men. Truly I say to you, They have their reward.
010606 But you, when you pray, enter into your room. And shutting your door, pray to your Father in secret; and your Father who sees in secret shall reward you openly.
010607 But when you pray, do not babble vain words, as the nations. For they think that in their much speaking they shall be heard.
010608 Therefore do not be like them, for your Father knows what things you have need of, before you ask Him.
010609 Therefore pray in this way: Our Father, who is in Heaven, Hallowed be Your name.
010610 Your kingdom come, Your will be done, on earth as it is in Heaven.
010611 Give us this day our daily bread;
010612 and forgive us our debts as we also forgive our debtors.
010613 And lead us not into temptation, but deliver us from the evil. For Yours is the kingdom, and the power, and the glory, forever. Amen.
010614 For if you forgive men their trespasses, your heavenly Father will also forgive you;
010615 but if you do not forgive men their trespasses, neither will your Father forgive your trespasses.
010616 And when you fast, do not be like the hypocrites, of a sad face. For they disfigure their faces so that they may appear to men to fast. Truly I say to you, they have their reward.
010617 But you, when you fast, anoint your head and wash your face,
010618 so that you do not appear to men to fast, but to your Father in secret. And your Father who sees in secret shall reward you openly.
010619 Do not lay up treasures on earth for yourselves, where moth and rust corrupt, and where thieves break through and steal.
010620 But lay up treasures in Heaven for yourselves, where neither moth nor rust corrupt, and where thieves do not break through nor steal.
010621 For where your treasure is, there will your heart be also.
010622 The light of the body is the eye. Therefore if your eye is sound, your whole body shall be full of light.
010623 But if your eye is evil, your whole body shall be full of darkness. If therefore the light that is in you is darkness, how great is that darkness!
010624 No one can serve two masters. For either he will hate the one and love the other, or else he will hold to the one and despise the other. You cannot serve God and mammon.
010625 Therefore I say to you, Do not be anxious for your life, what you shall eat, or what you shall drink; nor for your body, what you shall put on. Is not life more than food, and the body more than clothing?
010626 Behold the birds of the air; for they sow not, nor do they reap, nor gather into barns. Yet your heavenly Father feeds them; are you not much better than they are?
010627 Which of you by being anxious can add one cubit to his stature?
010628 And why are you anxious about clothing? Consider the lilies of the field, how they grow. They do not toil, nor do they spin,
010629 but I say to you that even Solomon in his glory was not arrayed like one of these.
010630 Therefore if God so clothes the grass of the field, which today is, and tomorrow is thrown into the oven, will He not much rather clothe you, little-faiths?
010631 Therefore do not be anxious, saying, What shall we eat? or, What shall we drink? or, With what shall we be clothed?
010632 For the nations seek after all these things. For your heavenly Father knows that you have need of all these things.
010633 But seek first the kingdom of God and His righteousness; and all these things shall be added to you.
010634 Therefore do not be anxious about tomorrow; for tomorrow shall be anxious for its own things. Sufficient to the day is the evil of it.
010701 Judge not, that you may not be judged.
010702 For with whatever judgment you judge, you shall be judged; and with whatever measure you measure out, it shall be measured to you again.
010703 And why do you look on the splinter that is in your brother's eye, but do not consider the beam that is in your own eye?
010704 Or how will you say to your brother, Let me pull the splinter out of your eye; and, behold, a beam is in your own eye?
010705 Hypocrite! First cast the beam out of your own eye, and then you shall see clearly to cast the splinter out of your brother's eye.
010706 Do not give that which is holy to the dogs; nor cast your pearls before swine, lest they trample them under their feet and turn again and tear you.
010707 Ask and it shall be given to you; seek and you shall find; knock and it shall be opened to you.
010708 For each one who asks receives; and he who seeks finds; and to him who knocks, it shall be opened.
010709 Or what man is there of you, if his son asks a loaf, will he give him a stone?
010710 Or if he asks a fish, will he give him a snake?
010711 If you then, being evil, know how to give good gifts to your children, how much more shall your Father in Heaven give good things to those who ask Him?
010712 Therefore all things, whatever you desire that men should do to you, do even so to them; for this is the Law and the Prophets.
010713 Go in through the narrow gate, for wide is the gate and broad is the way that leads to destruction, and many there are who go in through it.
010714 Because narrow is the gate and constricted is the way which leads to life, and there are few who find it.
010715 Beware of false prophets who come to you in sheep's clothing, but inwardly they are ravening wolves.
010716 You shall know them by their fruits. Do men gather grapes from thorns, or figs from thistles?
010717 Even so every good tree brings forth good fruit; but a corrupt tree brings forth evil fruit.
010718 A good tree cannot bring forth evil fruits, nor can a corrupt tree bring forth good fruit.
010719 Every tree that does not bring forth good fruit is cut down and thrown into the fire.
010720 Therefore by their fruits you shall know them.
010721 Not everyone who says to Me, Lord! Lord! shall enter the kingdom of Heaven, but he who does the will of My Father in Heaven.
010722 Many will say to Me in that day, Lord! Lord! Did we not prophesy in Your name, and through Your name throw out demons, and through Your name do many wonderful works?
010723 And then I will say to them I never knew you! Depart from Me, those working lawlessness!
010724 Therefore whoever hears these sayings of Mine, and does them, I will liken him to a wise man who built his house on a rock.
010725 And the rain came down, and the floods came, and the winds blew and beat on that house. And it did not fall, for it was founded on a rock.
010726 And everyone who hears these sayings of Mine and does not do them shall be compared to a foolish man who built his house on the sand.
010727 And the rain came down, and the floods came, and the wind blew and beat on that house. And it fell, and great was its fall.
010728 And it happened, when Jesus had ended these sayings, that the people were astonished at His doctrine.
010729 For He taught them as one having authority, and not as the scribes.
010801 When He had come down from the mountain, great crowds followed him.
010802 And behold, a leper came and worshiped him, saying, Lord, if You will, You can make me clean.
010803 And Jesus put out His hand and touched him, saying, I will; be clean! And immediately his leprosy was cleansed.
010804 And Jesus said to him, See that you tell no one; but go, show yourself to the priest. And offer the gift that Moses commanded, for a testimony to them.
010805 And when Jesus had entered into Capernaum, a centurion came to him, beseeching Him,
010806 and saying, Lord, my son lies at home paralyzed and grievously tormented.
010807 And Jesus says to him, I will come and heal him.
010808 The centurion answered and said, Lord, I am not worthy that You should come under my roof; but only speak the word, and my boy will be healed.
010809 For I am a man under authority, having soldiers under me. And I say to this one, Go! And he goes; and to another, Come! And he comes; and to my servant, Do this! And he does it .
010810 When Jesus heard, He marvelled and said to those who followed, Truly I say to you, I have not found such great faith, no, not in Israel.
010811 And I say to you that many shall come from the east and the west, and shall sit down with Abraham and Isaac and Jacob in the kingdom of Heaven.
010812 But the sons of the kingdom shall be cast out into outer darkness; there shall be weeping and gnashing of teeth.
010813 And Jesus said to the centurion, Go. And as you have believed, so let it be to you. And his boy was healed in that hour.
010814 And when Jesus had come into Peter's house, He saw his wife's mother laid out and in a fever.
010815 And He touched her hand, and the fever left her. And she arose and served them.
010816 And evening coming on, they brought to Him many who had been possessed with demons. And He cast out the spirits with a word, and healed all who were sick
010817 so that it might be fulfilled which was spoken by Isaiah the prophet, saying, "He took on Himself our weaknesses and bore our sicknesses."
010818 And seeing great crowds, Jesus gave orders to depart to the other side.
010819 And a certain scribe came and said to him, Master, I will follow You wherever You go.
010820 And Jesus said to him, The foxes have holes, and the birds of the air have nests, but the Son of man has nowhere to lay His head.
010821 And another of His disciples said to him, Lord, allow me first to go and bury my father.
010822 But Jesus said to him, Follow Me, and let the dead bury their dead.
010823 And He entering into a boat, His disciples followed Him.
010824 And behold, a great tempest arose in the sea, so much so that the boat was covered with the waves. But He was asleep.
010825 And His disciples came to Him and awakened Him, saying, Lord, save us! We perish!
010826 And He said to them, Why are you afraid, little-faiths? Then He arose and rebuked the winds and the sea; and there was a great calm.
010827 But the men marveled, saying, What kind of man is this, that even the winds and the sea obey him!
010828 And when He had come to the other side into the country of the Gergesenes, two demon-possessed ones met Him, coming out of the tombs, exceedingly fierce, so that no one might pass by that way.
010829 And behold, they cried out, saying, What have we to do with You, Jesus, Son of God? Have You come here to torment us before the time?
010830 And there was a good way off from them a herd of many swine, feeding.
010831 And the demons begged Him, saying, If You cast us out, allow us to go away into the herd of swine.
010832 And He said to them, Go! And when they had come out, they went into the herd of swine. And behold, the whole herd of swine ran violently down a steep place into the sea and perished in the waters.
010833 And those who fed them fled. And going into the city, they told everything, and what had happened to the ones who had been possessed of demons.
010834 And behold, the whole city came out to meet Jesus. And when they saw Him, they begged that He would depart out of their borders.
010901 And He entered into a boat, and passed over, and came to His own city.
010902 And behold, they brought to Him a paralytic, lying on a bed. And Jesus, seeing their faith, said to the paralytic, Child, be of good cheer. Your sins are forgiven you.
010903 And lo, some of the scribes said within themselves, This one blasphemes.
010904 And Jesus, knowing their thoughts, said, Why do you think evil in your hearts?
010905 For which is easier? To say, Your sins are forgiven you, or to say, Arise and walk!
010906 But so that you may know that the Son of man has authority on earth to forgive sins, then He said to the paralytic, Arise, take up your bed and go to your house.
010907 And he arose and departed to his house.
010908 But when the crowds saw, they marveled and glorified God, who had given such authority to men.
010909 And as Jesus passed on from there, He saw a man named Matthew sitting at the tax-office. And He said to him, Follow Me! And he arose and followed Him.
010910 And it happened as Jesus reclined in the house, behold, many tax-collectors and sinners came and were reclining with Him and His disciples.
010911 And when the Pharisees saw, they said to His disciples, Why does your master eat with tax-collectors and sinners?
010912 But when Jesus heard, He said to them, The ones who are whole do not need a physician, but the ones who are sick.
010913 But go and learn what this is , I will have mercy and not sacrifice. For I have not come to call the righteous, but sinners to repentance.
010914 Then the disciples of John came to Him saying, Why do we and the Pharisees fast often, but Your disciples do not fast?
010915 And Jesus said to them, Can the sons of the bridechamber mourn as long as the bridegroom is with them? But the days will come when the bridegroom shall be taken away from them, and then they shall fast.
010916 No one puts a piece of new cloth onto an old garment; for that which is put in to fill it up takes from the garment, and the tear is made worse.
010917 Nor do men put new wine into old wineskins; else the wineskins burst, and the wine runs out, and the wineskins perish. But they put new wine into new wineskins, and both are preserved together.
010918 While He spoke these things to them, behold, a certain ruler came and worshiped Him, saying, My daughter has just now died. But come and lay Your hand on her and she will live.
010919 And Jesus arose and followed him. And so did His disciples.
010920 And behold, a woman, who had a flow of blood for twelve years, came up behind Him and touched the hem of His garment.
010921 For she said within herself, If only I shall touch His robe, I will be whole.
010922 But turning and seeing her, Jesus said, Daughter, be comforted; your faith has saved you. And the woman was saved from that hour.
010923 And when Jesus came into the ruler's house and saw the minstrels and the people making a noise,
010924 He said to them, Go back, for the little girl is not dead, but sleeps. And they laughed Him to scorn.
010925 But when the people were put out, He went in and took her by the hand, and the little girl arose.
010926 And this report went out into all that land.
010927 And when Jesus passed on from there, two blind ones followed Him, crying and saying, Son of David, have mercy on us.
010928 And when He had come into the house, the blind men came to Him. And Jesus said to them, Do you believe that I am able to do this? They said to Him, Yes, Lord.
010929 Then He touched their eyes, saying, According to your faith let it be to you.
010930 And their eyes were opened. And Jesus strictly charged them, saying, See, let no one know.
010931 But going out, they made Him known in all that land.
010932 As they went out, behold, they brought to Him a dumb man, who had been demon-possessed.
010933 And when the demon had been cast out, the dumb one spoke. And multitudes marveled, saying, Never was it seen like this in Israel!
010934 But the Pharisees said, He throws out demons by the ruler of the demons.
010935 And Jesus went about all the cities and villages, teaching in their synagogues, and preaching the gospel of the kingdom, and healing every sickness and every disease among the people.
010936 But seeing the crowds, He was moved with compassion on them, because they were tired and scattered like sheep having no shepherd.
010937 Then He said to His disciples, The harvest truly is plenteous, but the laborers are few.
010938 Therefore pray to the Lord of the harvest that He will send out laborers into His harvest.
011001 And when He had called to Him His twelve disciples, He gave them authority over unclean spirits, to cast them out, and to heal all kinds of sickness and all kinds of disease.
011002 And the names of the twelve apostles are these: First, Simon, who is called Peter, and Andrew his brother; James the son of Zebedee and John his brother;
011003 Philip and Bartholomew; Thomas and Matthew the tax-collector; James the son of Alpheus, and Lebbeus, whose surname was Thaddeus;
011004 Simon the Canaanite, and Judas Iscariot, who also betrayed Him.
011005 Jesus sent out these twelve, commanding them, saying, Do not go into the way of the nations, and do not enter into any city of the Samaritans.
011006 But rather go to the lost sheep of the house of Israel.
011007 And as you go, proclaim, saying, The kingdom of Heaven is at hand.
011008 Heal the sick, cleanse the lepers, raise the dead, cast out demons. You have received freely, freely give.
011009 Do not provide gold nor silver, nor copper in your purses,
011010 nor a bag for the journey, nor two coats, nor sandals, nor staves. For the workman is worthy of his food.
011011 And into whatever city or village you enter, inquire who within it is worthy. And there abide until you go away from there.
011012 And when you come into a house, greet it.
011013 And if the house is worthy, let your peace come on it. But if it is not worthy, let your peace return to you.
011014 And whoever shall not receive you, nor hear your words, when you depart out of that house or city, shake off the dust of your feet.
011015 Truly I say to you, It shall be more tolerable for the land of Sodom and Gomorrah in the day of judgment than for that city.
011016 Behold, I send you out as sheep in the midst of wolves. Therefore be as wise as serpents and as harmless as doves.
011017 But beware of men, for they will deliver you up to the sanhedrins, and they will scourge you in their synagogues.
011018 And you shall be brought before governors and kings for My sake, for a testimony against them and the nations.
011019 But when they deliver you up, take no thought how or what you shall speak; for it shall be given you in that same hour what you shall speak.
011020 For it is not you who speak, but the Spirit of your Father who speaks in you.
011021 And brother will deliver up brother to death, and the father his child. And the children shall rise up against their parents and cause them to be put to death.
011022 And you will be hated of all men for My name's sake, but the one who endures to the end shall be kept safe.
011023 But when they persecute you in this city, flee into another; for truly I say to you, In no way shall you have finished the cities of Israel until the Son of Man comes.
011024 A disciple is not above his master, nor the servant above his lord.
011025 It is enough for the disciple that he is like his master, and the servant like his lord. If they have called the master of the house Beelzebub, how much more those of his household?
011026 Therefore do not fear them, for there is nothing covered that shall not be revealed, and nothing hidden which shall not be known.
011027 What I tell you in darkness, speak in the light; and what you hear, proclaim on the housetops.
011028 And do not fear those who kill the body, but are not able to kill the soul. But rather fear Him who can destroy both soul and body in hell.
011029 Are not two sparrows sold for an assarion? And one of them shall not fall on the ground without your Father.
011030 But even the hairs of your head are all numbered.
011031 Therefore do not fear, you are of more value than many sparrows.
011032 Then everyone who shall confess Me before men, I will confess him before My Father who is in Heaven.
011033 But whoever shall deny Me before men, I will also deny him before My Father in Heaven.
011034 Do not think that I have come to bring peace on earth. I did not come to send peace, but a sword.
011035 For I have come to set a man against his father, and the daughter against her mother, and the daughter-in-law against her mother-in-law.
011036 And a man's foes shall be those of his own household.
011037 He who loves father or mother more than Me is not worthy of Me. And he who loves son or daughter more than Me is not worthy of Me.
011038 And he who does not take up his cross and follow Me is not worthy of Me.
011039 He who finds his life shall lose it. And he who loses his life for My sake shall find it.
011040 He who receives you receives Me, and he who receives Me receives Him who sent Me.
011041 He who receives a prophet in the name of a prophet shall receive a prophet's reward. And he who receives a just one in the name of a just one will receive a just one's reward.
011042 And whoever shall give to one of these little ones a cup of cold water to drink, only in the name of a disciple, truly I say to you, He shall in no way lose his reward.
011101 And it happened, when Jesus had finished commanding His twelve disciples, He left there to teach and to proclaim in their cities.
011102 But when John heard in the prison of the works of Christ, he sent two of his disciples.
011103 And they said to Him, Are You he who should come, or do we look for another?
011104 Jesus answered and said to them, Go and tell John again those things which you hear and see:
011105 the blind receive their sight, and the lame walk; the lepers are cleansed, and the deaf hear; the dead are raised, and the poor have the gospel proclaimed to them.
011106 And blessed is he , whoever shall not be offended in Me.
011107 And as they departed, Jesus began to say to the crowds concerning John, What did you go out into the wilderness to see? A reed shaken with the wind?
011108 But what did you go out to see? A man clothed in soft clothing ? Behold, they who wear soft clothing are in kings' houses.
011109 But what did you go out to see? A prophet? Yea, I say to you, and one more excellent than a prophet.
011110 For this is the one of whom it is written, "Behold, I send My messenger before Your face, who shall prepare Your way before You."
011111 Truly I say to you, Among those who have been born of women there has not risen a greater one than John the Baptist. But the least in the kingdom of Heaven is greater than he.
011112 And from the days of John the Baptist until now the kingdom of Heaven is taken by violence, and the violent take it by force.
011113 For all the prophets and the law prophesied until John.
011114 And if you will receive it , this is Elijah who is to come.
011115 He who has ears to hear, let him hear.
011116 But to what shall I compare to this generation? It is like little children sitting in the markets and calling to their playmates,
011117 saying, We played the flute to you, and you did not dance! We mourned to you, but you did not wail!
011118 For John came neither eating nor drinking, and they say, He has a demon.
011119 The Son of man came eating and drinking, and they say, Behold a man who is a glutton and a winebibber, a friend of tax-collectors and sinners. But wisdom was justified by her children.
011120 Then He began to upbraid the cities in which most of His mighty works were done, because they did not repent.
011121 Woe to you, Chorazin! Woe to you, Bethsaida! For if the powerful acts which were done in you had been done in Tyre and Sidon, they would have repented long ago in sackcloth and ashes!
011122 But I say to you, It shall be more tolerable for Tyre and Sidon in the day of judgment than for you.
011123 And you, Capernaum, who are exalted to the heaven, shall be brought down to hell. For if the mighty works which have been done in you had been done in Sodom, it would have remained until this day.
011124 But I say to you, it shall be more tolerable for the land of Sodom in the day of judgment than for you.
011125 At that time Jesus answered and said, I thank You, O Father, Lord of Heaven and earth, because You have hidden these things from the sophisticated and cunning, and revealed them to babes.
011126 Even so, Father, for so it seemed good in Your sight.
011127 All things are delivered to Me by My Father. And no one knows the Son except the Father. Nor does anyone know the Father except the Son, and the one to whom the Son will reveal Him.
011128 Come to Me all you who labor and are heavy laden, and I will give you rest.
011129 Take My yoke on you and learn of Me, for I am meek and lowly in heart, and you shall find rest to your souls.
011130 For My yoke is easy, and My burden is light.
011201 At that time Jesus went through the grain fields on the sabbath day. And His disciples were hungry, and began to pluck the heads of grain and to eat.
011202 But when the Pharisees saw, they said to Him, Behold, your disciples do that which it is not lawful to do on the sabbath day.
011203 But He said to them, Have you not read what David did when he was hungry, and those who were with him,
011204 how he entered into the house of God and ate the showbread, which was not lawful for him to eat, nor for those who were with him, but only for the priests?
011205 Or have you not read in the Law that on the sabbath days the priests in the temple profane the sabbath and are blameless?
011206 But I say to you that One greater than the temple is in this place.
011207 But if you had known what this is, "I desire mercy and not sacrifice," you would not have condemned those who are not guilty.
011208 For the Son of man is Lord even of the sabbath.
011209 And when He had departed from there, He went into their synagogue.
011210 And behold, a man having a withered hand. And they asked Him, saying, Is it lawful to heal on the sabbaths? This so that they might accuse Him.
011211 And He said to them, What man among you will be, who will have one sheep, and if it falls into a pit on the sabbaths, will he not lay hold on it and lift it out?
011212 How much better is a man then than a sheep? Therefore it is lawful to do well on the sabbath days.
011213 Then He said to the man, Stretch out your hand. And he stretched it out, and it was restored whole like the other.
011214 Then the Pharisees went out and held council against Him, as to how they might destroy Him.
011215 But when Jesus knew it , He withdrew Himself from there. And great crowds followed Him, and He healed them all.
011216 And He warned them that they not make Him known,
011217 so that it might be fulfilled which was spoken by Isaiah the prophet, saying,
011218 "Behold My Child whom I have chosen; My Beloved, in whom My soul is well pleased. I will put My Spirit on Him, and He shall declare judgment to the nations.
011219 He shall not strive, nor cry, nor shall any one hear His voice in the streets.
011220 He will not break a bruised reed, and He will not quench a smoking wick, until He sends out judgment to victory.
011221 And in His name the nations shall trust."
011222 Then one who had been demon-possessed was brought to Him, blind and dumb. And He healed him, so much so that the blind and dumb one both spoke and saw.
011223 And all the people were amazed and said, Is not this the son of David?
011224 But when the Pharisees heard, they said, This one does not cast out demons except by Beelzebub the ruler of the demons.
011225 And Jesus knew their thoughts and said to them, Every kingdom divided against itself is brought to desolation. And every city or house divided against itself shall not stand.
011226 And if Satan casts out Satan, he is divided against himself; how then shall his kingdom stand?
011227 But if I cast out demons by Beelzebub, by whom do your sons cast them out? Therefore they shall be your judges.
011228 But if I cast out demons by the Spirit of God, then the kingdom of God has come to you.
011229 Or else how can one enter into a strong man's house and spoil his goods, unless first he binds the strong one, and then he will plunder his house.
011230 The one who is not with Me is against Me, and the one who does not gather with Me scatters.
011231 Therefore I say to you, All kinds of sin and blasphemy shall be forgiven to men, but the blasphemy against the Holy Spirit shall not be forgiven to men.
011232 And whoever speaks a word against the Son of man, it shall be forgiven him. But whoever speaks against the Holy Spirit, it shall not be forgiven him, either in this world or in the world to come.
011233 Either make the tree good and its fruit good, or else make the tree corrupt and its fruit corrupt; for the tree is known by its fruit.
011234 Offspring of vipers! How can you, being evil, speak good things? For out of the abundance of the heart the mouth speaks.
011235 A good man out of the good treasure of the heart brings out good things; and an evil man out of the evil treasure brings out evil things.
011236 But I say to you that every idle word, whatever men may speak, they shall give account of it in the day of judgment.
011237 For by your words you shall be justified, and by your words you shall be condemned.
011238 Then certain of the scribes and of the Pharisees answered, saying, Master, we want to see a sign from you.
011239 But He answered and said to them, An evil and adulterous generation seeks after a sign. And there shall be no sign given to it except the sign of the prophet Jonah.
011240 For as Jonah was three days and three nights in the belly of the huge fish, so the Son of man shall be three days and three nights in the heart of the earth.
011241 The men of Nineveh shall rise in judgment with this generation, and shall condemn it, because they repented at the proclaiming of Jonah, and behold, One greater than Jonah is here.
011242 The queen of the south shall rise up in the Judgment with this generation, and shall condemn it, for she came from the uttermost parts of the earth to hear the wisdom of Solomon, and behold, One greater than Solomon is here.
011243 When the unclean spirit has gone out of a man, he walks through dry places seeking rest, and finds none.
011244 Then he said, I will return into my house from where I came out. And when he has come, he finds it empty, swept, and decorated.
011245 Then he goes and takes with him seven other spirits more evil than himself, and they enter in and live there. And the last state of that man is worse than the first. Even so it also shall be to this evil generation.
011246 But while He yet talked with the people, behold, His mother and His brothers stood outside, desiring to speak with Him.
011247 Then one said to Him, Behold, Your mother and Your brothers stand outside, desiring to speak with You.
011248 And He answered and said to him who told Him, Who is My mother? And who are My brothers?
011249 And He stretched out His hand toward His disciples and said, Behold, My mother and My brothers!
011250 For whoever shall do the will of My Father in Heaven, the same is My brother and sister and mother.
011301 In that day Jesus went out of the house and sat by the seaside.
011302 And great crowds were gathered to Him, so that He went into a boat and sat. And all the crowd stood on the shore.
011303 And He spoke many things to them in parables, saying, Behold, the sower went out to sow.
011304 And as he sowed, some seeds fell by the wayside, and the birds came and devoured them.
011305 Some fell on stony places, where they did not have much earth. And they sprang up immediately, because they had no deepness of earth.
011306 And the sun rising, they were scorched, and because they had no root, they withered away.
011307 And some fell among thorns. And the thorns sprung up and choked them.
011308 And some fell on the good ground and yielded fruit, indeed one a hundredfold, and one sixty, and one thirty.
011309 He who has ears to hear, let him hear.
011310 And the disciples said to Him, Why do You speak to them in parables?
011311 He answered and said to them, Because it is given to you to know the mysteries of the kingdom of Heaven, but it is not given to them.
011312 For whoever has, to him shall be given, and he shall have more abundance. But whoever does not have, from him shall be taken away even that which he has.
011313 Therefore I speak to them in parables, because seeing they see not, and hearing they hear not; nor do they understand.
011314 And in them is fulfilled the prophecy of Isaiah which said, "By hearing you shall hear and shall not understand; and seeing you shall see and shall not perceive;
011315 for this people's heart has become gross, and their ears are dull of hearing, and they have closed their eyes, lest at any time they should see with their eyes and hear with their ears and should understand with their heart, and should be converted, and I should heal them."
011316 But blessed are your eyes, for they see; and your ears, for they hear.
011317 For truly I say to you that many prophets and righteous men have desired to see those things which you see, and have not seen them; and to hear what you hear, and have not heard them.
011318 Therefore hear the parable of the sower.
011319 When anyone hears the Word of the kingdom and does not understand it, then the wicked one comes and catches away that which was sown in his heart. This is the seed sown by the wayside.
011320 But that which was sown on the stony places is this: he who hears the Word and immediately receives it with joy.
011321 But he has no root in himself, and is temporary. For when tribulation or persecution arises on account of the word, he immediately stumbles.
011322 And that sown into the thorns is this: he who hears the Word; and the anxiety of this world, and the deceit of riches, choke the Word, and he becomes unfruitful.
011323 But that sown on the good ground is this: he who hears the Word and understands; who also bears fruit and produces one truly a hundredfold; and one sixty; and one thirty.
011324 He put out another parable to them, saying, The kingdom of heaven is compared to a man who sowed good seed in his field.
011325 But while men slept, his enemy came and sowed darnel among the wheat and went his way.
011326 But when the blade had sprung up and had produced fruit, then the darnel also appeared.
011327 So the servants of the householder came and said to him, Sir, did you not sow good seed in your field? Then where have the darnel come from?
011328 He said to them, An enemy has done this. The servants said to him, Then do you want us to go and gather them up?
011329 But he said, No, lest while you gather up the darnel you also root up the wheat with them.
011330 Let both grow together until the harvest. And in the time of harvest I will say to the reapers, First gather together the darnel and bind them in bundles to burn them, but gather the wheat into my granary.
011331 He put out another parable to them, saying, The kingdom of Heaven is like a grain of mustard seed, which a man took and sowed in his field;
011332 which indeed is the least of all seeds, but when it is grown it is the greatest among herbs and becomes a tree, so that the birds of the air come and lodge in its branches.
011333 He spoke another parable to them: The kingdom of Heaven is like leaven, which a woman took and hid in three measures of meal until the whole was leavened.
011334 Jesus spoke all these things to the crowds in parables, and He did not speak to them without a parable,
011335 so that it might be fulfilled which was spoken by the prophet, saying, "I will open my mouth in parables; I will utter things which have been kept secret from the foundation of the world."
011336 Then sending the crowds away, Jesus went into the house. And His disciples came to Him, saying, Explain to us the parable of the darnel of the field.
011337 He answered and said to them, He who sows the good seed is the Son of man;
011338 the field is the world; the good seed are the sons of the kingdom; but the darnel are the sons of the evil one .
011339 The enemy who sowed them is the Devil; the harvest is the end of the world; and the reapers are the angels.
011340 Therefore as the darnel are gathered and burned in the fire, so it shall be in the end of this world.
011341 The Son of man shall send out His angels, and they shall gather out of His kingdom all things that offend, and those who do iniquity,
011342 and shall cast them into a furnace of fire. There shall be wailing and gnashing of teeth.
011343 Then the righteous shall shine out like the sun in the kingdom of their Father. He who has ears to hear, let him hear.
011344 Again, the kingdom of Heaven is like treasure hidden in a field, which when a man has found it, he hides it, and for the joy of it goes and sells all that he has, and buys that field.
011345 Again, the kingdom of Heaven is like a merchant seeking beautiful pearls;
011346 who, when he had found one pearl of great price, went and sold all that he had, and bought it.
011347 Again, the kingdom of Heaven is like a net that was cast into the sea, and gathered some of every kind;
011348 which, when it was full, they drew to shore, and sat down and gathered the good into vessels, but threw the bad away.
011349 So it shall be at the end of the world. The angels shall come out and separate the wicked from among the just,
011350 and shall cast them into the furnace of fire. There shall be wailing and gnashing of teeth.
011351 Jesus said to them, Have you understood all these things? They said to Him, Yes, Lord.
011352 Then He said to them, Therefore every scribe who is instructed to the kingdom of Heaven is like a man who is a householder, who brings out things new and old out of his treasure.
011353 And it happened when Jesus finished these parables, He departed from there.
011354 And when He had come into His own country, He taught them in their synagogue, so much so that they were astonished and said, From where does this man have this wisdom and these mighty works?
011355 Is not this the carpenter's son? Is not his mother called Mary? And his brothers, James and Joses and Simon and Judas,
011356 and his sisters, are they not all with us? Then from where does this man have all these things?
011357 And they were offended in Him. But Jesus said to them, A prophet is not without honor, except in his own country and in his own house.
011358 And He did not do many mighty works there because of their unbelief.
011401 At that time Herod the tetrarch heard of the fame of Jesus
011402 and said to his servants, This is John the Baptist. He has risen from the dead, and therefore the powerful works are working in him.
011403 For Herod had laid hold on John, and had bound him, and had put him in prison because of Herodias his brother Philip's wife.
011404 For John said to him, It is not lawful for you to have her.
011405 And when he desired to put him to death, he feared the multitude, because they counted him as a prophet.
011406 But when Herod's birthday was kept, the daughter of Herodias danced before them and pleased Herod.
011407 So he promised with an oath to give her whatever she would ask.
011408 And she, being instructed before by her mother, said, Give me John the Baptist's head here on a platter.
011409 And the king was sorry. But for the oath's sake, and those reclining with him , he commanded it to be given.
011410 And he sent and beheaded John in the prison.
011411 And his head was brought on a platter and given to the girl. And she brought it to her mother.
011412 And his disciples came and took up the body and buried it, and went and told Jesus.
011413 When Jesus heard, He departed from there by boat into a deserted place apart. And hearing, the crowds followed Him on foot out of the cities.
011414 And Jesus went out and saw a great crowd, and He was moved with compassion toward them. And He healed their sick.
011415 And evening coming on, His disciples came to Him, saying, The place is deserted and the time has already gone by. Send the crowd away so that they may go into the villages and buy food for themselves.
011416 But Jesus said to them, They do not need to leave, you give them something to eat.
011417 And they said to Him, We have here only five loaves and two fish.
011418 And He said, Bring them here to Me.
011419 And He commanded the crowd to recline on the grass. And He took the five loaves and the two fish, and looking up to Heaven He blessed and broke, and gave the loaves to His disciples. And the disciples gave to the crowd.
011420 And they all ate and were filled. And they took up twelve hand baskets full from the fragments that remained.
011421 And they who had eaten were about five thousand men, besides women and children.
011422 And immediately Jesus constrained His disciples to get into a boat and to go before Him to the other side, while He sent the crowds away.
011423 And when He had sent the crowds away, He went up into a mountain apart to pray. And when evening had come, He was there alone.
011424 But the boat was now in the midst of the sea, tossed with waves; for the wind was against them.
011425 And in the fourth watch of the night Jesus went to them, walking on the sea.
011426 And when the disciples saw Him walking on the sea, they were troubled, saying, It is a phantom! And they cried out for fear.
011427 But immediately Jesus spoke to them, saying, Be of good cheer, I AM! Do not fear.
011428 And Peter answered Him and said, LORD, if it is You, tell me to come to You on the water.
011429 And He said, Come. And when Peter had come down out of the boat, he walked on the water to go to Jesus.
011430 But seeing that the wind was strong, he was afraid. And beginning to sink, he cried, saying, Lord, save me!
011431 And immediately Jesus stretched out His hand and caught him; and said to him, Little-faith! Why did you doubt?
011432 And when they had come into the boat, the wind ceased.
011433 And those in the boat came and worshiped Him, saying, Truly You are the Son of God.
011434 And when they had passed over, they came to the land of Gennesaret.
011435 And recognizing Him, the men of that place sent to all that neighborhood, and brought to Him all who were diseased.
011436 And they begged Him that they might only touch the hem of His robe. And as many as touched were made perfectly whole.
011501 Then the scribes and Pharisees who were from Jerusalem came to Jesus, saying,
011502 Why do your disciples transgress the tradition of the elders? For they do not wash their hands when they eat bread.
011503 But He answered and said to them, Why do you also transgress the commandment of God by your tradition?
011504 For God commanded, saying, "Honor your father and mother"; and, "He who speaks evil of father or mother, let him die by death."
011505 But you say, Whoever says to his father or mother, Whatever you would gain from me, It is a gift to God;
011506 and in no way he honors his father or his mother. And you voided the commandment of God by your tradition.
011507 Hypocrites! Well did Isaiah prophesy of you, saying,
011508 "This people draws near to Me with their mouth, and honors Me with their lips, but their heart is far from Me.
011509 But in vain they worship Me, teaching for doctrines the commandments of men."
011510 And He called the crowd and said to them, Hear and understand.
011511 Not that which goes into the mouth defiles a man; but that which comes out of the mouth, this defiles a man.
011512 Then His disciples came and said to Him, Do You know that the Pharisees were offended when they heard this saying?
011513 But He answered and said, Every plant which My heavenly Father has not planted shall be rooted up.
011514 Let them alone. They are blind leaders of the blind. And if the blind lead the blind, both shall fall into the ditch.
011515 Then Peter answered and said to Him, Explain this parable to us.
011516 And Jesus said, Are you also still without understanding?
011517 Do you not yet understand that whatever enters in at the mouth goes into the belly, and is cast out into the waste-bowl?
011518 But the things which come out of the mouth come from the heart, and they defile the man.
011519 For out of the heart come evil thoughts, murders, adulteries, fornications, thefts, false witness, blasphemies;
011520 these are the things which defile a man, but to eat with unwashed hands does not defile a man.
011521 And going out from there, Jesus withdrew to the parts of Tyre and Sidon.
011522 And behold, a woman of Canaan coming out of these borders cried to Him, saying, Have mercy on me, O Lord, Son of David! My daughter is grievously vexed with a demon.
011523 But He did not answer her a word. And His disciples came and begged Him, saying, Send her away, for she cries after us.
011524 But He answered and said, I am not sent except to the lost sheep of the house of Israel.
011525 Then she came and worshiped Him, saying, Lord, help me!
011526 But He answered and said, It is not good to take the children's bread and to throw it to dogs.
011527 And she said, True, O Lord; but even the little dogs eat of the crumbs which fall from their masters' tables.
011528 Then Jesus answered and said to her, O woman, great is your faith! So be it to you even as you wish. And her daughter was healed from that very hour.
011529 And moving from there Jesus came beside the Sea of Galilee. And He went up into a mountain and sat there.
011530 And great crowds came to Him, having with them the lame, blind, dumb, maimed, and many others. And they cast them down at Jesus' feet. And He healed them,
011531 so much so that the crowd wondered when they saw the dumb speak, the maimed sound, the lame walk, and the blind see. And they glorified the God of Israel.
011532 Then Jesus called His disciples and said, I have compassion on the crowd because they continue with Me for three days now and have nothing to eat. And I will not send them away fasting, lest they faint in the way.
011533 And His disciples said to Him, From where should we get so many loaves in the wilderness, so as to fill so great a crowd?
011534 And Jesus said to them, How many loaves do you have? And they said, Seven, and a few little fish.
011535 And He commanded the crowd to sit on the ground.
011536 And He took the seven loaves and the fish, and gave thanks, and broke, and gave to His disciples. And the disciples gave to the crowd.
011537 And they all ate, and were filled; and they took up seven lunch baskets full of the pieces that was left.
011538 And those who ate were four thousand men, besides women and children.
011539 And sending the crowd away, He went into the boat and came into the borders of Magdala.
011601 The Pharisees and the Sadducees came to Him, tempting Him. And they asked Him that He would show them a sign from Heaven.
011602 He answered and said to them, When it is evening, you say, Fair weather; for the sky is red.
011603 And in the morning, Foul weather today; for the sky is red and gloomy. Hypocrites! You can discern the face of the sky, but you cannot see the signs of the times!
011604 A wicked and adulterous generation seeks after a sign. And there shall no sign be given to it, except the sign of the prophet Jonah. And He left them and went away.
011605 And when His disciples had come to the other side, they forgot to take loaves.
011606 And Jesus said to them, Take heed, and beware the leaven of the Pharisees and of the Sadducees.
011607 And they reasoned among themselves, saying, It is because we have taken no loaves.
011608 And knowing Jesus said to them, Why do you reason among yourselves because you took no loaves, little-faiths?
011609 Do you not yet understand, nor remember the five loaves of the five thousand, and how many hand baskets you took up;
011610 nor the seven loaves of the four thousand, and how many lunch baskets you took up?
011611 How is it that you do not understand that I did not speak to you about loaves, but to beware of the leaven of the Pharisees and of the Sadducees?
011612 Then they understood that He did not say to beware of the leaven of bread, but of the doctrine of the Pharisees and Sadducees.
011613 And coming into the parts of Caesarea Philippi, Jesus asked His disciples, saying, Who do men say Me to be, the Son of man?
011614 And they said, Some say , John the Baptist; some, Elijah; and others, Jeremiah, or one of the prophets.
011615 He said to them, But who do you say I am?
011616 And Simon Peter answered and said, You are the Christ, the Son of the living God.
011617 Jesus answered and said to him, You are blessed, Simon, son of Jonah, for flesh and blood did not reveal it to you, but My Father in Heaven.
011618 And I also say to you that you are Peter, and on this rock I will build My church, and the gates of hell shall not prevail against it.
011619 And I will give the keys of the kingdom of Heaven to you. And whatever you may bind on earth shall occur, having been bound in Heaven, and whatever you may loose on earth shall occur, having been loosed in Heaven.
011620 Then He warned His disciples that they should tell no one that He was Jesus the Christ.
011621 From that time Jesus began to show His disciples that He must go to Jerusalem and suffer many things from the elders and chief priests and scribes, and be killed, and be raised again the third day.
011622 Then Peter took Him and began to rebuke Him, saying, God be gracious to You, Lord! This shall never be to You.
011623 But He turned and said to Peter, Go, Satan! You are an offense to Me, for you do not savor the things that are of God, but those that are of men.
011624 Then Jesus said to His disciples, If anyone desires to come after Me, let him deny himself and take up his cross and follow Me.
011625 For whoever desires to save his life shall lose it, and whoever desires to lose his life for My sake shall find it.
011626 For what is a man profited if he shall gain the whole world and lose his own soul? Or what shall a man give in exchange for his soul?
011627 For the Son of man shall come in the glory of His Father with His angels, and then He shall reward each one according to his works.
011628 Truly I say to you, There are some standing here who shall not taste of death until they see the Son of man coming in His kingdom.
011701 And after six days Jesus took Peter, James, and John his brother, and brought them up into a high mountain apart.
011702 And He was transfigured before them. And His face shone as the sun, and His clothing was white as the light.
011703 And behold, there appeared to them Moses and Elijah talking with Him.
011704 And Peter answered and said to Jesus, Lord, it is good for us to be here. If You will, let us make here three tabernacles; one for You, and one for Moses, and one for Elijah.
011705 While he yet spoke, behold, a bright cloud overshadowed them. And behold a voice out of the cloud which said, This is My beloved Son in whom I am well pleased, hear Him.
011706 And when the disciples heard, they fell on their face and were greatly terrified.
011707 And Jesus came and touched them, and said, Arise and do not be terrified.
011708 And lifting up their eyes, they saw no one except Jesus alone.
011709 And as they came down from the mountain, Jesus commanded them, saying, Tell the vision to no one until the Son of man has risen from the dead.
011710 And His disciples asked Him, saying, Why then do the scribes say that Elijah must come first?
011711 And answering Jesus said to them, Elijah truly shall come first and restore all things.
011712 But I say to you that Elijah has come already, and they did not know him, but have done to him whatever they desired. Likewise also the Son of man shall suffer from them.
011713 Then His disciples understood that He spoke to them about John the Baptist.
011714 And when they came to the crowd, a man came to Him, kneeling down to Him and saying,
011715 Lord, have mercy on my son, for he is a lunatic and grievously vexed; for oftentimes he falls into the fire, and often into the water.
011716 And I brought him to Your disciples, and they could not cure him.
011717 Then Jesus answered and said, O faithless and perverse generation, how long shall I be with you? How long shall I suffer you? Bring him here to Me.
011718 And Jesus rebuked the demon, and he departed out of him. And the child was cured from that very hour.
011719 Then the disciples came to Jesus apart, and said, Why could we not cast him out?
011720 And Jesus said to them, Because of your unbelief. For truly I say to you, If you have faith like a grain of mustard seed, you shall say to this mountain, Move from here to there. And it shall move. And nothing shall be impossible to you.
011721 However, this kind does not go out except by prayer and fasting.
011722 And while they stayed in Galilee, Jesus said to them, The Son of man shall be betrayed into the hands of men.
011723 And they will kill Him, and the third day He will be raised again. And they grieved exceedingly.
011724 And when they had come to Capernaum, those who received the didrachmas came to Peter and said, Does your master not pay the didrachmas?
011725 He said, Yes. And when he had come into the house, Jesus anticipated him, saying, What do you think, Simon? From whom do the kings of the earth take custom or tribute? From their sons, or from strangers?
011726 Peter said to Him, From strangers. Jesus said to him, Then truly the sons are free.
011727 But lest we should offend them, go to the sea and cast a hook, and take up the first fish that comes up. And when you have opened its mouth, you shall find a stater; take that, and give it to them for Me and you.
011801 At that hour the disciples came to Jesus, saying, Who is the greater in the kingdom of Heaven?
011802 And Jesus called a little child to Him and set him in their midst,
011803 and said, Truly I say to you, Unless you are converted and become as little children, you shall not enter into the kingdom of Heaven.
011804 Therefore whoever shall humble himself like this little child, this one is the greater in the kingdom of Heaven.
011805 And whoever shall receive one such little child in My name receives Me.
011806 But whoever shall offend one of these little ones who believes in Me, it would be better for him that an ass's millstone were hung around his neck, and he be sunk in the depth of the sea.
011807 Woe to the world because of offenses! For it is necessary that offenses come; but woe to that man by whom the offense comes!
011808 And if your hand or your foot causes you to offend, cut them off and throw them from you. It is better for you to enter into life lame or maimed, rather than having two hands or two feet to be cast into everlasting fire.
011809 And if your eye offends you, pluck it out and throw it from you. It is better for you to enter into life with one eye, rather than having two eyes to be cast into the hell of fire.
011810 Take heed that you do not despise one of these little ones . For I say to you that in Heaven their angels always behold the face of My Father in Heaven.
011811 For the Son of man has come to save that which was lost.
011812 What do you think? If a man has a hundred sheep and one of them strays, does he not leave the ninety and nine and go into the mountains and seek the straying one?
011813 And if it happens that he finds it, truly I say to you, he rejoices more over it than over the ninety and nine which did not stray.
011814 Even so it is not the will of your Father in Heaven that one of these little ones should perish.
011815 But if your brother shall trespass against you, go and tell him his fault between you and him alone. If he hears you, you have gained your brother.
011816 But if he will not hear you , take one or two more with you, so that in the mouth of two or three witnesses every word may be established.
011817 And if he shall neglect to hear them, tell it to the church. But if he neglects to hear the church, let him be to you as a heathen and a tax-collector.
011818 Truly I say to you, Whatever you shall bind on earth shall occur, having been bound in Heaven; and whatever you shall loose on earth shall occur, having been loosed in Heaven.
011819 Again I say to you that if two of you shall agree on earth as regarding anything that they shall ask, it shall be done for them by My Father in Heaven.
011820 For where two or three are gathered together in My name, there I am in their midst.
011821 Then Peter came to Him and said, Lord, how often shall my brother sin against me and I forgive him? Until seven times?
011822 Jesus said to him, I do not say to you, Until seven times; but, Until seventy times seven.
011823 Therefore the kingdom of Heaven has been compared to a certain king who desired to make an accounting with his servants.
011824 And when he had begun to count, one was brought to him who owed him ten thousand talents.
011825 But as he had nothing to pay, his lord commanded that he, and his wife and children, and all that he had, be sold, and payment be made.
011826 Then the servant fell down and worshiped him, saying, Lord, have patience with me and I will pay you all.
011827 Then the lord of that servant was moved with compassion and released him and forgave him the debt.
011828 But the same servant went out and found one of his fellow servants who owed him a hundred denarii. And he laid hands on him and took him by the throat, saying, Pay me what you owe.
011829 And his fellow servant fell down at his feet and begged him, saying, Have patience with me and I will pay you all.
011830 And he would not, but went and cast him into prison until he should pay the debt.
011831 So when his fellow servants saw what was done, they were very sorry. And they came and told their lord all that was done.
011832 Then his lord, after he had called him, said to him, O wicked servant, I forgave you all that debt because you begged me.
011833 Should you not also have pitied your fellow servant, even as I had pity on you?
011834 And his lord was angry, and delivered him to the tormentors until he should pay all that was due to him.
011835 So likewise shall My heavenly Father do also to you, unless each one of you from your hearts forgive his brother their trespasses.
011901 And it happened, when Jesus had finished these sayings, that He departed from Galilee and came into the borders of Judea beyond Jordan.
011902 And great crowds followed Him. And He healed them there.
011903 And the Pharisees came to Him, tempting Him and saying to Him, Is it lawful for a man to put away his wife for every cause?
011904 And He answered and said to them, Have you not read that He who made them at the beginning "made them male and female",
011905 and said, For this cause a man shall leave father and mother and shall cling to his wife, and the two of them shall be one flesh?
011906 Therefore they are no longer two, but one flesh. Therefore what God has joined together, let not man separate.
011907 They said to Him, Why did Moses then command to give a bill of divorce and to put her away?
011908 He said to them, Because of your hard-heartedness Moses allowed you to put away your wives; but from the beginning it was not so.
011909 And I say to you, Whoever shall put away his wife, except for fornication, and shall marry another, commits adultery; and whoever marries her who is put away commits adultery.
011910 His disciples said to Him, If this is the case of the man with his wife, it is not good to marry.
011911 But He said to them, Not all receive this word, except those to whom it is given.
011912 For there are some eunuchs who were born so from their mother's womb; and there are eunuchs who were made eunuchs by men; and there are eunuchs who have made themselves eunuchs for the kingdom of Heaven's sake. He who is able to receive it , let him receive it.
011913 Then little children were brought to Him, that He should put His hands on them and pray. And the disciples rebuked them.
011914 But Jesus said, Allow the little children to come to Me, and do not forbid them; for of such is the kingdom of Heaven.
011915 And He laid His hands on them, and departed from there.
011916 And behold, one came and said to Him, Good Master, what good thing shall I do that I may have eternal life?
011917 And He said to him, Why do you call Me good? There is none good but one, that is, God. But if you want to enter into life, keep the commandments.
011918 He said to Him, Which? Jesus said, You shall not murder, you shall not commit adultery, you shall not steal, you shall not bear false witness,
011919 honor your father and mother, and, you shall love your neighbor as yourself.
011920 The young man said to Him, I have kept all these things from my youth up; what do I lack yet?
011921 Jesus said to him, If you want to be perfect, go, sell what you have and give to the poor, and you shall have treasure in Heaven. And come, follow Me.
011922 But when the young man heard that saying, he went away sorrowful; for he had great possessions.
011923 Then Jesus said to His disciples, Truly I say to you that a rich man will with great difficulty enter into the kingdom of Heaven.
011924 And again I say to you, It is easier for a camel to go through the eye of a needle than for a rich man to enter into the kingdom of God.
011925 When His disciples heard, they were exceedingly amazed, saying, Who then can be saved?
011926 But Jesus looked on them and said to them, With men this is impossible, but with God all things are possible.
011927 Then answering Peter said to Him, Behold, we have forsaken all and have followed You. Therefore what shall we have?
011928 And Jesus said to them, Truly I say to you that you who have followed Me, in the regeneration, when the Son of man shall sit in the throne of His glory, you also shall sit on twelve thrones, judging the twelve tribes of Israel.
011929 And everyone who left houses, or brothers, or sisters, or father, or mother, or wife, or children, or lands, for My name's sake, shall receive a hundredfold, and shall inherit everlasting life.
011930 But many who are first shall be last; and the last shall be first.
012001 For the kingdom of Heaven is like a man, a housemaster, who went out early in the morning to hire laborers into his vineyard.
012002 And when he had agreed with the laborers for a denarius a day, he sent them into his vineyard.
012003 And he went out about the third hour and saw others standing idle in the marketplace.
