012004 And he said to them, You also go into the vineyard, and whatever is right I will give you. And they went.
012005 And he went out about the sixth and ninth hour and did likewise.
012006 And about the eleventh hour he went out and found others standing idle, and said to them, Why do you stand here all day idle?
012007 They said to him, Because no one has hired us. He said to them, You also go into the vineyard, and you shall receive whatever is right.
012008 So when evening had come, the lord of the vineyard said to his steward, Call the laborers and pay them their wage, beginning from the last to the first.
012009 And when they who were hired about the eleventh hour came, they each one received a denarius.
012010 But when the first came, they supposed that they would received more; and they also each one received a denarius.
012011 And receiving it they murmured against the master of the house,
012012 saying, These last have worked only one hour, and you have made them equal to us who have borne the burden and heat of the day.
012013 But he answered one of them and said, Friend, I do you no wrong. Did you not agree with me for a denarius?
012014 Take yours, and go; I will give to this last one the same as to you.
012015 Is it not lawful for me to do what I want with my own? Is your eye evil because I am good?
012016 So the last shall be first, and the first last, for many are called, but few are chosen.
012017 And going up to Jerusalem, Jesus took the twelve disciples apart in the way, and said to them,
012018 Behold, we go up to Jerusalem. And the Son of man shall be betrayed to the chief priests and to the scribes, and they shall condemn Him to death.
012019 And they shall deliver Him to the nations to mock and to scourge and to crucify. And the third day He shall rise again.
012020 Then the mother of Zebedee's children came to Him with her sons, worshiping and desiring a certain thing from Him.
012021 And He said to her, What do you desire? She said to Him, Grant that these my two sons may sit in Your kingdom, the one on Your right hand and the other on the left.
012022 But Jesus answered and said, You do not know what you ask. Are you able to drink of the cup that I shall drink of, and to be baptized with the baptism that I am baptized with? They said to Him, We are able.
012023 And He said to them, You shall indeed drink of My cup and be baptized with the baptism that I am baptized with; but to sit on My right hand and on My left is not Mine to give, but to those for whom it has been prepared by My Father.
012024 And when the ten heard it , they were indignant concerning the two brothers.
012025 But Jesus called them and said, You know that the rulers of the nations exercise dominion over them, and they who are great exercise authority over them.
012026 However, it shall not be so among you. But whoever desires to be great among you, let him be your servant.
012027 And whoever desires to be chief among you, let him be your servant;
012028 even as the Son of man did not come to be served, but to serve, and to give His life a ransom for many.
012029 And as they departed from Jericho, a great crowd followed Him.
012030 And behold, two blind men were sitting by the wayside. When they heard that Jesus passed by, they cried out, saying, Have mercy on us, O Lord, Son of David!
012031 And the crowd rebuked them, saying that they should be silent. But they cried the more, saying, Have mercy on us, O Lord, Son of David!
012032 And Jesus stood still and called them, and said, What do you desire that I should do to you?
012033 They said to Him, Lord, that our eyes may be opened.
012034 So Jesus had compassion on them and touched their eyes. And immediately their eyes received sight, and they followed Him.
012101 And when they drew near Jerusalem, and had come to Bethphage, to the Mount of Olives, then Jesus sent two disciples,
012102 saying to them, Go into the village across from you. And immediately you will find an ass tied, and a colt with her. Untie them and bring them to Me.
012103 And if anyone says anything to you, you shall say, The Lord has need of them, and immediately He will send them.
012104 All this was done so that it might be fulfilled which was spoken by the prophet, saying,
012105 "Tell the daughter of Zion, Behold, your King comes to you, meek, and sitting on an ass, even a colt the foal of an ass."
012106 And the disciples went and did as Jesus commanded them.
012107 And they brought the ass, even the colt, and put their clothes on them, and He sat on them.
012108 And a very great crowd spread their garments in the way. Others cut down branches from the trees and spread them in the way.
012109 And the crowds who went before, and those who followed, cried out, saying, Hosanna to the Son of David! Blessed is He who comes in the name of the Lord! Hosanna in the highest!
012110 And when He had come into Jerusalem, all the city was moved, saying, Who is this?
012111 And the crowd said, This is Jesus the prophet, from Nazareth of Galilee.
012112 And Jesus went into the temple of God and cast out all those who sold and bought in the temple, and overthrew the tables of the money-changers, and the seats of those who sold doves.
012113 And He said to them, It is written, "My house shall be called the house of prayer"; but you have made it a den of thieves.
012114 And the blind and the lame came to Him in the temple, and He healed them.
012115 And when the chief priests and scribes saw the wonderful things which He did, and the children crying in the temple, and saying, Hosanna to the Son of David, they were angry.
012116 And they said to Him, Do you hear what these say? And Jesus said to them, Yes, have you never read, "Out of the mouth of babes and sucklings You have perfected praise?"
012117 And leaving them, He went out of the city to Bethany, and spent the night there.
012118 And returning early to the city, He hungered.
012119 And seeing a fig tree in the way, He came to it and found nothing on it except leaves only. And He said to it, let no fruit grow on you forever. And immediately the fig tree withered away.
012120 And when the disciples saw, they marveled, saying, How quickly the fig tree has withered away!
012121 Jesus answered and said to them, Truly I say to you, If you have faith and do not doubt, you shall not only do this miracle of the fig tree, but also; if you shall say to this mountain, Be moved and be thrown into the sea; it shall be done.
012122 And all things, whatever you shall ask in prayer, believing, you shall receive.
012123 And when He had come into the temple, the chief priests and the elders of the people came to Him as He was teaching, and said, By what authority do you do these things? And who gave you this authority?
012124 And Jesus answered and said to them, I will also ask you one thing; which if you tell Me, I likewise will tell you by what authority I do these things.
012125 The baptism of John, where was it from? From Heaven or from men? And they reasoned within themselves, saying, If we shall say, From Heaven, he will say to us, Why then did you not believe him?
012126 But if we shall say From men, we fear the people; for all consider John as a prophet.
012127 And they answered Jesus and said, We cannot tell. And He said to them, Neither do I tell you by what authority I do these things.
012128 But what do you think? A man had two sons; and he came to the first and said, Son, go work in my vineyard today.
012129 He answered and said, I will not. But afterwards he repented and went.
012130 And he came to the second and said likewise. And he answered and said, I go , sir; and did not go.
012131 Which of the two did the will of his father? They said to Him, The first. Jesus said to them, Truly I say to you that the tax-collectors and the harlots go into the kingdom of God before you.
012132 For John came to you in the way of righteousness, and you did not believe him. But the tax-collectors and the harlots believed him. And when you had seen it , you did not repent afterwards so that you might believe him.
012133 Hear another parable. There was a certain housemaster who planted a vineyard and hedged it round about, and dug a winepress in it, and built a tower, and rented it to vinedressers, and went into a far country.
012134 And when the season of the fruits drew near, he sent his servants to the vinedressers to receive its fruits.
012135 And the vinedressers took his servants, and beat one, and killed another, and stoned another.
012136 Again he sent other servants, more than the first, and they did the same to them.
012137 But last of all he sent his son to them, saying, They will respect my son.
012138 But when the vinedressers saw the son, they said among themselves, This is the heir. Come, let us kill him, and get hold of his inheritance.
012139 And taking him, they threw him out of the vineyard and killed him .
012140 Therefore when the lord of the vineyard comes, what will he do to those vinedressers?
012141 They said to Him, Bad men! He will miserably destroy them and will rent out his vineyard to other vinedressers who will give him the fruits in their seasons.
012142 Jesus said to them, Did you never read in the Scriptures, "The stone which the builders rejected, this One has become the head of the corner; this is the Lord's doing, and it is marvelous in our eyes?"
012143 Therefore I say to you, The kingdom of God shall be taken from you and given to a nation bringing out its fruits.
012144 And he who falls on this Stone shall be broken, but on whomever it shall fall, it will grind him to powder.
012145 And when the chief priests and Pharisees heard His parables, they knew that He spoke of them.
012146 But seeking to lay hands on Him, they feared the crowd, because they held Him for a prophet.
012201 And Jesus answered and spoke to them again by parables, and said,
012202 The kingdom of Heaven is like a certain king who made a marriage for his son.
012203 And he sent out his servants to call those who were invited to the wedding; and they would not come.
012204 Again he sent out other servants, saying, Tell those who are invited, Behold, I have prepared my dinner; my oxen and fatlings are killed, and all things are ready. Come to the marriage.
012205 But not caring, they went their ways, one to his field, another to his trading.
012206 And the rest took his servants and treated them spitefully, and killed them .
012207 But when the king heard, he was angry. And he sent out his armies and destroyed those murderers, and burned up their city.
012208 Then he said to his servants, The wedding is ready, but they who were invited were not worthy.
012209 Therefore go into the exits of the highways, and as many as you shall find, invite them to the marriage.
012210 So the servants went out into the highways and gathered together as many as they found, both bad and good. And the wedding was filled with reclining guests.
012211 And the king coming in to look over the guests, he saw a man there who did not have on a wedding garment.
012212 And he said to him, Friend, how did you come in here without having a wedding garment? And he was speechless.
012213 Then the king said to the servants, Bind him hand and foot and take him away, and cast him into outer darkness. There shall be weeping and gnashing of teeth.
012214 For many are called, but few chosen.
012215 Then the Pharisees left and took counsel that they might entangle Him in words.
012216 And they sent their disciples out to Him along with the Herodians, saying, Master, we know that you are true, and that you teach the way of God in truth. Nor do you care for anyone, for you do not regard the person of men.
012217 Therefore tell us; what do you think? Is it lawful to give tribute to Caesar or not?
012218 But Jesus perceived their wickedness, and said, Why do you tempt Me, hypocrites?
012219 Show Me the tribute money. And they brought a denarius to Him.
012220 And He said to them, Whose image and inscription is this?
012221 They said to Him, Caesar's. Then He said to them, Therefore render to Caesar the things that are Caesar's, and to God the things which are God's.
012222 When they heard these words , they marveled, and they left Him and went away.
012223 On that day the Sadducees came to Him, who say that there is no resurrection. And they asked Him,
012224 saying, Master, Moses said, If a man dies, having no children, his brother shall marry his wife and raise up seed to his brother.
012225 Now there were with us seven brothers. And the first, when he had married a wife, died. And, having no issue, he left his wife to his brother.
012226 The second also did likewise, and the third, to the seventh.
012227 And last of all the woman also died.
012228 Therefore in the resurrection, whose wife shall she be, of the seven? For they all had her.
012229 Jesus answered and said to them, You err, not knowing the Scriptures nor the power of God.
012230 For in the resurrection they neither marry nor are given in marriage, but are as the angels of God in Heaven.
012231 But regarding the resurrection of the dead, have you not read that which was spoken to you by God, saying,
012232 "I am the God of Abraham, and the God of Isaac, and the God of Jacob?" God is not the God of the dead, but of the living.
012233 And when the crowd heard this , they were astonished at His doctrine.
012234 But hearing that He had silenced the Sadducees, the Pharisees were gathered together.
012235 Then one of them, a lawyer, asked, tempting Him and saying,
012236 Master, which is the great commandment in the Law?
012237 Jesus said to him, You shall love the Lord your God with all your heart, and with all your soul, and with all your mind.
012238 This is the first and great commandment.
012239 And the second is like it, You shall love your neighbor as yourself.
012240 On these two commandments hang all the Law and the Prophets.
012241 While the Pharisees were gathered, Jesus asked them,
012242 saying, What do you think of Christ? Whose son is he? They say to Him, David's.
012243 He said to them, How then does David by the Spirit call him Lord, saying,
012244 "the LORD said to my Lord, Sit on My right until I make Your enemies Your footstool for Your feet?"
012245 If David then calls Him Lord, how is He his son?
012246 And no one was able to answer Him a word, nor did anyone dare from that day to question Him any more.
012301 Then Jesus spoke to the crowd and to His disciples,
012302 saying, The scribes and the Pharisees sit in Moses' seat.
012303 Therefore whatever they tell you to observe, observe and do. But do not do according to their works; for they say, and do not do.
012304 For they bind heavy and hard-to-carry burdens and lay them on men's shoulders. But they will not move them with one of their finger.
012305 But they do all their works in order to be seen of men. They make their phylacteries broad and enlarge the borders of their garments.
012306 And they love the first couch at feasts, and the chief seats in the synagogues,
012307 and greetings in the market-places, and to be called, Rabbi! Rabbi! by men.
012308 But you must not be called Rabbi, for One is your teacher, Christ, and you are all brothers.
012309 And call no one your father on the earth, for One is your Father in Heaven.
012310 Nor be called teachers, for One is your Teacher, even Christ.
012311 But he who is greatest among you shall be your servant.
012312 And whoever shall exalt himself shall be abased, and he who shall humble himself shall be exalted.
012313 But woe to you, scribes and Pharisees, hypocrites! For you shut up the kingdom of Heaven against men. For you neither go in, nor do you allow those entering to go in.
012314 Woe to you, scribes and Pharisees, hypocrites! For you devour widows' houses, and pray at length as a pretense. Therefore you shall receive the greater condemnation.
012315 Woe to you, scribes and Pharisees, hypocrites! For you compass sea and the dry land to make one proselyte, and when he is made, you make him twofold more the child of hell than yourselves.
012316 Woe to you, blind guides, saying, Whoever shall swear by the temple, it is nothing; but whoever shall swear by the gold of the temple, he is a debtor.
012317 Fools and blind! For which is greater, the gold, or the temple that sanctifies the gold?
012318 And, Whoever shall swear by the altar, it is nothing; but whoever swears by the gift that is on it, he is a debtor!
012319 Fools and blind! For which is greater, the gift, or the altar that sanctifies the gift?
012320 Therefore whoever shall swear by the altar swears by it, and by all things on it.
012321 And whoever shall swear by the temple, swears by it and by Him who dwells in it.
012322 And he who shall swear by Heaven swears by the throne of God, and by Him who sits on it.
012323 Woe to you, scribes and Pharisees, hypocrites! For you pay tithes of mint and dill and cummin, and you have left undone the weightier matters of the Law, judgment, mercy, and faith. You ought to have done these and not to leave the other undone.
012324 Blind guides who strain out a gnat and swallow a camel!
012325 Woe to you, scribes and Pharisees, hypocrites! For you cleanse the outside of the cup and of the dish, but inside they are full of extortion and excess.
012326 Blind Pharisee! First cleanse the inside of the cup and of the dish, so that the outside of them may be clean also.
012327 Woe to you, scribes and Pharisees, hypocrites! For you are like whitewashed tombs, which indeed appear beautiful outside, but inside they are full of dead men's bones, and of all uncleanness.
012328 Even so you also appear righteous to men outwardly, but inside you are full of hypocrisy and iniquity.
012329 Woe to you, scribes and Pharisees, hypocrites! Because you build the tombs of the prophets, and decorate the tombs of the righteous,
012330 and say, If we had been in the days of our fathers, we would not have been partakers with them in the blood of the prophets.
012331 Therefore you are witnesses to yourselves, that you are the sons of those who killed the prophets;
012332 and you fill up the measure of your fathers.
012333 Serpents! Offspring of vipers! How can you escape the condemnation of hell?
012334 Therefore, behold, I send prophets and wise men and scribes to you. And you will kill and crucify some of them. And some of them you will scourge in your synagogues and persecute from city to city;
012335 so that on you may come all the righteous blood shed on the earth, from the blood of righteous Abel to the blood of Zechariah the son of Berachiah, whom you killed between the temple and the altar.
012336 Truly I say to you, All these things shall come on this generation.
012337 O Jerusalem, Jerusalem, the one killing the prophets and stoning those who are sent to her, how often would I have gathered your children together, even as a hen gathers her chicks under her wings, and you would not!
012338 Behold, your house is left to you desolate.
012339 For I say to you, You shall not see Me from now on until you say, "Blessed is He who comes in the name of the Lord."
012401 And Jesus went out and departed from the temple. And His disciples came to Him to show Him the buildings of the temple.
012402 And Jesus said to them, Do you not see all these things? Truly I say to you, There shall not be left here one stone on another that shall not be thrown down.
012403 And as He sat on the Mount of Olives, the disciples came to Him privately, saying, Tell us, when shall these things be? And what shall be the sign of Your coming, and of the end of the world?
012404 And Jesus answered and said to them, Take heed that no man deceive you.
012405 For many will come in My name, saying, I am Christ, and will deceive many.
012406 And you will hear of wars and rumors of wars. See that you are not troubled, for all these things must occur; but the end is not yet.
012407 For nation will rise against nation, and kingdom against kingdom. And there will be famines and pestilences and earthquakes in different places.
012408 All these are the beginning of sorrows.
012409 Then they will deliver you up to be afflicted and will kill you. And you will be hated of all nations for My name's sake.
012410 And then many will be offended, and will betray one another, and will hate one another.
012411 And many false prophets will rise and deceive many.
012412 And because iniquity shall abound, the love of many will become cold.
012413 But he who endures to the end, the same shall be kept safe.
012414 And this gospel of the kingdom shall be proclaimed in all the world as a witness to all nations. And then the end shall come.
012415 Therefore when you see the abomination of desolation, spoken of by Daniel the prophet, stand in the holy place (whoever reads, let him understand).
012416 Then let those in Judea flee into the mountains.
012417 Let him on the housetop not come down to take anything out of his house;
012418 nor let him in the field turn back to take his clothes.
012419 And woe to those who are with child, and to those who give suck in those days!
012420 But pray that your flight is not in the winter, nor on the sabbath day;
012421 for then shall be great tribulation, such as has not been since the beginning of the world to this time; no, nor ever shall be.
012422 And unless those days should be shortened, no flesh would be saved. But for the elect's sake, those days shall be shortened.
012423 Then if any man shall say to you, Lo, here is Christ! Or, There! Do not believe it.
012424 For false Christs and false prophets will arise and show great signs and wonders; so much so that, if it were possible, they would deceive even the elect.
012425 Behold, I have told you beforehand.
012426 Therefore if they shall say to you, Behold, He is in the desert! Do not go out. Behold, He is in the secret rooms! Do not believe it.
012427 For as the lightning comes out of the east and shines even to the west, so also will be the coming of the Son of man.
012428 For wherever the carcass is, there the eagles will be gathered.
012429 And immediately after the tribulation of those days, the sun shall be darkened and the moon shall not give her light, and the stars shall fall from the heaven, and the powers of the heavens shall be shaken.
012430 And then the sign of the Son of man shall appear in the heavens. And then all the tribes of the earth shall mourn, and they shall see the Son of man coming in the clouds of the heaven with power and great glory.
012431 And He shall send His angels with a great sound of a trumpet, and they shall gather His elect from the four winds, from one end of the heavens to the other.
012432 Now learn a parable of the fig tree. When its branch is still tender and puts out leaves, you know that summer is near.
012433 So you, likewise, when you see all these things, shall know that it is near, at the doors.
012434 Truly I say to you, This generation shall not pass until all these things are fulfilled.
012435 The heaven and the earth shall pass away, but My words shall not pass away.
012436 But of that day and hour no one knows, no, not the angels of Heaven, but only My Father.
012437 But as the days of Noah were , so shall be the coming of the Son of man.
012438 For as in the days before the flood, they were eating and drinking, marrying and giving in marriage, until the day Noah entered into the ark.
012439 And they did not know until the flood came and took them all away. So also will be the coming of the Son of man.
012440 Then two shall be in the field; the one shall be taken, and the other left.
012441 Two shall be grinding at the mill; the one shall be taken, and the other left.
012442 Therefore watch; for you do not know what hour your Lord comes.
012443 But know this, that if the steward of the house had known in what watch the thief would come, he would have watched and would not have allowed his house to be dug through.
012444 Therefore you also be ready, for in that hour you think not, the Son of man comes.
012445 Who then is a faithful and wise servant, whom his Lord has made ruler over His household, to give them food in due season?
012446 Blessed is that servant whom his Lord shall find him doing so when He comes.
012447 Truly I say to you that He shall make him ruler over all His goods.
012448 But if that evil servant shall say in his heart, My Lord delays His coming,
012449 and shall begin to strike his fellow servants, and to eat and drink with the drunken,
012450 the Lord of that servant shall come in a day when he does not look for Him , and in an hour which he does not know.
012451 And He shall cut him apart and appoint him his portion with the hypocrites. There shall be weeping and gnashing of teeth.
012501 Then shall the kingdom of Heaven be likened to ten virgins, who took their lamps and went out to meet the bridegroom.
012502 And five of them were wise, and five were foolish.
012503 The foolish ones took their lamps, but took no oil with them.
012504 But the wise took oil in their vessels with their lamps.
012505 While the bridegroom tarried, they all slumbered and slept.
012506 And at midnight there was a cry made, Behold, the bridegroom comes! Go out to meet him.
012507 Then all those virgins arose and trimmed their lamps.
012508 And the foolish said to the wise, Give us some of your oil, for our lamps have gone out.
012509 But the wise answered, saying, No , lest there be not enough for us and you. But rather go to those who sell, and buy for yourselves.
012510 And while they went to buy, the bridegroom came. And they who were ready went in with him to the marriage, and the door was shut.
012511 Afterwards the other virgins came also, saying, Lord, Lord, open to us.
012512 But he answered and said, Truly I say to you, I do not know you.
012513 Therefore watch, for you do not know either the day or the hour in which the Son of man comes.
012514 For it is as if a man going abroad called his own servants and gave them his goods.
012515 And to one he gave five talents, to another two, and to another one; to each according to his ability. And he went abroad at once.
012516 And going he who had received the five talents traded with them, and made another five talents.
012517 And likewise he who had received two, he also gained another two.
012518 But he who had received the one talent went and dug in the earth and hid his lord's silver.
012519 After a long time the lord of those servants came and took account with them.
012520 And so he who had received five talents came and brought another five talents, saying, Lord, you delivered five talents to me. Behold, I have gained five talents above them.
012521 His lord said to him, Well done , good and faithful servant! You have been faithful over a few things; I will make you ruler over many things. Enter into the joy of your lord.
012522 He also who had received two talents came and said, Lord, you delivered two talents to me. Behold, I have gained two other talents above them.
012523 His lord said to him, Well done , good and faithful servant! You have been faithful over a few things, I will make you ruler over many things. Enter into the joy of your lord.
012524 And he who had received the one talent came and said, Lord, I knew that you were a hard man, reaping where you did not sow, and gathering where you did not scatter.
012525 And I was afraid and went and hid your talent in the earth. Lo, you have yours.
012526 His lord answered and said to him, Evil and slothful servant! You knew that I reaped where I did not sow, and gathered where I did not scatter,
012527 then you should have put my money to the exchangers, and coming I would have received my own with interest.
012528 Therefore take the talent from him and give it to him who has ten talents.
012529 For to everyone who has, more shall be given, and he will abound. But from him who has not, even that which he has shall be taken away from him.
012530 And throw the unprofitable servant into outer darkness; there shall be weeping and gnashing of teeth.
012531 But when the Son of man comes in His glory, and all the holy angels with Him, then He shall sit on the throne of His glory.
012532 And all nations shall be gathered before Him. And He shall separate them from one another, as a shepherd divides the sheep from the goats.
012533 And indeed He shall set the sheep on His right hand, but the goats off the left.
012534 Then the King shall say to those on His right hand , Come, blessed of My Father, inherit the kingdom prepared for you from the foundation of the world.
012535 For I was hungry, and you gave me food; I was thirsty, and you gave Me drink; I was a stranger, and you took Me in;
012536 I was naked, and you clothed Me; I was sick, and you visited Me; I was in prison, and you came to Me.
012537 Then the righteous shall answer Him, saying, Lord, when did we see You hungry, and fed You ? Or thirsty, and gave You drink?
012538 When did we see You a stranger, and took You in? Or naked, and clothed You ?
012539 Or when did we see You sick, or in prison, and came to You?
012540 And the King shall answer and say to them, Truly I say to you, Inasmuch as you did it to one of the least of these My brothers, you have done it to Me.
012541 Then He also shall say to those on the left hand , Depart from Me, you cursed, into everlasting fire prepared for the Devil and his angels.
012542 For I was hungry, and you gave Me no food; I was thirsty, and you gave Me no drink;
012543 I was a stranger and you did not take Me in; I was naked, and you did not clothe Me; I was sick, and in prison, and you did not visit me.
012544 Then they will also answer Him, saying, Lord, when did we see You hungry, or thirsty, or a stranger, or naked, or sick, or in prison, and did not minister to You?
012545 Then He shall answer them, saying, Truly I say to you, Inasmuch as you did not do it to one of the least of these, you did not do it to Me.
012546 And these shall go away into everlasting punishment, but the righteous into everlasting life.
012601 And it happened when Jesus finished all these sayings, He said to His disciples,
012602 You know that after two days the Passover comes, and the Son of man is betrayed to be crucified.
012603 Then the chief priests, and the scribes, and the elders of the people, assembled together to the palace of the high priest, who was called Caiaphas.
012604 And they consulted so that they might take Jesus by guile and kill Him .
012605 But they said, Not on the feast day , lest there be an uproar among the people.
012606 And when Jesus was in Bethany, in the house of Simon the leper,
012607 a woman came to Him, having an alabaster box of very precious ointment, and poured it on His head as He reclined.
012608 But when His disciples saw it , they were indignant, saying, To what purpose is this waste?
012609 For this ointment might have been sold for very much and given to the poor.
012610 When Jesus understood it , He said to them, Why do you trouble the woman? For she has done a good work on Me.
012611 For you have the poor with you always, but you do not always have Me.
012612 For in putting ointment on My body, she did it for My burial.
012613 Truly I say to you, Wherever this gospel shall be proclaimed in the whole world, that which this woman has done shall be spoken of also, for a memorial of her.
012614 Then one of the twelve, called Judas Iscariot, went to the chief priests.
012615 And he said to them , What will you give me, and I will betray Him to you? And they appointed to him thirty pieces of silver.
012616 And from that time he sought opportunity to betray Him.
012617 And on the first day of the Feast of Unleavened Bread , the disciples came to Jesus, saying to Him, Where do You desire that we prepare for You to eat the Passover?
012618 And He said, Go into the city to such a man, and say to him, The Master said, My time is at hand. I will keep the Passover at your house with My disciples.
012619 And the disciples did as Jesus had appointed them. And they made the passover ready.
012620 And when evening had come, He sat down with the Twelve.
012621 And as they ate, He said, Truly I say to you that one of you will betray Me.
012622 And grieving sorrowfully, they began to say, each one of them, Lord, not I am the one ?
012623 And He answered and said, He who dips his hand with Me in the dish, the same shall betray Me.
012624 The Son of man goes, as it has been written of Him, but woe to that man by whom the Son of man is betrayed! It would have been good for that man if he had not been born.
012625 And answering, the one betraying Him, Judas, said, Master, Not am I the one ? He said to him, You said it .
012626 And as they were eating, Jesus took bread and blessed it , and broke it , and gave it to the disciples, and said, Take, eat, this is My body.
012627 And He took the cup and gave thanks, and gave it to them, saying, Drink all of it.
012628 For this is My blood of the new covenant, which is shed for many for the remission of sins.
012629 But I say to you, I will not drink of this fruit of the vine from now on, until that day when I drink it new with you in My Father's kingdom.
012630 And singing a hymn, they went out to the Mount of Olives.
012631 Then Jesus said to them, All of you will be offended because of Me this night. For it is written, "I will smite the Shepherd, and the sheep of the flock shall be scattered abroad."
012632 But after I have risen again, I will go before you into Galilee.
012633 Peter answered and said to Him, though all shall be offended because of You, I will never be offended.
012634 Jesus said to him, Truly I say to you that this night, before the cock crows, you shall deny Me three times.
012635 Peter said to Him, though I should die with You, yet I will not deny You. All the disciples also said the same.
012636 Then Jesus came with them to a place called Gethsemane. And He said to the disciples, Sit here while I go and pray there.
012637 And He took Peter and the two sons of Zebedee with Him, and He began to be sorrowful and very heavy.
012638 Then He said to them, My soul is exceedingly sorrowful, even to death. Wait here and watch with Me.
012639 And He went a little further and fell on His face, and prayed, saying, O My Father, if it is possible, let this cup pass from Me. Yet not as I will, but as You will .
012640 And He came to the disciples and found them asleep. And He said to Peter, What! Could you not watch with Me one hour?
012641 Watch and pray that you enter not into temptation. The spirit indeed is willing, but the flesh is weak.
012642 He went away again the second time and prayed, saying, My Father, if this cup may not pass away from Me unless I drink it, Your will be done.
012643 And He came and found them asleep again, for their eyes were heavy.
012644 And He left them and went away again, and prayed the third time, saying the same word.
012645 Then He came to His disciples and said to them, Sleep on now and take your rest. Behold, the hour is at hand, and the Son of man is betrayed into the hands of sinners.
012646 Rise, let us be going; behold, he who is betraying Me is at hand.
012647 And as He was yet speaking, behold, Judas came, one of the Twelve. And with him came a great crowd with swords and clubs, being sent from the chief priests and elders of the people.
012648 And he who betrayed Him gave them a sign, saying, Whomever I shall kiss, He is the one, lay hold on Him.
012649 And coming up to Jesus immediately, he said, Hail, Master! And he kissed Him.
012650 And Jesus said to him, Friend, why are you here? Then they came and laid hands on Jesus and took Him.
012651 And, behold, one of those who were with Jesus stretched out his hand and drew his sword, and he struck a servant of the high priest and cut off his ear.
012652 Then Jesus said to him, Put up your sword again into its place; for all who take the sword shall perish with a sword.
012653 Do you think that I cannot now pray to My Father, and He shall presently give Me more than twelve legions of angels?
012654 But how then shall the Scriptures be fulfilled, that it must be so?
012655 In that hour Jesus said to the crowds, Have you come out in order to take Me with swords and clubs, as against a thief? I sat daily with you, teaching in the temple, and you did not lay hands on Me.
012656 But all this happened that the Scriptures of the prophets might be fulfilled. Then all the disciples fled, forsaking Him.
012657 And they who had seized Jesus led Him away to Caiaphas the high priest, where the scribes and the elders had assembled.
012658 But Peter followed Him afar off to the high priest's court, and he went in and sat with the servants to see the end.
012659 And the chief priests and the elders and all the sanhedrin sought false witness against Jesus, in order to put Him to death.
012660 But they found none; yea, though many false witnesses came, they found none. But at last two false witnesses came up
012661 and said, This one said, I am able to destroy the temple of God and to build it in three days.
012662 And standing up, the high priest said to Him, Do you answer nothing? What is it that these witness against you?
012663 But Jesus was silent. And the high priest answered and said to Him, I adjure you by the living God that you tell us whether you are the Christ, the Son of God.
012664 Jesus said to him, You said it . I tell you more. From this time you shall see the Son of man sitting on the right hand of power, and coming on the clouds of the heavens.
012665 Then the high priest tore his clothes, saying, He has spoken blasphemy! What further need do we have of witnesses? Behold, now you have heard his blasphemy.
012666 What do you think? They answered and said, He is worthy of death.
012667 Then they spat in His face and beat Him with the fist. And others struck Him with the palms of their hands,
012668 saying, Prophesy to us, Christ; who is the one who struck you?
012669 And Peter sat outside in the court. And a girl came to him, saying, You also were with Jesus of Galilee.
012670 But he denied all before them , saying, I do not know what you say.
012671 And when he had gone out into the porch, another saw him and said to those there, This one was also with Jesus of Nazareth.
012672 And again he denied with an oath, I do not know the man.
012673 And after a little while those who stood by came and said to Peter, Surely you also are one of them, for your speech betrays you.
012674 Then he began to curse and to swear, I do not know the man. And immediately the cock crowed.
012675 And Peter remembered the word of Jesus, Who said to him, Before the cock crows, you shall deny Me three times. And he went out and wept bitterly.
012701 And it becoming early morning, all the chief priests and elders of the people took counsel against Jesus to put Him to death.
012702 And when they had bound Him, they led Him away and delivered Him to Pontius Pilate the governor.
012703 Then he who had betrayed Him, seeing that He was condemned, sorrowing, Judas returned the thirty pieces of silver again to the chief priests and elders,
012704 saying, I have sinned, betraying innocent blood. And they said, What is that to us? You see to that .
012705 And he threw the pieces of silver down in the temple and departed. And he went and hanged himself.
012706 And the chief priests took the silver pieces, and said, It is not lawful to put them into the treasury, because it is the price of blood.
012707 And they took counsel and bought the potter's field with them, to bury strangers in.
012708 Therefore that field was called, The Field of Blood, to this day.
012709 Then that which was spoken by Jeremiah the prophet was fulfilled, saying, "And they took the thirty pieces of silver, the price of Him who had been priced, whom they of the children of Israel valued,
012710 and gave them for the potter's field, as the Lord appointed me."
012711 And Jesus stood before the governor. And the governor asked Him, saying, Are you the king of the Jews? And Jesus said to him, You say it .
012712 And when He was accused by the chief priests and elders, He answered nothing.
012713 Then Pilate said to Him, Do you not hear how many things they witness against you?
012714 And He did not answer him a word, so that the governor greatly marveled.
012715 Now at that feast the governor was accustomed to release to the people a prisoner, whomever they desired.
012716 And they then had a notorious prisoner called Barabbas.
012717 Therefore when they were gathered together, Pilate said to them, Whom do you desire that I release to you? Barabbas, or Jesus who is called Christ?
012718 For he knew they had delivered Him because of envy.
012719 But as he was sitting down on the judgment seat, his wife sent to him, saying, Have nothing to do with that just man, for today because of Him I have suffered many things in a dream.
012720 But the chief priests and elders persuaded the crowd that they should ask for Barabbas and destroy Jesus.
012721 The governor answered and said to them, Which of the two do you desire that I release to you? They said, Barabbas.
012722 Pilate said to them, What then shall I do with Jesus, who is called Christ? They all said to him, Let Him be crucified.
012723 And the governor said, Why? What evil has He done? But they cried out the more, saying, let Him be crucified!
012724 But when Pilate saw that it gained nothing, but rather that a tumult was made, he took water and washed his hands before the crowd, saying, I am innocent of the blood of this just person. You see to it.
012725 Then all the people answered and said, Let His blood be on us and on our children.
012726 Then he released Barabbas to them. And when he had scourged Jesus, he delivered Him to be crucified.
012727 Then taking Jesus into the praetorium, the soldiers of the governor gathered the cohort against Him.
012728 And stripping Him, they put a scarlet robe around Him.
012729 And plaiting a crown of thorns, they put it on His head, and a reed in His right hand. And they bowed the knee before Him and mocked Him, saying, Hail, King of the Jews!
012730 And spitting at Him, they took the reed and struck at His head.
012731 And after they had mocked Him, they took the robe off of Him and put His own clothing on Him and led Him away to crucify Him .
012732 And going out, they found a man of Cyrene, Simon by name. They forced this one to carry His cross.
012733 And coming to a place called Golgotha, which is called, Place of a Skull,
012734 they gave Him vinegar mixed with gall to drink. And when He had tasted, He would not drink.
012735 And they crucified Him, dividing His garments, casting a lot; so that it might be fulfilled which was spoken by the prophet, "They parted My garments among them, and they cast a lot for My clothing."
012736 And sitting down they guarded Him there.
012737 And they put up over His head His accusation, written, THIS IS JESUS THE KING OF THE JEWS.
012738 Then two thieves were crucified with Him, one off the right, one off the left.
012739 And those who passed by blasphemed Him, shaking their heads,
012740 and saying, You destroying the temple and building it in three days, save yourself. If you are the Son of God, come down from the cross.
012741 And in the same way also the chief priests mocked, with the scribes and elders, saying,
012742 He saved others, but he cannot save himself. If he is the King of Israel, let him now come down from the cross, and we will believe him.
012743 He trusted in God, let Him deliver him now, if He will have him. (For He said, I am the Son of God.)
012744 And also the thieves who were crucified with Him reviled Him, saying the same.
012745 And from the sixth hour there was darkness over all the land until the ninth hour.
012746 And about the ninth hour, Jesus cried with a loud voice, saying, Eli, Eli, lama sabachthani? That is, My God, My God, why have You forsaken me?
012747 Some of those who stood there, when they heard, said, This one calls for Elijah.
012748 And immediately one of them ran and took a sponge and filled it with vinegar, and he put it on a reed and gave it to Him to drink.
012749 The rest said, Let Him alone, let us see whether Elijah will come to save Him.
012750 And crying again with a loud voice, Jesus released His spirit.
012751 And, behold! The veil of the temple was torn in two from top to bottom. And the earth quaked, and the rocks were sheared,
012752 and the tombs were opened, and many bodies of the saints who had fallen asleep arose,
012753 and coming out of the tomb after His resurrection they went into the holy city and appeared to many.
012754 But the centurion and those guarding Jesus, seeing the earthquake, and the things that took place, they feared greatly, saying, Truly this One was Son of God.
012755 And many of the women were there, watching from a distance, those who had followed Jesus from Galilee, ministering to Him, watching from a distance;
012756 among whom was Mary Magdalene, and Mary the mother of James and Joses, and the mother of Zebedee's children.
012757 When the evening had come, a rich man of Arimathea, named Joseph, came, who also himself was Jesus' disciple.
012758 He went to Pilate and begged the body of Jesus. Then Pilate commanded the body to be delivered.
012759 When Joseph had taken the body, he wrapped it in clean linen,
012760 and laid it in his new tomb, which he had cut out of the rock. And he rolled a great stone to the door of the tomb and departed.
012761 And Mary Magdalene, and the other Mary, were sitting there across from the tomb.
012762 And on the next day, which was after the Preparation, the chief priests and the Pharisees gathered to Pilate,
012763 saying, Sir, we remember that that deceiver said, while He was living, After three days I will rise again.
012764 Then command that the tomb be made secure until the third day, lest his disciples come by night and steal him away and say to the people, He has risen from the dead. So the last error will be worse than the first.
012765 Pilate said to them, You have a watch. Go and make it as secure as you can.
012766 And going they made the tomb secure, sealing the stone along with the guard.
012801 But late in the week, at the dawning into the first day of the week, Mary Magdalene and the other Mary came to see the tomb.
012802 And behold, a great earthquake occurred! For coming down from Heaven, and coming up, an angel of the Lord rolled back the stone from the door and was sitting on it.
012803 His countenance was like lightning, and his clothing white as snow.
012804 And the keepers shook for fear of him and became like dead men .
012805 And the angel answered and said to the women, Do not fear, for I know that you seek Jesus who was crucified.
012806 He is not here, for He has risen, as He said. Come, see the place where the Lord lay.
012807 And go quickly and tell His disciples that He has risen from the dead. And, behold, He goes before you into Galilee. There you shall see Him. Lo, I have told you.
012808 And they quickly departed from the tomb with fear and great joy, and ran to bring His disciples word.
012809 But as they were going to report to His disciples, behold, Jesus also met them, saying, Hail! And they came and held Him by the feet and worshiped Him.
012810 Then Jesus said to them, Do not be afraid; go tell My brothers that they should go into Galilee, and there they will see Me.
012811 And as they were going, behold, some of the guard came into the city and declared all the things that were done to the chief priests.
012812 And being assembled with the elders, and taking counsel, they gave enough silver to the soldiers,
012813 saying, Say that His disciples came by night and stole Him away while we slept.
012814 And if this comes to the governor's ears, we will persuade him and make you free from care.
012815 And taking the silver, they did as they were taught. And this saying was spread among the Jews until today.
012816 And the eleven disciples went into Galilee, to the mountain where Jesus had appointed them.
012817 And when they saw Him, they worshiped Him. But some doubted.
012818 And Jesus came and spoke to them, saying, All authority is given to Me in Heaven and in earth.
012819 Therefore go and teach all nations, baptizing them in the name of the Father and of the Son and of the Holy Spirit,
012820 teaching them to observe all things, whatever I commanded you. And, behold, I am with you all the days until the end of the world. Amen.
020101 The beginning of the gospel of Jesus Christ, the Son of God:
020102 as it is written in the Prophets, "Behold, I send My messenger before Your face, who shall prepare Your way before You.
020103 The voice of one crying in the wilderness, prepare the way of the Lord, make His paths straight."
020104 John came baptizing in the wilderness and proclaiming the baptism of repentance for the remission of sins.
020105 And all the land of Judea, and those of Jerusalem, went out to him and were all baptized by him in the Jordan River, confessing their sins.
020106 And John was clothed with camel's hair, and with a leather girdle about his loin. And he ate locusts and wild honey.
020107 And he proclaimed, saying, There is One coming after me who is mightier than I, the thong of whose sandals I am not worthy to stoop down to loosen.
020108 I indeed have baptized you in water, but He shall baptize you with the Holy Spirit.
020109 And it happened in those days that Jesus came from Nazareth of Galilee and was baptized by John in the Jordan.
020110 And immediately coming up out of the water, He saw the heavens opened, and the Spirit like a dove descending upon Him.
020111 And there came a voice from Heaven, saying , You are My beloved Son, in whom I am well pleased.
020112 And immediately the Spirit drove Him into the wilderness.
020113 And He was there in the wilderness forty days, tempted by Satan. And He was with the wild beasts, and the angels ministered to Him.
020114 And after John was delivered up, Jesus came into Galilee, proclaiming the gospel of the kingdom of God,
020115 and saying, The time is fulfilled, and the kingdom of God draws near. Repent, and believe the gospel.
020116 And walking along beside the sea of Galilee, He saw Simon and Andrew his brother casting a net into the sea; for they were fishermen.
020117 And Jesus said to them, Come after Me and I will make you fishers of men.
020118 And immediately they left their nets and followed Him.
020119 And when He going farther from there a little, He saw James the son of Zebedee, and John his brother, who also were in the boat mending their nets.
020120 And immediately He called them. And they left their father Zebedee in the boat with the hired servants and went after Him.
020121 And they went into Capernaum. And immediately on the sabbath day He entered into the synagogue and taught.
020122 And they were astonished at His doctrine. For He taught them as one who had authority, and not like the scribes.
020123 And in their synagogue was a man with an unclean spirit. And he cried out,
020124 saying, What is to us and to You, Jesus of Nazareth? Have You come to destroy us? I know You, who You are, the Holy One of God.
020125 And Jesus rebuked him, saying, Be quiet, and come out of him.
020126 And the unclean spirit, convulsing him, and crying with a loud voice, he came out of him.
020127 They all were amazed, so as to question among themselves, saying, What is this? What new doctrine is this? For He even commands the unclean spirits with authority, and they obey Him.
020128 And immediately His fame went out into all the Galilean neighborhood.
020129 And immediately after they had come out of the synagogue, they entered into the house of Simon and Andrew, with James and John.
020130 But Simon's wife's mother lay sick of a fever, and at once they told Him about her.
020131 And He came and took her by the hand and lifted her up. And instantly the fever left her, and she served them.
020132 And at evening, when the sun set, they brought all those who were diseased to Him, and those who had been demon-possessed.
020133 And all the city had gathered at the door.
020134 And He healed many who were sick of different diseases, and cast out many demons. And He did not allow the demons to speak, because they knew Him.
020135 And rising up quite early in the night, He went out and went away into a deserted place, and He was praying there.
020136 And Simon, and those with him, searched for Him.
020137 And finding Him, they said to Him, All are seeking You.
020138 And He said to them, Let us go into the next towns so that I may proclaim there also. For that reason I came forth.
020139 And He proclaimed in their synagogues throughout all Galilee, and cast out demons.
020140 And a leper came to Him, begging Him and kneeling down to Him, and saying to Him, If You will, You can make me clean.
020141 And Jesus, moved with compassion, put out His hand and touched him, and said to him, I will; be clean!
020142 And He having spoken, the leprosy instantly departed from him and he was cleansed.
020143 And He strictly charged him and immediately sent him away,
020144 and He said to him, See that you say nothing to anyone. But go and show yourself to the priest, and offer those things which Moses commanded for your cleansing, for a testimony to them.
020145 But going out, he began to proclaim it very much, and to spread about the matter, so that Jesus could no more openly enter into the city, but was outside in deserted places. And they came to Him from every quarter.
020201 And again He entered into Capernaum after some days. And it was heard that He was in a house.
020202 And immediately many were gathered, so that none any longer had room, even to the door. And He proclaimed the Word to them.
020203 Then they came to Him, bringing one who was paralyzed, who was carried by four.
020204 When they could not come near to Him because of the crowd, they unroofed the roof where He was. And digging through, they let down the cot on which the paralytic was lying.
020205 And seeing their faith, Jesus said to the paralytic, Child, your sins are forgiven to you.
020206 But some of the scribes were sitting there, and reasoning in their hearts,
020207 Why does this one speak such blasphemies? Who can forgive sins except God only?
020208 And instantly knowing in His spirit that they reasoned so within themselves, He said to them, Why do you reason these things in your heart?
020209 Which is easier, to say to the paralytic, Your sins are forgiven you; or to say, Arise, and take up your cot and walk?
020210 But so that you may know that the Son of man has authority upon earth to forgive sins, He said to the paralytic,
020211 I say to you, Arise, and take up your cot, and go to your house.
020212 And immediately he arose and took up his cot and went out before all. So that all were amazed and glorified God, saying, We never saw it this way.
020213 And He went out again by the seaside. And all the crowd came to Him, and He taught them.
020214 And as He passed on, He saw Levi the son of Alpheus sitting at the tax-office. And He said to him, Follow Me. And he arose and followed Him.
020215 And it happened as Jesus reclined in his house, many tax-collectors and sinners also reclined with Jesus and His disciples. For there were many, and they followed Him.
020216 And when the scribes and Pharisees saw Him eat with tax-collectors and sinners, they said to His disciples, How is it that He eats and drinks with tax-collectors and sinners?
020217 When Jesus heard, He said to them, They who are strong have no need of a physician, but the ones who have illness. I did not come to call the righteous, but sinners to repentance.
020218 The disciples of John and those of the Pharisees were fasting. And they came and said to Him, Why do John's disciples and those of the Pharisees fast, but your disciples do not fast?
020219 And Jesus said to them, Can the sons of the bridechamber fast while the bridegroom is with them? As long as they have the bridegroom with them they cannot fast.
020220 But the days will come when the bridegroom shall be taken away from them, and then they shall fast in those days.
020221 And no one sews a patch of new cloth on an old garment, else it takes away from its fullness, the new from the old, and a worse tear occurs.
020222 No one puts new wine into old wineskins, else the new wine bursts the wineskins, and the wine spills, and the wineskins will be ruined. The new wine must be put into new wineskins.
020223 And it happened that He went through the grainfields on the sabbath day. And as they walked His disciples began to pluck the heads of grain .
020224 And the Pharisees said to Him, Behold, why do they do that which is not lawful on the sabbath day?
020225 And He said to them, Have you never read what David did, when he had need and was hungry, he, and those with him?
020226 How he went into the house of God in the days of Abiathar the high priest and ate the showbread, which it is not lawful to eat, except for the priests, and also gave to those with him?
020227 And He said to them, The sabbath came into being for man's sake, and not man for the sabbath's sake.
020228 Therefore the Son of man is also Lord of the sabbath.
020301 And He again entered into the synagogue. And a man was there who had a withered hand.
020302 And they watched Him to see if He would heal him on the sabbath day, so that they might accuse Him.
020303 And He said to the man who had the withered hand, Arise! Come into the middle.
020304 And He said to them, Is it lawful to do good on the sabbath days, or to do evil? To save life, or to kill? But they were silent.
020305 And looking around on them with anger, being grieved because of the hardness of their hearts, He said to the man, Stretch out your hand! And he stretched it out. And his hand was restored whole, like the other.
020306 The Pharisees went out and immediately took counsel with the Herodians against Him, how they might destroy Him.
020307 And Jesus withdrew to the sea with His disciples. And a great crowd from Galilee followed Him, and from Judea,
020308 and from Jerusalem, and from Idumea, and from beyond Jordan, and those around Tyre and Sidon, a great throng came to him, having heard how much He was doing.
020309 And He spoke to His disciples, so that a small boat should stay near to Him, because of the crowd, lest they should press on Him.
020310 For He had healed many, so that they pressed on Him in order to touch Him, as many as had plagues.
020311 And unclean spirits, when they saw Him, they fell down before Him and cried, saying, You are the Son of God!
020312 And He strictly charged them that they should not make Him known.
020313 And He went up into a mountain and called near those whom He would. And they came to Him.
020314 And He ordained twelve, that they should be with Him, and that He might send them out to proclaim,
020315 and to have authority to heal sicknesses, and to cast out demons.
020316 And He put on Simon the name Peter.
020317 And He put on James the son of Zebedee, and John the brother of James, the names Boanerges, which is, the Sons of Thunder.
020318 And He appointed Andrew, and Philip, and Bartholomew, and Matthew, and Thomas, and James the son of Alpheus, and Thaddeus, and Simon the Canaanite,
020319 and Judas Iscariot, who also betrayed him. And they went into a house.
020320 And again a crowd came together, so that they could not even eat bread.
020321 And hearing, those with Him went out to take hold of Him; for they said, He is insane.
020322 And the scribes who came down from Jerusalem said, He has Beelzebub, and He casts out demons by the ruler of the demons.
020323 And He called them and said to them in parables, How can Satan cast out Satan?
020324 And if a kingdom is divided against itself, that kingdom cannot stand.
020325 And if a house is divided against itself, that house cannot stand.
020326 And if Satan rises up against himself, and is divided, he cannot stand, but has an end.
020327 No one can enter into a strong one's house and plunder his goods, except he first binds the strong man. And then he will plunder his house.
020328 Truly I say to you, all sins shall be forgiven to the sons of men, and blasphemies with which they shall blaspheme.
020329 But he who blasphemes against the Holy Spirit never shall have forgiveness, but is liable to eternal condemnation.
020330 Because they said, He has an unclean spirit.
020331 Then His brothers and His mother came. And standing outside, they sent to Him, calling Him.
020332 And the crowd sat about Him, and they said to Him, Behold, Your mother and Your brothers are outside seeking for You.
020333 And He answered them, saying, Who is My mother, or My brothers?
020334 And He looked around on those who sat about Him, and said, Behold My mother and My brothers!
020335 For whoever does the will of God, the same is My brother and My sister and My mother.
020401 And He began again to teach by the seaside. And there was a great crowd gathered to Him, so that He entered into a boat and sat in the sea. And the whole crowd was on the land by the seaside.
020402 And He taught them many things by a parable. And He said to them in His teaching:
020403 Listen! Behold, a sower went out to sow.
020404 And as he sowed, it happened that indeed some fell by the wayside, and the fowls of the air came and ate it up.
020405 And another fell on stony ground, where it did not have much earth. And it sprang up at once, due to not having deepness of earth.
020406 And when the sun rose, it was scorched. And because it had no root, it withered away.
020407 And another fell among the thorns, and the thorns grew up and choked it, and it yielded no fruit.
020408 And another fell on good ground and yielded fruit, going up and increasing. And one bore thirty, and one sixty, and one a hundredfold.
020409 And He said to them, He who has ears to hear, let him hear.
020410 And when He was alone, they who were about Him, with the Twelve, asked Him concerning the parable.
020411 And He said to them, To you it is given to know the mystery of the kingdom of God. But to those outside, all these things are given in parables
020412 so that seeing they may see, and not perceive; and hearing they may hear, and not understand; lest at any time they should be converted, and their sins should be forgiven them.
020413 And He said to them, Do you not know this parable? And how then will you know all parables?
020414 The sower sows the Word.
020415 And these are those by the wayside, where the Word is sown. And when they hear, Satan comes immediately and takes away the Word that was sown in their hearts.
020416 And these are those likewise being sown on stony places; who, when they hear the Word, immediately receive it with gladness.
020417 But they have no root in themselves, but are temporary. Afterward when affliction or persecution arises for the Word's sake, they are immediately offended.
020418 And these are those being sown among thorns; such as hear the Word,
020419 and the cares of this world, and the deceit of riches, and the lust about other things entering in, choke the Word, and it becomes unfruitful.
020420 And these are those sown on good ground, who hear the Word and welcome it , and bear fruit, one thirty, one sixty, and one a hundredfold.
020421 And He said to them, Does a lamp come to be put under a grain-measure, or under a bed? and not to be set on a lampstand?
020422 For there is nothing hidden which shall not be revealed; nor became covered, but that it might come to the light.
020423 If any man has ears to hear, let him hear.
020424 And He said to them, Take heed what you hear. With that measure which you measure, it shall be measured to you. And to you who hear, more shall be given.
020425 For he who has, more shall be given to him; and he who has not, from him shall be taken even that which he has.
020426 And He said, So is the kingdom of God, as if a man should cast seed into the ground;
020427 and should sleep, and rise night and day, and the seed should spring and grow up, he knows not how.
020428 For the earth brings out fruit of itself, first the blade, then the ear, after that the full grain in the ear.
020429 But when the fruit has been brought out, immediately he puts in the sickle, because the harvest has come.
020430 And He said, to what shall we compare the kingdom of God? Or by what parable shall we compare it?
020431 It is like a grain of mustard seed, which, when it is sown in the earth, is less than all the seeds that are in the earth.
020432 But when it has been sown, it grows up and becomes greater than all herbs, and shoots out great branches, so as to enable the birds of the air to roost under its shade.
020433 And with many such parables He spoke the Word to them, as they were able to hear it .
020434 But he did not speak to them without a parable. And when they were alone, He explained all things to His disciples.
020435 And evening having come, He said to them on that day, Let us pass over to the other side.
020436 And when they had sent away the crowd, they took Him with them as He was in the boat. And there were also other little boats with Him.
020437 And there arose a windstorm, and the waves beat into the boat, so that it was now full.
020438 And He was in the stern of the boat, asleep on a headrest. And they awakened Him and said to Him, Master, do You not care that we perish?
020439 And He awakened and rebuked the wind, and said to the sea, Peace! Be still! And the wind ceased, and there was a great calm.
020440 And He said to them, Why are you so fearful? How is it that you have no faith?
020441 And they feared exceedingly and said to one another, What kind of man is this, that even the winds and the sea obey Him?
020501 And they came over to the other side of the sea, to the country of the Gadarenes.
020502 And when He had come out of the boat, immediately a man with unclean spirits met Him out of the tombs,
020503 who had his dwelling among the tombs. And no one could bind him, no, not with chains
020504 because he had often been bound with fetters and chains, and the chains had been torn apart by him, and the fetters broken in pieces. Nor could anyone subdue him.
020505 And always, night and day, he was in the mountains and in the tombs, crying and cutting himself with stones.
020506 And when he saw Jesus afar off, he ran and worshiped Him,
020507 and cried with a loud voice, and said, What is to me and to You, Jesus, son of the Most High God? I adjure You by God not to torment me.
020508 For He said to him, Come out of the man, unclean spirit!
020509 And He asked him, What is your name? And he answered, saying, My name is Legion, for we are many.
020510 And he begged Him very much that He would not send them outside the country.
020511 And a great herd of pigs was feeding near the mountains.
020512 And all the demons begged Him, saying, Send us into the pigs, that we may enter into them.
020513 And immediately Jesus allowed them. And the unclean spirits went out and entered into the pigs. And the herd ran violently down a steep place into the sea (they were about two thousand), and were choked in the sea.
020514 And the ones who fed the pigs fled and told it in the city and in the country. And they went out to see what it was that was done.
020515 And they came to Jesus and saw him who had been demon-possessed, and had the legion, sitting and clothed and right-minded, the one who had the legion. And they were afraid.
020516 And those who had seen told them how it happened to the one who had been demon-possessed, and about the pigs.
020517 And they began to beg Him to leave their borders.
020518 And when He had come into the boat, the former demoniac begged Him that he might be with Him.
020519 However Jesus did not allow him, but said to him, Go home to your friends, and tell them what great things the Lord has done for you, and has had mercy on you.
020520 And he departed and began to proclaim in Decapolis how much Jesus had done for him. And all marvelled.
020521 And Jesus having crossed again by boat to the other side, a large crowd collected on Him. And He was near the sea.
020522 And, behold, one of the synagogue rulers came, Jairus by name. And when he saw Him, he fell at His feet.
020523 And he begged Him greatly, saying, My little daughter lies at the point of death. Come, lay Your hands on her, so that she may be healed, and she shall live.
020524 And Jesus went with him. And many people followed Him and thronged Him.
020525 And a certain woman who had had an issue of blood twelve years,
020526 and had suffered many things of many physicians, and had spent all that she had, and had not been bettered any, but rather came to worse,
020527 having heard about Jesus, she came in the press behind and touched His garment.
020528 For she said, If I may but touch only His clothes, I will be cured.
020529 And instantly the fountain of her blood dried up. And she felt in her body that she was healed of that plague.
020530 And knowing instantly within Himself that power had gone out of Him, Jesus turned Himself around in the press and said, Who touched My clothes?
020531 And His disciples said to Him, You see the crowd pressing on You, and do You say, Who touched Me?
020532 And He looked around to see her who had done this thing.
020533 But the woman, fearing and trembling, knowing what had been done in her, came and fell down before Him and told Him all the truth.
020534 And He said to her, Daughter, your faith has made you well. Go in peace, and be whole from your plague.
020535 While He still spoke, they came from the synagogue ruler's house, saying, Your daughter is dead; why do you still trouble the Teacher?
020536 But hearing the word spoken, Jesus said to the synagogue ruler, Do not be afraid, only believe.
020537 And He allowed no one to follow Him, except Peter and James and John, the brother of James.
020538 And He came to the synagogue ruler's and saw a tumult, and weeping and much wailing.
020539 And going in He said to them, Why do you make a tumult and weep? The girl is not dead, but sleeps.
020540 And they laughed at Him. But when He had put them all out, He took the father and the mother of the child, and those with Him, and went in where the child was lying.
020541 And He took the child's hand and said to her, Talitha koumi; (which interpreted is, Little girl, I say to you, arise!)
020542 And instantly the little girl arose and walked (for she was twelve years old ). And they were astonished with a great astonishment.
020543 And He strictly warned them that no one should know this. And He said to give her something to eat.
020601 And He went out from there and came into His native-place. And His disciples followed Him.
020602 And when the sabbath day had come, He began to teach in the synagogue. And many hearing Him , were astonished, saying, Where does this one get these things? And what wisdom is this which is given to him, that even such mighty works are done by his hands?
020603 Is not this the carpenter, the son of Mary, the brother of James and Joses and Judas and Simon? And are not his sisters here with us? And they were offended at Him.
020604 But Jesus said to them, A prophet is not without honor, except in his native-place, and among his own kin, and in his own house.
020605 And He could do no work of power there, except that He laid His hands on a few sick ones, He healed them .
020606 And He marveled because of their unbelief. And He went around the villages, in a circuit, teaching.
020607 And He called the Twelve and began to send them out by two and two. And He gave them authority over unclean spirits,
020608 and commanded them that they take nothing in the way, except only a staff; no bag, no bread, no copper in the belt,
020609 but tying on sandals, and not to put on two tunics.
020610 And He said to them, Wherever you enter into a house, abide there until you depart from that place .
020611 And whoever shall not receive you, nor hear you, when you depart from there, shake off the dust under your feet for a testimony against them. Truly I say to you, It shall be more tolerable for Sodom and Gomorrah in the day of judgment than for that city.
020612 And they went out and proclaimed that men should repent.
020613 And they cast out many demons, and anointed many who were sick with oil, and healed them .
020614 And king Herod heard of Him (for His name had become well-known,) and he said that John the Baptist had been raised from the dead, and therefore mighty works operate in him.
020615 Others said that it was Elijah. And others said that he is a prophet, or as one of the prophets.
020616 But hearing Herod said, It is John, whom I beheaded. He has risen from the dead!
020617 For Herod himself had sent out and laid hold on John and had bound him in prison because of Herodias, his brother Philip's wife. For he had married her,
020618 and John had said to Herod, It is not lawful for you to have your brother's wife.
020619 And Herodias held it against him, and desired to kill him, but she could not.
020620 For Herod feared John, knowing that he was a just and holy man. And he kept him safe. And when he heard him, he did many things and heard him gladly.
020621 And a convenient day came, when Herod made a supper to great men on his birthday, and to the chiliarchs, and to the first ones of Galilee.
020622 And when the daughter of Herodias herself came in and danced and pleased Herod, and those who reclined with him , the king said to the girl, Ask me whatever you desire from me, and I will give it to you.
020623 And he swore to her, Whatever you shall ask from me, I will give it to you, to the half of my kingdom.
020624 And she went out and said to her mother, What shall I ask? And she said, The head of John the Baptist.
020625 And immediately going in with haste to the king, she asked, saying, I desire that you give me at once the head of John the Baptist on a platter.
020626 And becoming deeply grieved, the king, because of his oath, and those reclining together, he did not wish to reject her.
020627 And immediately the king sent an executioner and commanded his head to be brought. And he went and beheaded him in the prison,
020628 and brought his head in a platter and gave it to the girl. And the girl gave it to her mother.
020629 And when his disciples heard, they came and took up his corpse and laid it in a tomb.
020630 And the apostles gathered themselves to Jesus and told Him all things, both what they had done and what they had taught.
020631 And He said to them, Come aside into a deserted place and rest a little. For there were many coming and going, and they had no opportunity even to eat.
020632 And they departed by boat into a deserted place.
020633 And the crowds saw them leaving, and many knew Him. And they ran together on foot there, out of the cities. And they went before them and came together to Him.
020634 And going out Jesus saw a large crowd. And He was moved with compassion toward them, because they were like sheep without a shepherd. And He began to teach them many things.
020635 And it now becoming a late hour, His disciples came to Him and said, This is a deserted place and it is now a late hour.
020636 Send them away so that they may go to the surrounding fields and villages and buy loaves for themselves. For they have nothing to eat.
020637 He answered and said to them, You give them food to eat. And they said to Him, Shall we go and buy two hundred denarii of loaves and give them to eat?
020638 He said to them, How many loaves do you have? Go and see. And when they knew, they said, Five, and two fish.
020639 And He commanded them all to recline, group by group, on the green grass.
020640 And they reclined group by group, by hundred and by fifty.
020641 And taking the five loaves and the two fish, He looked up to Heaven, He blessed and broke the loaves, and gave them to His disciples to set before them. And He divided the two fish to all.
020642 And they all ate and were filled.
020643 And they took up twelve hand baskets full of fragments, also from the fish.
020644 And those eating the loaves were about five thousand men.
020645 And immediately He constrained His disciples to get into the boat and to go before to the other side, to Bethsaida, while He sent away the crowd.
020646 And taking leave of them, He went away to the mountain to pray.
020647 And when evening had come, the boat was in the middle of the sea, and He was alone on the land.
020648 And He saw them toiling in rowing, for the wind was contrary to them. And about the fourth watch of the night He came toward them walking on the sea, and would have passed by them.
020649 But when they saw Him walking on the sea, they supposed that it was a phantom, and cried out.
020650 For they all saw Him and were troubled. And immediately He talked with them, and said, Be of good cheer. I AM! Do not be afraid.
020651 And He went up into the boat to them. And the wind was cut off. And they were very much amazed within themselves beyond measure, and marveled.
020652 For they did not understand the miracle of the loaves, for their hearts were hardened.
020653 And crossing over, they came into the land of Gennesaret and drew to the shore.
020654 And when they had come out of the boat, at once knowing Him,
020655 they ran all around that neighborhood, and began to carry on cots those who were sick, wherever they heard He was.
020656 And wherever He entered, into villages or cities or country, they laid the sick in the streets and begged Him if only they might touch but the fringe of His garment. And as many as touched Him were made whole.
020701 And the Pharisees and some of the scribes came together to Him, having come from Jerusalem.
020702 And when they saw some of His disciples eating loaves with unclean hands, that is with unwashed hands, they found fault.
020703 For the Pharisees and all the Jews do not eat unless they immerse their hands with the fist, holding the tradition of the elders.
020704 And coming from the market, they do not eat without immersing, and there are many other things which they have received to hold, the dippings of cups and pots, and of copper vessels, and of tables.
020705 Then the Pharisees and scribes asked Him, Why do your disciples not walk according to the tradition of the elders, but eat loaves with unwashed hands?
020706 But He answered and said to them, Well has Isaiah prophesied of you hypocrites, as it is written, "This people honors Me with their lips, but their heart is far from Me.
020707 However, they worship Me in vain, teaching for doctrines the commandments of men."
020708 For laying aside the commandment of God, you hold the tradition of men, the dippings of pots and cups. And many other such things you do.
020709 And He said to them, Do you do well to set aside the commandment of God, so that you may keep your own tradition?
020710 For Moses said, "Honor your father and your mother." And, "Whoever curses father or mother, let him die the death."
020711 But you say, If a man shall say to his father or mother, Corban! (that is, A gift to God , whatever you may profit by me)
020712 and you no longer allow him to do anything toward his father or mother,
020713 making the word of God of no effect through your tradition which you have delivered. And you do many such things.
020714 And calling near all the crowd, He said to them, Listen to Me, every one of you, and understand.
