020715 There is nothing from outside a man which entering into him can defile him . But the things which come out of him, those are the ones that defile the man.
020716 If anyone has ears to hear, let him hear.
020717 And when He had entered into the house away from the crowd, His disciples asked Him concerning the parable.
020718 And He said to them, Are you also without understanding? Do you not perceive that whatever enters into the man from outside cannot defile him,
020719 because it does not enter into his heart, but into the belly, and goes out into the waste-bowl, purifying all food?
020720 And He said, That which comes out of the man is what defiles the man.
020721 For from within, out of the heart of men, proceed evil thoughts, adulteries, fornications, murders,
020722 thefts, covetousness, wickedness, deceit, lasciviousness, an evil eye, blasphemy, pride, foolishness:
020723 All these evil things pass out from inside and defile the man.
020724 And He arose from there and went into the borders of Tyre and Sidon. And He entered into a house and desired no one to know it . But He could not be hidden.
020725 For a woman, whose young daughter had an unclean spirit, heard of Him and came and fell at His feet.
020726 The woman was a Greek, a Syro-phoenician by race. And she begged Him that He would cast the demon out of her daughter.
020727 But Jesus said to her, Let the children first be filled. For it is not right to take the children's loaves and to throw it to the dogs.
020728 And she answered and said to Him, Yes, Lord, yet the dogs under the table eat of the children's crumbs.
020729 And He said to her, For this saying go, the demon has gone out of your daughter.
020730 And when she had come to her house, she found the demon had gone out, and her daughter lay on the couch.
020731 And again, departing from the coasts of Tyre and Sidon, He came to the Sea of Galilee, in the midst of the borders of the Decapolis.
020732 And they brought a deaf one to Him, hardly speaking. And they begged Him to put His hand on him.
020733 And He took him aside from the crowd and put His fingers into his ears. And He spat and touched his tongue.
020734 And looking up to Heaven, He sighed and said to him, Ephphatha! (that is, Be opened!)
020735 And instantly his ears were opened and the bond of his tongue was loosened, and he spoke plainly.
020736 And He commanded them, that they should tell no one. But the more He commanded them, so much the more they proclaimed it .
020737 And they were astonished beyond measure, saying, He has done all things well. He makes both the deaf to hear and the dumb to speak.
020801 In those days, the crowd being very great and having nothing to eat, Jesus called His disciples and said to them,
020802 I have compassion on the crowd because they have now been with Me three days and have nothing to eat.
020803 And if I send them away fasting to their own houses, they will faint in the way. For many of them come from afar.
020804 And His disciples answered Him, From where can a man satisfy these with loaves here in the wilderness?
020805 And He asked them, How many loaves do you have? And they said, Seven.
020806 And He commanded the people to recline on the ground. And He took the seven loaves and gave thanks, and He broke and gave to His disciples to set before them. And they set them before the people.
020807 And they had a few fish. And He blessed and commanded them to also serve these.
020808 So they ate and were filled. And they took up over and above seven lunch baskets of fragments.
020809 And they who had eaten were about four thousand. And He sent them away.
020810 And immediately He entered into a boat with His disciples and came into the region of Dalmanutha.
020811 And the Pharisees came out and began to dispute with Him, seeking a sign from Heaven from Him, tempting Him.
020812 And He sighed deeply in His spirit and said, Why does this generation seek a sign? Truly I say to you, There shall no sign be given to this generation.
020813 And He left them. And entering into the boat again, He departed to the other side.
020814 And the disciples had forgotten to take loaves, and they did not have more than one loaf in the boat with them.
020815 And He charged them, saying, Take heed! Beware of the leaven of the Pharisees and of the leaven of Herod.
020816 And they reasoned among themselves, saying, It is because we have no loaves.
020817 And knowing it , Jesus said to them, Why do you reason that it is because you have no loaves? Do you not yet perceive nor understand? Have you still hardened your heart?
020818 Do you have eyes and do not see? Do you have ears and do not hear? And do you not remember?
020819 When I broke the five loaves among five thousand, how many hand baskets full of fragments did you take up? They said to Him, Twelve.
020820 And when the seven among four thousand, how many lunch baskets full of fragments did you take up? And they said, Seven.
020821 And He said to them, How do you not understand?
020822 And He came to Bethsaida. And they brought a blind man to Him and begged Him to touch him.
020823 And He took the blind man by the hand and led him out of the town. And when He had spat on his eyes and had put His hands on him, He asked Him if he saw anything.
020824 And he looked up and said, I see men as trees, walking.
020825 And after that He put His hands again on his eyes and made him look up. And he was restored and saw all clearly.
020826 And He sent him away to his house, saying, Neither go into the town, nor tell it to any in the town.
020827 And Jesus and His disciples went out into the towns of Caesarea Philippi. And in the way He asked His disciples, saying to them, Who do men say that I am?
020828 And they answered, John the Baptist. But others say Elijah, and others say one of the prophets.
020829 And He said to them, But who do you say that I am? And Peter answered and said to Him, You are the Christ.
020830 And He charged them that they should tell no one of Him.
020831 And He began to teach them that the Son of man must suffer many things and be rejected by the elders and the chief priests and scribes, and be killed, and after three days rise again.
020832 And He spoke that saying openly. And Peter took Him and began to rebuke Him.
020833 But when He had turned around and looked on His disciples, He rebuked Peter, saying, Go behind Me, Satan! For you do not mind the things of God, but of the things of men.
020834 And calling near the crowd with His disciples, He said to them, Whoever will come after Me, let him deny himself and take up his cross and follow Me.
020835 For whoever will save his life shall lose it; but whoever shall lose his life for My sake and the gospel's, he shall save it.
020836 For what shall it profit a man if he shall gain the whole world and lose his own soul?
020837 Or what shall a man give in exchange for his soul?
020838 Therefore whoever shall be ashamed of Me and of My words in this adulterous and sinful generation, the Son of man shall also be ashamed of him when He comes in the glory of His Father with the holy angels.
020901 And He said to them, Truly I say to you that there are some of those who stand here who shall not taste of death until they see the kingdom of God come with power.
020902 And after six days Jesus took Peter and James and John and led them up into a high mountain, apart by themselves. And He was transfigured before them.
020903 And His clothing became shining, exceedingly white as snow such as no fuller on earth could whiten them.
020904 And Elijah with Moses was seen by them, and they were talking with Jesus.
020905 And Peter answered and said to Jesus, Rabbi, it is good for us to be here. And let us make three tabernacles, one for You, and one for Moses, and one for Elijah.
020906 For he did not know what to say, for they were very much afraid.
020907 And there was a cloud that overshadowed them. And a voice came out of the cloud, saying, This is My beloved Son. Hear Him.
020908 And suddenly, looking around, they did not see anyone any more, except Jesus alone with themselves.
020909 And as they came down from the mountain, He commanded them that they should tell no one the things that they had seen until the Son of man had risen from the dead.
020910 And they kept that saying within themselves, debating with one another what the rising from the dead is .
020911 And they asked Him, saying, Why do the scribes say that Elijah must first come?
020912 And He answered and told them, Elijah truly does come first and restores all things. And how has it been written of the Son of man that He should suffer many things and be despised?
020913 But I say to you that Elijah has indeed come, and they have done to him whatever they desired, as it is written of him.
020914 And coming to His disciples, He saw a great crowd around them, and scribes arguing with them.
020915 And immediately all the crowd, seeing Him, were greatly amazed, and they were running to Him to greet Him.
020916 And He asked the scribes, What are you discussing with them?
020917 And one of the crowd answered and said, Teacher, I have brought my son who has a dumb spirit to You.
020918 And wherever he seizes him, he dashes him. And he foams and gnashes his teeth and pines away. And I spoke to Your disciples that they should cast him out, and they could not.
020919 He answered him and said, O faithless generation, how long shall I be with you? How long shall I bear with you? Bring him to Me!
020920 And they brought him to Him. And when he saw Him, the spirit immediately convulsed him. And he fell on the ground and wallowed, foaming.
020921 And He asked his father, How long ago has it been since this came to him? And he said, From childhood.
020922 And oftentimes it has cast him into the fire and into the waters to destroy him. But if You can do anything, have compassion on us and help us.
020923 Jesus said to him, If you can believe, all things are possible to him who believes.
020924 And immediately the father of the child cried out and said with tears, Lord, I believe. Help my unbelief.
020925 And seeing that a crowd is running together, Jesus rebuked the unclean spirit, saying to him, Dumb and deaf spirit, I command you, come out of him and enter no more into him!
020926 And the spirit cried out, throwing him into convulsions, and came out of him. And he was like one dead, so that many said, He is dead.
020927 But Jesus took him by the hand and lifted him up, and he arose.
020928 And He entering into a house, His disciples asked Him privately, Why could we not cast him out?
020929 And He said to them, This kind can come out by nothing except by prayer and fasting.
020930 And going out from there, they passed through Galilee. And He desired that no one should know.
020931 For He taught His disciples and said to them, The Son of man is delivered into the hands of men, and they shall kill him. And after He is killed, He shall rise the third day.
020932 But they did not understand that saying and were afraid to ask Him.
020933 And He came to Capernaum. And being in the house, He asked them, What was it that you disputed among yourselves in the way?
020934 But they were silent. For in the way they had disputed among themselves who was the greatest.
020935 And He sat down and called the Twelve and said to them, If anyone desires to be first, he shall be last of all and servant of all.
020936 And He took a child, and embraced it, and set him in their midst. And He said to them,
020937 Whoever receives one of such children on My name receives Me. And whoever receives Me does not only receives Me, but Him who sent Me.
020938 And John answered him, saying, Master, we saw one casting out demons in Your name, and he does not follow us. And we forbade him, because he does not follow us.
020939 But Jesus said, Do not forbid him. For there is no one who shall do a work of power in My name who can lightly speak evil of Me.
020940 For he who is not against us is for us.
020941 For whoever shall give you a cup of water to drink in My name, because you belong to Christ, truly I say to you, he shall not lose his reward.
020942 And whoever shall offend one of these little ones who believe in Me, it is better for him that a millstone were hanged around his neck and he were cast into the sea.
020943 And if your hand offends you, cut it off. It is better for you to enter into life maimed than to have two hands to go into hell, into the fire that never shall be quenched
020944 where their worm dies not, and the fire is not quenched.
020945 And if your foot offends you, cut it off. It is better for you to enter into life lame than to have two feet to be cast into hell, into the fire that never shall be quenched
020946 where their worm dies not, and the fire is not quenched.
020947 And if your eye offends you, pluck it out. It is better for you to enter into the kingdom of God with one eye than to have two eyes to be cast into hell fire
020948 where their worm dies not, and the fire is not quenched.
020949 For every one shall be salted with fire, and every sacrifice shall be salted with salt.
020950 Salt is good; but if the salt becomes saltless, with what will you season? Have salt in yourselves, and be at peace with one another.
021001 And He arose from there. And He came into the borders of Judea by the other side of the Jordan. And again a crowd came together to Him. And as was His custom, He taught them again.
021002 And tempting Him, the Pharisees came to Him and asked Him, Is it lawful for a man to put away his wife?
021003 And He answered and said to them, What did Moses command you?
021004 And they said, Moses allowed a bill of divorce to be written, and to put her away.
021005 And Jesus answered and said to them, He wrote you this precept because of the hardness of your hearts.
021006 But from the beginning of the creation God made them male and female.
021007 For this cause a man shall leave his father and mother and shall cleave to his wife.
021008 And the two of them shall be one flesh. So then they are no longer two, but one flesh.
021009 Therefore what God has joined together, let not man put apart.
021010 And in the house His disciples asked Him again about the same.
021011 And He said to them, Whoever shall put away his wife and marries another commits adultery against her.
021012 And if a woman shall put away her husband and marries to another, she commits adultery.
021013 And they brought children to Him, so that He should touch them. And His disciples rebuked those bringing them .
021014 But when Jesus saw, He was much displeased and said to them, Allow the little children to come to Me and do not hinder them . For of such is the kingdom of God.
021015 Truly I say to you, Whoever shall not receive the kingdom of God as a little child, he shall not enter into it.
021016 And taking them up in His arms, He put His hands on them and blessed them.
021017 And when He had gone out into the way, one came running up and kneeled to Him, and asked Him, Good Master, what shall I do that I may inherit eternal life?
021018 And Jesus said to him, Why do you call Me good? No one is good except one, God.
021019 You know the commandments: Do not commit adultery, do not kill, do not steal, do not bear false witness, do not defraud, honor your father and your mother.
021020 And he answered and said to Him, Teacher, all these I have observed from my youth.
021021 Then Jesus, beholding him, loved him and said to him, One thing you lack. Go, sell whatever you have and give it to the poor, and you shall have treasure in Heaven. And come, take up the cross and follow Me.
021022 And he was sad at that saying and went away grieved, for he had great possessions.
021023 And Jesus looked around and said to His disciples, How hardly those having riches will enter into the kingdom of God!
021024 And the disciples were astonished at His words. But Jesus answering again said to them, Children, how hard it is for those who trust in riches to enter into the kingdom of God!
021025 It is easier for a camel to go through the eye of a needle than for a rich one to enter into the kingdom of God.
021026 And they were astonished beyond measure, saying to themselves, And who can be saved?
021027 And Jesus looking on them said, With men it is impossible, but not with God; for with God all things are possible.
021028 Then Peter began to say to Him, Lo, we have left all and have followed You.
021029 And Jesus answered and said, Truly I say to you, There is no man that has left house or brothers or sisters or father or mother or wife or children or lands for my sake and the gospel's sake,
021030 but he shall receive a hundredfold now in this time, houses and brothers and sisters and mothers and children and lands with persecutions, and in the world to come, eternal life.
021031 But many that are first shall be last; and the last shall be first.
021032 And they were in the way going up to Jerusalem. And Jesus went before them. And they were amazed, and as they followed, they were afraid. And he took the Twelve again and began to tell them what would happen to Him,
021033 saying , Behold, we go up to Jerusalem. And the Son of man will be betrayed to the chief priests and to the scribes. And they will condemn Him to death and will deliver Him to the nations.
021034 And they will mock Him, and will scourge Him, and will spit on Him, and will kill Him. And the third day He shall rise again.
021035 And James and John, the sons of Zebedee, came up to Him, saying, Master, we desire that You should do for us whatever we shall ask.
021036 And He said to them, What do you desire that I should do for you?
021037 They said to Him, Grant to us that we may sit, one on Your right hand and the other on Your left hand, in Your glory.
021038 But Jesus said to them, You do not know what you ask. Can you drink of the cup that I drink of, and be baptized with the baptism that I am baptized with ?
021039 And they said to Him, We can. And Jesus said to them, You shall indeed drink of the cup that I drink of, and with the baptism that I am baptized with you shall be baptized.
021040 But to sit on My right hand and on My left is not Mine to give, but to those for whom it is prepared.
021041 And when the ten heard, they began to be indignant with James and John.
021042 But Jesus called them and said to them, You know that they who are accounted rulers over the nations exercise lordship over them. And their great ones exercise authority on them.
021043 But it shall not be so among you. But whoever desires to be great among you, let him be your servant.
021044 And whoever of you desires to become first, he shall be servant of all.
021045 For even the Son of man did not come to be served, but to serve, and to give His life as a ransom for many.
021046 And they came to Jericho. And as He with His disciples and a large crowd went out of Jericho, blind Bartimeus, the son of Timeus, was sitting by the side of the highway, begging.
021047 And when he heard that it was Jesus of Nazareth, he began to cry out and say, Jesus, son of David, have mercy on me!
021048 And many warned him that he should be quiet, but he cried a great deal more, Son of David, have mercy on me!
021049 And Jesus stood still and commanded him to be called. And they called the blind man , saying to him, Be of good comfort; rise up, He is calling you.
021050 And casting away his garment, he rose up and came to Jesus.
021051 And answering Jesus said to him, What do you desire that I should do to you? The blind man said to Him, My Lord, that I may see again.
021052 And Jesus said to him, Go, your faith has healed you. And instantly he saw again, and he followed Jesus in the way.
021101 And when they drew near to Jerusalem, to Bethphage and Bethany, at the Mount of Olives, He sent out two of His disciples.
021102 And He said to them, Go into the village over across from you. And as soon as you have entered into it, you will find a colt tied, on which no one of men has ever sat. Untie it and bring it .
021103 And if anyone says to you, Why do you do this? Say that the Lord has need of him, and immediately he will send him here.
021104 And they went, and they found the colt tied by the door outside, in a place where two ways met. And they untied him.
021105 And certain of those who stood there said to them, What are you doing, untying the colt?
021106 And they said to them even as Jesus had commanded. And they let them go.
021107 And they brought the colt to Jesus, and they threw their garments on it. And He sat on it.
021108 And many spread their garments in the way, and others cut down branches off the trees and scattered them in the way.
021109 And those going before, and those following, cried out, saying, Hosanna! Blessed is He who comes in the name of the Lord!
021110 Blessed is the kingdom of our father David, who comes in the name of the Lord! Hosanna in the highest!
021111 And Jesus entered into Jerusalem and into the temple. And when He had looked around on all things, the hour already being late, He went out to Bethany with the Twelve.
021112 And on the next day, they going out of Bethany, He was hungry.
021113 And seeing a fig-tree with leaves afar off, He went to it , if perhaps He might find anything on it. And when He came to it, He found nothing but leaves, for it was not the season of figs.
021114 And Jesus answered and said to it, No one shall eat fruit of you forever. And His disciples heard.
021115 And they came to Jerusalem. And entering into the temple, Jesus began to cast out those who bought and sold in the temple. And He overthrew the tables of the money-changers and the seats of those who sold doves.
021116 And He would not allow any to carry a vessel through the temple.
021117 And He taught, saying to them, Is it not written, "My house shall be called the house of prayer for all nations?" But you have made it a den of thieves.
021118 And the scribes and the chief priests heard. And they sought how they might destroy Him. For they feared Him, because all the people were astonished at His doctrine.
021119 And when evening came, He went out of the city.
021120 And passing on early, they saw the fig-tree dried up from the roots.
021121 And Peter, remembering, said to Him, Rabbi, behold, the fig tree which You cursed has withered away.
021122 And answering Jesus said to them, Have faith of God.
021123 For truly I say to you that whoever shall say to this mountain, Be moved and be cast into the sea, and shall not doubt in his heart, but shall believe that what he said shall occur, he shall have whatever he said.
021124 Therefore I say to you, All things, whatever you ask, praying, believe that you shall receive them , and it will be to you.
021125 And when you stand praying, if you have anything against anyone, forgive it so that also your Father in Heaven may forgive you your trespasses.
021126 But if you do not forgive, neither will your Father in Heaven forgive your trespasses.
021127 And they came again to Jerusalem. And as He was walking in the temple, the chief priests and the scribes and the elders came to Him
021128 and said to Him, By what authority do you do these things? And who gave you this authority to do these things?
021129 And Jesus answered and said to them, I will also ask of you one thing, and answer Me, and I will tell you by what authority I do these things.
021130 The baptism of John, was it from Heaven, or from men? Answer Me.
021131 And they reasoned within themselves, saying, If we shall say, From Heaven, he will say, Why then did you not believe him?
021132 But if we shall say, From men, they feared the people, for all held John to be a prophet indeed.
021133 And they answered and said to Jesus, We cannot tell. And answering Jesus said to them, Neither do I tell you by what authority I do these things.
021201 And He began to speak to them by parables. A man planted a vineyard, and set a fence about it , and dug a wine-vat, and built a tower, and he let it out to vinedressers, and went away.
021202 And at the season he sent a servant to the vinedressers, so that he might receive from the vinedressers the fruit of the vineyard.
021203 And taking him , they beat him and sent him away empty.
021204 And again he sent to them another servant. And stoning that one, they struck him in the head, and sent him away, insulting him.
021205 And again he sent another. And they killed him, and many others, beating some and killing some.
021206 Therefore, still having one son, his own beloved, he also sent him to them last of all, saying, They will respect my son.
021207 But those vinedressers said among themselves, This is the heir! Come, let us kill him and the inheritance shall be ours.
021208 And they took him and killed him and cast him out of the vineyard.
021209 Therefore what will the lord of the vineyard do? He will come and destroy the vinedressers and will give the vineyard to others.
021210 And have you not read this scripture " The Stone which the builders rejected has become the Head of the corner:
021211 this was from the Lord, and it is marvelous in our eyes"?
021212 And they sought to seize him, but feared the crowd. For they knew that He spoke the parable against them. And leaving Him, they went away.
021213 And they sent certain of the Pharisees and of the Herodians to Him, to catch Him in His words.
021214 And coming, they said to Him, Teacher, we know that you are true and you care about no one. For you do not look to the face of men, but teach the way of God in truth. Is it lawful to give tribute to Caesar, or not?
021215 Shall we give, or shall we not give? But knowing their hypocrisy, He said to them, Why do you tempt Me? Bring me a denarius so that I may see.
021216 And they brought it . And He said to them, Whose image and inscription is this? And they said to Him, Caesar's.
021217 And answering Jesus said to them, Render to Caesar the things that are Caesar's, and to God the things that are God's. And they marvelled at Him.
021218 Then the Sadducees came to Him, who say there is no resurrection. And they asked Him, saying,
021219 Teacher, Moses wrote to us, If a man's brother die and leaves his wife, and leaves no children, his brother should take his wife and raise up seed to his brother.
021220 And there were seven brothers. And the first took a wife, and dying left no seed.
021221 And the second took her, and died; neither did he leave any seed. And the third likewise.
021222 And the seven had her, and left no seed. Last of all the woman also died.
021223 In the resurrection therefore, when they shall rise, whose wife will she be? For the seven had her as a wife.
021224 And answering Jesus said to them, Do you not err because of this, not knowing Scriptures, nor the power of God?
021225 For when they shall rise from the dead, they neither marry nor are given in marriage, but they are as the angels in Heaven.
021226 And as regards the dead, that they rise, have you not read in the book of Moses how God spoke to him in the Bush, saying, "I am the God of Abraham and the God of Isaac and the God of Jacob?"
021227 He is not the God of the dead, but the God of the living. Therefore you greatly err.
021228 And coming up one of the scribes heard them reasoning, knowing that He had answered them well, he asked Him, Which is the first commandment of all?
021229 And Jesus answered him, The first of all the commandments is , "Hear, O Israel, the Lord our God is one Lord;
021230 and you shall love the Lord your God with all your heart, and with all your soul, and with all your mind, and with all your strength." This is the first commandment.
021231 And the second is like this: You shall love your neighbor as yourself. There is no other commandment greater than these.
021232 And the scribe said to Him, Right, Teacher, according to truth You have spoken, that God is one, and there is no other besides Him.
021233 And to love Him with all the heart, and with all the understanding, and with all the soul, and with all the strength, and to love the neighbor as himself, is more than all the burnt offerings and sacrifices.
021234 And seeing that he had answered intelligently, Jesus said to him, You are not far from the kingdom of God. And no one dared to question Him any more.
021235 And answering, teaching in the temple, Jesus said, How do the scribes say that Christ is the Son of David?
021236 For David himself said by the Holy Spirit: "The LORD said to my Lord, Sit at My right hand until I place Your enemies as Your footstool."
021237 David therefore himself calls Him Lord, and why then is He his son? And the great crowd heard Him gladly.
021238 And He said to them in His teaching, Beware of the scribes, who love to walk about in robes, and love greetings in the markets,
021239 and the chief seats in the synagogues, and the uppermost places at feasts
021240 who devour widows' houses, and as a pretense make long prayers. These shall receive greater condemnation.
021241 And sitting down opposite the treasury, Jesus watched how the people threw copper coins into the treasury. And many rich ones threw in much.
021242 And a certain poor widow came, and she threw in two lepta, which is a kodrantes.
021243 And He called His disciples and said to them, Truly I say to you that this poor widow has cast in more than all those who have cast into the treasury.
021244 For all cast in from their abundance. But she, out of her poverty, has cast in all that she had, all her livelihood.
021301 And as He went out of the temple, one of His disciples said to Him, Master, see! What stones and what buildings!
021302 And answering Jesus said to him, Do you see these great buildings? There shall not be one stone left on another that shall not be thrown down.
021303 And as He sat on the Mount of Olives, across from the temple, Peter and James and John and Andrew asked Him privately,
021304 Tell us, When shall all these things be? And what shall be the sign when all these things shall be fulfilled?
021305 And Jesus answering them began to say, Beware that no one deceive you.
021306 For many shall come in My name, saying, I AM, and shall deceive many.
021307 And when you shall hear of wars and rumors of wars, do not be troubled. For it must happen, but the end shall not be yet.
021308 For nation shall rise against nation, and kingdom against kingdom. And there shall be earthquakes in different places, and there shall be famines and troubles. These things are the beginnings of sorrows.
021309 But take heed to yourselves. For they shall deliver you up to sanhedrins, and in the synagogues you shall be beaten. And you shall be brought before rulers and kings for My sake, for a testimony against them.
021310 And the gospel must first be proclaimed to all nations.
021311 But whenever they lead you away and deliver you up, take no thought beforehand what you should speak or think. But speak whatever shall be given to you in that hour. For it is not you who speaks, but the Holy Spirit.
021312 And a brother will betray a brother to death, and a father his son. And children will rise up against their parents and will cause them to be put to death.
021313 And you will be hated by all for My name's sake, but he enduring to the end, that one will be kept safe.
021314 But when you see the abomination of desolation, that spoken of by Daniel the prophet, standing where it ought not (let him who reads understand), then let those who are in Judea flee to the mountains.
021315 And let him who is on the housetop not go down into the house, nor enter to take anything out of his house.
021316 And let him who is in the field not turn back again in order to take up his garment.
021317 But woe to those with babe in womb, and to those who give suck in those days!
021318 And pray that your flight is not in the winter.
021319 For in those days shall be affliction, such as has not been from the beginning of the creation which God created until now, and never shall be.
021320 And unless the Lord had shortened those days, no flesh would be saved. But for the elect's sake, whom He has chosen, He has shortened the days.
021321 And then if anyone shall say to you, Lo, here is Christ! Or, lo, there! Do not believe him.
021322 For false Christs and false prophets will arise and will give miraculous signs and wonders in order to seduce, if possible, even the elect.
021323 But take heed; behold, I have told you all things beforehand.
021324 But in those days, after that tribulation, the sun shall be darkened, and the moon shall not give her light,
021325 and the stars of Heaven shall fall, and the powers in the heavens shall be shaken.
021326 And then they will see the Son of man coming in the clouds with great power and glory.
021327 And then He shall send His angels and shall gather His elect from the four winds, from the end of the earth to the end of heaven.
021328 And learn the parable of the fig-tree: when her branch is still tender and puts out leaves, you know that summer is near.
021329 So you also, when you see these things happening, you know that it is near, at the doors.
021330 Truly I say to you that this generation shall not pass away until all these things occur.
021331 Heaven and earth shall pass away, but My words shall not pass away.
021332 But of that day and hour no one knows, no, not the angels in Heaven, nor the Son, but the Father.
021333 Take heed, watch and pray, for you do not know when the time is.
021334 As a man going away, leaving his house, and giving authority to his servants, and each man's work to him, and commanded the doorkeeper to watch.
021335 Then you watch, for you do not know when the lord of the house is coming, at evening, or at midnight, or at cockcrowing, or early;
021336 lest he come suddenly and find you sleeping.
021337 And what I say to you, I say to all. Watch.
021401 And after two days it was the Passover and the Feast of Unleavened Bread. And the chief priests and the scribes sought how they might take Him by craft and kill Him.
021402 But they said, Not during the Feast, lest there be an uproar of the people.
021403 And being in Bethany in the house of Simon the leper, as He reclined, a woman came with an alabaster vial of pure, costly ointment of spikenard. And she broke the vial and poured it on His head.
021404 And some were indignant to themselves, and said, Why was this waste of the ointment made?
021405 For it might have been sold for more than three hundred denarii, and be given to the poor. And they were incensed with her.
021406 And Jesus said, Let her alone! Why do you trouble her? She has done a good work towards Me.
021407 For you have the poor with you always, and whenever you desire you may do them good. But you do not have Me always.
021408 She has done what she could. She has come beforehand to anoint My body for the burying.
021409 Truly I say to you, Wherever this gospel shall be proclaimed in all the world, this also that she has done will be spoken of for a memorial of her.
021410 And Judas Iscariot, one of the Twelve, went to the chief priests in order to betray Him to them.
021411 And when they heard, they were glad and promised to give him silver. And he sought how he might conveniently betray Him.
021412 And the first day of Unleavened Bread , when they killed the passover, His disciples said to Him, Where do You desire that we go and prepare that You may eat the passover?
021413 And He sent out two of His disciples and said to them, Go into the city, and there you shall meet a man bearing a pitcher of water. Follow him.
021414 And wherever he may go in, you say to the housemaster, The Teacher says, Where is the guest room where I shall eat the passover with My disciples?
021415 And he will show you a large upper room, furnished and prepared. Prepare there for us.
021416 And His disciples went out and came into the city and found it as He had said to them. And they made the passover ready.
021417 And in the evening He came with the Twelve.
021418 And as they reclined and ate, Jesus said, Truly I say to you, One of you will betray Me, the one eating with Me.
021419 And they began to be grieved, and to say to Him one by one, Not at all I, is it ? And another said, Not at all I, is it ?
021420 And answering He said to them, It is one of the Twelve, the one dipping with Me in the dish.
021421 The Son of man indeed goes, as it has been written of Him, but woe to that man by whom the Son of man is betrayed! It were good for that man if he had never been born.
021422 And as they ate, Jesus took a loaf and blessed and broke it , and He gave to them and said, Take, eat; this is My body.
021423 And taking the cup, giving thanks, He gave to them. And they all drank out of it.
021424 And He said to them, This is My blood of the New Covenant, which is poured out for many.
021425 Truly I say to you, I will no more drink of the fruit of the vine until that day that I drink it new in the kingdom of God.
021426 And when they had sung a hymn, they went out to the Mount of Olives.
021427 And Jesus said to them, All of you will be offended because of Me this night. For it is written, "I will smite the Shepherd, and the sheep shall be scattered."
021428 But after I am raised, I will go before you into Galilee.
021429 But Peter said to Him, Although all shall be offended, yet I will not.
021430 And Jesus said to him, Truly I say to you that today, in this night, before the cock crows twice, you shall deny Me three times.
021431 But he spoke the more fervently, If I should die with You, I will not deny You in any way. Also they all said likewise.
021432 And they came to a place named Gethsemane. And He said to His disciples, Sit here while I pray.
021433 And He took with Him Peter and James and John. And He began to be greatly amazed, and to be very heavy.
021434 And He said to them, My soul is exceedingly sorrowful to death. Stay here and watch.
021435 And He went forward a little and fell on the ground. And He prayed that, if it were possible, the hour might pass from Him.
021436 And He said, Abba, Father, all things are possible to You. Take away this cup from Me. Yet not what I will, but what You will .
021437 And He came and found them sleeping, and said to Peter, Simon, do you sleep? Could you not watch one hour?
021438 Watch and pray, lest you enter into temptation. Truly the spirit is willing, but the flesh is weak.
021439 And again He went away and prayed and spoke the same words.
021440 And when He returned, He found them asleep again (for their eyes were heavy), neither did they know what to answer Him.
021441 And He came the third time and said to them, Sleep on now and take your rest. It is enough, the hour has come. Behold, the Son of man has been betrayed into the hands of sinners.
021442 Rise up, let us go. Lo, he who betrays Me is at hand.
021443 And immediately, while He still spoke, Judas, being one of the Twelve, came, and with him a great crowd with swords and clubs, from the chief priests and the scribes and the elders.
021444 And he who betrayed Him had given them a sign, saying, Whomever I shall kiss, it is He. Take Him and lead Him away safely.
021445 And coming, at once drawing near to Him, he said, Rabbi, Rabbi! And he ardently kissed Him.
021446 And they laid their hands on Him and seized Him.
021447 And one of those standing by, drawing a sword, struck a servant of the high priest, and cut off his ear.
021448 And answering Jesus said to them, Have you come out with swords and clubs, as against a robber, to take Me?
021449 I was with you daily in the temple teaching, and you did not seize Me. But the Scriptures must be fulfilled.
021450 And leaving Him, all fled.
021451 And one, a certain young man, followed Him, having thrown a linen cloth around his naked body . And the young men caught him.
021452 And he left the linen cloth and fled from them naked.
021453 And they led Jesus away to the high priest. And with him were assembled all the chief priests and the elders and the scribes.
021454 And Peter followed Him from a distance to the inside of the court of the high priest. And he sat with the servants and warmed himself at the fire.
021455 And the chief priests and all the sanhedrin sought for witness against Jesus, to put Him to death. And they found none.
021456 For many testified falsely against Him, but the testimonies were not identical.
021457 And certain ones rose up and bore false witness against Him, saying,
021458 We heard Him say, I will destroy this temple that is made with hands, and within three days I will build another made without hands.
021459 But neither was their testimony identical.
021460 And standing up in the middle, the high priest questioned Jesus, saying, Do you answer nothing? What do these witness against you?
021461 But He was silent and answered nothing. Again the high priest asked Him, saying to Him, Are you the Christ, the son of the Blessed?
021462 And Jesus said, I AM! And you will see the Son of man sitting on the right hand of power and coming in the clouds of the heaven.
021463 Then the high priest tore his clothes and said, What further need do we have of witnesses?
021464 You have heard the blasphemy; what do you think? And they all condemned Him to be guilty of death.
021465 And some began to spit on Him, and to cover His face and to beat Him, and to say to Him, Prophesy! And the under-officers struck Him with slaps.
021466 And as Peter was below in the palace, one of the servant women of the high priest came.
021467 And when she saw Peter warming himself, she looked on him and said, And you also were with Jesus the Nazarene.
021468 But he denied, saying, I do not know nor even understand what you are saying. And he went out into the forecourt. And a cock crowed.
021469 And a servant woman saw him again and began to say to those who stood by, This one is of them.
021470 And he denied it again. And a little after, those who stood by said again to Peter, Surely you are one of them, for you are a Galilean, and your speech agrees.
021471 But he began to curse and to swear, saying , I do not know this man of whom you speak.
021472 And the second time a cock crowed. And Peter remembered the word that Jesus said to him, Before a cock crows twice, you will deny Me three times. And thinking on it , he wept.
021501 And immediately in the morning the chief priests held a consultation with the elders and scribes and the whole council. And they bound Jesus and led Him away and delivered Him to Pilate.
021502 And Pilate asked Him, Are you the king of the Jews? And answering He said to him, You say it .
021503 And the chief priests accused Him of many things, but He answered nothing.
021504 And Pilate asked Him again, saying, Do you answer nothing? Behold how many things they witness against you!
021505 But Jesus still answered nothing, so that Pilate marveled.
021506 And at that feast he released to them one prisoner, whomever they desired.
021507 And there was one named Barabbas, bound with the insurgents, who had committed murder in the insurrection.
021508 And the crowd, crying aloud, began to beg him to do as he had always done to them.
021509 But Pilate answered them, saying, Do you desire that I release to you the King of the Jews?
021510 For he knew that the chief priests had delivered Him because of envy.
021511 But the chief priests moved the people that he should rather release Barabbas to them.
021512 And Pilate answered and said again to them, What then do you desire that I should do to him whom you call the King of the Jews?
021513 And they cried out again, Crucify him!
021514 Then Pilate said to them, Why? What evil has he done? And they much more cried out, Crucify him!
021515 And deciding to do the easiest to the crowd, Pilate released Barabbas to them, and having scourged Him , delivered up Jesus to be crucified.
021516 And the soldiers led Him away inside the court, which is the praetorium. And they called together all the cohort.
021517 And they clothed Him with purple and plaited a crown of thorns and put it around His head .
021518 And they began to salute Him, Hail, King of the Jews!
021519 And they struck Him on the head with a reed, and spat on Him, and placing the knees, they bowed to Him.
021520 And when they had mocked Him, they took the purple off Him and put His own clothes on Him and led Him out to crucify Him.
021521 And they made one who was passing by, Simon a Cyrenian, coming out of the country, the father of Alexander and Rufus, to bear His cross.
021522 And they brought Him to Golgotha Place (which translated is, Place of a Skull).
021523 And they gave Him wine mixed with myrrh to drink. But He did not take it .
021524 And when they had crucified Him, they divided His garments, casting lots on them, as, to what each should take.
021525 And it was the third hour, and they crucified Him.
021526 And the inscription of His accusation was written over Him , THE KING OF THE JEWS.
021527 And with Him they crucified two thieves, the one off the right, and one off the left.
021528 And the Scripture was fulfilled which said, "And he was numbered with the lawless."
021529 And those who passed by blasphemed Him, wagging their heads and saying, Aha! You razing the temple and building it in three days,
021530 save yourself and come down from the cross!
021531 And also the chief priests mocking, with the scribes, said to one another, He saved others but he cannot save himself.
021532 Let Christ the King of Israel now come down from the cross, so that we may see and believe. And they who were crucified with Him insulted Him.
021533 And it being the sixth hour, darkness came over all the land until the ninth hour.
021534 And at the ninth hour Jesus cried with a loud voice, saying, Eloi, Eloi, lama sabachthani? (which being translated is, My God, My God, why did You forsake Me?)
021535 And hearing, some of those standing by said, Behold, he calls Elijah.
021536 And one ran and filled a sponge full of vinegar and put it on a reed and gave it to him to drink. But they said , Let alone, let us see if Elijah comes to take him down.
021537 And letting out a loud voice, Jesus expired.
021538 And the veil of the temple was torn in two from top to bottom.
021539 And when the centurion, who stood across from him, saw that He cried out so, and expired, he said, Truly this man was Son of God.
021540 And also women were watching from a distance, among whom also was Mary Magdalene, and Mary the mother of James the less, and of Joses, and Salome,
021541 (who also, when He was in Galilee, followed Him and ministered to Him), and many other women who came up with Him to Jerusalem.
021542 And it, becoming evening already, since it was the Preparation, that is, the day before sabbath,
021543 Joseph of Arimathea, an honorable counsellor, who also waited for the kingdom of God, came and went in boldly to Pilate and asked for the body of Jesus.
021544 And Pilate wondered if He were already dead. And calling the centurion, he asked him whether He had died already.
021545 And when he knew it from the centurion, he gave the body to Joseph.
021546 And he bought a linen cloth, and took Him down, and wrapped Him in the linen, and laid Him in a tomb which was cut out of a rock, and rolled a stone to the door of the tomb.
021547 And Mary Magdalene and Mary the mother of Joses saw where He was laid.
021601 And when the sabbath was past, Mary Magdalene and Mary, the mother of James and Salome, had bought sweet spices so that they might come and anoint Him.
021602 And very early in the morning, the first day of the week, they came upon the tomb, the sun having risen.
021603 And they said among themselves, Who will roll away the stone from the door of the tomb for us?
021604 And looking up, they saw that the stone had been rolled back, for it was very great.
021605 And entering into the tomb, they saw a young man sitting on the right, clothed in a long white garment. And they were frightened.
021606 And he said to them, Do not be frightened. You seek Jesus of Nazareth, who was crucified. He is risen, He is not here. Behold the place where they laid Him.
021607 But go tell His disciples and Peter that He goes before you into Galilee. There you will see Him, as He said to you.
021608 And they went out quickly and fled from the tomb. For they trembled and were amazed. Neither did they say anything to anyone, for they were afraid.
021609 And when Jesus had risen early the first day of the Sabbath, He appeared first to Mary Magdalene, out of whom He had cast seven demons.
021610 She went and told those who had been with Him, as they mourned and wept.
021611 And those hearing that He lives, and was seen by her, they did not believe.
021612 After that He appeared in another form to two of them, walking and going into the country.
021613 And they went and told it to the rest. Neither did they believe those.
021614 Afterward He appeared to the Eleven as they reclined. And He reproached their unbelief and hardness of heart, because they did not believe those who had seen Him after He had risen.
021615 And He said to them, Go into all the world, proclaim the gospel to all the creation.
021616 He who believes and is baptized will be saved, but he who does not believe will be condemned.
021617 And miraculous signs will follow to those believing these things: in My name they will cast out demons; they will speak new tongues;
021618 they will take up serpents; and if they drink any deadly thing, it will not hurt them. They will lay hands on the sick, and they will be well.
021619 Then indeed, after speaking to them, the Lord was taken up into Heaven, and sat on the right hand of God.
021620 And going out, they proclaimed everywhere, the Lord working with them and confirming the word by miraculous signs following. Amen.
030101 Since many took in hand to draw up an account concerning the matters which have been borne out among us,
030102 even as those who from the beginning delivered to us, becoming eye-witnesses and ministers of the word,
030103 it seemed good to me also, following all things accurately from the very first, to write to you in order, most excellent Theophilus,
030104 so that you might know the certainty of those things in which you have been instructed.
030105 In the days of Herod, the king of Judea, there was a certain priest named Zacharias, of the course of Abijah. And his wife was of the daughters of Aaron, and her name was Elizabeth.
030106 And they were both righteous before God, walking blameless in all the commandments and ordinances of the Lord.
030107 And they had no child, because Elizabeth was barren. And both were advanced in their days.
030108 And it happened in his serving in the order of his course, before God,
030109 according to the custom of the priests, it was his lot to burn incense when he went into the temple of the Lord.
030110 And all the multitude of the people were praying outside at the time of incense.
030111 And an angel of the Lord appeared to him as he was standing on the right of the altar of incense.
030112 And seeing this , Zacharias was troubled, and fear fell on him.
030113 But the angel said to him, Do not fear, Zacharias. For your prayer is heard, and your wife Elizabeth shall bear you a son, and you shall call his name John.
030114 And you shall have joy and gladness, and many shall rejoice at his birth.
030115 For he shall be great in the sight of the Lord, and shall neither drink wine nor strong drink. And he shall be filled with the Holy Spirit, even from his mother's womb.
030116 And he shall turn many of the sons of Israel to the Lord their God.
030117 And he shall go before Him in the spirit and power of Elijah, to turn the hearts of the fathers to the children, and the disobedient to the wisdom of the just, to make ready a people prepared for the Lord.
030118 And Zacharias said to the angel, By what shall I know this? For I am old, and my wife is advanced in her days.
030119 And answering, the angel said to him, I am Gabriel, who stands before God. And I am sent to speak to you and to show you these glad tidings.
030120 And behold, you shall be silent and not able to speak until the day that these things shall be performed, because you did not believe my words which shall be fulfilled in their time.
030121 And the people waited for Zacharias and marveled that he stayed so long in the temple.
030122 And when he came out, he could not speak to them. And they perceived that he had seen a vision in the temple. And he was making signs to them, and remained speechless.
030123 And as soon as the days of his service were accomplished, he departed to his own house.
030124 And after those days his wife Elizabeth conceived and hid herself five months, saying,
030125 So the Lord has dealt with me in the days in which He looked on me , to take away my reproach among men.
030126 And in the sixth month the angel Gabriel was sent from God into a city of Galilee, named Nazareth,
030127 to a virgin betrothed to a man whose name was Joseph, of the house of David. And the virgin's name was Mary.
030128 And the angel came in to her and said, Hail, one receiving grace, the Lord is with you. Blessed are you among women.
030129 And when she saw him , she was troubled at his saying, and considered what kind of greeting this might be.
030130 And the angel said to her, Do not fear, Mary, for you have found favor with God.
030131 And behold! You shall conceive in your womb and bear a son, and you shall call His name JESUS.
030132 He shall be great and shall be called the Son of the Highest. And the Lord God shall give Him the throne of His father David.
030133 And He shall reign over the house of Jacob forever, and of His kingdom there shall be no end.
030134 Then Mary said to the angel, How shall this be, since I do not know a man?
030135 And the angel answered and said to her, The Holy Spirit shall come on you, and the power of the Highest shall overshadow you. Therefore also that Holy One which will be born of you shall be called Son of God.
030136 And behold, your cousin Elizabeth also conceived a son in her old age. And this is the sixth month with her who was called barren.
030137 For with God nothing shall be impossible.
030138 And Mary said, Behold the servant of the Lord. Let it be to me according to your word. And the angel departed from her.
030139 And Mary arose in those days and went into the hill country with haste, to a city of Judah.
030140 And she entered into the house of Zacharias and greeted Elizabeth.
030141 And it happened as Elizabeth heard the greeting of Mary, the babe leaped in her womb. And Elizabeth was filled with the Holy Spirit,
030142 and cried out with a loud voice and said, Blessed are you among women, and blessed is the fruit of your womb.
030143 And from where is this to me, that the mother of my Lord should come to me?
030144 For lo, as the voice of your greeting sounded in my ears, the babe leaped in my womb for joy.
030145 And blessed is she who believes, for there shall be a perfecting of those things which were told her from the Lord.
030146 And Mary said, My soul magnifies the Lord,
030147 and my spirit has rejoiced in God my Savior.
030148 For He looked on the humiliation of His slave woman. For, behold, from now on all generations shall count me blessed.
030149 For the Mighty One has done great things for me; and holy is His name.
030150 And His mercy is on those who fear Him from generation to generation.
030151 He has worked power with His arm, He has scattered the proud in the imagination of their heart.
030152 He has put down rulers from their seats and exalted the lowly,
030153 He has filled the hungry with good things, and He has sent away the rich empty.
030154 He has helped His servant Israel, in remembrance of His mercy,
030155 as He spoke to our fathers, to Abraham and to his seed forever.
030156 And Mary stayed with her about three months, and returned to her own house.
030157 And the time was fulfilled to Elizabeth for her to bear. And she bore a son.
030158 And her neighbors and her kinsfolk heard how the Lord had magnified His mercy with her, and they rejoiced with her.
030159 And it happened that on the eighth day they came to circumcise the child, and were calling it Zacharias, after his father's name.
030160 And his mother answered and said, No, but he shall be called John.
030161 And they said to her, There is none of your kindred that is called by this name.
030162 And they made signs to his father as to how he would have him called.
030163 And he asked for a writing tablet and wrote, saying, His name is John. And they all marveled.
030164 And his mouth was opened immediately, and his tongue loosened . And he spoke and praised God.
030165 And fear came on all who lived all around them. And all these things were talked about throughout all the hill country of Judea.
030166 And all those who heard laid them up in their hearts, saying, What kind of child shall this be! And the hand of the Lord was with him.
030167 And his father Zacharias was filled with the Holy Spirit, and prophesied, saying,
030168 Blessed is the Lord, the God of Israel, for He has visited and redeemed His people
030169 and has raised up a horn of salvation for us in the house of His servant David,
030170 as He spoke by the mouth of His holy prophets from eternity;
030171 that we should be saved from our enemies and from the hand of all who hate us,
030172 to perform the mercy promised to our fathers, and to remember His holy covenant,
030173 the oath which He swore to our father Abraham,
030174 that He would grant to us, that we , being delivered out of the hand of our enemies, might serve Him without fear
030175 in holiness and righteousness before Him all the days of our life.
030176 And you, child, will be called the prophet of the Highest, for you shall go before the face of the Lord to prepare His ways,
030177 to give knowledge of salvation to His people by the remission of their sins,
030178 through the tender mercy of our God; by which the Dayspring from on high has visited us,
030179 to give light to those who sit in darkness and in the shadow of death, to guide our feet into the way of peace.
030180 And the child grew and became strong in spirit and was in the deserts until the day of his showing to Israel.
030201 And it happened in those days that a decree went out from Caesar Augustus that all the world should be taxed.
030202 (This taxing was first made when Cyrenius was governor of Syria.)
030203 And all went to be registered, each to his own city.
030204 And Joseph also went up from Galilee to be taxed (out of the city of Nazareth, into Judea, to the city of David which is called Bethlehem, because he was of the house and family line of David).
030205 And he took Mary his betrothed wife, being with child.
030206 And while they were there, the days for her deliverance were fulfilled.
030207 And she brought forth her son, the First-born, and wrapped Him, and laid Him in a manger-- because there was no room for them in the inn.
030208 And in the same country there were shepherds living in the field, keeping watch over their flock by night.
030209 And lo, the angel of the Lord came on them, and the glory of the Lord shone around them. And they were grievously afraid.
030210 And the angel said to them, Do not fear. For behold, I give to you good tidings of great joy, which shall be to all people.
030211 For to you is born today, in the city of David, a Savior, who is Christ the Lord.
030212 And this is a sign to you. You will find the babe wrapped, lying in a manger.
030213 And suddenly there was with the angel a multitude of the heavenly host, praising God and saying,
030214 Glory to God in the highest, and on earth peace, good will toward men.
030215 And it happened as the angels departed from them into Heaven, the shepherds said to one another, Indeed, let us go to Bethlehem and see this thing which has happened, which the Lord made known to us.
030216 And hurrying they came and sought out both Mary and Joseph, and the babe lying in the manger.
030217 And seeing, they publicly told about the word spoken to them concerning this Child.
030218 And all those who heard marveled about the things spoken to them by the shepherds.
030219 But Mary kept all these sayings, meditating in her heart.
030220 And the shepherds returned, glorifying and praising God for all the things that they had heard and seen, as was spoken to them.
030221 And when eight days were fulfilled to circumcise the child, His name was called JESUS, the name called by the angel before He was conceived in the womb.
030222 And when the days of her purification according to the law of Moses were fulfilled, they brought Him to Jerusalem, to present Him to the Lord
030223 (as it is written in the Law of the Lord, Every male that opens the womb shall be called holy to the Lord)
030224 and to offer a sacrifice according to that said in the Law of the Lord, A pair of turtledoves or two young pigeons.
030225 And behold, there was a man in Jerusalem whose name was Simeon. And this man was just and devout, waiting for the Consolation of Israel. And the Holy Spirit was on him.
030226 And it happened to him, being instructed by the Holy Spirit, he was not to see death before he would see the Christ of the Lord.
030227 And he came by the Spirit into the temple. And as the parents brought in the child Jesus, to do according to the custom of the law concerning Him,
030228 even he received Him in his arms and blessed God, and said,
030229 Lord, now You will let Your servant depart in peace, according to Your word.
030230 For my eyes have seen Your Salvation
030231 which You have prepared before the face of all the peoples,
030232 a light for revelation to the nations, and the glory of Your people Israel.
030233 And Joseph and His mother marveled at those things which were spoken by him.
030234 And Simeon blessed them and said to Mary His mother, Behold, this One is set for the fall and rising again of many in Israel, and for a sign spoken against
030235 (yea, a sword shall pierce through your own soul also), so that the thoughts of many hearts may be revealed.
030236 And there was a prophetess, Anna, the daughter of Phanuel, of the tribe of Asher. She was advanced in many days, and had lived with a husband seven years from her virginity.
030237 And she was a widow of eighty-four years, who did not depart from the temple, serving God with fastings and prayers night and day.
030238 And she coming in at that instant gave thanks to the Lord and spoke of Him to all those in Jerusalem eagerly expecting redemption.
030239 And when they had finished all things according to the Law of the Lord, they returned into Galilee, to their own city Nazareth.
030240 And the Child grew and became strong in spirit, filled with wisdom. And the grace of God was on Him.
030241 And His parents went to Jerusalem every year at the Feast of the Passover.
030242 And when He was twelve years old , they went up to Jerusalem according to the custom of the Feast.
030243 And fulfilling the days, as they returned, the boy Jesus stayed in Jerusalem. And Joseph and His mother did not know.
030244 But they, supposing Him to have been in the company, went a day's journey. And they looked for Him among the kinsfolk and acquaintances.
030245 And when they did not find Him, they turned back to Jerusalem, seeking Him.
030246 And it happened that after three days they found Him in the temple, sitting in the midst of the teachers, both hearing them and questioning them.
030247 And all who heard Him were astonished at His understanding and answers.
030248 And seeing Him, they were amazed. And His mother said to Him, Child, why have you done so to us? Behold, your father and I have looked for you, greatly distressed.
030249 And He said to them, Why did you look for Me? Do you not know that I must be about My Father's business ?
030250 And they did not understand the word which He spoke to them.
030251 And He went with them and came to Nazareth, and He was subject to them. But His mother kept all these sayings in her heart.
030252 And Jesus increased in wisdom and stature, and in favor with God and man.
030301 And in the fifteenth year of the government of Tiberius Caesar, Pontius Pilate being governor of Judea, and Herod being tetrarch of Galilee, and his brother Philip tetrarch of Iturea and the Trachonitus country, and Lysanias the tetrarch of Abilene--
030302 Annas and Caiaphas being the high priests-- the word of God came to John the son of Zacharias in the wilderness.
030303 And he came into all the country around Jordan, proclaiming the baptism of repentance for the remission of sins,
030304 as it is written in the book of the words of Isaiah the prophet, saying, " The voice of one crying in the wilderness, prepare the way of the Lord, make His paths straight.
030305 Every valley shall be filled, and every mountain and hill shall be brought low, and the crooked shall be straight, and the rough ways shall be made smooth.
030306 And all flesh shall see the salvation of God."
030307 Then he said to the crowd that came forth to be baptized by him, O generation of vipers! Who has warned you to flee from the wrath to come?
030308 Therefore bring forth fruits worthy of repentance, and do not begin to say within yourselves, We have Abraham for our father. For I say to you that God is able to raise up children to Abraham from these stones.
030309 And now also the axe is laid to the root of the trees. Therefore every tree which does not bring forth good fruit is cut down and cast into the fire.
030310 And the people asked him, saying, What shall we do then?
030311 He answered and said to them, He who has two coats, let him give to him who has none. And he who has food, let him do likewise.
030312 And tax-collectors also came to be baptized and said to him, Teacher, what shall we do?
030313 And he said to them, Continue to do no more than that commanded to you.
030314 And the soldiers also asked of him, saying, And what shall we do? And he said to them, Do not forcibly extort anyone, nor accuse any falsely. And be content with your wages.
030315 And as the people were in expectation, and all men mused in their hearts concerning John, lest perhaps he was the Christ,
030316 John answered all, saying, I indeed baptize you with water, but He who is mightier than I comes, the thong of whose sandals I am not worthy to loose. He shall baptize you with the Holy Spirit and with fire,
030317 whose fan is in His hand, and He will thoroughly purge His floor and will gather the wheat into His storehouse. But He will burn the chaff with unquenchable fire.
030318 And then indeed exhorting many things, he proclaimed the gospel to the people.
030319 But Herod the tetrarch (being reproved by him on account of Herodias, his brother Philip's wife, and for all the evils which Herod had done)
030320 added still this above all, that he even shut John up in prison.
030321 And it happened in the baptizing of all the people, Jesus also being baptized, and praying, and the heaven was opened.
030322 And the Holy Spirit came down in a bodily shape, like a dove on Him. And a voice came from Heaven, which said, You are My Son, the Beloved; I am delighted in You.
030323 And Jesus Himself was beginning to be about thirty years of age, being (as was supposed) son of Joseph, son of of Heli,
030324 son of of Matthat, son of of Levi, son of of Melchi, son of of Janna, son of of Joseph,
030325 son of of Mattathias, son of of Amos, son of of Nahum, son of of Esli, son of of Naggai,
030326 son of of Maath, son of of Mattathias, son of of Semei, son of of Joseph, son of of Juda,
030327 son of of Joanna, son of of Rhesa, son of of Zerubbabel, son of of Shealtiel, son of of Neri,
030328 son of of Melchi, son of of Addi, son of of Cosam, son of of Elmodam, son of of Er,
030329 son of of Joses, son of of Eliezer, son of of Jorum, son of of Matthat, son of of Levi,
030330 son of of Simeon, son of of Juda, son of of Joseph, son of of Jonan, son of of Eliakim,
030331 son of of Melea, the son of Menan, son of of Mattatha, son of of Nathan, son of of David,
030332 son of of Jesse, son of of Obed, son of of Boaz, son of of Salma, son of of Nahshon,
030333 son of of Amminadab, son of of Ram, son of of Hezron, son of of Pharez, son of of Judah,
030334 son of of Jacob, son of of Isaac, son of of Abraham, son of of Terah, son of of Nahor,
030335 son of of Serug, son of of Reu, son of of Peleg, son of of Eber, son of of Shelah,
030336 son of of Cainan, son of of Arphaxad, son of of Shem, son of of Noah, son of of Lamech,
030337 son of of Methuselah, son of of Enoch, son of of Jared, son of of Mahalaleel, son of of Cainan,
030338 son of of Enos, son of of Seth, son of of Adam, son of of God.
030401 And Jesus, full of the Holy Spirit, returned from Jordan and was led by the Spirit into the wilderness
030402 forty days, being tempted by the Devil. And in those days He ate nothing. And they being ended, He afterward was hungry.
030403 And the Devil said to Him, If you are the Son of God, speak to this stone that it might become bread.
030404 And Jesus answered him, saying, It is written that "man shall not live by bread alone, but by every word of God."
030405 And the Devil, leading Him up into a high mountain, showed Him all the kingdoms of the world in a moment of time.
030406 And the Devil said to Him, All this power I will give you, and the glory of them; for it has been delivered to me. And I give it to whomever I will.
030407 Therefore if you will worship me, all shall be yours.
030408 And Jesus answered and said to him, Get behind me, Satan! For it is written, "You shall worship the Lord your God, and Him only shall you serve."
030409 And he brought Him to Jerusalem and sat Him on a pinnacle of the temple and said to Him, If you are the Son of God, cast yourself down from here.
030410 For it is written, "He shall give His angels charge over You, to keep You;
030411 and in their hands they shall bear You up, lest at any time You dash Your foot against a stone."
030412 And Jesus answering said to him, It has been said, "You shall not tempt the Lord your God."
030413 And when the Devil had ended every temptation, he departed from Him for a time.
030414 And Jesus returned in the power of the Spirit into Galilee. And a report went out throughout all the neighborhood concerning Him.
030415 And He taught in their synagogues, being glorified by all.
030416 And He came to Nazareth, where He had been brought up. And, as His custom was, He went in to the synagogue on the Sabbath day and stood up to read.
030417 And the book of the prophet Isaiah was handed to Him. And unrolling the book, He found the place where it was written,
030418 "The Spirit of the Lord is on Me; because of this He has anointed Me to proclaim the Gospel to the poor. He has sent me to heal the brokenhearted, to proclaim deliverance to the captives, and new sight to the blind, to set at liberty those having been crushed,
030419 to proclaim the acceptable year of the Lord."
030420 And rolling up the book, returning it to the attendant, He sat down. And the eyes of all in the synagogue were fastened on Him.
030421 And He began to say to them, Today this Scripture is fulfilled in your ears.
030422 And all bore witness to Him and wondered at the gracious words which came out of His mouth. And they said, Is this not Joseph's son?
030423 And He said to them, You will surely say this proverb to Me, Physician, heal yourself. Whatever we have heard done in Capernaum, do also here in your native-place.
030424 And He said, Truly I say to you, No prophet is accepted in his native-place.
030425 But I tell you truly, many widows were in Israel in the days of Elijah, when the heaven was shut up three years and six months, when great famine was throughout all the land.
030426 But Elijah was not sent to any of them, except to Zarephath, a city of Sidon, to a woman, a widow.
030427 And many lepers were in Israel in the time of Elisha the prophet, and none of them was cleansed except Naaman the Syrian.
030428 And hearing these things, all in the synagogue were filled with wrath.
030429 And they rose up and thrust Him outside the city, and led Him up to the brow of the hill on which their city was built, in order to throw Him down.
030430 But passing through the midst of them, He went away.
030431 And He came down to Capernaum, a city of Galilee, and taught them on the sabbath days.
030432 And they were astonished at His doctrine, for His word was with authority.
030433 And in the synagogue there was a man who had a spirit of an unclean demon and cried out with a loud voice,
030434 saying, Let us alone! What is to us and to You, Jesus of Nazareth? Have You come to destroy us? I know You, who You are, the Holy One of God.
030435 And Jesus rebuked him, saying, Be quiet and come out of him! And when the demon had thrown him into the midst, he came out of him, not harming him.
030436 And they were all amazed and spoke among themselves, saying, What a word is this! For with authority and power He commands the unclean spirits, and they come out.
030437 And a report about Him went out into every place of the neighborhood.
030438 And rising up from the synagogue, He entered into Simon's house. And Simon's wife's mother was being seized with a great fever. And they asked Him for her.
030439 And standing over her, He rebuked the fever. And it left her. And immediately she arose and served them.
030440 And the sun sinking, all, as many as had sick ones with different kinds of diseases brought them to Him. And laying hands on each of them, He healed them.
030441 And also demons came out of many, crying out and saying, You are the Christ, the Son of God! And rebuking them , He did not allow them to speak; for they knew Him to be the Christ.
030442 And day coming on, going out, He went into a deserted place. And the crowds looked for Him and came to Him, and held Him fast, not to pass away from them.
030443 And He said to them, I must proclaim the gospel, the kingdom of God, to other cities, because I was sent on this mission ,
030444 And He proclaimed in the synagogues of Galilee.
030501 And it happened that the crowd pressed on Him to hear the word of God, He stood by the lake of Gennesaret.
030502 And He saw two boats standing by the lake. But the fishermen had left them and were washing their nets.
030503 And He entered into one of the boats, which was Simon's, He asked him to thrust out a little from the land. And He sat down and taught the people out of the boat.
030504 And as He stopped speaking, He said to Simon, Launch out into the deep and let your nets down for a haul.
030505 And answering, Simon said to Him, Master, we have toiled all the night and have taken nothing. Yet at Your word I will let down the net.
030506 And doing this, they enclosed a great multitude of fish. And their net was being torn.
030507 And they signaled the partners, those in the other boat, to come and help them. And they came and filled both the boats, so that they were sinking.
030508 And seeing, Simon Peter fell at the knees of Jesus, saying, Depart from me, for I am a sinful man, Lord.
030509 For he and all who were with him were astonished at the haul of fish which they had taken,
030510 and so also were James and John, the sons of Zebedee, who were partners with Simon. And Jesus said to Simon, Do not fear, from now on you will be taking men alive.
030511 And bringing their boats onto land, forsaking all things, they followed Him.
030512 And it happened, as He was in a certain city, behold, a man full of leprosy! And seeing Jesus, he fell on his face and begged Him, saying, Lord, if You will, You can cleanse me.
030513 And stretching out the hand, He touched him, saying, I will! Be clean! And immediately the leprosy departed from him.
030514 And He commanded him, Tell no one, but go and show yourself to the priest and offer for your cleansing, as Moses commanded, for a testimony to them.
030515 But the word about Him spread even more. And great crowds were coming to hear, and to be healed from their infirmities by Him.
030516 But He was drawing back in the wilderness, and praying.
030517 And it happened on one of the days, even He was teaching. And Pharisees and teachers of the Law were sitting by, who had come out of every village of Galilee and Judea and Jerusalem. And the power of the Lord was there, for the curing of them.
030518 And behold, men carrying, on a cot, a man who was paralyzed. And they sought to bring him in and to lay him before Him.
030519 And not finding a way by which they might bring him in through the crowd, going up on the housetop, they let him down through the tiles with his cot into the midst, before Jesus.
030520 And seeing their faith, He said to him, Man, your sins are forgiven you.
030521 And the scribes and Pharisees began to reason, saying, Who is this who speaks blasphemies? Who can forgive sins, except God alone?
030522 But knowing their thoughts, answering, Jesus said to them, Why do you reason in your hearts?
030523 Which is easier, to say, Your sins are forgiven you; or to say, Rise up and walk?
030524 But so that you may know that the Son of man has authority on earth to forgive sins, He said to the paralytic, I say to you, Arise, and take up your cot and go to your house.
030525 And immediately he rose up before them and took up that on which he lay. And he departed to his own house, glorifying God.
030526 And they were all amazed, and they glorified God and were filled with fear, saying, We saw wonderful things today.
030527 And after these things He went out and saw a tax-collector named Levi, sitting at the tax-office. And He said to him, Follow Me.
030528 And leaving all, he rose up and followed Him.
030529 And Levi made a great feast in his own house for Him. And there was a great company of tax-collectors and of others who were reclining with them.
030530 But their scribes and Pharisees murmured against His disciples, saying, Why do you eat and drink with tax-collectors and sinners?
030531 And Jesus answered and said to them, Those who are sound do not need a physician, but those who are sick.
030532 I did not come to call the righteous to repentance, but sinners.
030533 And they said to Him, Why do John's disciples fast often and make prayers, and also the disciples of the Pharisees, but yours eat and drink?
030534 But He said to them, Can you make the sons of the bridechamber fast while the bridegroom is with them?
030535 But the days will come when the bridegroom shall be taken away from them, and then they shall fast in those days.
030536 And He also spoke a parable to them: No one puts a piece of a new garment on an old garment. Otherwise, both the new will tear, and the old does not match the piece from the new.
030537 And no one puts new wine into old wineskins. Else the new wine will burst the wineskins and be spilled, and the wineskin will perish.
030538 But new wine must be put into new wineskins, and both are preserved together.
030539 Also no one having drunk old wine immediately desires new, for he says, The old is better.
030601 And it happened on the second chief sabbath, He went through the grain fields. And His disciples plucked the heads of grain and ate, rubbing them in their hands.
030602 And certain of the Pharisees said to them, Why do you do that which is not lawful to do on the sabbath days?
030603 And answering, Jesus said to them, Have you not read this, what David did when he was hungry, and those who were with him;
