030604 how he went into the house of God and took the showbread, and ate (and also gave to those who were with him) which it is not lawful to eat, except for the priests alone?
030605 And He said to them, The Son of man is Lord also of the sabbath.
030606 And it happened, also on another sabbath, that He entered into the synagogue and taught. And there was a man whose right hand was withered.
030607 And the scribes and Pharisees watched him to see if He would heal on the sabbath day, so that they might find an accusation against Him.
030608 But He knew their thoughts and said to the man who had the withered hand, Rise up and stand in the middle. And he arose and stood.
030609 Then Jesus said to them, I will ask you one thing: Is it lawful to do good on the sabbath days, or to do evil, to save life, or to destroy it ?
030610 And looking around on them all, He said to the man, Stretch out your hand! And he did so. And his hand was restored whole like the other.
030611 And they were filled with madness, and talked with one another as to what they might do to Jesus.
030612 And it happened in those days that He went out into a mountain to pray, and He was spending the night in prayer to God.
030613 And when it was day, He called His disciples. And He chose twelve of them, whom He also named apostles:
030614 Simon, whom He also named Peter, and Andrew his brother; James and John; Philip and Bartholomew;
030615 Matthew and Thomas; James the son of Alpheus, and Simon who was called Zelotes;
030616 Judas the brother of James, and Judas Iscariot, who also became the betrayer.
030617 And coming down with them, He stood on a level place. And a crowd of His disciples, and a great multitude of people from all Judea and Jerusalem, and the sea coast of Tyre and Sidon (who came to hear Him and to be healed of their diseases) were there;
030618 also those tormented by unclean spirits; and they were healed.
030619 And all the crowd sought to touch Him, for power went out of Him and healed them all.
030620 And lifting up His eyes to His disciples, He said, Blessed are the poor, for yours is the kingdom of God.
030621 Blessed are you who hunger now, for you shall be filled. Blessed are you who weep now, for you shall laugh.
030622 Blessed are you when men shall hate you, and when they shall cut you off, and when they shall reproach you and shall cast out your name as evil, for the sake of the Son of man.
030623 Rejoice in that day and leap for joy. For behold, your reward is great in Heaven. For so their fathers did according to these things to the prophets.
030624 But woe to you who are rich! For you have received your consolation.
030625 Woe to you who are full! For you shall hunger. Woe to you who laugh now! For you shall mourn and weep.
030626 Woe to you when all men shall speak well of you! For so their fathers did to the false prophets.
030627 But I say to you who hear: Love your enemies, do good to those who hate you,
030628 bless those who curse you, and pray for those who despitefully use you.
030629 And to him who strikes you on the one cheek, also offer the other. And to him who takes away your garment, do not forbid your tunic also.
030630 Give to everyone who asks of you, and from him who takes away your goods, do not ask them again.
030631 And as you desire that men should do to you, you do also to them likewise.
030632 For if you love those who love you, what thanks do you have? For sinners also love those who love them.
030633 And if you do good to those who do good to you, what thanks do you have? For sinners also do the same.
030634 And if you lend to those of whom you hope to receive, what thanks do you have? For sinners also lend to sinners, to receive as much again.
030635 But love your enemies, and do good, and lend, hoping for nothing in return . And your reward shall be great, and you shall be the sons of the Highest. For He is kind to the unthankful and to the evil.
030636 Therefore be merciful, even as your Father is merciful.
030637 Judge not, and you shall not be judged. Condemn not, and you shall not be condemned. Forgive, and you shall be forgiven.
030638 Give, and it shall be given to you, good measure pressed down and shaken together and running over, they shall give into your bosom. For with the same measure that you measure, it shall be measured to you again.
030639 And He spoke a parable to them: Can the blind lead the blind? Shall they not both fall into the ditch?
030640 The disciple is not above his master, but everyone who is perfect shall be like his master.
030641 And why do you look at the splinter that is in your brother's eye, but do not see the beam that is in your own eye?
030642 Or how can you say to your brother, Brother, let me pull out the splinter in your eye, when you yourself do not see the beam that is in your own eye? Hypocrite! First cast out the beam out of your own eye, and then you shall see clearly to pull out the splinter that is in your brother's eye.
030643 For a good tree does not bring forth corrupt fruit, neither does a corrupt tree bring forth good fruit.
030644 For every tree is known by its own fruit. For men do not gather figs from thorns, nor do they gather grapes from a bramble bush.
030645 A good man out of the good treasure of his heart brings forth the good. And an evil man out of the evil treasure of his heart brings forth the evil. For out of the abundance of the heart his mouth speaks.
030646 And why do you call Me Lord, Lord, and do not do what I say?
030647 Whoever comes to Me and hears My words, and does them, I will show you to whom he is like.
030648 He is like a man who built a house and dug deep and laid the foundation on a rock; and a flood occurring, the stream burst against that house and could not shake it; for it was founded on a rock.
030649 But he who hears and does not perform, is like a man who built a house on the earth without a foundation, on which the stream burst, and immediately it fell. And the ruin of that house was great.
030701 And when He had ended all His words in the ears of the people, He entered into Capernaum.
030702 And a certain servant of a centurion who was dear to him, was sick and ready to die.
030703 And when he heard of Jesus, he sent the elders of the Jews to Him, begging Him that He would come and heal his servant.
030704 And coming to Jesus, they begged Him earnestly, saying that he was worthy, he for whom You give this;
030705 for, they said , He loves our nation, and he has built us a synagogue.
030706 Then Jesus went with them. But He being yet not far off from the house, the centurion sent friends to Him, saying to Him, Lord, do not trouble Yourself. For I am not worthy that You should enter under my roof.
030707 Therefore neither did I think myself worthy to come to You; but say a word, and my servant will be healed.
030708 For I also am a man set under authority, having under me soldiers. And I say to one, Go, and he goes; and to another, Come, and he comes; and to my servant, Do this, and he does it .
030709 And hearing these things, Jesus marveled at him. And turning to the crowd following Him, He said, I say to you, I have not found such faith, no, not in Israel.
030710 And they who were sent, returning to the house, found the sick servant well.
030711 And it happened on the next day, He went into a city called Nain. And many of His disciples and a great crowd went with Him.
030712 And drawing near the gate of the city, even behold, one having died was being carried out, an only son of his mother, and she was a widow. And a considerable crowd of the city was with her.
030713 And when the Lord saw her, He had compassion on her and said to her, Do not weep.
030714 And He came and touched the bier. And the ones who bore him stood still. And He said, Young man, I say to you, Arise!
030715 And the one who was dead sat up and began to speak. And He delivered him to his mother.
030716 And fear came on all. And they glorified God, saying, A great prophet has risen up among us; and, God has visited His people.
030717 And this report of Him went out in all Judea, and in all the neighborhood.
030718 And his disciples reported all these things to John.
030719 And John, calling near a certain two of his disciples, sent them to Jesus, saying, Are You He that should come, or do we look for another?
030720 And coming to Him, the men said, John the Baptist has sent us to You, saying, Are You He who should come, or do we look for another?
030721 And in the same hour He cured many of infirmities and plagues, and of evil spirits. And He gave sight to many who were blind.
030722 And answering, Jesus said to them, Go and tell John what you have seen and heard; that the blind see, the lame walk, the lepers are cleansed, the deaf hear, the dead are raised, and the gospel is proclaimed to the poor.
030723 And blessed is he who shall not be offended in Me.
030724 And when the messengers of John had departed, He began to speak to the people concerning John. What did you go out into the wilderness to see? A reed shaken with the wind?
030725 But what did you go out to see? A man clothed with soft clothing? Behold, those in splendid clothing and being in luxury are in kings' palaces.
030726 But what did you go out to see? A prophet? Yes, I say to you, and much more than a prophet.
030727 This is he of whom it is written, "Behold, I send My messenger before Your face, who shall prepare Your way before You."
030728 For I say to you, Among those who are born of woman there is not a greater prophet than John the Baptist. But he who is least in the kingdom of God is greater than he.
030729 And all the people and the tax-collectors who heard Him justified God, being baptized with the baptism of John.
030730 But the Pharisees and lawyers rejected the counsel of God against themselves, not being baptized by him.
030731 And the Lord said, To what then shall I compare the men of this generation? And to what are they like?
030732 They are like children sitting in a market and calling to one another, and saying, We have played the flute to you, and you have not danced; we have mourned to you, and you did not weep.
030733 For John the Baptist came neither eating bread nor drinking wine, and you say, He has a demon.
030734 The Son of man has come eating and drinking, and you say, Behold a gluttonous man and a winebibber, a friend of tax-collectors and sinners!
030735 But wisdom has been justified by all her children.
030736 And one of the Pharisees asked Him to eat with him. And going into the Pharisee's house, He reclined.
030737 And behold, a woman, a sinner in the city, knowing that He reclined in the Pharisee's house, brought an alabaster vial of ointment.
030738 And she stood behind Him , weeping at His feet, and she began to wash His feet with tears and wipe them with the hair of her head. And she ardently kissed His feet and anointed them with the ointment.
030739 But seeing this, the Pharisee who had invited Him, spoke within himself, saying, This man, if he were a prophet, would have known who and what kind of woman this is who touches him, for she is a sinner.
030740 And answering, Jesus said to him, Simon, I have something to say to you. And he said, Teacher, speak.
030741 There was a certain creditor who had two debtors. The one owed five hundred denarii, and the other fifty.
030742 And they having nothing to pay, he freely forgave both. Then which of them do you say will love him most?
030743 And answering, Simon said, I suppose that one to whom he forgave most. And He said to him, You have judged rightly.
030744 And He turned to the woman and said to Simon, Do you see this woman? I entered into your house, yet you gave Me no water for My feet. But she has washed My feet with tears, and has wiped them with the hair of her head.
030745 You gave Me no kiss, but this woman, since the time I came in, has not ceased to kiss My feet.
030746 You did not anoint My head with oil, but this woman has anointed My feet with ointment.
030747 Therefore I say to you, Her sins, which are many, are forgiven, for she loved much. But to whom little is forgiven, he loves little.
030748 And He said to her, Your sins are forgiven.
030749 And those reclining with Him began to say within themselves, Who is this who even forgives sins?
030750 And He said to the woman, Your faith has saved you, go in peace.
030801 And it happened afterwards, He traveled in every city and village, proclaiming and announcing the gospel of the kingdom of God. And the Twelve were with Him,
030802 and also certain women who had been healed of evil spirits and infirmities; Mary called Magdalene, out of whom went seven demons,
030803 and Joanna the wife of Chuza, Herod's steward, and Susanna, and many others, who ministered to Him of their possessions.
030804 And a great crowd coming together, and those in each city coming to Him, He spoke by a parable:
030805 A sower went out to sow his seed. And as he sowed, the one fell by the roadside and was trampled; and the birds of the air devoured it.
030806 And other fell on a rock, and sprouting, it withered away, because it lacked moisture.
030807 And other fell amidst thorns, and springing up with the thorns, they choked it.
030808 And other fell on good ground and sprang up, and bore fruit a hundredfold. And when He had said these things, He cried, He who has ears to hear, let him hear.
030809 And His disciples asked Him, saying, What might this parable be?
030810 And He said, To you it is given to know the mysteries of the kingdom of God. But to others I speak in parables, so that seeing they might not see and hearing they might not understand.
030811 And the parable is this: The seed is the Word of God.
030812 Those by the roadside are the ones who hear; then the Devil comes and takes the Word out of their hearts, lest they should believe and be saved.
030813 Those on the rock are the ones who, when they hear, receive the Word with joy. And these have no root, who for a while believe, and in time of temptation fall away.
030814 And those which fell among thorns are the ones who, when they have heard, go forth and are choked with cares and riches and pleasures of life, and do not bear to maturity.
030815 But those on the good ground are the ones who, in an honest and good heart, having heard the Word, keep it and bring forth fruit with patience.
030816 And no one lighting a lamp covers it with a vessel or puts it under a couch; but he sets it on a lampstand so that those who enter in may see the light.
030817 For nothing is secret that shall not be revealed; nor secret which shall not be known and come to be revealed.
030818 Therefore be careful how you hear. For whoever has, to him shall be given; and whoever has not, from him shall be taken even that which he seems to have.
030819 And His mother and His brothers came to Him. And they could not come near Him because of the crowd.
030820 And it was told to Him by some , who said, Your mother and Your brothers are standing outside desiring to see You.
030821 And He answered and said to them, My mother and My brothers are those who hear the Word of God and do it.
030822 And it happened on a certain day that He went into a boat with His disciples. And He said to them, Let us go over to the other side of the lake. And they put out to sea.
030823 But as they sailed, He fell asleep. And a storm of wind came onto the lake. And they were being filled with water and were in jeopardy.
030824 And they came to Him and awakened Him, saying, Master, Master, we are perishing! Then being aroused, He rebuked the wind and the raging of the water. And they ceased, and there was a calm.
030825 And He said to them, Where is your faith? And being afraid, they marveled, saying to one another, Who then is this One? For He commands even the winds and water, and they obey Him!
030826 And they sailed down to the country of the Gadarenes, which is across from Galilee.
030827 And He going out onto land, He met a certain man out of the city, who had had demons a long time, and put on no clothes, nor stayed in a house, but among the tombs.
030828 And seeing Jesus, he cried out and fell down before Him and said with a loud voice, What is to me and to You, Jesus, Son of God the Most High? I beseech You, Do not torment me!
030829 (For He had commanded the unclean spirit to come out of the man. For oftentimes it had seized him. And he had been kept bound in chains and in fetters, and he broke the bands and was driven into the deserted places by the demons.)
030830 And Jesus asked him, saying, What is your name? And he said, Legion; because many demons had entered into him.
030831 And they begged Him that He would not command them to go out into the abyss.
030832 And there was there a herd of many pigs feeding on the mountain. And they begged Him that He would allow them to enter into them. And He allowed them.
030833 And coming out of the man, the demons entered into the pigs. And the herd ran violently down a steep place into the lake and were choked.
030834 And those feeding the pigs , and seeing the thing, fled. And leaving, they reported to the city and to the farms.
030835 And they went out to see what had been done. And they came to Jesus and found the man from whom the demons had departed sitting at the feet of Jesus, clothed and in his right mind. And they were afraid.
030836 Also those who saw it told them how the demon-possessed one was healed.
030837 And all the multitude of the neighborhood of the Gadarenes were seized with a great fear, and asked Him to depart from them. And entering into the boat, He returned.
030838 And the man out of whom the demons had gone out begged Him, desiring to be with Him. But Jesus sent him away, saying,
030839 Return to your own house and declare what God has done to you. And he went his way and proclaimed throughout all the city what great things Jesus had done to him.
030840 And it happened when Jesus had returned, the people received Him. For they were all waiting for Him.
030841 And behold, a man named Jairus came, and he was a synagogue-ruler. And he fell down at Jesus' feet and begged Him that He would come into his house.
030842 For he had an only daughter, about twelve years of age, and she lay dying. But as He went, the people thronged Him.
030843 And a woman who had a flow of blood twelve years (who had spent all her living on physicians, and could not be healed by any)
030844 came behind Him and touched the border of His garment. And instantly her flow of blood was staunched.
030845 And Jesus said, Who touched Me? And all having denied, Peter and those with Him said, Master, the crowd presses and jostles You, and You say, Who touched Me?
030846 And Jesus said, Someone has touched Me, for I know that power has gone out of Me.
030847 And seeing that she was not hidden, the woman came trembling. And falling down before Him, she declared to Him before all the people why she had touched Him, and how she was instantly healed.
030848 And He said to her, Daughter, be comforted. Your faith has saved you; go in peace.
030849 He was still speaking when someone came from the synagogue-ruler, saying to him, Your daughter is dead, do not trouble the Teacher.
030850 But when Jesus heard, He answered Him, saying, Do not fear, only believe and she shall be healed.
030851 And coming into the house, He allowed no one to go in, except Peter and James and John, and the father and the mother of the girl.
030852 And all were weeping and bewailing her. But He said, Do not weep; she has not died, but sleeps.
030853 And they ridiculed, knowing that she was dead.
030854 And He put them all out. And He took her by the hand and called, saying, Little girl, arise!
030855 And her spirit came again, and she arose immediately. And He commanded that food be given her to eat.
030856 And her parents were astonished. But He charged them to tell no one the thing that happened.
030901 And He called His twelve disciples together and gave them power and authority over all demons and to cure diseases.
030902 And He sent them to proclaim the kingdom of God and to heal the sick.
030903 And He said to them, Take nothing for your journey, neither staffs, nor a bag, nor bread, nor money, nor each to have two tunics.
030904 And whatever house you enter into, abide there and depart from there.
030905 And whoever will not receive you, when you go out of that city shake off the very dust from your feet for a testimony against them.
030906 And they departed and went through the towns, proclaiming the gospel and healing everywhere.
030907 And Herod the tetrarch heard of all the things happening by Him. And he was perplexed, because it was said by some that John had risen from the dead;
030908 and by some, that Elijah had appeared; and by others, that one of the old prophets had risen again.
030909 And Herod said, John I have beheaded, but who is this of whom I hear such things? And he desired to see Him.
030910 And returning, the apostles told Him all that they had done. And He took them and went aside privately into a deserted place of a city called Bethsaida.
030911 But knowing this , the crowds followed Him. And He received them and spoke to them of the kingdom of God, and He healed those who had need of healing.
030912 But the day began to wear away, and coming up the Twelve said to Him, Send the crowd away so that they may go into the villages and farms all around, and lodge, and get food. For we are here in a deserted place.
030913 But He said to them, You give them something to eat. And they said, We have no more than five loaves and two fish, unless we go and buy food for all these people.
030914 (For they were about five thousand men.) And He said to His disciples, Make them recline by fifties in a company.
030915 And they did so, and made them all recline.
030916 And He took the five loaves and the two fish. And looking up to Heaven, He blessed them and broke, and He gave to the disciples to set before the crowd.
030917 And they ate and were all filled. And there was taken up twelve hand baskets full of fragments of that left over to them.
030918 And it happened as He was alone praying, the disciples were with Him. And He asked them, saying, Whom do the crowds say that I am?
030919 Answering, they said, John the Baptist; but some say , Elijah, and others say that one of the old prophets has risen again.
030920 He said to them, But who do you say that I am? Answering, Peter said, The Christ of God.
030921 And He strictly charged them and commanded to tell no one this,
030922 saying, The Son of man must suffer many things and be rejected by the elders and chief priests and scribes, and be slain, and be raised the third day.
030923 And He said to all, If anyone desires to come after Me, let him deny himself and take up his cross daily and follow Me.
030924 For whoever will save his life shall lose it, but whoever will lose his life for My sake, he shall save it.
030925 For what is a man profited if he gains the whole world and loses himself, or is cast away?
030926 For whoever shall be ashamed of Me and of My words, the Son of man shall be ashamed of him when He shall come in His own and in His Father's glory, and that of the holy angels.
030927 But I tell you truly, there are some standing here who shall not taste of death until they see the kingdom of God.
030928 And about eight days after these sayings, He took Peter and John and James and went up into a mountain to pray.
030929 And as He prayed, the appearance of His countenance was altered, and His clothing was dazzling white.
030930 And behold, two men talked with Him, who were Moses and Elijah,
030931 who appeared in glory and spoke of His exodus, which He was about to accomplish at Jerusalem.
030932 But Peter and those with him were heavy with sleep. But fully awakening, they saw His glory, and the two men who stood with Him.
030933 And in their parting from Him, it happened that Peter said to Jesus, Master, it is good for us to be here. And let us make three tabernacles, one for You and one for Moses and one for Elijah; not knowing what he said.
030934 And as he was saying these things, a cloud came and overshadowed them. And they feared as they entered into the cloud.
030935 And a voice came out of the cloud, saying, This is My Son, the Beloved, hear Him.
030936 And when the voice occurred, Jesus was found alone. And they were silent, and told no one in those days anything which they had seen.
030937 And it happened on the next day, they coming down from the mountain, a huge crowd met Him.
030938 And behold, a man cried aloud from the crowd, saying, Teacher, I beseech You, look on my son, for he is my only-born son.
030939 And lo, a spirit takes him, and he suddenly cries out. And it throws him into convulsions, with foaming, and with pain departs from him, bruising him.
030940 And I begged Your disciples to cast him out, and they could not.
030941 And answering, Jesus said, O unbelieving generation, one having been perverted, how long shall I be with you and endure you? Bring your son here.
030942 And as he was still coming, the demon violently convulsed and tore him . And Jesus rebuked the unclean spirit and healed the child and delivered him again to his father.
030943 And they were all amazed at the majesty of God. But as all were marveling at all things which Jesus did, He said to His disciples,
030944 Let these words sink down into your ears. For the Son of man shall be betrayed into the hands of men.
030945 But they did not understand this, and it was hidden from them so that they did not perceive it. And they feared to ask Him of this word.
030946 And an argument came in among them, who might be the greater of them.
030947 And seeing the argument of their heart, Jesus took a child and set him beside Him.
030948 And He said to them, Whoever shall receive this child in My name receives Me. And whoever shall receive Me receives Him who sent Me. For he who is least among you all, he shall be great.
030949 And John answered and said, Master, we saw one casting out demons in Your name. And we prevented him, because he does not follow us.
030950 And Jesus said to him, Do not prevent him , for he who is not against us is for us.
030951 And it happened in the fulfilling of the days of His taking up, He steadfastly set His face to go to Jerusalem.
030952 And He sent messengers before His face. And they went and entered into a village of the Samaritans to make ready for Him.
030953 And they did not receive Him, because His face was going toward Jerusalem.
030954 And seeing, His disciples James and John said, Lord, do You desire that we command fire to come down from Heaven and consume them, even as Elijah did?
030955 But He turned and rebuked them and said, You do not know of what spirit you are.
030956 For the Son of man has not come to destroy men's lives, but to save. And they went to another village.
030957 And it happened as they were going in the way, one said to Him, Lord, I will follow You wherever You go.
030958 And Jesus said to him, Foxes have holes, and birds of the air have nests, but the Son of man has nowhere to lay His head.
030959 And He said to another, Follow Me! But he said, Lord, first allow me to go and bury my father.
030960 Jesus said to him, Let the dead bury their dead, but you go and proclaim the kingdom of God.
030961 And another also said, Lord, I will follow You, but first allow me to take leave of those in my house.
030962 And Jesus said to him, No one, having put his hand to the plow and looking back, is fit for the kingdom of God.
031001 And after these things the Lord appointed seventy others, And He sent them two and two before His face into every city and place where He was about to come.
031002 Then He said to them, The harvest truly is great, but the laborers are few. Therefore pray to the Lord of the harvest that He may send forth laborers into His harvest.
031003 Go! Behold, I send you forth as lambs among wolves.
031004 Carry neither purse nor bag nor sandals. And greet no one by the way.
031005 And into whatever house you enter, first say, Peace to this house.
031006 And if a son of peace is there, your peace shall rest on it. If not, it shall return to you,
031007 And remain in the same house, eating and drinking the things shared by them; for the laborer is worthy of his hire. Do not move from house to house.
031008 And into whatever city you enter, and they receive you, eat such things as are set before you.
031009 And heal the sick that are in it, and say to them, The kingdom of God has come near you!
031010 And into whatever city you enter, and they do not receive you, going out into the streets say,
031011 Even the dust of your city which clings to us, we wipe off against you. Yet be sure of this, that the kingdom of God has come near you.
031012 But I say to you that it shall be more tolerable in that day for Sodom than for that city.
031013 Woe to you, Chorazin! Woe to you, Bethsaida! For if the mighty works which have been done in you had been done in Tyre and Sidon, they would have repented a long while ago, sitting in sackcloth and ashes.
031014 But it shall be more tolerable for Tyre and Sidon at the Judgment than for you.
031015 And you, Capernaum, which has been lifted up to Heaven, you shall be thrust down into hell.
031016 The one hearing you hears Me, and he who despises you despises Me; he who rejects you also rejects Him who sent Me.
031017 And the seventy returned again with joy, saying, Lord, even the demons are subject to us through Your name.
031018 And He said to them, I saw Satan fall from Heaven like lightning.
031019 Behold, I give to you authority to tread on serpents and scorpions, and over all the authority of the enemy. And nothing shall by any means hurt you.
031020 Yet do not rejoice in this, that the evil spirits are subject to you, rather rejoice because your names are written in Heaven.
031021 In that hour Jesus rejoiced in Spirit and said, I thank You, Father, Lord of Heaven and earth, that You have hidden these things from the sophisticated and cunning, and have revealed them to babes. Yes, Father, for so it was pleasing before You.
031022 All things are delivered to Me by My Father; and no one knows who the Son is except the Father, and who the Father is except the Son, and the one to whom the Son will reveal Him .
031023 And He turned to His disciples and said privately, Blessed are the eyes which see the things that you see.
031024 For I tell you that many prophets and kings have desired to see what you see, and have not seen them , and to hear what you hear, and have not heard them .
031025 And, behold, a certain lawyer stood up and tempted Him, saying, Master, what shall I do to inherit eternal life?
031026 He said to him, What is written in the law? How do you read it?
031027 And answering, he said, You shall love the Lord your God with all your heart, and with all your soul, and with all your strength, and with all your mind, and your neighbor as yourself.
031028 And He said to him, You have answered right; do this and you shall live.
031029 But he, willing to justify himself, said to Jesus, And who is my neighbor?
031030 And answering, Jesus said, A certain man went down from Jerusalem to Jericho and fell among robbers, who stripped him of his clothing and wounded him, and departed, leaving him half dead.
031031 And by coincidence a certain priest came down that way and seeing him, he passed by on the opposite side .
031032 And in the same way a Levite, also being at the place, coming and seeing him , he passed on the opposite side .
031033 But a certain traveling Samaritan came upon him, and seeing him, he was filled with pity.
031034 And coming near, he bound up his wounds, pouring on oil and wine, and set him on his own animal and brought him to an inn, and took care of him.
031035 And going on the next day, he took out two denarii and gave them to the innkeeper, and said to him, Take care of him. And whatever more you spend, when I come again I will repay you.
031036 Then which of these three, do you think, was neighbor to him who fell among the robbers?
031037 And he said, The one doing the deed of mercy to him. And Jesus said to him, Go and do likewise.
031038 And as they went, it happened that He entered into a certain village. And a certain woman named Martha received Him into her house.
031039 And she had a sister called Mary, who also sat at Jesus' feet and heard His word.
031040 But Martha was distracted with much serving. And she came to Him and said, Lord, do You not care that my sister has left me to serve alone? Therefore tell her to help me.
031041 And Jesus answered and said to her, Martha, Martha, you are anxious and troubled about many things.
031042 But one thing is needful, and Mary has chosen that good part, which shall not be taken away from her.
031101 And it happened as He was praying in a certain place, when He ceased, one of His disciples said to Him, Lord, teach us to pray, as John also taught His disciples.
031102 And He said to them, When you pray, say: Our Father, who is in Heaven, hallowed be Your name. Your kingdom come, Your will be done, as in Heaven, so also on the earth.
031103 Give us day by day our daily bread,
031104 and forgive us our sins, for we ourselves also forgive everyone who is indebted to us. And lead us not into temptation, but deliver us from evil.
031105 And He said to them, which of you shall have a friend and shall go to him at midnight and say to him, Friend, lend me three loaves,
031106 for a friend of mine has come from a journey, and I have nothing to set before him?
031107 And he answering from inside may say, Do not trouble me. The door is now shut and my children are in bed with me. I cannot rise and give to you.
031108 I say to you, though he will not rise and give to him because he is his friend, yet because of his importunity he will arise and give him as many as he needs.
031109 And I say to you, Ask and it shall be given you. Seek and you shall find. Knock and it shall be opened to you.
031110 For everyone who asks receives. And he who seeks finds. And to him who knocks it shall be opened.
031111 For what father of you, if the son asks for bread, will he give him a stone? Or if he asks for a fish, will he give him a snake for a fish?
031112 Or if he shall ask for an egg, will he give him a scorpion?
031113 If you then, being evil, know how to give good gifts to your children, how much more shall your heavenly Father give the Holy Spirit to those who ask Him?
031114 And He was casting out a demon, and it was dumb. And it happened as the demon was going out, the dumb one spoke. And the people marveled.
031115 But some of them said, He casts out demons through Beelzebub the chief of the demons.
031116 And others, tempting Him , sought a sign from Heaven from him.
031117 But knowing their thoughts, He said to them, Every kingdom divided against itself is brought to desolation. And a house divided against a house falls.
031118 If Satan also is divided against himself, how shall his kingdom stand? For you say that I cast out demons through Beelzebub.
031119 And if I cast out demons by Beelzebub, by whom do your sons cast them out? Therefore they shall be your judges.
031120 But if I cast out demons with the finger of God, no doubt the kingdom of God has come on you.
031121 When the strong man, fully armed, guards his dwelling, his goods are in peace.
031122 But when one stronger than he comes, he overcomes him. He takes from him all his armor in which he trusted, and he distributes his arms.
031123 He who is not with Me is against Me, and he who does not gather with Me scatters.
031124 When the unclean spirit has gone out of a man, he walks through dry places seeking rest. And finding none, he says, I will return to my house from which I came out.
031125 And when he comes, he finds it swept and decorated.
031126 And he goes and takes seven other spirits more wicked than himself, and entering in, they dwell there. And the last state of that man is worse than the first.
031127 And it happened as He spoke these things, a certain woman of the company lifted up her voice and said to Him, Blessed is the womb that bore You, and the breasts which You have sucked.
031128 But He said, No; rather, blessed are they who hear the Word of God and keep it.
031129 But the crowds pressing on Him , He began to say, This is an evil generation. It seeks a sign, and no sign will be given to it, except the sign of Jonah the prophet.
031130 For as Jonah was a sign to the Ninevites, so also shall the Son of man be to this generation.
031131 The queen of the south shall rise up in the Judgment with the men of this generation and condemn them. For she came from the ends of the earth to hear the wisdom of Solomon. And behold, One greater than Solomon is here.
031132 The men of Nineveh shall rise up in the Judgment with this generation and shall condemn it. For they repented at the preaching of Jonah. And behold, One greater than Jonah is here.
031133 No one, when he has lighted a lamp, puts it in a secret place, or under a grain-measure, but on a lampstand, so that they who come in may see the light.
031134 The light of the body is the eye. Therefore when your eye is sound, your whole body also is full of light. But when your eye is evil, your body also is full of darkness.
031135 Therefore take heed that the light in you is not darkness.
031136 Therefore if your whole body is full of light, having no part dark, the whole shall be full of light, as when the shining of a lamp enlightens you.
031137 And as He spoke , a certain Pharisee asked Him to dine with him. And He went in and reclined.
031138 And when the Pharisee saw it , he was amazed that He had not first washed before dinner.
031139 And the Lord said to him, Now you Pharisees make the outside of the cup and the platter clean, but your inward part is full of plunder and wickedness.
031140 Fools! Did not He who made the outside also make the inside?
031141 But give alms of such things as you have, and behold, all things are clean to you.
031142 But woe to you, Pharisees! For you tithe mint and rue and every herb, and pass over judgment and the love of God. You ought to have done these, and not to leave the other undone.
031143 Woe to you, Pharisees! For you love the chief seats in the synagogues and greetings in the markets.
031144 Woe to you, scribes and Pharisees, hypocrites! For you are like unseen tombs and the men walking above are not aware of them.
031145 And one of the lawyers answered and said to Him, Master, you reproach us also when you say this.
031146 And He said, Woe to you also, lawyers! For you load men with burdens grievous to be carried, and you yourselves do not touch the burdens with one of your fingers.
031147 Woe to you! For you build the tombs of the prophets, and your fathers killed them.
031148 Truly you bear witness that you consent to the deeds of your fathers. For they indeed killed them, and you build their tombs.
031149 Therefore the wisdom of God also said, I will send them prophets and apostles, and some of them they shall slay and persecute,
031150 so that the blood of all the prophets, which was shed from the foundation of the world, may be required of this generation;
031151 from the blood of Abel to the blood of Zechariah, who perished between the altar and the temple. Truly I say to you, It shall be required of this generation.
031152 Woe to you, lawyers! For you have taken away the key of knowledge. You did not enter in yourselves, and you have hindered those who were entering in.
031153 And as He said these things to them, the scribes and Pharisees began to be terribly angry, and to draw Him out concerning many things,
031154 lying in ambush for Him, and seeking to catch something out of His mouth, so that they might accuse Him.
031201 In the meantime, when there had gathered together an innumerable crowd of people, so as to trample on one another, He began to say to His disciples first, Beware of the leaven of the Pharisees, which is hypocrisy.
031202 For there is nothing covered that shall not be revealed, nor anything hidden that shall not be known.
031203 Therefore whatever you have spoken in darkness shall be heard in the light. And that which you have spoken in the ear in secret rooms shall be proclaimed on the housetops.
031204 And I say to you, My friends, do not be afraid of those who kill the body, and after that have no more that they can do.
031205 But I will warn you of whom you shall fear: Fear Him who, after He has killed, has authority to cast into hell. Yea, I say to you, fear Him.
031206 Are not five sparrows sold for two assaria? And not one of them is forgotten before God.
031207 But even the very hairs of your head are all numbered. Therefore do not fear, you are of more value than many sparrows.
031208 Also I say to you, Whoever shall confess Me before men, the Son of man also shall confess him before the angels of God.
031209 But he who denies Me before men shall be denied before the angels of God.
031210 And whoever shall speak a word against the Son of man, it shall be forgiven him. But to him who blasphemes against the Holy Spirit, it shall not be forgiven.
031211 And when they bring you into the synagogues, and to rulers and authorities, take no thought as to how or what thing you shall answer, or what you shall say.
031212 For the Holy Spirit shall teach you in the same hour what you ought to say.
031213 And one of the company said to Him, Master, speak to my brother to divide the inheritance with me.
031214 And He said to him, Man, who made Me a judge or a divider over you?
031215 And He said to them, Watch and keep yourselves from covetousness. For a man's life is not in the abundance of the things which he possesses.
031216 And He spoke a parable to them, saying, The ground of a certain rich man brought forth plentifully.
031217 And he thought within himself, saying, What shall I do, because I have no room in which to store my fruits?
031218 And he said, I will do this. I will pull down my barns and build bigger ones, and I will store all my fruits and my goods there.
031219 And I will say to my soul, Soul, you have many goods laid up for many years. Take your ease, eat drink and be merry.
031220 But God said to him, Fool! This night your soul shall be required of you, then whose shall be those things which you have prepared?
031221 So is he who lays up treasure for himself and is not rich toward God.
031222 And He said to His disciples, Therefore I say to you, Be not anxious as to your life, what you shall eat; nor for the body, what you shall put on.
031223 Life is more than food, and the body is more than clothing.
031224 Consider the ravens: for they neither sow nor reap, having neither storehouse nor barn, and God feeds them. How much more are you better than the birds?
031225 And which of you by being anxious can add one cubit to his stature?
031226 If then you are not able to do even the least, why are you anxious about the rest?
031227 Consider the lilies, how they grow; they do not toil, they do not spin. And yet I say to you that Solomon in all his glory was not arrayed like one of these.
031228 If then God so clothes the grass (which today is in the field, and tomorrow is cast into the oven) how much more will He clothe you, O little-faiths?
031229 And do not seek what you shall eat, nor what you shall drink, and stop being in anxiety.
031230 For all these things the nations of the world seek after, and your Father knows that you have need of these things.
031231 But rather seek the kingdom of God, and all these things shall be added to you.
031232 Do not fear, little flock, for it is your Father's good pleasure to give you the kingdom.
031233 Sell what you have and give alms. Make for yourselves purses which do not become old, an unfailing treasure in Heaven, where no thief comes nor moth corrupts.
031234 For where your treasure is, there your heart will be also.
031235 Let your loins be girded about, and your lights burning.
031236 And you yourselves be like men who wait for their lord, whenever he shall return from the wedding, so that when he comes and knocks, they may open to him immediately.
031237 Blessed are those servants whom the lord will find watching when he comes. Truly I say to you that he shall gird himself and make them recline; and coming up he will serve them.
031238 And if he comes in the second watch, or comes in the third watch, and find it so, blessed are those servants.
031239 And know this, that if the master of the house had known what hour the thief would come, he would have watched and would not have allowed his house to be dug through.
031240 Therefore be ready also, for the Son of man comes at an hour when you think not.
031241 And Peter said to Him, Lord, do You speak this parable to us or also to all?
031242 And the Lord said, Who then is that faithful and wise steward whom his lord shall set over his houseservants, to give them their portion of food in season?
031243 Blessed is that servant when his lord comes and finds him so doing.
031244 Truly I say to you that he will set him over all his possessions.
031245 But if that servant says in his heart, My lord delays his coming, and shall begin to beat the male servants and women servants, and to eat and drink and to be drunk,
031246 the lord of that servant will come in a day when he does not expect, and at an hour when he does not know. And he will cut him apart, and will appoint him his portion with the unbelievers.
031247 And that servant who knew his lord's will and did not prepare, nor did according to His will, shall be beaten with many stripes .
031248 But he not knowing, and doing things worthy of stripes, shall be beaten with few stripes . For to whomever much is given, of him much shall be required. And to whom men have committed much, of him they will ask the more.
031249 I have come to send fire on the earth. And what will I do if it is already kindled?
031250 But I have a baptism to be baptized with, and how I am pressed down until it is accomplished!
031251 Do you suppose that I have come to give peace on earth? I tell you, no, but rather division.
031252 For from now on, there shall be five in one house divided, three against two, and two against three.
031253 The father shall be divided against the son, and the son against the father; the mother against the daughter, and the daughter against the mother; the mother-in-law against her daughter-in-law, and the daughter-in-law against her mother-in-law.
031254 And He also said to the crowd, When you see a cloud rise out of the west, immediately you say, There is a shower coming. And so it is.
031255 And when you see the south wind blow, you say, There will be heat; and it occurs.
031256 Hypocrites! You know to discern the face of the heaven and the earth, but how is it that you do not discern this time?
031257 And why, even of yourselves, do you not judge what is right?
031258 For as you go with your adversary to the judge, give pains in the way to be set free from him, lest he drag you to the judge, and the judge deliver you to the officer, and the officer cast you into the prison.
031259 I tell you, you shall not depart from there until you have paid the very last lepton.
031301 And some were present at the same time reporting to Him of the Galileans whose blood Pilate had mixed with their sacrifices.
031302 And answering, Jesus said to them, Do you suppose that these Galileans were sinners above all the Galileans because they suffered such things?
031303 I tell you, No. But unless you repent, you will all likewise perish.
031304 Or those eighteen on whom the tower in Siloam fell and killed them, do you think that they were sinners above all men who lived in Jerusalem?
031305 I tell you, No. But unless you repent, you will all likewise perish.
031306 He also spoke this parable: A certain man had a fig-tree planted in his vineyard. And he came and sought fruit on it, and found none.
031307 And he said to the dresser of his vineyard, Behold, these three years I come seeking fruit on this fig-tree, and find none. Cut it down, why does it encumber the ground?
031308 And answering, he said to him, Lord, let it alone this year also, until I dig around it and throw manure.
031309 And if it bears fruit, well ; and if not, then after that you shall cut it down.
031310 And He was teaching in one of the synagogues on the sabbath.
031311 And behold, there was a woman who had a spirit of infirmity eighteen years, and she was bowed together and was not able to be completely erect.
031312 And when Jesus saw her, He called and said to her, Woman, you are delivered from your infirmity.
031313 And He laid His hands on her. And instantly she was made erect, and she glorified God.
031314 And answering, the synagogue ruler, being angry because Jesus had healed on the sabbath day, said to the crowd, There are six days in which it is right to work. Therefore in them come and be healed, and not on the sabbath day.
031315 And the Lord answered him and said, Hypocrite! Does not each one of you on the sabbath loosen his ox or ass from the stall and lead it away, to give it drink?
031316 And ought not this woman , being a daughter of Abraham whom Satan has bound, lo these eighteen years, be loosened from this bond on the Sabbath day?
031317 And when He had said these things, all His adversaries were ashamed. And all the people rejoiced for all the glorious things that were done by Him.
031318 And He said, What is the kingdom of God like? And to what shall I compare it?
031319 It is like a grain of mustard seed which a man took and threw into his garden. And it grew and became a great tree, and the birds of the air lodged in its branches.
031320 And again He said, To what shall I compare the kingdom of God?
031321 It is like leaven which a woman took and hid in three measures of meal, until the whole was leavened.
031322 And He went through the cities and villages, teaching and progressing toward Jerusalem.
031323 And one said to Him, Lord, are the ones being saved few? And He said to them,
031324 Strive to enter in at the narrow gate. For I say to you, many will seek to enter in and shall not be able.
031325 And once the Master of the house has risen up and has shut the door, and you begin to stand outside and to knock at the door, saying, Lord, Lord, open to us, and He shall answer and say to you, I do not know you; from where are you;
031326 then you shall begin to say, We ate and drank in Your presence, and You have taught in our streets.
031327 But He shall say, I tell you, I do not know you; from where you are. Depart from Me, all workers of unrighteousness!
031328 There will be weeping and gnashing of teeth when you will see Abraham and Isaac and Jacob, and all the prophets, in the kingdom of God, and yourselves being thrust out.
031329 And they will come from the east and the west, and from the north and the south, and will recline in the kingdom of God.
031330 And behold, there are last ones which will be first, and there are first ones which will be last.
031331 The same day there came certain of the Pharisees, saying to Him, Go out and depart from here, for Herod will kill you.
031332 And He said to them, You go and tell that fox, Behold, today and tomorrow, I cast out demons and I complete cures, and the third day I will be finished.
031333 Yet I must walk today and tomorrow and the day following. For it cannot be that a prophet perish outside of Jerusalem.
031334 Jerusalem! Jerusalem! the one killing the prophets, and stoning those having been sent to her; how often I desired to gather your children in the way a hen gathers her brood under the wings, and you did not desire it .
031335 Behold, your house is left to you desolate. And truly I say to you, You will not see Me until it come when you say, Blessed is He who comes in the name of the Lord.
031401 And as He went into the house of one of the chief Pharisees to eat bread on the sabbath day, it happened that they watched Him.
031402 And behold, a certain man was dropsical before Him.
031403 And answering, Jesus spoke to the lawyers and Pharisees, saying, Is it lawful to heal on the sabbath day ?
031404 And they were silent. And taking him , He healed him and let him go.
031405 And He answered them, saying, Which of you shall have an ass or an ox fall into a pit and will not immediately pull him out on the sabbath day?
031406 And they could not answer Him again as to these things.
031407 And He put forth a parable to those who were invited, when He noted how they chose out the chief places, saying to them,
031408 When you are invited by anyone to a wedding, do not recline in the chief seat, lest a more honorable man than you may be invited by him.
031409 And he who invited you and him shall come and say to you, Give place to this man; and then you begin with shame to take the last place.
031410 But when you are invited, go and recline in the lowest place, so that when he who invited you comes, he may say to you, Friend, go up higher. Then glory shall be to you before those reclining with you.
031411 For whoever exalts himself shall be abased, and he who humbles himself shall be exalted.
031412 And He also said to him who invited Him, When you make a dinner or a supper, do not call your friends or your brothers, or your kinsmen, or your rich neighbors; lest they also invite you again, and a recompense be made to you.
031413 But when you make a feast, call the poor, the maimed, the lame, the blind,
031414 and you shall be blessed, for they cannot repay you; for you shall be repaid at the resurrection of the just.
031415 And one of those who reclined with Him heard these things, and he said to Him, Blessed are those eating bread in the kingdom of God.
031416 And He said to him, A certain man made a great supper and invited many.
031417 And he sent his servant at supper time to say to those who were invited, Come, for all things are now ready.
031418 And all with one consent began to make excuse. The first said to him, I have bought a piece of ground, I must go and see it. I beg you, have me excused.
031419 And another said, I have bought five yoke of oxen, and I am going to test them. I beg you, have me excused.
031420 And another said, I have married a wife, and therefore I cannot come.
031421 And coming up that servant reported these things to his lord. And the master of the house, being angry, said to his servant, Go out quickly into the streets and lanes of the city and bring in here the poor and the maimed, and the lame and the blind.
031422 And the servant said, Lord, it is done as you have commanded, and still there is room.
031423 And the lord said to the servant, Go out into the highways and hedges and compel them to come in, so that my house may be filled.
031424 For I say to you that none of these men who were invited shall taste of my supper.
031425 And great crowds went with Him. And He turned and said to them,
031426 If anyone comes to Me and does not hate his father and mother and wife and children and brothers and sisters, yes, and his own life also, he cannot be My disciple.
031427 And whoever does not bear his cross and come after Me, he cannot be My disciple.
031428 For which of you, intending to build a tower, does not sit down first and count the cost, whether he may have enough to finish it;
031429 lest perhaps, after he has laid the foundation and is not able to finish, all those seeing begin to mock him,
031430 saying, This man began to build and was not able to finish.
031431 Or what king, going to make war against another king, does not first sit down and consult whether he is able with ten thousand to meet him who comes against him with twenty thousand?
031432 Or else, while the other is still a great way off, he sends a delegation and asks conditions of peace.
031433 So then, everyone of you who does not forsake all his possessions, he cannot be My disciple.
031434 Salt is good, but if the salt has become tasteless, with what shall it be seasoned?
031435 It is not fit for the land, nor for manure, but men throw it out. He who has ears to hear, let him hear.
031501 And all the tax-collectors and sinners drew near to Him in order to hear Him.
031502 And the Pharisees and scribes murmured, saying, This man receives sinners and eats with them.
031503 And He spoke this parable to them, saying,
031504 What man of you, having a hundred sheep, if he loses one of them, does not leave the ninety-nine in the wilderness and go after that which is lost until he finds it?
031505 And when he has found it , he lays it on his shoulders, rejoicing.
031506 And when he comes home, he calls together his friends and neighbors, saying to them, Rejoice with me, for I have found my sheep which was lost.
031507 I say to you that likewise joy shall be in Heaven over one sinner who repents, more than over ninety-nine just persons who need no repentance.
031508 Or what woman having ten drachmas, if she loses one drachma, does she not light a lamp and sweep the house, and seek carefully until she finds it ?
031509 And when she has found it , she calls her friends and her neighbors together, saying, Rejoice with me, for I have found the drachma which I had lost.
031510 Likewise I say to you, there is joy before the angels of God over one sinner who repents.
031511 And He said, A certain man had two sons.
031512 And the younger of them said to his father, Father, give me the portion of goods that is coming to me . And he divided his living to them.
031513 And not many days afterward, the younger son gathered all together and went away into a far country. And there he wasted his property, living dissolutely.
031514 And when he had spent all, there arose a mighty famine in that land. And he began to be in want.
031515 And he went and joined himself to a citizen of that country. And he sent him into his fields to feed pigs.
031516 And he was longing to fill his belly with the husks that the pigs ate, and no one gave to him.
031517 And when he came to himself, he said, How many hired servants of my father abound in loaves, and I perish with hunger!
031518 I will arise and go to my father, and will say to him, Father, I have sinned against Heaven and before you
031519 and am no more worthy to be called your son. Make me like one of your hired servants.
031520 And he arose and came to his father. But when he was still a great way off, his father saw him and had compassion, and ran and fell on his neck and kissed him.
031521 And the son said to him, Father, I have sinned against Heaven and before you, and am no more worthy to be called your son.
031522 But the father said to his servants, Bring the best robe and put it on him. And put a ring on his hand and shoes on his feet.
031523 And bring the fattened calf here and kill it . And let us eat and be merry,
031524 for this my son was dead and is alive again, he was lost and is found. And they began to be merry.
031525 And his elder son was in the field. And as he came and drew near the house, he heard music and dancing.
031526 And he called one of the servants and asked what these things meant.
031527 And he said to him, Your brother has come, and your father has killed the fattened calf because he has received him safe and sound.
031528 And he was angry and would not go in. Therefore his father came out and entreated him.
031529 And answering he said to his father, Lo, these many years I have served you, neither did I transgress your commandment at any time. And yet you never gave me a kid so that I might make merry with my friends.
031530 But when this son of yours came, who has devoured your living with harlots, you have killed for him the fattened calf.
031531 And he said to him, Son, you are always with me, and all that I have is yours.
031532 It was right that we should make merry and be glad, for this brother of yours was dead and is alive again; and was lost, and is found.
031601 And He also said to His disciples, There was a certain rich man who had a steward. And he was accused to him, that he had wasted his goods.
031602 And he called him and said to him, What is this I hear about you? Give an account of your stewardship, for you may no longer be steward.
031603 And the steward said within himself, What shall I do? For my lord is taking the stewardship away from me. I cannot dig; I am ashamed to beg.
031604 I know what I will do, so that when I am put out of the stewardship they may receive me into their houses.
031605 So he called every one of his lord's debtors and said; to the first, How much do you owe my lord?
031606 And he said, A hundred baths of oil. And he said to him, Take your bill and sit down quickly and write fifty.
031607 And he said to another, And how much do you owe? And he said, A hundred cors of wheat. And he said to him, Take your bill and write eighty.
031608 And the unjust steward's lord commended him because he had done wisely. For the children of this world are in their generation wiser than the children of light.
031609 And I say to you, Make friends by the mammon of unrighteousness for yourselves, so that when you fail, they may receive you into everlasting dwellings.
031610 He who is faithful in the least is also faithful in much. And he who is unjust in the least is also unjust in much.
031611 Therefore if you have not been faithful in the unrighteous mammon, who will entrust the true riches to you?
031612 And if you have not been faithful in that which is another's, who shall give you that which is your own?
031613 No servant can serve two masters. For either he will hate the one and love the other, or else he will hold to the one and despise the other. You cannot serve God and mammon.
031614 And being money-lovers, all the Pharisees also heard all these things. And they derided Him.
031615 And He said to them, You are those who justify yourselves before men, but God knows your hearts. For that which is highly esteemed among men is abomination in the sight of God.
031616 The law and the prophets were until John. Since that time the kingdom of God is proclaimed, and everyone is pressing into it.
031617 And it is easier for the heaven and earth to pass than for one tittle of the law to fail.
031618 Everyone putting away his wife and marrying another commits adultery; and everyone marrying her who is put away from her husband commits adultery.
031619 There was a certain rich man who was customarily clothed in purple and fine linen and making merry in luxury every day.
031620 And there was a certain beggar named Lazarus, who was laid at his gate, full of sores
031621 and desiring to be fed with the crumbs which fell from the rich man's table. But even the dogs came and licked his sores.
031622 And it happened that the beggar died and was carried by the angels into Abraham's bosom. The rich one also died and was buried.
031623 And in hell he lifted up his eyes, being in torments, and saw Abraham afar off, and Lazarus in his bosom.
031624 And he cried and said, Father Abraham, have mercy on me and send Lazarus so that he may dip the tip of his finger in water and cool my tongue, for I am tormented in this flame.
031625 But Abraham said, Son, remember that you in your lifetime received your good things, and likewise Lazarus evil things. But now he is comforted and you are tormented.
031626 And besides all this, there is a great chasm fixed between you and us; so that they desiring to pass from here to you cannot, nor can they pass over to us from there.
031627 And he said, I beg you therefore, father, that you would send him to my father's house,
031628 for I have five brothers, so that he may testify to them, lest they also come into this place of torment.
031629 Abraham said to him, They have Moses and the prophets, let them hear them.
031630 And he said, No, father Abraham, but if one should go to them from the dead, they would repent.
031631 And he said to him, If they do not hear Moses and the Prophets, they will not be persuaded, even though one rose from the dead.
031701 And He said to the disciples, It is impossible but that offenses will come. But woe to him through whom they come!
031702 It were better for him that a millstone were hanged around his neck and he were cast into the sea, than that he should offend one of these little ones.
031703 Take heed to yourselves. If your brother trespasses against you, rebuke him. And if he repents, forgive him.
031704 And if he trespasses against you seven times in a day, and seven times in a day turns again to you, saying, I repent, you shall forgive him.
031705 And the apostles said to the Lord, Give us more faith.
031706 And the Lord said, If you had faith as a grain of mustard seed, you might say to this sycamine tree, Be rooted up and be planted in the sea! And it would obey you.
031707 But which of you who has a servant plowing or feeding will say to him immediately after he has come from the field, Come, recline?
031708 Will he not say to him, Prepare something so that I may eat, and gird yourself and serve me until I eat and drink. And afterward you shall eat and drink.
031709 Does he thank that servant because he did the things that were commanded him? I think not.
031710 So likewise you, when you shall have done all the things commanded you, say, We are unprofitable servants, for we have done what we ought to do.
031711 And as He went to Jerusalem, it happened that he went through the midst of Samaria and Galilee.
031712 And as He entered into a certain village, ten leprous men met Him, who stood afar off.
031713 And they lifted voice and said, Jesus, Master, pity us!
031714 And seeing them , He said to them, Go show yourselves to the priests. And it happened, as they went, that they were cleansed.
031715 And one of them, when he saw that he was healed, turned back and glorified God with a loud voice.
031716 And he fell down on his face at His feet, thanking Him. And he was a Samaritan.
031717 And answering, Jesus said, Were there not ten cleansed? But where are the nine?
031718 Were none found who returned to give glory to God except this foreigner?
031719 And He said to him, Rise and go; your faith has cured you.
031720 And being asked by the Pharisees when the kingdom of God would come, He answered and said, The kingdom of God does not come with observation.
031721 Nor shall they say, Lo here! or, behold, there! For behold, the kingdom of God is in your midst.
031722 And He said to the disciples, The days will come when you will desire to see one of the days of the Son of man, and you shall not see it .
031723 And they shall say to you, Lo, here! or, behold, there! Do not go away, nor follow.
031724 For as the lightning which lights up, flashing from the one part under heaven, and shines to the other part under heaven, so also shall the Son of man be in His day.
031725 But first He must suffer many things and be rejected of this generation.
031726 And as it was in the days of Noah, so it also shall be in the days of the Son of man.
031727 They ate, they drank, they married wives, they were given in marriage, until the day that Noah entered into the ark; and the flood came and destroyed them all.
031728 So also as it was in the days of Lot: they ate, they drank, they bought, they sold, they planted, they built;
031729 but the day Lot went out of Sodom, it rained fire and brimstone from the heaven and destroyed them all.
031730 Even so it shall be in the day when the Son of man is revealed.
031731 In that day he who shall be on the housetop, and his goods in the house, let him not come down to take them away. And likewise, he who is in the field, let him not return to the things behind.
031732 Remember Lot's wife.
031733 Whoever shall seek to save his life shall lose it, and whoever shall lose his life shall preserve it.
031734 I tell you, in that night there shall be two in one bed, the one shall be taken, and the other shall be left.
031735 Two shall be grinding together, one will be taken, and the other left.
031736 Two shall be in the field, one will be taken, and the other left.
031737 And they answered and said to Him, Where, Lord? And He said to them, Wherever the body is , there the eagles will be gathered together.
031801 And He also spoke a parable to them to teach it is always right to pray, and not to faint,
031802 saying, A certain judge was in a certain city, not fearing God, nor respecting man.
031803 And a widow was in that city. And she came to Him, saying, Avenge me of my adversary.
031804 And he would not do so for a time. But afterward he said within himself, Though I do not fear God nor regard man,
031805 yet because this widow troubles me, I will avenge her, that she not wear me down in the end.
031806 And the Lord said, Hear what the unjust judge says.
031807 And shall not God avenge His own elect who cry day and night to Him, though He has been long-suffering over them?
031808 I say to you that He will avenge them speedily. Yet when the Son of man comes, shall He find faith on the earth?
031809 And He spoke this parable to certain ones who trusted in themselves, that they were righteous, and despised others:
031810 Two men went up into the temple to pray; the one a Pharisee, and the other a tax-collector.
031811 The Pharisee stood and prayed within himself in this way: God, I thank You that I am not as other men are , extortioners, unjust, adulterers, or even like this tax-collector.
031812 I fast twice on the Sabbath, I give tithes of all that I possess.
031813 And standing afar off, the tax-collector would not even lift up his eyes to Heaven, but struck on his breast, saying, God be merciful to me a sinner!
031814 I tell you, this man went down to his house justified rather than the other. For everyone who exalts himself shall be abased, and he who humbles himself shall be exalted.
031815 And they also brought infants to Him, that He might touch them. But when the disciples saw, they rebuked them.
031816 But Jesus called them and said, Allow the little children to come to Me, and forbid them not. For of such is the kingdom of God.
031817 Truly I say to you, Whoever shall not receive the kingdom of God as a little child shall in no way enter into it.
031818 And a certain ruler asked Him, saying, Good Teacher, what shall I do to inherit eternal life?
031819 And Jesus said to him, Why do you call Me good? None is good except One, God.
031820 You know the commandments: Do not commit adultery, do not kill, do not steal, do not bear false witness, honor your father and your mother.
031821 And he said, I have kept all these from my youth up.
031822 And when Jesus heard these things, He said to him, Yet you lack one thing. Sell all that you have and distribute to the poor, and you shall have treasure in Heaven. And come, follow Me.
031823 And when he heard this, he was very sorrowful, for he was very rich.
031824 And when Jesus saw that he was very sorrowful, He said, How hardly those having riches shall enter into the kingdom of God!
031825 For it is easier for a camel to go through a needle's eye than for a rich one to enter into the kingdom of God.
031826 And the ones who heard said, And who can be saved?
031827 And He said, The things which are impossible with men are possible with God.
031828 And Peter said, Lo, we have left all and have followed You.
031829 And He said to them, Truly I say to you, There is no one who has left house, or parents, or brothers, or wife, or children for the sake of the kingdom of God,
031830 who shall not receive many times more in this present time, and, in the world to come everlasting life.
031831 And He took the Twelve and said to them, Behold, we go up to Jerusalem and all things that are written by the prophets concerning the Son of man will be accomplished.
031832 For He will be delivered to the nations and will be mocked and insulted and spat on.
031833 And they will scourge Him and put Him to death, and the third day He will rise again.
031834 And they did not understand any of these things. And this saying was hidden from them, nor did they know the things which were spoken.
031835 And as He came near Jericho, it happened that a certain blind man sat by the roadside begging.
031836 And hearing the crowd pass by, he asked what it meant.
031837 And they told him that Jesus of Nazareth passed by.
031838 And he cried, saying, Jesus, Son of David! Have mercy on me.
031839 And they who were in front rebuked him that he should be quiet. But he cried so much the more, Son of David! Have mercy on me.
031840 And Jesus stood and commanded him to be brought to Him. And when he had come near, He asked him,
031841 saying, What do you desire that I should do to you? And he said, Lord, that I may receive my sight.
031842 And Jesus said to him, Receive your sight! Your faith has saved you.
031843 And immediately he received his sight and followed him, glorifying God. And when they saw, all the people gave praise to God.
031901 And going in, He passed through Jericho.
031902 And behold, there was a man named Zaccheus, who was a chief tax-collector. And he was rich.
031903 And he sought to see Jesus, to see who He was. And he could not because of the press, because he was little in stature.
031904 And he ran in front and climbed up into a sycamore tree to see Him. For He was to pass through that way .
031905 And when Jesus came to the place, He looked up and saw him. And He said to him, Zaccheus! Hurry and come down, for today I must stay at your house.
031906 And hurrying he came down, and received Him joyfully.
031907 And seeing, they all murmured, saying, He has gone in to stay with a sinful man.
031908 And Zaccheus stood and said to the Lord, Behold, Lord, I give half of my goods to the poor. And in anything I accused anyone falsely, I restore it fourfold.
031909 And Jesus said to him, This day salvation has come to this house, because he also is a son of Abraham.
031910 For the Son of man has come to seek and to save that which was lost.
031911 And as they heard these things, He added and spoke a parable, because He was near Jerusalem, and because they thought that the kingdom of God was about to appear immediately.
031912 Therefore He said, A certain nobleman went into a far country to receive a kingdom for himself, and to return.
031913 And He called his ten servants and delivered ten minas, and said to them, Trade until I come back.
031914 But his citizens hated him. And they sent a message after him, saying, We will not have this one to reign over us.
031915 And when he had received his kingdom and had returned, then it happened that he commanded these servants to be called to him; the ones to whom he had given the silver; so that he might know what each had gained by trading.
031916 And came the first, saying, Lord, your mina has gained ten minas.
031917 And he said to him, Well done , good servant, because you have been faithful in a least thing, have authority over ten cities.
031918 And the second came, saying, Lord, your mina has made five minas.
031919 And he said the same to him, You be over five cities.
031920 And another came, saying, Lord, behold, here is your mina, which I have kept in a handkerchief.
031921 For I feared you, because you are a harsh man. You take up what you did not lay down, and you reap what you did not sow.
031922 And he said to him, I will judge you out of your own mouth, wicked servant! You knew that I was a harsh man, taking up what I had not laid down and reaping what I did not sow.
031923 And why did you not give my silver on the bank table, and coming I might have exacted it with interest?
031924 And he said to those who stood by, Take the mina from him and give it to him who has ten minas.
031925 And they said to him, Lord, he has ten minas.
031926 For I say to you that to everyone who has, more will be given. And from him who has not, even that which he has will be taken from him.
031927 But those who are my enemies, who did not desire that I should reign over them, bring them here and slay them before me.
031928 And saying these things, He went in front, going up to Jerusalem.
031929 And it happened as He drew near Bethphage and Bethany, toward the mount called Mount of Olives, He sent two of the disciples,
031930 saying, Go into the village across from you , and having entered, you will find a colt tied up, on which no one of men has yet sat. Untie it and bring it .
031931 And if anyone asks you, Why are you untying it ? You will say this to him, Because the Lord has need of it.
031932 And going, those who were sent found as He had said to them.
031933 And as they were untying the colt, its owners said to them, Why are you untying the colt?
031934 And they said, The Lord has need of him.
031935 And they brought him to Jesus. And they threw their garments on the colt. And they set Jesus on it .
031936 And as He went, they spread their clothes in the way.
031937 And when He had come near, even now at the descent of the Mount of Olives, all the multitude of the disciples began to rejoice and praise God with a loud voice for all the mighty works which they had seen,
031938 saying, Blessed is the King coming in the name of the Lord! Peace in Heaven and glory in the highest!
031939 And some of the Pharisees from the crowd said to Him, Teacher, rebuke your disciples.
031940 And He answered and said to them, I tell you that if these should be silent, the stones would cry out.
031941 And as He drew near, He beheld the city and wept over it,
031942 saying, If you had known, even you, even at least in this day of yours, the things for your peace! But now they are hidden from your eyes.
031943 For the days will come on you that your enemies will raise up a rampart to you, and will surround you, and will keep you in on every side.
031944 And they will tear you down, and your children within you, and will not leave a stone on a stone because you did not know the time of your visitation.
031945 And entering into the temple, He began to cast out those selling and buying in it,
031946 saying to them, It is written, "My house is a house of prayer," but you have made it a den of thieves.
031947 And He taught in the temple daily. But the chief priests and the scribes and the chief of the people sought to destroy Him.
031948 And they could not find what they might do, for all the people were hanging on Him, listening.
032001 And on one of those days, as He taught the people in the temple and proclaimed the gospel, it happened that the chief priests and the scribes along with the elders came on Him .
032002 And they spoke to Him, saying, Tell us, by what authority do you do these things? Or who is he who gave you this authority?
032003 And He answered and said to them, I will also ask you one thing, and you answer me:
032004 The baptism of John, was it from Heaven or from men?
032005 And they reasoned within themselves, saying, If we shall say, From Heaven, he will say, Why then did you not believe him?
032006 But if we say, From men, then all the people will stone us, for they are persuaded that John was a prophet.
032007 And they answered that they could not tell from where it was .
032008 And Jesus said to them, Neither do I tell you by what authority I do these things.
032009 And He began to speak to the people this parable: A certain man planted a vineyard and let it out to vinedressers. And he went into a far country for a long time.
032010 And in season he sent a servant to the vinedressers, so that they should give him the fruit of the vineyard. But the vinedressers beat him and sent him away empty.
032011 And again he sent another servant. And they also beat him and treated him shamefully, and sent him away empty.
