032012 And again he sent a third. And they also wounded him and cast him out.
032013 And the lord of the vineyard said, What shall I do? I will send my beloved son. It may be that they will respect him when they see him.
032014 But when the vinedressers saw him, they reasoned among themselves, saying, This is the heir! Come, let us kill him so that the inheritance may be ours.
032015 So they threw him out of the vineyard and killed him . What then shall the lord of the vineyard do to them?
032016 He shall come and destroy these vinedressers and shall give the vineyard to others. And when they heard this, they said, Let it not be!
032017 And He looked at them and said, What then is this which is written, " The Stone which the builders rejected, the same has become the Head of the corner?
032018 Whoever shall fall on that Stone shall be broken, but on whomever it shall fall, it will grind him to powder."
032019 And the chief priests and the scribes sought to lay hands on Him the same hour. And they feared the people, for they perceived that He had spoken this parable against them.
032020 And they watched and sent forth spies, pretending themselves to be righteous men, so that they might seize upon a word of His, that they might deliver Him in this way to the power and authority of the governor.
032021 And they asked Him, saying, Teacher, we know that you say and teach rightly, and do not accept the person of anyone, but truly teach the way of God.
032022 Is it lawful for us to give tribute to Caesar or not?
032023 But He perceived their craftiness and said to them, Why do you tempt Me?
032024 Show Me a coin. Whose image and inscription does it have? They answered and said, Caesar's.
032025 And He said to them, Therefore render to Caesar the things which are Caesar's, and to God the things which are God's.
032026 And they could not take hold of His words before the people. And they marveled at His answer and were silent.
032027 And certain of the Sadducees came, those speaking against a resurrection, that it was not to be. And they asked Him,
032028 saying, Teacher, Moses wrote to us, If anyone's brother dies, having a wife, and if he dies without children, his brother should take his wife and raise up seed to his brother.
032029 Therefore there were seven brothers. And the first took a wife and died without children.
032030 And the second took her as a wife, and he died childless.
032031 And the third took her. And likewise the seven left no children and died.
032032 Last of all the woman also died.
032033 Therefore in the resurrection whose wife shall she be? For the seven had her as a wife.
032034 And answering, Jesus said to them, The sons of this world marry and are given in marriage,
032035 but they who shall be counted worthy to obtain that world, and the resurrection from the dead, neither marry nor are given in marriage.
032036 Nor can they die any more, for they are equal to the angels, and are the sons of God, being the sons of the resurrection.
032037 But that the dead are raised, even Moses pointed out at the Bush, when he called the Lord the God of Abraham, and the God of Isaac, and the God of Jacob.
032038 For He is not God of the dead, but of the living. For all live to Him.
032039 And answering, certain of the scribes said, Teacher, you have spoken well.
032040 And after that they did not dare ask Him anything.
032041 And He said to them, How do they say that Christ is the Son of David?
032042 Even David himself says in the Book of Psalms, "The LORD said to my Lord, Sit at My right hand
032043 until I place Your enemies as Your footstool."
032044 David then calls Him Lord; how then is He his son?
032045 And as all the people were listening, He said to the disciples,
032046 Beware of the scribes who desire to walk in long robes, and love greetings in the markets, and the first seats in the synagogues, and the chief places at the feasts;
032047 who devour widows' houses, and make long prayers for a show; the same shall receive a more severe condemnation.
032101 And looking up, He saw the rich men casting their gifts into the treasury.
032102 And He also saw a certain poor widow casting two lepta in there.
032103 And He said, Truly I say to you that this poor widow has cast in more than all of them.
032104 For all these have cast in to the offerings of God from their abundance, but out of her poverty she has cast in all the living she had.
032105 And as some spoke of the temple, how it was adorned with beautiful stones and gifts, He said,
032106 As to these things which you see, days will come in which there shall not be left a stone on a stone, which shall not be thrown down.
032107 And they asked Him, saying, Teacher, but when shall these things be? And what shall be the sign when these things are about to take place?
032108 And He said, Take heed that you are not deceived, for many shall come in My name, saying, I AM! Also, The time has come! Do not go after them.
032109 But when you hear of wars and disturbances, do not be terrified, for all these things must first occur, but the end is not at once.
032110 And He said to them, Nation shall rise against nation, and kingdom against kingdom.
032111 And great earthquakes shall be in different places, and famines and plagues. And there shall be terrors and great signs from Heaven.
032112 But before all these, they shall lay their hands on you and persecute you , delivering you up to the synagogues and prisons, being brought before kings and rulers for My name's sake.
032113 And it shall return to you for a testimony.
032114 Therefore settle it in your hearts not to meditate beforehand what you shall answer.
032115 For I will give you a mouth and wisdom which all your adversaries shall not be able to gainsay nor resist.
032116 And you shall be betrayed also by parents and brothers and kinsmen and friends. And they will cause some of you to be put to death.
032117 And you shall be hated by all for My name's sake.
032118 But there shall not a hair of your head perish.
032119 By your patience you will gain your souls.
032120 And when you see Jerusalem compassed with armies, then know that its destruction has come.
032121 And let those in Judea flee to the mountains. And those in its midst, let them go out. And those in the open spaces, let them not go into her.
032122 For these are the days of vengeance, that all things which are written may be fulfilled.
032123 But woe to those who are with child, and to those suckling in those days! For there shall be great distress in the land and wrath on this people.
032124 And they shall fall by the sword's edge. And shall be led away captive into all nations. And Jerusalem shall be trodden down by the nations until the times of the nations is fulfilled.
032125 And there shall be signs in the sun, and in the moon, and in the stars. And on the earth will be anxiety of nations with perplexity; the sea and the waves roaring;
032126 men fainting from fear, and expecting those things which have come on the earth. For the powers of the heavens shall be shaken.
032127 And then they shall see the Son of man coming in a cloud with power and great glory.
032128 And when these things begin to happen, then look up and lift up your heads, for your redemption draws near.
032129 And He spoke a parable to them: Behold the fig-tree and all the trees.
032130 Now when they sprout leaves, seeing it you will know that summer is now near.
032131 So also, when you see these things happening, know that the kingdom of God is near.
032132 Truly I say to you, This generation shall not pass away until all these things are fulfilled.
032133 The heaven and the earth shall pass away, but My words shall not pass away.
032134 And take heed to yourselves, lest your hearts are weighed down with headaches and drinking and anxieties of this life; and that day should suddenly come on you;
032135 for it shall come as a snare on all those sitting on the face of the whole earth.
032136 Watch therefore, praying in every season that you may be counted worthy to escape all these things which shall occur, and to stand before the Son of man.
032137 And in the days He was teaching in the temple. And in the nights He went out, and lodged in the mount called the Mount of Olives.
032138 And all the people came early in the morning to Him in the temple, in order to hear Him.
032201 And the Feast of Unleavened Bread, which is called the Passover, drew near.
032202 And the chief priests and scribes sought how they might kill Him, for they feared the people.
032203 And Satan entered into Judas, surnamed Iscariot, being of the number of the Twelve.
032204 And going, he talked with the chief priests and captains, how he might betray Him to them.
032205 And they were glad and they agreed to give him silver.
032206 And he fully consented, and he sought opportunity to betray Him to them, away from the crowd.
032207 And the day of the Unleavened Bread came, when the passover must be killed.
032208 And He sent Peter and John, saying, Go and prepare the passover for us, so that we may eat.
032209 And they said to Him. Where do You desire that we prepare?
032210 And He said to them, Behold, when you have entered into the city, you will meet a man bearing a pitcher of water. Follow him into the house where he enters.
032211 And you shall say to the master of the house, The Teacher says to you, Where is the guest room where I shall eat the passover with My disciples?
032212 And he shall show you a large, furnished upper room. Prepare there.
032213 And they went and found it as He had said to them. And they prepared the passover.
032214 And when the hour came, He and the twelve apostles with Him reclined.
032215 And He said to them, With desire I have desired to eat this passover with you before I suffer.
032216 For I say to you, I will not any more eat of it until it is fulfilled in the kingdom of God.
032217 And He took the cup and gave thanks and said, Take this and divide it among yourselves.
032218 For I say to you, I will not drink of the fruit of the vine until the kingdom of God shall come.
032219 And He took bread and gave thanks, and He broke it and gave it to them, saying, This is My body which is given for you, this do in remembrance of Me.
032220 In the same way He took the cup, after having dined, saying, This cup is the new covenant in My blood, which is being poured out for you.
032221 But, behold, the hand of My betrayer is with Me on the table.
032222 And truly the Son of man goes, as it has been determined, but woe to that man by whom He is betrayed!
032223 And they began to inquire among themselves which of them it was that should do this thing.
032224 And there was also a dispute among them as to which of them seems to be greater.
032225 And He said to them, The kings of the nations exercise lordship over them. And they who exercise authority on them are called benefactors.
032226 But you shall not be so: but the greater among you, let him be as the lesser, and he who governs, as one who serves.
032227 For which is the greater; he who reclines, or he who serves? Is it not he who reclines? But I am among you as He who serves.
032228 You are those who have continued with Me in My trials.
032229 And I appoint a kingdom to you, as My Father has appointed to Me,
032230 that you may eat and drink at My table in My kingdom, and sit on thrones judging the twelve tribes of Israel.
032231 And the Lord said, Simon, Simon, behold, Satan has desired you, that he may sift you as wheat.
032232 But I have prayed for you, that your faith fail not. And when you are converted, strengthen your brothers.
032233 And he said to Him, Lord, I am ready to go with You, both into prison and into death.
032234 And He said, I say to you, Peter, the cock shall not crow this day before you shall deny knowing Me three times.
032235 And He said to them, When I sent you without purse and wallet and sandals, did you lack anything? And they said, Nothing.
032236 And He said to them, But now, he who has a purse, let him take it , and likewise his wallet. And he who has no sword, let him sell his garment and buy one.
032237 For I say to you that this which is written must yet be accomplished in Me, "And he was reckoned among the transgressors"; for the things concerning Me have an end.
032238 And they said, Lord, behold, here are two swords. And He said to them, It is enough.
032239 And going out, according to His custom, He went to the Mount of Olives. And His disciples also followed Him.
032240 And when He was at the place, He said to them, Pray that you do not enter into temptation.
032241 And He was withdrawn from them about a stone's throw. And He kneeled down and prayed,
032242 saying, Father, if You are willing, remove this cup from Me. Yet not My will, but Yours be done.
032243 And an angel appeared to Him from Heaven, strengthening Him.
032244 And being in an agony He prayed more earnestly. And His sweat was as it were great drops of blood falling down to the ground.
032245 And when He rose up from prayer and had come to His disciples, He found them sleeping because of sorrow.
032246 And He said to them, Why do you sleep? Rise and pray lest you enter into temptation.
032247 And as He was yet speaking, behold a crowd! And he who was called Judas, one of the Twelve, went before them. And he drew near Jesus to kiss Him.
032248 But Jesus said to him, Judas, do you betray the Son of man with a kiss?
032249 And those around Him seeing what was about to occur, they said to him, Lord, shall we strike with the sword?
032250 And one of them struck the servant of the high priest and cut off his right ear.
032251 And Jesus answered and said, Let it go until now. And touching his ear, He healed him.
032252 And Jesus said to the chief priests and commanders of the temple, and the elders, who had come to Him, Have you come out as against a robber, with swords and staves?
032253 When I was with you in the temple daily, you did not stretch out your hand on Me. But this is your hour, and the authority of the darkness.
032254 And laying hold on Him, they led Him away and brought Him into the high priest's house. And Peter followed afar off.
032255 And lighting a fire in the middle of the court, and they sitting down, Peter sat in their midst.
032256 But a certain slave-girl saw him as he sat by the fire and earnestly looked on him and said, This man was with him also.
032257 And he denied Him, saying, Woman, I do not know Him.
032258 And after a little while another saw him and said, You also are of them. And Peter said, Man, I am not!
032259 And about an hour afterward, another confidently affirmed, saying, Truly this one was also with him, for he is a Galilean.
032260 And Peter said, Man, I do not know what you say. And immediately, while he still spoke, the cock crowed.
032261 And the Lord turned and looked on Peter. And Peter remembered the word of the Lord, how He had said to him, Before the cock crows, you shall deny Me three times.
032262 And Peter went out and wept bitterly.
032263 And the men who held Jesus mocked Him, beating Him .
032264 And blindfolding Him, they struck Him on His face. And they asked Him, saying, Prophesy! Who is it who struck you?
032265 And they spoke many other things blasphemously against Him.
032266 And when day came, the body of elders of the people, and the chief priests and the scribes, came together. And they led Him to the sanhedrin, saying,
032267 Are you the Christ? Tell us. And He said to them, If I tell you, you will not believe.
032268 Also if I ask you , you will not answer Me nor let Me go.
032269 From now on the Son of man shall sit at the right hand of the power of God.
032270 And they all said, Are you then the Son of God? And He said to them, You say it , because I AM!
032271 And they said, What need do we have for any witness? For we ourselves have heard it from his own mouth.
032301 And rising up, all the multitude of them led Him before Pilate.
032302 And they began to accuse Him, saying, We have found this one perverting the nation and forbidding them to give tribute to Caesar, saying himself to be a king, Christ.
032303 And Pilate asked Him, saying, Are you the king of the Jews? And He answered him and said, You say it .
032304 And Pilate said to the chief priests and to the people, I find no fault in this man.
032305 And they were the more fierce, saying, He stirs up the people, teaching throughout all Judea, beginning from Galilee to this place.
032306 And hearing Galilee, Pilate asked if the man is a Galilean.
032307 And knowing that He belonged to Herod's jurisdiction, he sent Him to Herod, who himself was also at Jerusalem at that time.
032308 And seeing Jesus, Herod greatly rejoiced, for he had desired to see Him for a long time , because he had heard many things about Him. And he hoped to see some miracle done by Him.
032309 And he questioned Him in many words, but He answered him nothing.
032310 And the chief priests and scribes stood and vehemently accused Him.
032311 And humiliating Him with his guardsmen, and mocking Him by putting luxurious clothing around Him, Herod sent Him again to Pilate.
032312 And that same day Pilate and Herod became friends with one another, for before they were at enmity between themselves.
032313 And when he had called together the chief priests and the rulers and the people,
032314 Pilate said to them, You have brought this Man to me as perverting the people. And behold, having examined Him before you, I have found no fault in this Man regarding those things of which you accuse Him;
032315 no, nor even Herod, for I sent you to him, and lo, nothing worthy of death has been done by Him.
032316 Therefore I will chastise Him and release Him .
032317 (For it was necessary for him to release one to them at the feast.)
032318 And they all cried out at once, saying, Away with this One! And release to us Barabbas
032319 (who was thrown into prison because of a certain sedition made in the city, and for murder).
032320 And Pilate, willing to release Jesus, spoke again to them.
032321 But they cried, saying, Crucify! Crucify Him!
032322 And he said to them the third time , Why? What evil has He done? I have found no cause of death in Him, therefore I will chastise Him and let Him go.
032323 But they pressed on him , with loud voices, requesting that He might be crucified. And their voices and those of the chief priests prevailed.
032324 And Pilate gave judgment that their request should be granted.
032325 And he released to them the one who had been thrown into prison for sedition and murder, for whom they had asked. But he delivered up Jesus to their will.
032326 And as they led Him away, they laid hold on one Simon, a Cyrenian, coming out of the country. And they laid the cross on him, that he might carry it after Jesus.
032327 And a great multitude of people were following Him, and of women who also were bewailing and lamenting Him.
032328 But turning to them, Jesus said, Daughters of Jerusalem, do not weep for Me, but weep for yourselves and for your children.
032329 For behold, the days are coming in which they shall say, Blessed are the barren, and the wombs that never bore, and the breasts which did not suckle.
032330 And they shall begin to say to the mountains, Fall on us! And to the hills, Cover us!
032331 For if they do these things in a green tree, what shall be done in the dry?
032332 And two others, two criminals, were led with Him to be put to death.
032333 And when they came to the place which is called Calvary, they crucified Him and the criminals there, one on the right, and one on the left.
032334 And Jesus said, Father, forgive them, for they do not know what they do. And parting His clothing, they cast lots.
032335 And the people stood watching. And also the rulers with them, scoffing, saying, He saved others, let Him save Himself, if He is the Christ, the chosen of God.
032336 And coming near, the soldiers also mocked Him, and offering Him sour wine,
032337 and saying, If You are the king of the Jews, save Yourself.
032338 And an inscription also was written over Him in letters of Greek and Latin and Hebrew, THIS IS THE KING OF THE JEWS.
032339 And one of the hanged criminals blasphemed Him, saying, If you are Christ, save Yourself and us.
032340 But answering, the other rebuked him, saying, Do you not fear God, since you are in the same condemnation.
032341 And we indeed justly so, for we receive the due reward of our deeds, but this Man has done nothing amiss.
032342 And he said to Jesus, Lord, remember me when You come into Your kingdom.
032343 And Jesus said to him, Truly I say to you, Today you shall be with Me in Paradise.
032344 And it was about the sixth hour, and there was a darkness over all the earth until the ninth hour.
032345 And the sun was darkened, and the veil of the temple was torn in the middle.
032346 And crying with a loud voice, Jesus said, Father, into Your hands I commit My spirit. And when He had said this, He breathed out the spirit.
032347 And when the centurion saw what had been done, he glorified God, saying, Truly this Man was righteous.
032348 And all the crowd arriving together at this sight, beholding the things happening, struck their breasts and returned.
032349 And all those known to Him stood at a distance; and the women, those accompanying Him from Galilee, were seeing these things.
032350 And behold, a man named Joseph, a councillor, a good man and a just one,
032351 this one was not assenting to their counsel and deed. He was from Arimathea, a city of the Jews; and he also himself waited for the kingdom of God.
032352 This man went to Pilate and begged the body of Jesus.
032353 And he took it down and wrapped it in linen. And he laid it in a tomb that had been cut in the stone, in which no man had before been laid.
032354 And that day was the Preparation, and the sabbath drew on.
032355 And also women were following, who were accompanying Him out of Galilee, who watched the tomb, and how His body was placed.
032356 And they returned and they prepared spices and ointment. And they rested on the sabbath day according to the commandment.
032401 And on the first of the sabbaths, while still very early, they came to the tomb bringing the spices which they had prepared, and certain others with them.
032402 But they found the stone rolled away from the tomb.
032403 And going in, they did not find the body of the Lord Jesus.
032404 And as they were much perplexed about it, it happened that, behold, two men stood by them in shining garments.
032405 And as they were afraid, and bowed their faces down to the earth, they said to them, Why do you seek the living among the dead?
032406 He is not here, but has risen. Remember how He spoke to you when He was still in Galilee,
032407 saying, The Son of man must be delivered into the hands of sinful men and be crucified, and the third day rise again?
032408 And they remembered His words
032409 and returned from the tomb and told all these things to the Eleven and to the rest.
032410 It was Mary Magdalene, and Joanna, and Mary the mother of James, and the rest with them, who told these things to the apostles.
032411 And their words seemed to them like foolishness, and they did not believe them.
032412 And Peter arose and ran to the tomb, and stooping down he saw the linens lying alone. And he went away wondering to himself at what had happened.
032413 And behold, two of them went that same day to a village called Emmaus, it being about sixty stadia from Jerusalem.
032414 And they talked to each other of all these things which had happened.
032415 And while they talked and reasoned, it happened that Jesus Himself drew near and went with them.
032416 But their eyes were held so that they could not know Him.
032417 And He said to them, What words are these that you have with one another as you walk, and are so sad?
032418 And one of them, whose name was Cleopas, answered and said to Him, Are you only a stranger in Jerusalem and have not known the things which have occurred there in these days?
032419 And He said to them, What things? And they said to Him, The things concerning Jesus of Nazareth, who was a man, a prophet mighty in deed and word before God and all the people,
032420 and how the chief priests and our rulers delivered Him to the judgment of death, and have crucified Him.
032421 But we had trusted that He was the One who was about to redeem Israel. And besides all this, today is the third day since these things were done.
032422 Yes, and also some of our women astounded us, having been early at the tomb;
032423 and when they did not find His body, they came saying that they had also seen a vision of angels, who said that He was alive.
032424 And some of those with us went to the tomb and found it even as the women had said. But they did not see Him.
032425 And He said to them, O fools and slow of heart to believe all things that the prophets spoke!
032426 Was it not necessary for the Christ to suffer these things and to enter into His glory?
032427 And beginning at Moses and all the prophets, He expounded to them in all the Scriptures the things concerning Himself.
032428 And they drew near the village where they were going. And He appeared to be going further.
032429 But they constrained Him, saying, Stay with us, for it is toward evening and the day is far spent. And He went in to stay with them.
032430 And it happened as He reclined with them, taking the loaf, He blessed it , and breaking it, He gave to them.
032431 And their eyes were opened, and they knew Him. And He became invisible to them.
032432 And they said to one another, Did not our heart burn within us while He talked with us by the way and while He opened the Scriptures to us?
032433 And they rose up the same hour and returned to Jerusalem and found assembled the Eleven and those with them.
032434 And they said, the Lord has indeed risen, and has appeared to Simon.
032435 And in the way they related the things happening, and how He had been known by them in breaking of the loaf.
032436 And as they spoke this, Jesus Himself stood in their midst, and said to them, Peace to you!
032437 But they were terrified and filled with fear, for they thought they saw a spirit.
032438 And He said to them, Why are you troubled, and why do thoughts arise in your hearts?
032439 Behold My hands and My feet, that I am He! Handle Me and see, for a spirit does not have flesh and bones as you see Me have.
032440 And when He had spoken this, He showed them His hands and feet.
032441 And while they still did not believe for joy, and wondered, He said to them, Have you any food here?
032442 And they handed to Him a piece of a broiled fish and of a honeycomb.
032443 And He took it and ate before them.
032444 And He said to them, These are the words which I spoke to you while I was still with you, that all things must be fulfilled which were written in the law of Moses and in the Prophets and in the Psalms about Me.
032445 And He opened their mind to understand the Scriptures.
032446 And He said to them, So it is written, and so it behoved Christ to suffer and to rise from the dead the third day,
032447 and that repentance and remission of sins should be proclaimed in His name among all nations, beginning at Jerusalem.
032448 And you are witnesses of these things.
032449 And behold, I send the promise of My father on you. But you sit in the city of Jerusalem until you are clothed with power from on high.
032450 And He led them out as far as Bethany. And lifting up His hands, He blessed them.
032451 And it happened as He blessed them, He withdrew from them and was carried up into Heaven.
032452 And worshiping Him, they returned to Jerusalem with great joy.
032453 And they were continually in the temple, praising and blessing God. Amen.
040101 In the beginning was the Word, and the Word was with God, and the Word was God.
040102 He was in the beginning with God.
040103 All things came into being through Him, and without Him not even one thing came into being that has come into being.
040104 In Him was life, and the life was the light of men.
040105 And the light shines in the darkness, and the darkness did not overtake it.
040106 There was a man sent from God; his name was John.
040107 This one came as a witness, to bear witness concerning the Light, so that all might believe through him.
040108 He was not that Light, but was sent to bear witness of that Light.
040109 He was the true Light; He enlightens every man coming into the world.
040110 He was in the world, and the world came into being through Him, and the world did not know Him.
040111 He came to His own, and His own received Him not.
040112 But as many as received Him, He gave to them authority to become the children of God, to those who believe on His name,
040113 who were born, not of bloods, nor of the will of the flesh, nor of the will of man, but were born of God.
040114 And the Word became flesh, and tabernacled among us. And we beheld His glory, the glory as of the only begotten of the Father, full of grace and of truth.
040115 John bore witness of Him and cried out, saying, This was He of whom I spoke: He who comes after me has been before me, for He was preceding me.
040116 And out of His fullness we all have received, and grace for grace.
040117 For the law came through Moses, but grace and truth came through Jesus Christ.
040118 No one has seen God at any time; the Only-begotten Son, who is in the bosom of the Father, He has declared Him .
040119 And this is the witness of John, when the Jews sent priests and Levites from Jerusalem to ask him, Who are you?
040120 And he confessed and did not deny, but confessed, I am not the Christ.
040121 And they asked him, What then? Are you Elijah? And he says, I am not. Are you that prophet? And he answered, No.
040122 Then they said to him, Who are you so that we may give an answer to those who sent us? What do you say of yourself?
040123 He said, I am "the voice of one crying in the wilderness: Make straight the way of the Lord," as the prophet Isaiah said.
040124 And they who were sent were from the Pharisees.
040125 And they asked him and said, Why then do you baptize, if you are not the Christ, nor Elijah, nor that Prophet?
040126 John answered them, saying, I baptize with water, but One stands among you whom you do not know.
040127 He it is who, coming after me, who has been before me; of whom I am not worthy to loosen the thong of His sandal.
040128 These things were done in Bethabara beyond Jordan, where John was baptizing.
040129 The next day John sees Jesus coming to him and says, Behold the Lamb of God who takes away the sin of the world!
040130 This is He of whom I said, After me comes a Man who has been before me, for He preceded me.
040131 And I did not know Him, but that He be revealed to Israel, therefore I have come baptizing with water.
040132 And John bore record, saying, I saw the Spirit descending from Heaven like a dove, and He abode on Him.
040133 And I did not know Him, but He who sent me to baptize with water, that One said to me, Upon whom you shall see the Spirit descending, and remaining upon Him, He is the One who baptizes with the Holy Spirit.
040134 And I saw and bore record that this is the Son of God.
040135 Again, the next day afterward, John stood with two of his disciples.
040136 And looking upon Jesus as He walked, he says, Behold the Lamb of God!
040137 And the two disciples heard him speak, and they followed Jesus.
040138 Then Jesus turned and saw them following and said to them, What do you seek? They said to Him, Rabbi (which is called, being translated, Teacher), where do you live?
040139 He says to them, Come and see. They came and saw where He lived, and stayed with Him that day, for it was about the tenth hour.
040140 One of the two who heard John and followed Him was Andrew, Simon Peter's brother.
040141 He first found his own brother Simon and said to him, We have found the Messiah (which is, being translated, the Christ).
040142 And he brought him to Jesus. And when Jesus saw him, He said, You are Simon the son of Jonah; you shall be called Cephas (which translated is, A stone).
040143 The day after, Jesus desired to go forth into Galilee. And He found Philip and said to him, Follow Me.
040144 Now Philip was of Bethsaida, the city of Andrew and Peter.
040145 Philip found Nathanael and said to him, We have found Him of whom Moses wrote in the law and the prophets, Jesus of Nazareth, the son of Joseph.
040146 And Nathanael said to him, Can there be any good thing come out of Nazareth? Philip said to him, Come and see.
040147 Jesus saw Nathanael coming to Him and said of him, Behold an Israelite indeed in whom is no guile!
040148 Nathanael said to Him, From where do You know me? Jesus answered and said to him, Before Philip called you, when you were under the fig tree, I saw you.
040149 Nathanael answered and said to Him, Rabbi, You are the Son of God. You are the King of Israel!
040150 Jesus answered and said to him, Because I said to you, I saw you under the fig tree, do you believe? You shall see greater things than these.
040151 And He said to him, Truly, truly, I say to you, Hereafter you shall see Heaven open, and the angels of God ascending and descending upon the Son of man.
040201 And the third day there was a marriage in Cana of Galilee. And the mother of Jesus was there.
040202 And Jesus and His disciples were both invited to the marriage.
040203 And when they lacked wine, the mother of Jesus said to Him, They have no wine.
040204 Jesus said to her, Woman, what do I have to do with you? My hour has not yet come.
040205 His mother said to the servants, Whatever He says to you, do it .
040206 And there were six stone waterpots there, according to the purification of the Jews, each containing two or three measures.
040207 Jesus said to them, Fill the waterpots with water. And they filled them up to the brim.
040208 And He said to them, Now draw out and carry it to the master of the feast. And they carried it .
040209 When the ruler of the feast had tasted the water which was made wine (and did not know where it was from, but the servants who drew the water knew), the master of the feast called the bridegroom.
040210 And he said to him, Every man at the beginning sets forth good wine, and when men have drunk well, then that which is worse. You have kept the good wine until now.
040211 This beginning of miracles Jesus did in Cana of Galilee. And it revealed His glory. And His disciples believed on Him.
040212 After this He went down to Capernaum, He and His mother and His brothers and His disciples. And they did not stay there many days.
040213 And the Passover of the Jews was near, and Jesus went up to Jerusalem.
040214 And He found in the temple those who sold oxen and sheep and doves, and the money-changers sitting.
040215 And when He had made a scourge of small cords, He drove them all out of the temple, also the sheep and the oxen. And He poured out the money-changers' money and overthrew the tables.
040216 And He said to those who sold doves, Take these things away from here. Do not make My Father's house a house of merchandise.
040217 And His disciples remembered that it was written, "The zeal of Your house has eaten Me up."
040218 Then the Jews answered and said to Him, What sign do you show us, since you do these things?
040219 Jesus answered and said to them, Destroy this temple and in three days I will raise it up.
040220 Then the Jews said, This temple was forty-six years building, and will you rear it up in three days?
040221 But He spoke of the temple of His body.
040222 Therefore when He had risen from the dead, His disciples remembered that He had said this to them, and they believed the Scripture and the word which Jesus had said.
040223 And as He was in Jerusalem at the Passover, at the feast, many believed in His name when they saw the miracles which He did.
040224 But Jesus did not commit Himself to them, because He knew all
040225 and did not need that anyone should testify of man. For He knew what was in man.
040301 And there was a man of the Pharisees named Nicodemus, a ruler of the Jews.
040302 He came to Jesus by night and said to Him, Rabbi, we know that you are a teacher come from God; for no man can do these miracles which you do unless God is with him.
040303 Jesus answered and said to him, Truly, truly, I say to you, Unless a man is born again, he cannot see the kingdom of God.
040304 Nicodemus said to Him, How can a man be born when he is old? Can he enter the second time into his mother's womb and be born?
040305 Jesus answered, Truly, truly, I say to you, Unless a man is born of water and the Spirit, he cannot enter into the kingdom of God.
040306 That which is born of the flesh is flesh, and that which is born of the Spirit is spirit.
040307 Do not marvel that I said to you, You must be born again.
040308 The Spirit breathes where He desires, and you hear His voice, but you do not know from where He comes, and where He goes; so is everyone who is born of the Spirit.
040309 Nicodemus answered and said to Him, How can these things be?
040310 Jesus answered and said to him, Are you the teacher of Israel and do not know these things?
040311 Truly, truly, I say to you, We speak what we know and testify what we have seen. And you do not receive our witness.
040312 If I have told you earthly things and you do not believe, how shall you believe if I tell you heavenly things?
040313 And no one has ascended up to Heaven except He who came down from Heaven, the Son of man who is in Heaven.
040314 But even as Moses lifted up the serpent in the wilderness, even so must the Son of man be lifted up,
040315 so that whosoever believes in Him should not perish, but have everlasting life.
040316 For God so loved the world that He gave His only-begotten Son, that whoever believes in Him should not perish but have everlasting life.
040317 For God did not send His Son into the world to condemn the world, but so that the world might be saved through Him.
040318 He who believes on Him is not condemned, but he who does not believe is condemned already, because he has not believed in the name of the only-begotten Son of God.
040319 And this is the condemnation, that the Light has come into the world, and men loved darkness rather than the Light, because their deeds were evil.
040320 For everyone who does evil hates the Light, and does not come to the Light, lest his deeds should be exposed.
040321 But he who practices truth comes to the Light so that his works may be revealed, that they exist, having been worked in God.
040322 After these things Jesus and His disciples came into the land of Judea. And He stayed there with them and baptized.
040323 And John was also baptizing in Enon near Salim, because there was much water there. And they came and were baptized.
040324 For John had not yet been cast into prison.
040325 Then a question from John's disciples arose with the Jews about purification.
040326 And they came to John and said to him, Rabbi, He who was with you beyond Jordan, to whom you bore witness, behold, He baptizes, and all come to Him!
040327 And John answered and said, A man can receive nothing unless it is given to him from Heaven.
040328 You yourselves bear witness to me that I said, I am not the Christ, but that I am sent before Him.
040329 He who has the bride is the bridegroom, but the friend of the bridegroom who stands and hears him rejoices greatly because of the bridegroom's voice. Then my joy is fulfilled.
040330 He must increase, but I must decrease.
040331 He who comes from above is above all; he who is from the earth is earthly and speaks from the earth. He who comes from Heaven is above all,
040332 and what He has seen and heard, that He testifies, and no one receives His testimony.
040333 He who has received His testimony has set his seal to this, that God is true.
040334 For He whom God has sent speaks the words of God, for God does not give the Spirit by measure.
040335 The Father loves the Son and has given all things into His hand.
040336 He who believes on the Son has everlasting life, and he who does not believe the Son shall not see life, but the wrath of God abides upon him.
040401 Therefore when the Lord knew how the Pharisees had heard that Jesus made and baptized more disciples than John
040402 (though Jesus Himself did not baptize, but His disciples),
040403 He left Judea and went away again into Galilee.
040404 And it was necessary for Him to go through Samaria,
040405 Then He came to a city of Samaria, called Sychar, near the parcel of ground that Jacob gave to his son Joseph.
040406 And Jacob's well was there. Jesus, therefore, being wearied with His journey, sat thus upon the well. It was about the sixth hour.
040407 A woman of Samaria came to draw water. Jesus said to her, Give me to drink.
040408 (For His disciples had gone away into the city to buy food.)
040409 Then the woman of Samaria said to Him, How do you, being a Jew, ask a drink of me, who am a woman of Samaria? For the Jews do not associate with Samaritans.
040410 Jesus answered and said to her, If you knew the gift of God, and who it is that says to you, Give Me to drink, you would have asked of Him, and He would have given you living water.
040411 The woman said to Him, Sir, you have no vessel, and the well is deep. From where then do you have that living water?
040412 Are you greater than our father Jacob, who gave us the well, and drank of it himself, and his children and his cattle?
040413 Jesus answered and said to her, Whoever drinks of this water shall thirst again,
040414 but whoever drinks of the water that I shall give him shall never thirst, but the water that I shall give him shall be in him a well of water springing up into everlasting life.
040415 The woman said to Him, Sir, give me this water, so that I may not thirst nor come here to draw.
040416 Jesus said to her, Go, call your husband and come here.
040417 The woman answered and said, I have no husband. Jesus said to her, You have well said, I have no husband
040418 for you have had five husbands, and he whom you now have is not your husband. In that you spoke truly.
040419 The woman said to Him, Sir, I perceive that you are a prophet.
040420 Our fathers worshiped in this mountain, and you say that in Jerusalem is the place where men ought to worship.
040421 Jesus said to her, Woman, believe Me, the hour is coming when you shall neither worship the Father in this mountain nor yet at Jerusalem.
040422 You worship what you do not know, we know what we worship, for salvation is of the Jews.
040423 But the hour is coming, and now is, when the true worshipers shall worship the Father in spirit and truth, for the Father seeks such to worship Him.
040424 God is a spirit, and they who worship Him must worship in spirit and in truth.
040425 The woman said to Him, I know that Messiah is coming, who is called Christ. When He has come, He will tell us all things.
040426 Jesus said to her, I AM, the One speaking to you.
040427 And upon this His disciples came and marveled that He talked with the woman. However, no one said, What do You seek, or why do You talk with her?
040428 The woman then left her waterpot and went into the city and said to the men,
040429 Come see a man who told me all things that I ever did. Is this One not the Christ?
040430 And they went out of the city and came to Him.
040431 In the meantime His disciples were asking Him, saying, Master, eat.
040432 But He said to them, I have food to eat which you do not know.
040433 Therefore the disciples said to one another, No one brought Him anything to eat?
040434 Jesus said to them, My food is to do the will of Him who sent Me and to finish His work.
040435 Do you not say, It is yet four months, and the harvest comes? Behold, I say to you, Lift up your eyes and look on the fields, for they are white to harvest already.
040436 And he who reaps receives wages and gathers fruit to life eternal, so that both he who sows and he who reaps may rejoice together.
040437 And in this is the saying true, One sows and another reaps.
040438 I sent you to reap that on which you bestowed no labor. Other men labored, and you have entered into their labor.
040439 And many of the Samaritans of that city believed upon Him because of the saying of the woman, who testified, He told me all that I ever did.
040440 Then as the Samaritans had come to Him, they begged Him that He would stay with them. And He stayed there two days.
040441 And many more believed because of His own word.
040442 And they said to the woman, Now we believe, not because of your saying, for we have heard Him ourselves and know that this is truly the Christ, the Savior of the world.
040443 And after two days He departed from there and went into Galilee.
040444 For Jesus Himself testified that a prophet has no honor in his own native-place.
040445 Then when He had come into Galilee, the Galileans received Him, having seen all the things that He did at Jerusalem at the feast; for they also went to the feast.
040446 Then Jesus came again to Cana of Galilee, where He made the water wine. And there was a certain nobleman whose son was sick at Capernaum.
040447 When He heard that Jesus had come out of Judea into Galilee, he went to Him and begged Him that He would come down and heal his son, for he was at the point of death.
040448 Then Jesus said to him, Unless you see signs and wonders you will not believe.
040449 The nobleman said to Him, Sir, come down before my child dies.
040450 Jesus said to him, Go, your son lives. And the man believed the word that Jesus had spoken to him, and he went away.
040451 And as he was now going down, his servants met him and told him , saying, Your son lives.
040452 Then he asked of them the hour when he began to get better. And they said to him, Yesterday at the seventh hour the fever left him.
040453 So the father knew that it was at the same hour in which Jesus said to him, Your son lives. And he himself believed, and his whole house.
040454 This is the second miracle Jesus did, when He had come out of Judea into Galilee.
040501 After this there was a feast of the Jews, and Jesus went up to Jerusalem.
040502 Now there is a pool at the Sheep Gate at Jerusalem, which is called in Hebrew Bethesda, having five porches.
040503 In these lay a great multitude of those who were sick, of blind, lame, withered, waiting for the moving of the water.
040504 For an angel went down at a certain time into the pool and troubled the water. Then whoever first stepped in after the troubling of the water was made whole of whatever disease he had.
040505 And a certain man was there, who had an infirmity thirty-eight years.
040506 When Jesus saw him lying, and knowing that he had spent much time, He said to him, Do you desire to be made whole?
040507 The infirm man answered Him, Sir, when the water is troubled, I have no one to put me into the pool. But while I am coming, another steps down before me.
040508 Jesus says to him, Rise, take up your bed and walk.
040509 And immediately the man was made whole and took up his bed and walked. And it was a sabbath on that day.
040510 Therefore the Jews said to him who had been healed, It is the sabbath. It is not lawful for you to take up the bed.
040511 He answered them, He who made me whole said to me, Take up your bed and walk.
040512 Then they asked him, Who is the man who said to you, Take up your bed and walk?
040513 And he did not know Him who had cured him, for Jesus had moved away, a crowd being in the place.
040514 Afterward Jesus found him in the temple and said to him, Behold, you are made whole. Sin no more lest a worse thing come to you.
040515 The man departed and told the Jews that it was Jesus who had made him whole.
040516 And therefore the Jews persecuted Jesus and sought to kill Him, because He had done these things on the sabbath day.
040517 But Jesus answered them, My Father works until now, and I work.
040518 Then, because of this, the Jews sought the more to kill Him, because He not only had broken the sabbath, but also said that God was His father, making Himself equal with God.
040519 Then Jesus answered and said to them, Truly, truly, I say to you, the Son can do nothing of Himself but what He sees the Father do. For whatever things He does, these also the Son does likewise.
040520 For the Father loves the Son and shows Him all the things that He Himself does. And He will show Him greater works than these, so that you may marvel.
040521 For as the Father raises the dead and makes alive, even so the Son of man makes alive whomever He wills.
040522 For the Father judges no man, but has committed all judgment to the Son,
040523 so that all should honor the Son, even as they honor the Father. He who does not honor the Son does not honor the Father who sent Him.
040524 Truly, truly, I say to you, he who hears My word and believes on Him who sent Me has everlasting life and shall not come into condemnation, but has passed from death to life.
040525 Truly, truly, I say to you, the hour is coming and now is, when the dead shall hear the voice of the Son of God, and they who hear shall live.
040526 For as the Father has life in Himself, so He has given to the Son to have life within Himself,
040527 and has given Him authority to execute judgment also, because He is the Son of man.
040528 Do not marvel at this, for the hour is coming in which all who are in the graves shall hear His voice,
040529 and shall come forth, those who have done good to the resurrection of life, and those who have practiced evil to the resurrection of condemnation.
040530 I can do nothing of My own self. As I hear, I judge, and My judgment is just, because I do not seek My own will, but the will of the Father who has sent Me.
040531 If I bear witness of Myself, My witness is not true.
040532 There is another who bears witness of Me, and I know that the witness which He witnesses of Me is true.
040533 You sent to John, and he bore witness to the truth.
040534 But I do not receive testimony from man, but these things I say so that you might be saved.
040535 He was a burning and shining light, and you were willing for a time to rejoice in his light.
040536 But I have greater witness than that of John, for the works which the Father has given Me that I should finish them, the works which I do themselves witness of Me, that the Father has sent Me.
040537 And He sending Me, the Father Himself, has borne witness of Me. Neither have you heard His voice at any time nor seen His shape.
040538 And you do not have His Word abiding in you, for you do not believe Him whom He has sent.
040539 You search the Scriptures, for in them you think you have eternal life. And they are the ones witnessing of Me,
040540 and you will not come to Me that you might have life.
040541 I do not receive honor from men.
040542 But I know you, that you do not have the love of God in you.
040543 I have come in My Father's name, and you do not receive Me. If another shall come in his own name, him you will receive.
040544 How can you believe, you who receive honor from one another and do not seek the honor that comes from God only?
040545 Do not think that I will accuse you to the Father; there is one who accuses you, Moses, in whom you trust.
040546 For if you had believed Moses, you would have believed Me, for he wrote of Me.
040547 But if you do not believe his writings, how shall you believe My words?
040601 After these things Jesus went over the Sea of Galilee, the Sea of Tiberias.
040602 And a great multitude followed Him, because they saw His miracles which He did on the sick ones.
040603 And Jesus went up into a mountain and sat there with His disciples.
040604 And the Passover was near, a feast of the Jews.
040605 Then Jesus lifted up His eyes and saw a great crowd come to Him. He said to Philip, Where shall we buy loaves so that these may eat?
040606 And He said this to test him, for He Himself knew what He would do.
040607 Philip answered Him, Loaves for two hundred denarii are not enough for them, that every one may take a little.
040608 One of His disciples, Andrew, Simon Peter's brother, said to Him,
040609 There is a boy here who has five barley loaves and two small fish, but what are these among so many?
040610 And Jesus said, Make the men recline. And there was much grass in the place. So the men reclined, about five thousand in number.
040611 And Jesus took the loaves, and when He had given thanks, He distributed to the disciples, and the disciples to those who had reclined; and likewise of the fish, as much as they wanted.
040612 And when they were filled, He said to His disciples, Gather up the fragments left over, so that nothing is lost.
040613 Therefore they gathered and filled twelve handbaskets with fragments of the five barley loaves which were left over to those who had eaten.
040614 Then seeing the miracle that Jesus did, those men said, This is truly the Prophet, the One coming into the world.
040615 Therefore when Jesus perceived that they would come and take Him by force, that they might make Him a king, Jesus withdrew again to the mountain alone by Himself.
040616 And when evening had come, the disciples went down to the sea
040617 and entered into a boat, and went over the sea toward Capernaum. And it was now dark, and Jesus had not come to them.
040618 And the sea rose up because of a great wind that blew.
040619 Then having rowed about twenty-five or thirty furlongs, they saw Jesus walking on the sea and drawing near the ship. And they were afraid.
040620 But He said to them, I AM! Do not be afraid.
040621 Then they willingly received Him into the boat. And immediately the boat was at the land where they were going.
040622 The following day, the crowd standing on the other side of the sea had seen that there was no other little boat there except that one into which His disciples had entered, and when they saw that Jesus did not go with His disciples into the little boat, but that His disciples had gone away alone,
040623 (however, other boats from Tiberias came near the place where they ate the loaves, the Lord having given thanks),
040624 therefore, when the crowd saw that Jesus was not there, nor His disciples, they themselves also entered into the boats and came to Capernaum seeking Jesus.
040625 And when they had found Him on the other side of the sea, they said to Him, Rabbi, when did you come here?
040626 Jesus answered them and said, Truly, truly, I say to you, You seek Me not because you saw the miracles, but because you ate the loaves and were filled.
040627 Do not labor for the food that perishes, but for that food which endures to everlasting life, which the Son of man will give you. For God the Father sealed Him.
040628 Then they said to Him, What shall we do that we might work the works of God?
040629 Jesus answered and said to them, This is the work of God, that you believe on Him whom He has sent.
040630 Therefore they said to Him, What sign do you show then, so that we may see and believe you? What do you work?
040631 Our fathers ate the manna in the desert, as it is written, "He gave them bread from Heaven to eat."
040632 Then Jesus said to them, Truly, truly, I say to you, Moses did not give you that bread from Heaven, but My Father gives you the true bread from Heaven.
040633 For the bread of God is He who comes down from Heaven and gives life to the world.
040634 Then they said to him, Lord, evermore give us this bread.
040635 And Jesus said to them, I am the bread of life. He who comes to Me shall never hunger, and he who believes on Me shall never thirst.
040636 But I said to you that you also have seen Me and do not believe.
040637 All that the Father gives Me shall come to Me, and the one who comes to Me I will in no way cast out.
040638 For I came down from Heaven, not to do My own will but the will of Him who sent Me.
040639 And this is the will of the Father who sent Me, that of all which He has given Me I should lose nothing but should raise it up again at the last day.
040640 And this is the will of Him who sent Me, that everyone who sees the Son and believes on Him should have everlasting life. And I will raise him up at the last day.
040641 Then the Jews murmured about Him, because He said, I am the bread which came down from Heaven.
040642 And they said, Is this not Jesus the son of Joseph, whose father and mother we know? How now does this One say, I have come down from Heaven?
040643 Jesus therefore answered and said to them, Do not murmur with one another.
040644 No one can come to Me unless the Father who has sent Me draw him, and I will raise him up at the last day.
040645 It is written in the prophets, "And they shall all be taught of God." Therefore everyone who hears and learns from the Father comes to Me.
040646 Not that anyone has seen the Father, except He who is from God, He has seen the Father.
040647 Truly, truly, I say to you, he who believes on Me has everlasting life.
040648 I am the Bread of life.
040649 Your fathers ate the manna in the wilderness, and died.
040650 This is the Bread which comes down from Heaven, so that a man may eat of it and not die.
040651 I am the Living Bread which came down from Heaven. If anyone eats of this Bread, he shall live forever. And truly the bread that I will give is My flesh, which I will give for the life of the world.
040652 Then the Jews argued with one another, saying, How can this man give us his flesh to eat?
040653 Then Jesus says to them, Truly, truly, I say to you, unless you eat the flesh of the Son of man, and drink His blood, you do not have life in yourselves.
040654 Whoever partakes of My flesh and drinks My blood has eternal life, and I will raise him up at the last day.
040655 For My flesh is food indeed, and My blood is drink indeed.
040656 He who partakes of My flesh and drinks My blood dwells in Me, and I in him.
040657 As the living Father has sent Me, and I live through the Father, so he who partakes of Me, even he shall live by Me.
040658 This is the Bread which came down from Heaven, not as your fathers ate the manna, and died; he who partakes of this Bread shall live forever.
040659 He said these things in the synagogue as He taught in Capernaum.
040660 Then when they had heard, many of His disciples said, This is a hard saying, who can hear it?
040661 But knowing in Himself that His disciples murmured about it, Jesus said to them, Does this offend you?
040662 Then what if you should see the Son of man going up where He was before?
040663 It is the Spirit that makes alive, the flesh profits nothing. The words that I speak to you are spirit and are life.
040664 But there are some of you who do not believe. For Jesus knew from the beginning who they were who did not believe, and who is the one betraying Him.
040665 And He said, Because of this I said to you that no one can come to Me unless it was given to him from My Father.
040666 From this time many of His disciples went back into the things behind, and walked no more with Him.
040667 Then Jesus said to the Twelve, Do you also wish to go away?
040668 Then Simon Peter answered Him, Lord, to whom shall we go? You have the words of eternal life.
040669 And we have believed and have known that You are the Christ, the Son of the living God.
040670 Jesus answered them, Have I not chosen you, the Twelve? And one of you is a devil?
040671 But he spoke of Judas Iscariot, the son of Simon; for it was he who was about to betray Him, being one of the Twelve.
040701 After these things Jesus walked in Galilee, for He did not desire to walk in Judea, because the Jews sought to kill Him.
040702 And the Jewish Feast of Tabernacles was near.
040703 Therefore His brothers said to Him, Move away from here and go into Judea, so that Your disciples also may see the works that You do.
040704 For no one does anything in secret, while he himself seeks to be in public. If you do these things, reveal yourself to the world.
040705 For His brothers did not believe in Him.
040706 Then Jesus said to them, My time has not yet come, but your time is always ready.
040707 The world cannot hate you, but it hates Me because I testify of it, that its works are evil.
040708 You go up to this feast; I am not yet going up to this feast; for My time is not yet fulfilled.
040709 And having said these things to them, He remained in Galilee.
040710 But when His brothers had gone up, then He also went up to the feast, not openly, but as in secret.
040711 Then the Jews sought Him at the feast and said, Where is He?
040712 And there was much murmuring among the crowd concerning Him, for some said, He is a good man; others said, No, but he deceives the crowd.
040713 However, no one spoke openly of Him, because of the fear of the Jews.
040714 Now about the middle of the feast, Jesus went up into the temple and taught.
040715 And the Jews marveled, saying, How does this man know letters, not being taught?
040716 Jesus answered them and said, My doctrine is not Mine, but His who sent Me.
040717 If anyone desires to do His will, he shall know of the doctrine, whether it is of God, or I speak from Myself.
040718 He who speaks of himself seeks his own glory, but he who seeks the glory of Him who sent Him is true, and no unrighteousness is in Him.
040719 Did not Moses give you the law? And yet not one of you keeps the law! Why do you seek to kill Me?
040720 The crowd answered and said, You have a demon! Who seeks to kill you?
040721 Jesus answered and said to them, I have done one work, and you all marvel.
040722 Because of this Moses gave you circumcision (not because it is of Moses, but of the fathers,) and you circumcise a man on the sabbath day.
040723 If a man receives circumcision on the sabbath day so that the law of Moses should not be broken, are you angry at Me because I have made a man entirely sound on the sabbath day?
040724 Do not judge according to sight, but judge righteous judgment.
040725 Then some of those from Jerusalem said, Is this not the one they seek to kill?
040726 But lo, he speaks publicly, and they say nothing to him. Perhaps the rulers truly know that this is the Christ indeed?
040727 However, we know this one, from where he is; but when Christ comes, no one knows from where He is.
040728 Then Jesus cried in the temple as He taught, saying, You both know Me, and you know from where I come. And I have not come of Myself, but He who sent Me is true, whom you do not know.
040729 But I know Him, for I am from Him, and He has sent Me.
040730 Then they sought to seize Him, but no one laid a hand on Him, because His hour had not yet come.
040731 And many of the crowd believed on Him, and said, When the Christ comes, will He do more miracles than these which this One has done?
040732 The Pharisees heard that the crowd murmured such things concerning Him. And the Pharisees and the chief priests sent officers to seize Him.
040733 Then Jesus said to them, Yet a little while I am with you, and then I go to Him who sent Me.
040734 You shall seek Me and shall not find Me . And where I am, you cannot come.
040735 Then the Jews said among themselves, Where is he about to go that we shall not find him? Is he about to go to the Dispersion of the Greeks, and to teach the Greeks?
040736 What saying is this that He said, You shall seek Me and shall not find Me , and where I am, you cannot come?
040737 And in the last day of the great feast, Jesus stood and cried out, saying, If anyone thirsts, let him come to Me and drink.
040738 He who believes on Me, as the Scripture has said, "Out of his belly shall flow rivers of living water."
040739 (But He spoke this about the Spirit, which they who believed on Him should receive; for the Holy Spirit was not yet given , because Jesus was not yet glorified.)
040740 Then when they heard the Word, many of the people said, Truly this is the Prophet.
040741 Others said, This is the Christ. But others said, Does the Christ come out of Galilee?
040742 Has the Scripture not said that Christ comes from the seed of David and out of the town of Bethlehem, where David was?
040743 So a division occurred in the crowd because of Him.
040744 And some of them desired to seize Him, but no one laid hands on Him.
040745 Then the officers came to the chief priests and Pharisees. And they said to them, Why have you not brought him?
040746 The officers answered, Never did any man speak as does this Man.
040747 Then the Pharisees answered them, Also, have you not been deceived?
040748 Is it not true that not any of the rulers or of the Pharisees have believed into him?
040749 But this crowd, not knowing the law, is cursed.
040750 Nicodemus said to them, (he who came to Jesus by night, being one of them),
040751 Does our law judge the Man before it hears Him and knows what He does?
040752 They answered and said to him, Are you also from Galilee? Search the scriptures and see that a prophet has not been raised out of Galilee.
040753 And they each went to his own house.
040801 But Jesus went to the Mount of Olives.
040802 And early in the morning He came again into the temple, and all the people came to Him. And He sat down and taught them.
040803 And the scribes and Pharisees brought to Him a woman taken in adultery. And standing her in the midst,
040804 they said to Him, Teacher, this woman was taken in adultery, in the very act.
040805 Now Moses in the law commanded us that such should be stoned. You, then, what do you say?
040806 They said this, tempting Him so that they might have reason to accuse Him. But bending down, Jesus wrote on the ground with His finger, not appearing to hear .
040807 But as they continued to ask Him, He lifted Himself up and said to them, He who is without sin among you, let him cast the first stone at her.
040808 And again bending down, He wrote on the ground.
040809 And hearing, and being convicted by conscience, they went out one by one, beginning at the oldest, until the last. And Jesus was left alone, and the woman standing in the midst.
040810 And bending back up, and seeing no one but the woman, Jesus said to her, Woman, where are the ones who accused you? Did not one give judgment against you?
040811 And she said, No one, Lord. And Jesus said to her, Neither do I give judgment. Go, and sin no more.
040812 Then Jesus spoke again to them, saying, I am the Light of the world. He who follows Me shall not walk in darkness, but shall have the light of life.
040813 Therefore the Pharisees said to Him, You bear record concerning yourself; your witness is not true.
040814 Jesus answered and said to them, Though I bear record concerning Myself, My witness is true. For I know from where I came, and where I go. But you do not know from where I came, and where I go.
040815 You judge after the flesh, I judge no one.
040816 And yet if I do judge, My judgment is true; for I am not alone, but I and the Father who sent Me.
040817 It is also written in your law that the testimony of two men is true.
040818 I am one who bears witness of Myself, and the Father who sent Me bears witness concerning Me.
040819 Then they said to Him, Where is your father? Jesus said to them, You neither know Me nor My Father. If you had known Me, you would have known My Father also.
040820 Jesus spoke these words in the treasury, as He taught in the temple. And no man laid hands upon Him, for His hour had not yet come.
040821 Then Jesus said again to them, I go away, and you shall seek Me and shall die in your sins. Where I go, you cannot come.
040822 Then the Jews said, Will he kill himself? Because he says, Where I go you cannot come.
040823 And He said to them, You are from beneath; I am from above. You are of this world; I am not of this world.
040824 Therefore I said to you that you shall die in your sins, for if you do not believe that I AM, you shall die in your sins.
040825 Then they said to Him, Who are you? And Jesus said to them, Even the same which I also say to you.
040826 I have many things to say and to judge of you, but He who sent Me is true, and I speak to the world those things what I heard of Him.
040827 They did not understand that He spoke to them of the Father.
040828 Then Jesus said to them, When you have lifted up the Son of man, then you shall know that I AM, and that I do nothing of Myself, but as My Father has taught Me, I speak these things.
040829 And He who sent Me is with Me. The Father has not left Me alone, for I always do those things which please Him.
040830 As He spoke these words, many believed upon Him.
040831 Then Jesus said to the Jews who believed on Him, If you continue in My Word, you are My disciples indeed.
040832 And you shall know the truth, and the truth shall make you free.
040833 They answered Him, We are Abraham's seed and were never in bondage to anyone. How do you say, You will be made free?
040834 Jesus answered them, Truly, truly, I say to you, Whoever practices sin is the slave of sin.
040835 And the slave does not abide in the house forever, but the Son abides forever.
040836 Therefore if the Son shall make you free, you shall be free indeed.
040837 I know that you are Abraham's seed, but you seek to kill Me because My Word has no place in you.
040838 I speak what I have seen with My Father, and you, then, do what you have seen with your father.
040839 They answered and said to Him, Abraham is our father. Jesus answered them, If you were Abraham's children, you would do the works of Abraham.
040840 But now you seek to kill Me, a man who has told you the truth which I have heard beside God; this Abraham did not do.
040841 You do the deeds of your father. Then they said to Him, We are not born of fornication; we have one father, even God.
040842 Jesus said to them, If God were your father, you would love Me, for I went forth and came from God; for I did not come of Myself, but He sent Me.
040843 Why do you not know My speech? Because you cannot hear My word.
040844 You are of the Devil as father, and the lusts of your father you will do. He was a murderer from the beginning, and did not abide in the truth because there is no truth in him. When he speaks a lie, he speaks of his own, for he is a liar and the father of it.
040845 And because I tell you the truth, you do not believe Me.
040846 Which of you convicts Me of sin? And if I say the truth, why do you not believe Me?
040847 He who is of God hears God's words. Therefore you do not hear them because you are not of God.
040848 Then the Jews answered and said to Him, Do we not say well that you are a Samaritan and have a demon?
040849 Jesus answered, I do not have a demon, but I honor My Father, and you dishonor Me.
040850 And I do not seek My own glory, but there is One who seeks and judges.
040851 Truly, truly, I say to you, If a man keeps My Word, he shall never see death.
040852 Then the Jews said to Him, Now we know that you have a demon. Abraham and the prophets are dead, and you say, If a man keeps my Word, he shall never taste of death.
040853 Are you greater than our father Abraham, who died? And the prophets are dead; whom do you make yourself?
040854 Jesus answered, If I glorify Myself, My glory is nothing; it is My Father who glorifies Me, of whom you say that He is your God.
040855 Yet you have not known Him, but I know Him. And if I should say I do not know Him, I would be a liar like you. But I know Him and I keep His Word.
040856 Your father Abraham rejoiced to see My day, and He saw and was glad.
040857 Then the Jews said to Him, You are not yet fifty years old, and have you seen Abraham?
040858 Jesus said to them, Truly, truly, I say to you, Before Abraham came into being, I AM!
040859 Then they took up stones to throw at Him. But Jesus hid Himself and went forth out of the temple, going through the midst of them, and passed on by.
040901 And passing by, He saw a man who was blind from birth.
040902 And His disciples asked Him, saying, Master, who sinned, this man or his parents, that he was born blind?
040903 Jesus answered, Neither has this man nor his parents sinned, but that the works of God might be revealed in him.
040904 I must work the works of Him who sent Me, while it is day. Night comes when no man can work.
040905 As long as I am in the world, I am the Light of the world.
040906 And when He had spoken these things, He spat on the ground and made clay from the spittle. And He anointed the eyes of the blind man with the clay.
040907 And He said to him, Go, wash in the pool of Siloam (which translated is Sent). Therefore he went and washed and came seeing.
040908 Then the neighbors and those who had seen him before, that he was blind, said, Is this not he who was sitting and begging?
040909 Some said, This is he. Others said , He is like him. He said, I am he.
040910 Then they said to him, How were your eyes opened?
040911 He answered and said, A man called Jesus made clay and anointed my eyes and said to me, Go to the pool of Siloam and wash. And going and washing, I received sight.
040912 Then they said to him, Where is he? He said, I do not know.
040913 They brought him who once was blind to the Pharisees.
040914 And it was a sabbath when Jesus made the clay and opened his eyes.
040915 Then again the Pharisees also asked him how he had received his sight. He said to them, He put clay upon my eyes, and I washed, and I see.
040916 Therefore some of the Pharisees said, This man is not from God, because he does not keep the sabbath. Others said, How can a man, a sinner, do such miracles? And there was a division among them.
040917 They said to the blind man again, What do you say about him, for he has opened your eyes? He said, He is a prophet.
040918 But the Jews did not believe concerning him, that he had been blind and had received his sight, until they called the parents of him having received sight.
040919 And they asked them, saying, Is this your son, whom you say was born blind? How then does he now see?
040920 His parents answered them and said, We know that this is our son, and that he was born blind.
040921 But by what means he now sees, we do not know. Or who has opened his eyes, we do not know. He is of age, ask him. He will speak for himself.
040922 His parents spoke these things because they feared the Jews, for the Jews had already agreed that if anyone confessed that He was Christ, he should be put out of the synagogue.
040923 Therefore his parents said, He is of age, ask him.
040924 Then a second time they called the man who was blind and said to him, Give glory to God. We know that this man is a sinner.
040925 He answered and said, Whether He is a sinner, I do not know; one thing I do know, that being blind, now I see.
040926 Then they said to him again, What did he do to you? How did he open your eyes?
040927 He answered them, I have told you already, and you did not hear. Why do you want to hear it again? Do you also desire to be His disciples?
040928 Then they reviled him and said, You are his disciple, but we are Moses' disciples.
040929 We know that God spoke to Moses, but we do not know from where this man is.
040930 The man answered and said to them, Why, this is a marvelous thing, that you do not know from where He is, and He has opened my eyes.
040931 But we know that God does not hear sinners, but if anyone is God-fearing and does His will, He hears him.
040932 From everlasting it was not heard that anyone opened the eyes of one who was born blind.
040933 If this One were not of God, He could do nothing.
040934 They answered and said to him, You were altogether born in sins, and do you teach us? And they cast him out.
040935 Jesus heard that they had cast him out; and finding him, He said to him, Do you believe on the Son of God?
040936 And he answered and said, Who is He, Lord, that I might believe on Him?
040937 And Jesus said to him, You have both seen Him, and it is He who is speaking with you.
040938 And he said, Lord, I believe. And he worshiped Him.
040939 And Jesus said, I have come into this world for judgment, that they who do not see might see, and that they who see might be made blind.
040940 And those of the Pharisees who were with Him heard these words, and said to Him, Are we also blind?
040941 Jesus said to them, If you were blind, you would have no sin. But now you say, We see. Therefore your sin remains.
041001 Truly, truly, I say to you, he who does not enter into the sheepfold by the door, but going up by another way, that one is a thief and a robber.
041002 But he who enters in by the door is the shepherd of the sheep.
041003 The doorkeeper opens to him, and the sheep hear his voice, and he calls his own sheep by name and leads them out.
041004 And when he puts forth his own sheep, he goes before them, and the sheep follow him. For they know his voice.
041005 And they will not follow a stranger, but will flee from him, for they do not know the voice of strangers.
041006 Jesus spoke this parable to them, but they did not understand what it was which He spoke to them.
041007 Then Jesus said to them again, Truly, truly, I say to you, I am the door of the sheep.
041008 All who came before Me are thieves and robbers, but the sheep did not hear them.
041009 I am the door. If anyone enters in by Me, he shall be saved and shall go in and out and find pasture.
041010 The thief does not come except to steal and to kill and to destroy. I have come so that they might have life, and that they might have it more abundantly.
041011 I am the Good Shepherd. The Good Shepherd lays down His life for the sheep.
041012 But he who is a hireling and not the shepherd, who does not own the sheep, sees the wolf coming and leaves the sheep and runs away. And the wolf catches them and scatters the sheep.
041013 The hireling flees, because he is a hireling and does not care for the sheep.
041014 I am the Good Shepherd, and I know those that are Mine, and I am known by those who are Mine.
041015 Even as the Father knows Me, I also know the Father. And I lay down My life for the sheep.
041016 And I have other sheep who are not of this fold. I must also lead those, and they shall hear My voice, and there shall be one flock, one Shepherd.
041017 Therefore My Father loves Me, because I lay down My life so that I might take it again.
041018 No one takes it from Me, but I lay it down from Myself. I have authority to lay it down, and I have authority to take it again. I have received this commandment from My Father.
041019 Then a division occurred again among the Jews because of these words.
041020 And many of them said, He has a demon and is insane. Why do you hear him?
041021 Others said, These are not words of one who has been possessed by a demon. A demon is not able to open the eyes of blind ones.
041022 And the Feast of Dedication took place at Jerusalem, and it was winter.
041023 And Jesus walked in the temple in Solomon's Porch.
041024 Then the Jews encircled Him and said to Him, How long do you make us doubt? If you are the Christ, tell us plainly.
041025 Jesus answered them, I told you and you did not believe. The works that I do in My Father's name, they bear witness of Me.
041026 But you did not believe because you are not of My sheep. As I said to you,
041027 My sheep hear My voice, and I know them, and they follow Me.
041028 And I give to them eternal life, and they shall never ever perish, and not anyone shall pluck them out of My hand.
041029 My Father who gave them to me is greater than all, and no one is able to pluck them out of My Father's hand.
041030 I and the Father are one!
041031 Then the Jews took up stones again to stone Him.
