041032 Jesus answered them, I have shown you many good works from My Father; for which of these do you stone Me?
041033 The Jews answered Him, saying, We do not stone you for a good work, but for blasphemy, and because you, being a man, make yourself God.
041034 Jesus answered them, Is it not written in your law, "I said, You are gods?"
041035 If He called those gods with whom the Word of God was, and the Scripture cannot be broken,
041036 do you say of Him whom the Father has sanctified and sent into the world, You blaspheme, because I said, I am the Son of God?
041037 If I do not do the works of My Father, do not believe Me.
041038 But if I do, though you do not believe Me, believe the works so that you may know and believe that the Father is in Me, and I in Him.
041039 Then they again sought to seize Him, but He went forth out of their hand.
041040 And He went away again beyond Jordan into the place where John baptized at the first, and He stayed there.
041041 And many came to Him and said, John indeed did no miracle, but all things that John said concerning this One were true.
041042 And many believed on Him there.
041101 And there was a certain sick one, Lazarus of Bethany, the town of Mary and her sister Martha.
041102 (And it was that Mary who anointed the Lord with ointment and wiped His feet with her hair, whose brother Lazarus was sick.)
041103 Then his sisters sent to Him, saying, Lord, behold, he whom You love is sick.
041104 When Jesus heard, He said, This sickness is not to death, but for the glory of God, so that the Son of God might be glorified by it.
041105 And Jesus loved Martha and her sister and Lazarus.
041106 Therefore, when He had heard that he was sick, then indeed He remained two days in the place where He was.
041107 Then after that He said to the disciples, Let us go into Judea again.
041108 The disciples said to Him, Rabbi, the Jews lately have sought to stone You, and do You go there again?
041109 Jesus answered, Are there not twelve hours in the day? If anyone walks in the day, he does not stumble because he sees the light of the world.
041110 But if anyone walks in the night, he stumbles because there is no light in him.
041111 He said these things; and after that He said to them, Our friend Lazarus sleeps. But I go so that I may awaken him out of sleep.
041112 Then His disciples said, Lord, if he sleeps, he will get well.
041113 But Jesus spoke of his death, but they thought that He had spoken of taking rest in sleep.
041114 Then Jesus said to them plainly, Lazarus is dead.
041115 And I am glad for your sakes that I was not there, in order that you may believe. But let us go to him.
041116 Then Thomas (he being called Twin) said to his fellow disciples, Let us also go, that we may die with Him.
041117 Then when Jesus came, He found him already being held in the tomb four days.
041118 And Bethany was near Jerusalem, fifteen stadia away.
041119 And many of the Jews came to Martha and Mary in order to comfort them concerning their brother.
041120 Then when Martha heard that Jesus was coming, she met Him. But Mary was sitting in the house.
041121 Then Martha said to Jesus, Lord, if You had been here, my brother would not have died.
041122 But I know that even now, whatever You will ask of God, God will give You.
041123 Jesus said to her, Your brother shall rise again.
041124 Martha said to Him, I know that he shall rise again in the resurrection at the last day.
041125 Jesus said to her, I am the Resurrection and the Life! He who believes in Me, though he die, yet he shall live.
041126 And whoever lives and believes in Me shall never die. Do you believe this?
041127 She said to Him, Yes, Lord, I have believed that You are the Christ, the Son of God, who has come into the world.
041128 And saying these things, she went away and called Mary her sister secretly, saying, The Teacher has come and calls you.
041129 As soon as she heard, she arose quickly and came to him.
041130 Now Jesus had not yet come into the town, but was in that place where Martha met Him.
041131 Then the Jews who were with her in the house, and comforted her, when they saw that Mary rose up hastily and went out, they followed her, saying, She is going to the tomb to weep there.
041132 Then when Mary had come where Jesus was, seeing Him, Mary fell down at His feet, saying to Him, Lord, if You had been here, my brother would not have died.
041133 Then when He saw her weeping, and also the Jews who came with her weeping, Jesus groaned in the spirit and troubled Himself.
041134 And He said, Where have you laid him? They said to Him, Lord, come and see.
041135 Jesus wept.
041136 Then the Jews said, Behold how He loved him!
041137 And some of them said, Was not this Man who opened the eyes of the blind able also to cause that even this one should not have died?
041138 Then Jesus, groaning in Himself again, came to the tomb. And it was a cave, and a stone lay upon it.
041139 Jesus said, Take away the stone. Martha, the sister of him who died, said to Him, Lord, by this time he stinks. For it is the fourth day .
041140 Jesus answered her, Did I not say to you that if you would believe you would see the glory of God?
041141 Then they took away the stone where the dead was laid. And Jesus lifted up His eyes and said, Father, I thank You that You have heard Me.
041142 And I know that You hear Me always, but because of the people who stand by I said it , so that they may believe that You have sent Me.
041143 And saying these things, He cried with a loud voice, Lazarus, Here! Outside!
041144 And he who had died came out, bound hand and foot with sheets, and his face was bound with a cloth. Jesus said to them, Untie him and let him go!
041145 Then many of the Jews who came to Mary, and had seen the things which Jesus did, believed on Him.
041146 But some of them went to the Pharisees and told them what Jesus had done.
041147 Then the chief priests and Pharisees gathered a sanhedrin, and said, What can we do? For this man does many miracles.
041148 If we let him alone this way, all will believe on him. And the Romans will come and take away both our place and nation.
041149 And one of them, Caiaphas, being the high priest of that year, said to them, You do not know anything at all,
041150 nor do you consider that it is expedient for us that one man should die for the people, and not that the whole nation perish.
041151 And he did not speak this of himself, but being high priest that year, he prophesied that Jesus should die for the nation;
041152 and not for that nation only, but also that He should gather together in one the children of God who were scattered abroad.
041153 Then from that day they took counsel together that they might kill Him.
041154 Therefore Jesus walked no more openly among the Jews; but He went away from there to a country near the wilderness, into a city called Ephraim, and continued there with His disciples.
041155 And the Jews' Passover was near. And many went out of the country up to Jerusalem before the Passover in order to purify themselves.
041156 Then they sought Jesus, and spoke with one another as they stood in the temple, What does it seem to you, that He will not at all come to the feast?
041157 And all the chief priests and the Pharisees had given commands, that if anyone knew where He was, he should make it known so that they might seize Him.
041201 Then, six days before the Passover, Jesus came to Bethany, where Lazarus was (who had died, whom He raised from the dead).
041202 Then they made a supper there for Him. And Martha served, but Lazarus was one of those reclining with Him.
041203 Then Mary took a pound of ointment of pure spikenard, very costly, and anointed the feet of Jesus, and wiped His feet with her hair. And the house was filled with the odor of the ointment.
041204 Then said one of His disciples (Judas Iscariot, Simon's son , who was to betray Him)
041205 Why was this ointment not sold for three hundred denarii and given to the poor?
041206 He said this, not that he cared for the poor, but because he was a thief and held the moneybag and carried the things put in .
041207 Then Jesus said, Let her alone. She has kept this for the day of My burial.
041208 For you have the poor with you always; but you do not always have Me.
041209 Then a great crowd of the Jews learned that He was there. And they did not come for Jesus' sake only, but also that they might see Lazarus, whom He had raised from the dead.
041210 But the chief priests consulted that they might put Lazarus to death also,
041211 because many of the Jews went away and believed on Jesus because of him.
041212 On the next day, when they heard that Jesus was coming to Jerusalem, a great crowd who had come to the Feast
041213 took branches of palm trees and went out to meet Him. And they cried, Hosanna! "Blessed is the King of Israel who comes in the name of the Lord!"
041214 And finding an ass colt, Jesus sat on it; as it is written,
041215 "Fear not, daughter of Zion; behold, your King comes sitting on the foal of an ass."
041216 But His disciples did not know these things at the first. But when Jesus was glorified, then they remembered that these things were written of Him, and that they had done these things to Him.
041217 Then the crowd witnessed, those who were with Him when He called Lazarus out of the tomb and raised him from the dead.
041218 Because of this the crowd also met Him, because they heard that He had done this miracle.
041219 Then the Pharisees said among themselves, Do you see how you gain nothing? Behold, the world has gone after Him.
041220 And there were certain Greeks among those who came up to worship at the Feast.
041221 Then these came to Philip, who was from Bethsaida of Galilee, and asked him, saying, Sir, we want to see Jesus.
041222 Philip came and told Andrew. And again Andrew and Philip told Jesus.
041223 And Jesus answered them, saying, The hour has come that the Son of man should be glorified.
041224 Truly, truly, I say to you, Unless a grain of wheat falls into the ground and dies, it abides alone; but if it dies, it brings forth much fruit.
041225 He who loves his life shall lose it. And he who hates his life in this world shall keep it to life eternal.
041226 If anyone serves Me, let him follow Me; and where I am, there also My servant shall be. If anyone serves Me, the Father will honor him.
041227 And My soul is troubled, and what shall I say? Father, save Me from this hour? But for this cause I came to this hour.
041228 Father, glorify Your name! Then there came a voice from the heaven saying , I have both glorified it and will glorify it again.
041229 Then the crowd who stood by and heard said that it thundered. Others said, An angel spoke to Him.
041230 Jesus answered and said, This voice did not come because of Me, but for your sakes.
041231 Now is the judgment of this world. Now shall the prince of this world be cast out.
041232 And I, if I am lifted up from the earth, I will draw all to Myself.
041233 But He said this, signifying what kind of death He was about to die.
041234 The crowd answered Him, We have heard out of the law that Christ lives forever. How do you say, The Son of man must be lifted up? Who is this Son of man?
041235 Then Jesus said to them, Yet a little while the Light is with you. Walk while you have the Light, lest darkness come upon you. For he who walks in darkness does not know where he goes.
041236 While you have the Light, believe in the Light so that you may become sons of Light. Jesus spoke these things and departed and was hidden from them.
041237 But though He had done so many miracles before them, yet they did not believe on Him,
041238 so that the saying of Isaiah the prophet might be fulfilled, which he spoke, "Lord, who has believed our report? And to whom has the arm of the Lord been revealed?"
041239 Therefore they could not believe, because Isaiah said again,
041240 "He has blinded their eyes and hardened their heart, so that they should not see with their eyes nor understand with their heart, and be converted, and I should heal them."
041241 Isaiah said these things when he saw His glory and spoke of Him.
041242 Still, however, even out of the rulers, many did believe on Him. But because of the Pharisees they did not confess, lest they should be put out of the synagogue;
041243 for they loved the glory of men more than the glory of God.
041244 But Jesus cried out and said, He who believes on Me does not believe on Me but on Him who sent Me.
041245 And he who sees Me sees Him who sent Me.
041246 I have come as a Light into the world, so that whoever believes on Me should not remain in darkness.
041247 And if any one hears My words and does not believe, I do not judge him, for I do not come to judge the world, but to save the world.
041248 He who rejects Me and does not receive My words has one who judges him; the Word that I have spoken, the same shall judge him in the last day.
041249 For I have not spoken of Myself, but the Father who sent Me gave Me a command, what I should say, and what I should speak.
041250 And I know that His command is life everlasting. Therefore whatever I speak, even as the Father said to Me, so I speak.
041301 And before the feast of the Passover, when Jesus knew that His hour had come when He should depart out of this world to the Father, having loved His own in the world, He loved them to the end.
041302 And when supper had ended, the Devil now having put into the heart of Judas Iscariot the son of Simon to betray Him,
041303 Jesus knowing that the Father had given all things into His hands, and that He had come from God and went to God,
041304 He rose up from supper and laid aside His garments. And He took a towel and girded Himself.
041305 After that He poured water into a basin and began to wash the disciples' feet, and to wipe them with the towel with which He was girded.
041306 Then He came to Simon Peter. And Peter said to Him, Lord, do You wash my feet?
041307 Jesus answered and said to him, You do not know what I do now, but you shall know hereafter.
041308 Peter said to Him, You shall never wash my feet. Jesus answered him, Unless I wash you, you have no part with Me.
041309 Simon Peter said to Him, Lord, not my feet only, but also my hands and head.
041310 Jesus said to him, He who is bathed has no need except to wash his feet, but is clean every whit. And you are clean, but not all.
041311 For He knew who would betray Him. Therefore He said, You are not all clean.
041312 So after He had washed their feet and had taken His garments and had reclined again, He said to them, Do you know what I have done to you?
041313 You call Me the Teacher, and Lord, and you say well, for I AM.
041314 If then I, the Lord and the Teacher, have washed your feet, you also ought to wash one another's feet.
041315 For I have given you an example, that you should do as I have done to you.
041316 Truly, truly, I say to you, A servant is not greater than his master, neither is he who is sent greater than he who sent him.
041317 If you know these things, blessed are you if you do them.
041318 I do not speak of you all; I know whom I have chosen; but that the Scripture might be fulfilled, "He who eats bread with me has lifted up his heel against me."
041319 From now I tell you before it comes, so that when it happens you may believe that I AM.
041320 Truly, truly, I say to you, He who receives whomever I send receives Me. And he who receives Me receives Him who sent Me.
041321 When Jesus had said this, He was troubled in spirit, and testified and said, Truly, truly, I say to you that one of you shall betray Me.
041322 Then the disciples looked upon one another, wondering of whom He spoke.
041323 But there was one of His disciples leaning upon Jesus' bosom, the one whom Jesus loved.
041324 Simon Peter therefore signaled to him to ask whom it might be of whom He spoke.
041325 And lying on Jesus' breast, he said to him, Lord, who is it?
041326 Jesus answered, It is he to whom I shall give the morsel when I have dipped it . And dipping the morsel, He gave it to Judas Iscariot, the son of Simon.
041327 And after the morsel, then Satan entered into him. Then Jesus said to him, What you do, do quickly.
041328 But no one reclining knew for what reason He spoke this to him.
041329 For some thought, because Judas had the moneybag, that Jesus had said to him, Buy what we have need of for the feast; or that he should give something to the poor.
041330 He then, having received the morsel, went out immediately. And it was night.
041331 Then when he had left, Jesus said, Now the Son of man is glorified, and God is glorified in him.
041332 If God is glorified in Him, God shall also glorify Him in Himself, and shall immediately glorify Him.
041333 Little children, I am with you yet a little while. You shall seek Me; and as I said to the Jews, Where I go, you cannot come, so I now say to you.
041334 I give you a new commandment, that you love one another. As I have loved you, you should also love one another.
041335 By this all shall know that you are My disciples, if you have love toward one another.
041336 Simon Peter said to Him, Lord, where do You go? Jesus answered him, Where I go you cannot now follow Me, but you shall follow Me afterward.
041337 Peter said to Him, Lord, why cannot I follow You now? I will lay down my life for Your sake.
041338 Jesus answered him, Will you lay down your life for My sake? Truly, truly, I say to you, The cock shall not crow until you have denied Me three times.
041401 Let not your heart be troubled. You believe in God, believe also in Me.
041402 In My Father's house are many mansions; if it were not so , I would have told you. I go to prepare a place for you.
041403 And if I go and prepare a place for you, I will come again and receive you to Myself, so that where I am, you may be also.
041404 And where I go you know, and the way you know.
041405 Thomas said to Him, Lord, we do not know where You go, and how can we know the way?
041406 Jesus said to him, I am the Way, the Truth, and the Life; no one comes to the Father but by Me.
041407 If you had known Me, you would have known My Father also. And from now on you know Him and have seen Him.
041408 Philip said to Him, Lord, show us the Father, and it is enough for us.
041409 Jesus said to him, Have I been with you such a long time and yet you have not known Me, Philip? He who has seen Me has seen the Father. And how do you say, Show us the Father?
041410 Do you not believe that I am in the Father and the Father in Me? The words that I speak to you I do not speak of Myself, but the Father who dwells in Me, He does the works.
041411 Believe Me that I am in the Father and the Father in Me, or else believe Me for the very works themselves.
041412 Truly, truly, I say to you, He who believes on Me, the works that I do he shall do also, and greater works than these he shall do, because I go to My Father.
041413 And whatever you may ask in My name, that I will do, so that the Father may be glorified in the Son.
041414 If you ask anything in My name, I will do it .
041415 If you love Me, keep My commandments.
041416 And I will pray the Father, and He shall give you another Comforter, so that He may be with you forever,
041417 the Spirit of Truth, whom the world cannot receive because it does not see Him nor know Him. But you know Him, for He dwells with you and shall be in you.
041418 I will not leave you orphans. I will come to you.
041419 Yet a little while and the world does not see Me any more. But you see Me. Because I live, you shall live also.
041420 At that day you shall know that I am in My Father, and you in Me, and I in you.
041421 He who has My commandments and keeps them, he it is who loves Me. And he who loves Me shall be loved by My Father, and I will love him and will reveal Myself to him.
041422 Judas (not Iscariot) said to Him, Lord, how is it that You will reveal Yourself to us and not to the world?
041423 Jesus answered and said to him, If a man loves Me, he will keep My Word. And My Father will love him, and We will come to him and make Our abode with him.
041424 He who does not love Me does not keep My words, and the Word which you hear is not Mine, but the Father's who sent Me.
041425 I have spoken these things to you, being present with you.
041426 But the Comforter, the Holy Spirit whom the Father will send in My name, He shall teach you all things and bring all things to your remembrance, whatever I have said to you.
041427 Peace I leave with you, My peace I give to you. Not as the world gives do I give to you. Let not your heart be troubled, neither let it be afraid.
041428 You have heard how I said to you, I go away and I am coming to you again . If you loved Me, you would rejoice because I said, I go to the Father, for My Father is greater than I.
041429 And now I have told you before it happens, so that when it happens you might believe.
041430 I shall no longer speak many things with you, for the ruler of this world comes, and he has nothing in Me.
041431 But that the world may know that I love the Father, and as the Father has given Me commandment, even so I do. Arise, let us go away from here.
041501 I am the True Vine, and My Father is the Vinedresser.
041502 Every branch in Me that does not bear fruit, He takes away. And every one that bears fruit, He prunes it so that it may bring forth more fruit.
041503 Now you are clean through the Word which I have spoken to you.
041504 Abide in Me, and I in you. As the branch cannot bear fruit of itself unless it remains in the vine, so neither can you unless you abide in Me.
041505 I am the Vine, you are the branches. He who abides in Me, and I in him, the same brings forth much fruit; for without Me you can do nothing.
041506 If anyone does not abide in Me, he is cast out as a branch and is withered. And they gather and cast them into the fire, and they are burned.
041507 If you abide in Me, and My words abide in you, you shall ask what you will, and it shall be done to you.
041508 In this My Father is glorified, that you bear much fruit, so you shall be My disciples.
041509 As the Father has loved Me, so I have loved you; continue in My love.
041510 If you keep My commandments, you shall abide in My love, even as I have kept My Father's commandments and abide in His love.
041511 I have spoken these things to you so that My joy might remain in you and your joy might be full.
041512 This is My commandment, that you love one another as I have loved you.
041513 No one has greater love than this, that a man lay down his life for his friends.
041514 You are My friends if you do whatever I command you.
041515 No longer do I call you servants, for the servant does not know what his master does. But I have called you friends, for all things that I have heard from My Father I have made known to you.
041516 You have not chosen Me, but I have chosen you and ordained you that you should go and bring forth fruit, and that your fruit should remain; that whatever you shall ask of the Father in My name, He may give it to you.
041517 These things I command you, that you love one another.
041518 If the world hates you, you know that it hated Me before it hated you.
041519 If you were of the world, the world would love its own. But because you are not of the world, but I have chosen you out of the world, therefore the world hates you.
041520 Remember the word that I said to you, The servant is not greater than his master. If they have persecuted Me, they will also persecute you. If they have kept My saying, they will also keep yours.
041521 But all these things they will do to you for My name's sake, because they do not know Him who sent Me.
041522 If I had not come and spoken to them, they would not have had sin; but now they have no excuse for their sin.
041523 He who hates Me hates My Father also.
041524 If I had not done among them the works which no other did, they would not have had sin. But now they have both seen and hated Me and My Father.
041525 But that the Word might be fulfilled that is written in their law, "They hated Me without a cause."
041526 And when the Comforter has come, whom I will send to you from the Father, the Spirit of truth who proceeds from the Father, He shall testify of Me.
041527 And you also shall bear witness, because you have been with Me from the beginning.
041601 I have spoken these things to you so that you should not be offended.
041602 They shall put you out of the synagogue. But an hour is coming that everyone who kills you will think that he bears God service.
041603 And they will do these things to you because they have not known the Father nor Me.
041604 But I have told you these things so that when the hour shall come you may remember that I told you of them. And I did not say these things to you at the beginning because I was with you.
041605 But now I go to Him who sent Me, and none of you asks Me, Where do You go?
041606 But because I have said these things to you, sorrow has filled your heart.
041607 But I tell you the truth, it is expedient for you that I go away; for if I do not go away, the Comforter will not come to you. But if I depart, I will send Him to you.
041608 And when that One comes, He will convict the world concerning sin, and concerning righteousness, and concerning judgment.
041609 Concerning sin, because they do not believe on Me;
041610 concerning righteousness, because I go to My Father and you see Me no more;
041611 concerning judgment, because the ruler of this world is judged.
041612 I have yet many things to say to you, but you cannot bear them now.
041613 However, when He, the Spirit of Truth, has come, He will guide you into all truth. For He shall not speak of Himself, but whatever He hears, He shall speak. And He will announce to you things to come.
041614 He will glorify Me, for He will receive of Mine and will announce it to you.
041615 All things that the Father has are Mine. Therefore I said that He will take of Mine and will announce it to you.
041616 A little while and you will not see Me; and again a little while , and you will see Me, because I go to the Father.
041617 Then His disciples said to one another, What is this that He says to us, A little while and you will not see Me, and again a little and you will see Me? And, Because I go to the Father?
041618 Therefore they said, What is this that He says, A little while ? We do not know what He is saying.
041619 Then Jesus knew that they desired to ask Him, and said to them, Do you seek answers with one another concerning this, because I said, A little while and you shall not see Me; and again a little while, and you shall see Me?
041620 Truly, truly, I say to you that you will weep and lament, but the world will rejoice. And you will be sorrowful, but your sorrow shall be turned into joy.
041621 The woman has grief when she bears, because her hour has come. But when she brings forth the child, she no longer remembers the anguish, because of the joy that a man is born into the world.
041622 And therefore you now have sorrow. But I will see you again, and your heart will rejoice, and no one will take your joy from you.
041623 And in that day you shall ask Me nothing. Truly, truly, I say to you, Whatever you shall ask the Father in My name, He will give you.
041624 Before now you have asked nothing in My name; ask and you shall receive, that your joy may be full.
041625 I have spoken these things to you in parables, but the time is coming when I shall no more speak to you in parables, but I will show you plainly of the Father.
041626 At that day you will ask in My name; and I do not say to you that I will pray to the Father for you,
041627 for the Father Himself loves you, because you have loved Me and have believed that I came out from God.
041628 I came forth from the Father, and have come into the world. Again I leave the world and go to the Father.
041629 The disciples said to Him, Lo, now You speak plainly and speak no parable.
041630 Now we know that You know all things and do not need that anyone should ask You. By this we believe that You have come forth from God.
041631 Jesus answered them, Do you now believe?
041632 Behold, the hour comes, yea, has now come, that you will be scattered, each man to his own things, and you will leave Me alone. And yet I am not alone, because the Father is with Me.
041633 I have spoken these things to you so that you might have peace in Me. In the world you shall have tribulation, but be of good cheer. I have overcome the world.
041701 Jesus spoke these words and lifted up His eyes to Heaven and said, Father, the hour has come. Glorify Your Son so that Your Son also may glorify You,
041702 even as You have given Him authority over all flesh so that He should give eternal life to all You have given Him.
041703 And this is life eternal, that they might know You, the only true God, and Jesus Christ whom You have sent.
041704 I have glorified You upon the earth. I have finished the work which You have given Me to do.
041705 And now Father, glorify Me with Yourself with the glory which I had with You before the world was.
041706 I have revealed Your name to the men whom You gave to Me out of the world. They were Yours, and You gave them to Me, and they have kept Your word.
041707 Now they have known that all things, whatever You have given Me, are from You.
041708 For I have given to them the words which You gave Me, and they have received them and have known surely that I came out from You. And they have believed that You sent Me.
041709 I pray for them. I do not pray for the world, but for those whom You have given Me, for they are Yours.
041710 And all Mine are Yours, and Yours are Mine; and I am glorified in them.
041711 And now I am in the world no longer, but these are in the world, and I come to You, Holy Father. Keep them in Your name, those whom You have given Me, so that they may be one as We are .
041712 While I was with them in the world, I kept them in Your name. Those that You have given Me I have kept, and none of them is lost, but the son of perdition, that the Scripture might be fulfilled.
041713 And now I come to You, and these things I speak in the world that they might have My joy fulfilled in them.
041714 I have given them Your Word, and the world has hated them because they are not of the world, even as I am not of the world.
041715 I do not pray for You to take them out of the world, but for You to keep them from the evil.
041716 They are not of the world, even as I am not of the world.
041717 Sanctify them through Your truth. Your Word is truth.
041718 As You have sent Me into the world, even so I have sent them into the world.
041719 And I sanctify Myself for their sakes, so that they also might be sanctified in truth.
041720 And I do not pray for these alone, but for those also who shall believe on Me through their word,
041721 that they all may be one, as You, Father, are in Me, and I in You, that they also may be one in Us, so that the world may believe that You have sent Me.
041722 And I have given them the glory which You have given Me, that they may be one, even as We are one,
041723 I in them, and You in Me, that they may be made perfect in one; and that the world may know that You have sent Me and have loved them as You have loved Me.
041724 Father, I desire that those whom You have given Me, that they may be with Me where I am, that they may behold My glory which You have given Me, for You have loved Me before the foundation of the world.
041725 O righteous Father, indeed the world has not known You; but I have known You, and these have known that You have sent me.
041726 And I made known to them Your name, and will make it known, so that the love with which You have loved Me may be in them, and I in them.
041801 Having spoken these words, Jesus went out with His disciples over the winter stream Kidron, where there was a garden. He and His disciples entered into it.
041802 And Judas who betrayed Him also knew the place. For Jesus oftentimes went there with His disciples.
041803 Then Judas, having received a band and officers from the chief priests and Pharisees, came there with lanterns and torches and weapons.
041804 Then Jesus, knowing all things that were coming upon Him, went out and said to them, Whom do you seek?
041805 They answered Him, Jesus of Nazareth. Jesus said to them, I AM! And Judas who betrayed Him also stood with them.
041806 Then as soon as He had said to them, I AM, they went backward and fell to the ground.
041807 Then He asked them again, Whom do you seek? And they said, Jesus of Nazareth.
041808 Jesus answered, I have told you that I AM. Therefore if you seek Me, let these go away;
041809 (that the word might be fulfilled which He spoke, " Of those whom You have given Me, I have lost not one of them").
041810 Then Simon Peter, having a sword, drew it and struck the high priest's servant and cut off his right ear. And the servant's name was Malchus.
041811 Then Jesus said to Peter, Put up your sword into the sheath. The cup which My Father has given Me, shall I not drink it?
041812 Then the band, and the chiliarch, and under-officers of the Jews together seized Jesus and bound Him.
041813 And they led Him away to Annas first, for he was father-in-law to Caiaphas, who was the high priest that year.
041814 And Caiaphas was he who gave counsel to the Jews, that it was expedient that one man should die for the people.
041815 And Simon Peter and another disciple followed Jesus. That disciple was known to the high priest, and he went in with Jesus into the court of the high priest.
041816 But Peter stood at the door outside. Then the other disciple went out, the one who was known to the high priest, and spoke to her who kept the door and brought Peter in.
041817 Then the girl who kept the door said to Peter, Are you not also one of this man's disciples? He said, I am not.
041818 And the servants and officers who had made a fire of coals stood there, for it was cold. And they warmed themselves . And Peter stood with them and warmed himself.
041819 Then the high priest asked Jesus of His disciples and of His teaching.
041820 Jesus answered him, I spoke openly to the world. I always taught in the synagogue and in the temple, where the Jews always resort, and I have said nothing in secret.
041821 Why do you ask Me? Ask those who heard me what I have said to them. Behold, they know what I said.
041822 And when He had spoken this way, one of the officers who stood by struck Jesus with the palm of his hand, saying, Do you answer the high priest so?
041823 Jesus answered him, If I have spoken evil, bear witness of the evil; but if well, why do you strike Me?
041824 Then Annas had sent Him bound to Caiaphas the high priest.
041825 And Simon Peter stood and warmed himself. Then they said to him, Are you not also one of his disciples? He denied and said, I am not.
041826 One of the servants of the high priest, being kinsman to him whose ear Peter cut off, said, Did I not see you in the garden with him?
041827 Peter then denied again. And immediately a cock crowed.
041828 Then they led Jesus from Caiaphas into the praetorium. And it was early. And they did not go into the praetorium, that they should not be defiled, and that they might eat the Passover.
041829 Then Pilate went out to them and said, What charge do you bring against this man?
041830 They answered and said to him, If he were not an evildoer, then we would not have delivered him up to you.
041831 Then Pilate said to them, You take him and judge him according to your law. Then the Jews said to him, It is not lawful for us to put anyone to death
041832 (that the word of Jesus might be fulfilled, which He spoke signifying what death He was about to die).
041833 Then Pilate entered into the praetorium again and called Jesus and said to him, Are you the king of the Jews?
041834 Jesus answered him, Do you say this thing of yourself, or did others say it to you about Me?
041835 Pilate answered, Am I a Jew? Your own nation and the chief priests have delivered you to me. What have you done?
041836 Jesus answered, My kingdom is not of this world. If My kingdom were of this world, then My servants would fight so that I might not be delivered to the Jews. But now My kingdom is not from here.
041837 Pilate then said to Him, Are you a king then? Jesus answered, You say it that I am a king. To this end I was born, and for this cause I came into the world, that I should bear witness to the truth. Everyone who is of the truth hears My voice.
041838 Pilate said to Him, What is truth? And when he had said this, he went out again to the Jews and said to them, I find no fault in him.
041839 But you have a custom that I should release one to you at the Passover. Then do you desire that I release to you the king of the Jews?
041840 Then they all cried again, saying, Not this man, but Barabbas! But Barabbas was a robber.
041901 Then Pilate therefore took Jesus and flogged Him .
041902 And the soldiers plaited a crown of thorns and put it on His head. And they put a purple robe on Him,
041903 and said, Hail, King of the Jews! And they struck Him with their hands.
041904 Then Pilate went out again and said to them, Behold, I bring him out to you so that you may know that I find no fault in him.
041905 Then Jesus came out wearing the crown of thorns and the purple robe. And Pilate said to them, Behold the man!
041906 Then when the chief priests and under-officers saw Him, they cried out, saying, Crucify! Crucify Him ! Pilate said to them, You take Him and crucify Him, for I find no fault in him.
041907 The Jews answered him, We have a law, and by our law he ought to die, because he made himself the Son of God.
041908 Then when Pilate heard that saying, he was the more afraid.
041909 And he went again into the praetorium and said to Jesus, Where are you from? But Jesus gave him no answer.
041910 Then Pilate said to him, Do you not speak to me? Do you not know that I have authority to crucify you, and I have authority to release you?
041911 Jesus answered, You could have no authority against Me unless it were given to you from above. Therefore he who delivered Me to you has the greater sin.
041912 From this time , Pilate sought to release Him. But the Jews cried out, saying, If you let this man go, you are not Caesar's friend. Whoever makes himself a king speaks against Caesar.
041913 Then when Pilate heard that saying, he brought Jesus out and sat down in the judgment seat at a place called the Pavement (but in the Hebrew, Gabbatha).
041914 And it was the preparation of the Passover, and about the sixth hour. And he said to the Jews, Behold your king!
041915 But they cried out, Away with him ! Away with him ! Crucify him! Pilate said to them, Shall I crucify your king? The chief priests answered, We have no king but Caesar.
041916 Then he delivered Him up to them that He might be crucified. And they took Jesus and led Him away.
041917 And bearing His cross, He went out to a place called, The Place of a Skull (which is called in the Hebrew, Golgotha)
041918 where they crucified Him, and two others with Him, one on either side, and Jesus in the middle.
041919 And Pilate wrote a title and put it on the cross. And the writing was, JESUS OF NAZARETH, THE KING OF THE JEWS.
041920 Then many of the Jews read this title, for the place where Jesus was crucified was near the city, and it was written in Hebrew, Greek, and Latin.
041921 Then the chief priests of the Jews said to Pilate, Do not write, the king of the Jews, but that he said, I am king of the Jews.
041922 Pilate answered, What I have written I have written.
041923 Then when they had crucified Jesus, the soldiers took His garments and made four parts, one part to each soldier; and also His tunic. And the tunic was without seam, woven from the top throughout.
041924 Therefore they said among themselves, Let us not tear it, but cast lots for it to find whose it shall be (that the Scripture might be fulfilled which says, "They parted my garments among them, and for my garment they cast lots"). Therefore the soldiers did these things.
041925 And His mother stood by the cross of Jesus, and His mother's sister, Mary the wife of Clopas, and Mary Magdalene.
041926 Then when Jesus saw His mother and the disciple whom He loved standing by, He said to His mother, Woman, behold your son!
041927 Then He said to the disciple, Behold your mother! And from that hour that disciple took her into his own home .
041928 After this, knowing that all things were now accomplished, that the Scripture might be fulfilled, Jesus said, I thirst.
041929 Then a vessel full of vinegar was set. And they filled a sponge with sour wine and put it upon hyssop, and put it to His mouth.
041930 Then when Jesus had received the sour wine, He said, It is finished! And He bowed His head and gave up the spirit.
041931 Then the Jews, because it was Preparation, begged Pilate that their legs might be broken, and that they might be taken away, so that the bodies should not remain on the cross on the sabbath. For that sabbath was a high day.
041932 Then the soldiers came and broke the legs of the first, and of the other who was crucified with Him.
041933 But when they came to Jesus and saw that He was already dead, they did not break His legs.
041934 But one of the soldiers pierced His side with a lance, and instantly there came out blood and water.
041935 And he who saw bore record, and his record is true. And he knows that he speaks true, so that you might believe.
041936 For these things were done so that the Scripture might be fulfilled, "Not a bone of Him shall be broken."
041937 And again another Scripture says, "They shall look upon Him whom they pierced."
041938 And after these things, Joseph of Arimathea, being a disciple of Jesus (but secretly for fear of the Jews) begged of Pilate that he might take away the body of Jesus. And Pilate gave permission. Then he came and took the body of Jesus.
041939 And Nicodemus also came, who at the first came to Jesus by night, and brought a mixture of myrrh and aloes, about a hundred pounds.
041940 Then they took the body of Jesus and wound it with linens with the spices, as is the custom of the Jews to bury.
041941 And in the place where He was crucified there was a garden, and in the garden a new tomb in which no one yet had been placed.
041942 There, then, because of the Preparation of the Jews, because the tomb was near, they laid Jesus.
042001 The first of the sabbaths Mary Magdalene came early to the tomb, darkness still being on it , and she saw the stone taken away from the tomb.
042002 Then she ran and came to Simon Peter, and to the other disciple whom Jesus loved, and said to them, They have taken away the Lord out of the tomb, and we do not know where they have laid Him.
042003 Therefore Peter and that other disciple went forth and came to the tomb.
042004 So they both ran together. And the other disciple outran Peter and came first to the tomb.
042005 And stooping down he saw the linens lying, yet he did not go in.
042006 Then Simon Peter came following him and went into the tomb. And he saw the linens lying there .
042007 And the grave-cloth that was on His head was not lying with the linens, but was wrapped up in one place by itself.
042008 Therefore, then, that other disciple also went in, the one who came first to the tomb. And he saw and believed.
042009 For as yet they did not know the Scripture that He must rise again from the dead.
042010 Then the disciples went away again to themselves.
042011 But Mary stood outside of the tomb, weeping. And as she wept, she stooped down into the tomb.
042012 And she saw two angels in white sitting there, the one at the head and the other at the feet, where the body of Jesus had lain.
042013 And they said to her, Woman, why do you weep? She said to them, Because they have taken away my Lord, and I do not know where they have laid Him.
042014 And when she had said this, she turned backward and saw Jesus standing, but she did not know that it was Jesus.
042015 Jesus said to her, Woman, why do you weep? Whom do you seek? Supposing Him to be the gardener, she said to Him, Sir, if you have carried Him away from here, tell me where you have laid Him and I will take Him away.
042016 Jesus said to her, Mary! She turned herself and said to Him, Rabboni! (which is to say, Master!)
042017 Jesus said to her, Do not touch Me, for I have not yet ascended to My Father. But go to My brothers and say to them, I ascend to My Father and Your Father, and to My God and your God.
042018 Mary Magdalene came and told the disciples that she had seen the Lord and that He had spoken these things to her.
042019 Then the same day at evening, being the first of the sabbaths, when the doors were shut where the disciples were assembled for fear of the Jews, Jesus came and stood in the midst, and said to them, Peace to you!
042020 And when He had said this, He showed them His hands and His side. Then the disciples were glad when they saw the Lord.
042021 Then Jesus said to them again, Peace to you. As My Father has sent Me, even so I send you.
042022 And when He had said this, He breathed on them and said to them, Receive the Holy Spirit.
042023 Of whomever sins you remit, they are remitted to them. Of whomever sins you retain, they are retained.
042024 But Thomas, one of the twelve, called the Twin, was not with them when Jesus came.
042025 The other disciples therefore said to him, We have seen the Lord. But he said to them, Unless I shall see the print of the nails in His hands, and put my finger into the print of the nails, and thrust my hand into His side, I will not believe.
042026 And after eight days the disciples were inside again, and Thomas was with them. Jesus came, the doors being shut, and stood in the midst and said, Peace to you!
042027 Then He said to Thomas, Reach your finger here and behold My hands; and reach your hand here and thrust it into My side; and do not be unbelieving, but believing.
042028 And Thomas answered and said to Him, My Lord and my God!
042029 Jesus said to him, Thomas, because you have seen Me you have believed. Blessed are they who have not seen and have believed.
042030 And truly Jesus did many other signs in the presence of His disciples, which are not written in this book.
042031 But these are written so that you might believe that Jesus is the Christ, the Son of God, and that believing you might have life in His name.
042101 After these things Jesus revealed Himself again to the disciples at the Sea of Tiberias. And He revealed Himself this way:
042102 Simon Peter, and Thomas called the Twin, and Nathanael from Cana in Galilee, and the sons of Zebedee, and two others of His disciples were together.
042103 Simon Peter said to them, I am going out to fish. They said to him, We will go with you also. They went out and entered into a boat immediately. And that night they caught nothing.
042104 But when the morning had come, Jesus stood on the shore. But the disciples did not know that it was Jesus.
042105 Then Jesus said to them, Children, do you have anything to eat? They answered Him, No.
042106 And He said to them, Cast the net on the right side of the boat and you will find. Therefore they cast, and now they no longer had the strength to draw, from the multitude of fish.
042107 Then that disciple whom Jesus loves said to Peter, It is the Lord! Then hearing that it is the Lord, Simon Peter girded on his coat (for he was naked), and cast himself into the sea.
042108 And the other disciples came in a little boat (for they were not far from land, only about two hundred cubits), dragging the net of fish.
042109 Then when they went up on the land, they saw a fire of coals there, and a fish lying on it , and bread.
042110 And Jesus said to them, Bring from the fish which you have now caught.
042111 Simon Peter went up and drew the net to land, full of big fish, a hundred and fifty-three. And though there were so many, the net was not torn.
042112 Jesus said to them, Come, break fast. And none of the disciples dared to ask Him, Who are You? knowing that it was the Lord.
042113 Then Jesus came and took the bread and gave to them, and in the same way the little fish.
042114 This is now the three times Jesus was revealed to His disciples, He being risen from the dead.
042115 Then when they broke fast, Jesus said to Simon Peter, Simon, son of Jonah, do you love Me more than these? He said to Him, Yes, Lord, You know that I love You. He said to him, Feed My lambs.
042116 He said to him the second time, Simon, son of Jonah, do you love Me? He said to Him, Yes, Lord, You know that I love You. He said to him, Feed My sheep.
042117 He said to him the third time, Simon, son of Jonah, do you love Me? Peter was grieved because He said to him a third time , Do you love Me? And he said to Him, Lord, You know all things, You know that I love You. Jesus said to him, Feed My sheep.
042118 Truly, truly, I say to you, When you were young, you girded yourself and walked where you wished. But when you grow old, you shall stretch forth your hands and another shall gird you and carry you where you do not wish.
042119 He spoke this signifying by what death he should glorify God. And when He had spoken this, He said to him, Follow Me.
042120 Then Peter, turning around, saw the disciple whom Jesus loved following (the one who also leaned on His breast at supper, and said, Lord, who is he who betrays You?)
042121 Seeing him, Peter said to Jesus, Lord, and what of this one?
042122 Jesus said to him, If I desire that he remain until I come, what is that to you? You follow Me.
042123 Then this saying went abroad among the brothers, that that disciple should not die. Yet Jesus did not say to him, He shall not die, but, If I desire that he remain until I come, what is that to you?
042124 This is the disciple who testifies of these things and wrote these things. And we know that his testimony is true.
042125 And there are also many things, whatever Jesus did, which, if they should be written singly, I suppose the world itself could not contain the books that would be written. Amen.
050101 Truly, O Theophilus, I made the first report as to all things that Jesus began both to do and teach
050102 until the day He was taken up, having given directions to the apostles whom He chose, through the Holy Spirit;
050103 to whom He also presented Himself living after His suffering by many infallible proofs, being seen by them through forty days, and speaking of the things pertaining to the kingdom of God.
050104 And having met with them , He commanded them not to depart from Jerusalem, but to await the promise of the Father which you heard from Me.
050105 For John truly baptized with water, but you shall be baptized in the Holy Spirit not many days from now.
050106 Then, indeed, these coming together, they asked Him, saying, Lord, do You at this time restore the kingdom to Israel?
050107 And He said to them, It is not for you to know the times or the seasons, which the Father has put in His own authority.
050108 But you shall receive power, the Holy Spirit coming upon you. And you shall be witnesses to Me both in Jerusalem and in all Judea, and in Samaria, and to the end of the earth.
050109 And saying these things, as they watched, He was taken up. And a cloud received Him out of their sight.
050110 And while they were looking intently into the heaven, He having gone, even behold, two men in white clothing stood beside them,
050111 who also said, Men of Galilee, why do you stand gazing up into the heaven? This same Jesus who is taken up from you into Heaven, will come in the way you have seen Him going into Heaven.
050112 Then they returned to Jerusalem from the mount Of Olive Grove, which is a sabbath day's journey from Jerusalem.
050113 And when they had come in, they went up into an upper room, where Peter and James, and John and Andrew, Philip and Thomas, Bartholomew and Matthew, James the son of Alpheus and Simon Zelotes, and Judas the brother of James;
050114 these all were continuing with one accord in prayer and supplication, with the women and Mary the mother of Jesus, and with His brothers.
050115 And in those days Peter stood up in the midst of the disciples and said, ( the number of names together was about a hundred and twenty,)
050116 Men, brothers, this Scripture must have been fulfilled, which the Holy Spirit by the mouth of David spoke before concerning Judas, who became guide to those who seized Jesus.
050117 For he was numbered with us and had obtained part of this ministry.
050118 Indeed, then, this one purchased a field with the reward of unrighteousness. And falling headlong, he burst apart in the middle, and all his bowels gushed out.
050119 And it was known to all the dwellers at Jerusalem, so much so that that field is called in their own dialect, Akeldama, that is to say, Field of Blood.
050120 For it is written in the Book of Psalms, "Let his estate become forsaken, and he not be living in it." And, "Let another take his overseership."
050121 Therefore, it is right that one of these men who have companied with us all the time that the Lord Jesus came in and went out among us,
050122 beginning from the baptism of John to that same day that He was taken up from us, to become a witness with us of His resurrection.
050123 And they appointed two, Joseph called Barsabas, who was surnamed Justus, and Matthias.
050124 And they prayed and said, You, Lord, knower of all hearts, show which one You chose from these two,
050125 to take the share of this ministry and apostleship from which Judas fell, to go to his own place.
050126 And they gave forth their lots. And the lot fell upon Matthias. And he was numbered with the eleven apostles.
050201 And in the fulfilling of the day of Pentecost, they were all with one accord in one place.
050202 And suddenly a sound came out of the heaven as borne along by the rushing of a mighty wind, and it filled all the house where they were sitting.
050203 And tongues as of fire appeared to them, being distributed; and it sat upon each of them.
050204 And they were all filled of the Holy Spirit, and began to speak in other languages, as the Spirit gave them utterance.
050205 And dwelling at Jerusalem there were Jews, devout men out of every nation under heaven.
050206 But this sound occurring, the multitude came together and were confounded, because they each heard them speaking in his own dialect.
050207 And they were all amazed and marveled, saying to one another, Behold, are not these who speak all Galileans?
050208 And how do we each hear in our own dialect in which we were born?
050209 Parthians, and Medes, and Elamites, and the dwellers in Mesopotamia, and in Judea, and Cappadocia, in Pontus, and Asia,
050210 Phrygia, and Pamphylia, in Egypt, and in the parts of Libya around Cyrene, and strangers of Rome, Jews and proselytes,
050211 Cretans and Arabians, we hear them speaking the great things of God in our own languages.
050212 And they were all amazed, and were in doubt, saying to one another, What does this mean?
050213 But others mocking said, These men are full of sweet wine.
050214 But Peter, standing up with the Eleven, lifted up his voice and said to them, Men, Jews, and all who dwell at Jerusalem, let this be known to you, and listen to my words.
050215 For these are not drunk as you suppose, for it is the third hour of the day.
050216 But this is that which was spoken by the prophet Joel:
050217 "And it shall be in the last days, says God, I will pour out of My Spirit upon all flesh. And your sons and your daughters shall prophesy, and your young men shall see visions, and your old men shall dream dreams.
050218 And in those days I will pour out My Spirit upon My slaves and My slave women, and they shall prophesy.
050219 And I will give wonders in the heaven above, and miracles on the earth below, blood and fire and vapor of smoke.
050220 The sun shall be turned into darkness and the moon into blood, before that great and glorious Day of the Lord.
050221 And it shall be that everyone who shall call upon the name of the Lord shall be saved."
050222 Men, Israelites, hear these words. Jesus of Nazareth, a man approved of God among you by powerful works, and wonders and miracles, which God did through Him in your midst, as you yourselves also know,
050223 this One given to you by the before-determined counsel and foreknowledge of God, you have taken and by lawless hands, crucifying Him , you put Him to death;
050224 whom God raised up, having loosed the pains of death, because it was not possible that He should be held by it.
050225 For David speaks concerning Him, "I foresaw the Lord always before me, because He is at my right hand, that I should not be moved.
050226 Therefore my heart rejoiced and my tongue was glad; and also My flesh shall rest in hope,
050227 because You will not leave My soul in Hades, nor will You allow Your holy One to see corruption.
050228 You revealed to Me the ways of life. You will fill Me with joy with Your countenance."
050229 Men, brothers, it is permitted to say to you with plainness as to the patriarch David, that he is both dead and buried, and his tomb is with us to this day.
050230 Therefore being a prophet, and knowing that God had sworn with an oath to him that of the fruit of his loins, according to the flesh, He would raise up Christ to sit upon his throne,
050231 seeing this beforehand, he spoke of the resurrection of Christ, that His soul was not left in Hades, nor would His flesh see corruption,
050232 God raised up this Jesus, of which we all are witnesses.
050233 Therefore being exalted to the right of God, and having received from the Father the promise of the Holy Spirit, He has poured out this which you now see and hear.
050234 For David has not ascended into the heavens, but he says himself, "The LORD said to my Lord, Sit at My right hand
050235 until I place Your enemies as a footstool to Your feet."
050236 Therefore let all the house of Israel know assuredly that God made this same Jesus, whom you crucified, both Lord and Christ.
050237 And hearing this , they were stabbed in the heart, and said to Peter and to the other apostles, Men, brothers, what shall we do?
050238 Then Peter said to them, Repent and be baptized, every one of you, in the name of Jesus Christ to remission of sins, and you shall receive the gift of the Holy Spirit.
050239 For the promise is to you and to your children, and to all those afar off, as many as the Lord our God shall call.
050240 And with many other words he earnestly testified and exhorted, saying, Be saved from this perverse generation.
050241 Then those who gladly received his word were baptized. And the same day there were added about three thousand souls.
050242 And they were continuing steadfastly in the apostles' doctrine, and in fellowship and in the breaking of the loaves, and in prayers.
050243 And fear came on every soul. And many wonders and miracles took place through the apostles.
050244 And all who believed were together and had all things common.
050245 And they sold their possessions and goods and distributed them to all, according as anyone had need.
050246 And continuing with one accord in the temple, and breaking bread from house to house, they shared food with gladness and simplicity of heart,
050247 praising God and having favor with all the people. And the Lord added to the church daily those who were being saved.
050301 And on the same day Peter and John went up into the temple at the hour of prayer, the ninth hour .
050302 And a certain man, who was lame from his mother's womb, was being carried. And they laid him daily at that temple gate which is called Beautiful, to ask alms from those who entered into the temple.
050303 Seeing Peter and John about to go into the temple, he asked to receive alms.
050304 And fastening his eyes on him, Peter with John said, Look on us!
050305 And he paid heed to them, expecting to receive something from them.
050306 But Peter said, Silver and gold have I none, but what I have I give you. In the name of Jesus Christ of Nazareth, rise up and walk!
050307 And taking him by the right hand, he lifted him up. And immediately his feet and ankle-bones received strength.
050308 And leaping up, he stood and walked and entered with them into the temple, walking and leaping and praising God.
050309 And all the people saw him walking and praising God.
050310 And they recognized him, that it was him who sat for alms at the Beautiful Gate of the temple. And they were filled with wonder and amazement at what had happened to him.
050311 And as the lame one who was healed held Peter and John, all the people ran together to them in the porch that is called Solomon's, greatly wondering.
050312 And seeing this , Peter answered the people, Men, Israelites, why do you marvel at this? Or why do you stare at us, as though we had made this man to walk by our own power or holiness?
050313 The God of Abraham and of Isaac and of Jacob, the God of our fathers, has glorified His son Jesus, whom you delivered up, denying Him in the presence of Pilate, when he had decided to let Him go.
050314 But you denied the Holy and Just One and desired a murderer to be given to you.
050315 And you killed the Prince of Life, whom God has raised from the dead, of which we are witnesses.
050316 And His name, through faith in His name, has made this man strong, this one whom you see and know, His name made firm. And the faith which came through Him has given him this perfect soundness before you.
050317 And now, brothers, I know that you did it through ignorance, as also your rulers did .
050318 But those things which God before had shown by the mouth of all His prophets, that Christ should suffer, He fulfilled in this manner.
050319 Therefore repent and convert so that your sins may be blotted out, when the times of refreshing shall come from the presence of the Lord.
050320 And He shall send Jesus Christ, who before was proclaimed to you,
050321 whom Heaven truly needs to receive until the times of restoration of all things, which God has spoken by the mouth of His holy prophets since the world began.
050322 For Moses truly said to the fathers, " The Lord your God shall raise up a Prophet to you from your brothers, One like me. You shall hear Him in all things, whatever He may say to you.
050323 And it shall be that every soul who will not hear that Prophet shall be destroyed from among the people."
050324 And also all the prophets from Samuel and those following after, as many as spoke, have likewise foretold of these days.
050325 You are the sons of the prophets and of the covenant which God made with our fathers, saying to Abraham, "And in your Seed shall all the kindreds of the earth be blessed."
050326 Having raised up His son Jesus, God sent Him to you first, to bless you in turning every one of you away from his iniquities.
050401 And as they spoke to the people, the priests, and the temple commander, and the Sadducees came on them,
050402 being grieved that they taught the people, even to announce through Jesus the resurrection from the dead.
050403 And they laid hands on them and put them under guard until the next day, for it was already evening.
050404 But many of those who heard the Word believed; and the number of the men was about five thousand.
050405 And it happened on the next day that their rulers and elders and scribes, gathered to Jerusalem,
050406 and Annas the high priest, and Caiaphas, and John, and Alexander, and as many as were of the kindred of the high priest.
050407 And when they had set them in the midst, they asked, By what power, or by what name have you done this?
050408 Then Peter, filled with the Holy Spirit, said to them, Rulers of the people and elders of Israel,
050409 if we are examined today on a good work for an infirm man, by what this one has been healed,
050410 be it known to you all, and to all the people of Israel, that by the name of Jesus Christ of Nazareth, whom you crucified, whom God raised from the dead, in this name does this man stand before you whole.
050411 This is the Stone which you builders have counted worthless, and He has become the Head of the Corner.
050412 And there is salvation in no other One; for there is no other name under Heaven given among men by which we must be saved.
050413 But seeing the boldness of Peter and John, and perceiving that they were unlearned and uneducated men, they marveled. And they recognized them, that they had been with Jesus.
050414 And beholding the man who was healed standing with them, they could say nothing against it .
050415 And when they had commanded them to go aside out of the sanhedrin, they conferred among themselves,
050416 saying, What shall we do to these men? For that indeed a notable miracle has been done by them is plain to all those dwelling in Jerusalem. And we cannot deny it .
050417 But, so that it spread no further among the people, let us strictly threaten them, that they speak to no man in this name from now on.
050418 And they called them and commanded them not to speak at all, nor to teach in the name of Jesus.
050419 But Peter and John answered and said to them, Whether it is right before God to listen to you more than to God, you judge.
050420 For we cannot but speak the things which we have seen and heard.
050421 So when they had further threatened them, they let them go, finding no way as to how they might punish them, because of the people. For all glorified God for that which was done.
050422 For the man on whom this miracle of healing occurred was more than forty years old .
050423 And being let go, they went to their own company and reported what the chief priests and elders had said to them .
050424 And having heard, they lifted up their voice to God with one accord and said, Lord, You are the God who made the heaven and earth, and the sea, and all that is in them;
050425 who by the mouth of Your servant David has said, "Why did the nations rage and the people imagine vain things?
050426 The kings of the earth stood up, and the rulers were gathered together against the Lord and against His Christ."
050427 For truly, against Your holy child Jesus, whom You have anointed, both Herod and Pontius Pilate, with the nations, and the people of Israel, were gathered together
050428 in order to do whatever Your hand and Your counsel determined before to be done.
050429 And now, Lord, behold their threatenings, and grant to Your servants that with all boldness they may speak Your Word,
050430 by stretching forth of Your hand for healing, and miracles, and wonders may be done by the name of Your holy child Jesus.
050431 And when they had prayed, the place where they were assembled was shaken. And they were all filled with the Holy Spirit, and they spoke the Word of God with boldness.
050432 And the multitude of those who believed were of one heart and one soul. And not one said that any of the things which he possessed was his own. But they had all things common.
050433 And the apostles gave witness of the resurrection of the Lord Jesus with great power. And great grace was on them all.
050434 For neither was anyone needy among them, for as many as were owners of lands or houses sold them and brought the prices of the things that were sold,
050435 and they laid them down at the apostles' feet. And distribution was made to every man according as he had need.
050436 And Joses, who was surnamed Barnabas by the apostles (which is, being translated, The son of consolation), a Levite, a Cypriot by race,
050437 a field being his, selling it , he bore the proceeds and placed them at the apostles' feet.
050501 And a certain man named Ananias, with Sapphira his wife, sold a possession.
050502 And he kept back part of the price, his wife also knowing, and brought a certain part and laid it at the apostles' feet.
050503 But Peter said, Ananias, why has Satan filled your heart for you to lie to the Holy Spirit, and to keep back part of the price of the land?
050504 While it remained, was it not your own? And after it was sold, was it not in your own authority? Why have you conceived this thing in your heart? You have not lied to men, but to God.
050505 And hearing these words, Ananias fell down and expired. And great fear came on all those who heard these things.
050506 And the younger ones arose, wound him up, and carrying him out, they buried him .
050507 And it was about the space of three hours afterward, when his wife (not knowing what was done) came in.
050508 And Peter answered her, Tell me whether you sold the land for so much? And she said, Yes, for so much.
050509 Then Peter said to her, How is it that you have agreed together to tempt the Spirit of the Lord? Behold, the feet of those who have buried your husband are at the door and they will carry you out.
050510 Then at once she fell down at his feet and expired. And the younger ones found her dead, and, carrying her out, buried her beside her husband.
050511 And great fear came on all the church and on as many as heard these things.
050512 And many miracles and wonders were done among the people by the hands of the apostles; and they were all with one accord in Solomon's Porch.
050513 And of the rest no one dared to join himself to them, but the people magnified them;
050514 and more believing ones were added to the Lord, multitudes both of men and women;
050515 So as to carry out the sick into the streets and place them on cots and mattresses, so that at least the shadow of Peter passing by might overshadow some of them.
050516 And also a multitude came from the cities around Jerusalem, bringing sick ones, and those being tormented by unclean spirits, who were all healed.
050517 And rising up, the high priest, and all those who were with him (which is the sect of the Sadducees) were filled with anger,
050518 And laid their hands on the apostles and put them in the public custody.
050519 But the angel of the Lord opened the prison doors by night and brought them out, and said,
050520 Go! Stand and speak all the words of this Life to the people in the temple.
050521 And hearing, they went into the temple about dawn, and taught. But the high priest came, and those with him. And they called the sanhedrin together, and all the elderhood of the sons of Israel, and sent to the prison to have them brought.
050522 But having come near, the officers did not find them in the prison. And returning, reported,
050523 saying, We indeed found the prison shut with all safety, and the keepers standing outside in front of the doors. But having opened it, we found no one inside.
050524 And when the high priest and the temple commander and the chief priests heard these things, they were bewildered about them, what this might be.
050525 But one came, reporting to them, saying, Behold, the men whom you put in prison are standing in the temple and teaching the people.
050526 Then the commander went with the officers and brought them, not with force, for they feared the people, lest they should be stoned.
050527 And bringing them, they stood in the sanhedrin. And the high priest asked them,
050528 saying, Did we not strictly command you that you not teach in this name? And behold, you have filled Jerusalem with your doctrine and intend to bring this man's blood on us.
050529 And Peter and the apostles answered and said, We ought to obey God rather than men.
050530 The God of our fathers raised up Jesus, whom you killed and hanged on a tree.
050531 This One God has exalted to be a Ruler and Savior to His right hand in order to give repentance and remission of sins to Israel.
050532 And we are His witnesses of these things. And so also is the Holy Spirit, whom God has given to those who obey Him.
050533 But those hearing were cut to the heart , and they took counsel to kill them.
050534 Then there stood up one in the sanhedrin, a Pharisee named Gamaliel, a doctor of the law honored among all the people. And he commanded the apostles to be put outside a little space.
050535 And he said to them, Men of Israel, take heed to yourselves what you intend to do regarding these men.
050536 For before these days Theudas rose up, boasting himself to be somebody; a number of men, about four hundred, joined themselves to him; who was slain. And all, as many as obeyed him, were scattered and brought to nothing.
050537 After this one, Judas of Galilee rose up in the days of the Registration, and drew away considerable people after him. Yet that one perished; and all, as many as obeyed him, were scattered.
050538 And now I say to you, withdraw from these men and let them alone. For if this counsel or this work is of men, it will come to nothing.
050539 But if it is of God, you cannot overthrow it, lest perhaps you be found even to fight against God.
050540 And they obeyed him. And calling the apostles, beating them , they commanded not to speak in the name of Jesus, and let them go.
050541 Then indeed they departed from the presence of the sanhedrin, rejoicing that they were counted worthy to be shamed for His name.
050542 And every day in the temple, and from house to house, they did not cease teaching and preaching the gospel: Jesus Christ.
050601 And in those days, the disciples having multiplied, a murmuring of the Hellenists against the Hebrews occurred, because their widows were overlooked in the daily serving.
050602 And the Twelve called near the multitude of the disciples and said, It is not pleasing to us, leaving the Word of God, to serve tables.
050603 Therefore, brothers, look out among you seven men being witnessed to, full of the Holy Spirit and wisdom, whom we may appoint over this duty.
050604 But we will give ourselves continually to prayer and to the ministry of the Word.
050605 And the saying pleased all the multitude. And they chose Stephen, a man full of faith and of the Holy Spirit, and Philip, and Prochorus, and Nicanor, and Timon, and Parmenas, and Nicholas, a proselyte of Antioch.
050606 They set these before the apostles. And having prayed, they laid hands on them.
050607 And the word of God was increasing. And the number of the disciples in Jerusalem was multiplying exceedingly; even a great crowd of the priests obeyed the faith.
050608 And Stephen, full of faith and power, did great wonders and miracles among the people.
050609 Then there arose certain of the synagogue which is called the synagogue of the Libertines, and Cyrenians, and Alexandrians, and of those from Cilicia and from Asia, disputing with Stephen.
050610 And they were not able to resist the wisdom and the Spirit by which he spoke.
050611 And they induced men to be saying, We have heard him speak blasphemous words against Moses and God.
050612 And they stirred up the people and the elders and the scribes. And coming on, they seized him and brought him to the sanhedrin.
050613 And they set up false witnesses, who said, This man does not cease speaking blasphemous words against this holy place and the Law.
050614 For we have heard him say that this Jesus of Nazareth shall destroy this place, and shall change the customs which Moses delivered to us.
050615 And looking intently at him. all those sitting in the sanhedrin saw his face as if it were the face of an angel.
050701 Then the high priest said, Then do you so hold these things?
050702 And he said, Men, brothers, and fathers, listen: The God of glory appeared to our father Abraham when he was in Mesopotamia, before he lived in Haran.
050703 And He said to him, "Go out from your land and from your kindred, and come into a land which I shall show you."
050704 Then he came out of the land of the Chaldeans and lived in Haran. And from there, when his father was dead, he moved into this land in which you now dwell.
050705 And He gave him no inheritance in it, no, not even a foot-breadth. And He promised that He would give it to him for a possession, and to his seed after him, there being no child to him.
050706 And God spoke in this way, that his seed would be a tenant in another land, and that they would enslave it and oppress it four hundred years.
050707 And God said, "I will judge the nation to whom they shall be in bondage," and "after these things they will come out and will serve Me in this place."
050708 And He gave him the covenant of circumcision. And so Abraham fathered Isaac and circumcised him the eighth day. And Isaac fathered Jacob, and Jacob the twelve patriarchs.
050709 And being jealous of Joseph, the patriarchs sold Joseph into Egypt. But God was with him
050710 and plucked him out from all his afflictions, and He gave him favor and wisdom over against Pharaoh king of Egypt. And he appointed him governor over Egypt and all his household.
050711 But a famine came over all the land of Egypt and Canaan, and a great affliction. And our fathers found no food.
050712 But hearing grain was in Egypt, Jacob sent out our fathers first.
050713 And at the second time Joseph was made known to his brothers, and Joseph's race was made known to Pharaoh.
050714 And seeing, Joseph called his father Jacob, and all his kindred, seventy-five souls.
050715 And Jacob went down into Egypt and died, he and our fathers,
050716 and were carried over into Shechem. And they were laid in the tomb that Abraham bought for a price of silver from the sons of Emmor the father of Shechem.
050717 But as the time was drawing near, of the promise which God had sworn to Abraham, the people grew and multiplied in Egypt,
050718 until another king arose who did not know Joseph.
050719 Dealing subtly with our race, this one oppressed our fathers, causing their infants to be exposed, so as not to be left alive.
050720 In this time Moses was born, and was beautiful to God, who was brought up three months in his father's house.
050721 And he being cast out, Pharaoh's daughter took him up and reared him for a son to her.
050722 And Moses was learned in all the wisdom of the Egyptians and was mighty in words and in deeds.
050723 And when a period of forty years was fulfilled to him, it arose in his heart to look upon his brothers, the sons of Israel.
050724 And seeing one being wronged, he defended him . and avenged him who was oppressed and struck the Egyptian.
050725 For he thought his brothers would understand that God would give them deliverance by his hand. But they did not understand.
050726 And the next day he appeared to them while fighting. And he urged them to peace, saying, Men, you are brothers, why do you wrong one another?
050727 But he who wronged his neighbor thrust him away, saying, Who made you a ruler and a judge over us?
050728 Will you not kill me as you did the Egyptian yesterday?
050729 And Moses fled at this word, and became a temporary resident in the land of Midian, where he fathered two sons.
050730 And forty years being fulfilled to him, the Angel of the Lord appeared to him in the desert of Mount Sinai in a flame of fire in a bush.
050731 And seeing it , Moses marveled at the sight. And as he drew near to see, the voice of the Lord came to him:
050732 saying , "I am the God of your fathers, the God of Abraham, and the God of Isaac, and the God of Jacob." But Moses trembled and dared not look.
050733 Then the Lord said to him, "Loosen the sandal on your feet, for the place where you stand is holy ground."
050734 "I have seen, the affliction of My people in Egypt, and I have heard their groan; and I came down to pluck them out. And now come, I will send you into Egypt."
