050735 This Moses whom they refused, saying, Who made you a ruler and a judge? God has sent this one to be a ruler and a redeemer by the hand of the Angel who appeared to him in the Bush.
050736 He brought them out after he had worked wonders and miracles in the land of Egypt and in the Red Sea and in the wilderness forty years.
050737 This is that Moses who said to the sons of Israel, " The Lord your God shall raise up a Prophet to you from your brothers, One like me; you shall hear Him."
050738 This is he who was in the congregation in the wilderness with the Angel who spoke to him in Mount Sinai, and with our fathers, who received the living words to give to us,
050739 to whom our fathers would not be obedient, but thrust him away and turned back again to Egypt in their hearts,
050740 saying to Aaron, "Make us gods to go before us, for as for this Moses who brought us out of the land of Egypt, we do not know what has become of him."
050741 And they made a calf in those days and offered sacrifice to the idol and rejoiced in the work of their own hands.
050742 Then God turned and gave them over to serve the host of the heavens, as it is written in the book of the Prophets: "O house of Israel, have you offered to Me slain beasts and sacrifices forty years in the wilderness?
050743 Yea, you took up the tabernacle of Moloch, and the star of your god Remphan, images which you made in order to worship them; and I will remove you beyond Babylon."
050744 The tabernacle of witness was among our fathers in the wilderness, as commanded by God , speaking to Moses to make it according to the pattern that he had seen.
050745 Which also having received it by inheritance with Joshua, our fathers, with Joshua, in taking possession of the nations whom God drove out before the face of our fathers until the days of David,
050746 who found favor with God and desired to find a tabernacle for the God of Jacob;
050747 but Solomon built Him a house.
050748 But, the Most High does not dwell in temples made with hands, as the prophet says,
050749 "Heaven is My throne and earth is My footstool. What house will you build Me, says the Lord, or what is the place of My rest?
050750 Has not My hand made all these things?"
050751 O stiff-necked and uncircumcised in heart and ears! You always resist the Holy Spirit. As your fathers did , so you do.
050752 Which of the prophets did your fathers not persecute? And they killed those who foretold the coming of the Just One, of whom you have now been the betrayers and murderers;
050753 who received the Law through disposition of angels, and did not keep it.
050754 And hearing these things, they were cut to their hearts. And they gnashed on him with their teeth.
050755 But being full of the Holy Spirit, looking up intently into Heaven, he saw the glory of God, and Jesus standing at the right hand of God.
050756 And he said, Behold, I see Heaven opened and the Son of man standing on the right hand of God.
050757 And crying out with a loud voice, they stopped their ears and ran on him with one accord.
050758 And throwing him outside the city, they stoned him . And the witnesses laid their clothes down at the feet of a young man named Saul.
050759 And they stoned Stephen, who was calling on God and saying, Lord Jesus, receive my spirit.
050760 And kneeling down, he cried with a loud voice, Lord, do not lay this sin to their charge. And when he had said this, he fell asleep.
050801 And Saul was consenting to his death. And in that day there was a great persecution on the church at Jerusalem, and all were scattered throughout the regions of Judea and Samaria, except the apostles.
050802 And devout men buried Stephen and made a great mourning over him.
050803 But Saul ravaged the church, entering into every house. And dragging men and women, he delivered them up to prison.
050804 Then, indeed, the ones who had been scattered passed through, preaching the gospel, the Word.
050805 And Philip went down to the city of Samaria and proclaimed Christ to them.
050806 And the people with one accord gave heed to those things which Philip spoke, hearing and seeing the many miracles which he did.
050807 For out of those having unclean spirits, many came out, crying with loud voice. And many who had been paralyzed and lame were healed.
050808 And there was great joy in that city.
050809 But a certain man called Simon had long been conjuring in the city, and amazing the nation of Samaria, claiming himself to be some great one.
050810 All gave heed to him , from the least to the greatest, saying, This one is the great power of God.
050811 And they were paying attention to him, because for a long time he had amazed them with conjuring.
050812 But when they believed Philip preaching the gospel, the things concerning the kingdom of God and the name of Jesus Christ, they were baptized, both men and women.
050813 Then Simon himself believed also, and being baptized, he continued with Philip. And seeing miracles and mighty works happening, he was amazed.
050814 And the apostles in Jerusalem hearing that Samaria had received the Word of God, they sent Peter and John to them;
050815 who when they had come down, prayed for them that they might receive the Holy Spirit.
050816 For as yet He had not fallen on any of them, they were baptized only in the name of the Lord Jesus.
050817 Then they laid their hands on them, and they received the Holy Spirit.
050818 And when Simon saw that the Holy Spirit was given through laying on of the apostles' hands, he offered them money,
050819 saying, Give me this power also, that on whomever I lay hands, he may receive the Holy Spirit.
050820 But Peter said to him, May your silver perish with you, because you have thought that the gift of God may be purchased with money.
050821 You have neither part nor lot in this matter, for your heart is not right in the sight of God.
050822 Therefore repent of this wickedness of yours, and pray God if perhaps the thought of your heart may be forgiven you.
050823 For I see that you are in the gall of bitterness and in the bond of iniquity.
050824 And answering Simon said, You pray to the Lord for me that none of these things which you have spoken may come on me.
050825 Then, indeed, having earnestly testified and having spoken the Word of the Lord also having preached the gospel to many villages of the Samaritans, they returned to Jerusalem.
050826 And the angel of the Lord spoke to Philip, saying, Arise and go toward the south, on the way that goes down from Jerusalem to Gaza, which is a deserted place .
050827 And he arose and went. And behold, a man of Ethiopia, a eunuch of great authority under Candace queen of the Ethiopians, who had charge of all her treasure and had come to Jerusalem to worship,
050828 was returning. And sitting in his chariot he read Isaiah the prophet.
050829 Then the Spirit said to Philip, Go near and join yourself to this chariot.
050830 And Philip ran there to him and heard him read the prophet Isaiah, and said, Do you indeed understand what you are reading?
050831 And he said, How can I unless some man should guide me? And he asked Philip to come up and sit with him.
050832 And the content of the Scripture which he read was this: "He was led as a sheep to the slaughter, and like a lamb dumb before his shearer, so He opened not His mouth.
050833 In His humiliation His judgment was taken away, and who shall declare His generation? For His life is taken from the earth."
050834 And the eunuch answered Philip and said, I beg you, of whom does the prophet speak this? Of himself or of some other man?
050835 Then Philip opened his mouth and began at the same Scripture and preached the gospel of Jesus to him.
050836 And as they passed along the way, they came on some water. And the eunuch said, See, here is water, what hinders me from being baptized?
050837 Philip said, If you believe with all your heart, it is lawful. And he answered and said, I believe that Jesus Christ is the Son of God.
050838 And he commanded the chariot to stand still. And they both went down into the water, both Philip and the eunuch. And he baptized him.
050839 And when they had come up out of the water, the Spirit of the Lord caught Philip away, so that the eunuch saw him no more. And he went on his way rejoicing.
050840 But Philip was found at Azotus. And passing through, he preached the gospel in all the cities until he came to Caesarea.
050901 And Saul, still breathing out threatenings and slaughter against the disciples of the Lord, went to the high priest
050902 and asked letters from him to Damascus to the synagogues; so that if he found any of the Way, whether they were men or women, he might bring them bound to Jerusalem.
050903 But in going, it happened as he drew near to Damascus, even suddenly a light from the heaven shone around him.
050904 And he fell to the earth and heard a voice saying to him, Saul, Saul, why do you persecute Me?
050905 And he said, Who are you, lord? And the Lord said, I am Jesus whom you persecute. It is hard for you to kick against the goads.
050906 And trembling and astonished, he said, Lord, what will You have me to do? And the Lord said to him, Arise and go into the city, and you shall be told what you must do.
050907 And the men who journeyed with him stood speechless, indeed hearing a voice but seeing no one.
050908 And Saul was lifted up from the earth, his eyes were opened, but he saw no one. But they led him by the hand and brought him into Damascus.
050909 And he was three days not seeing, and did not eat or drink.
050910 And there was a certain disciple in Damascus named Ananias. And the Lord said to him in a vision, Ananias! And he said, Behold me, Lord.
050911 And the Lord said to him, Arise and go into the street which is called Straight and inquire in the house of Judas for one called Saul of Tarsus. For behold, he is praying,
050912 and has seen in a vision a man named Ananias coming in and putting his hand on him so that he might receive his sight.
050913 And Ananias answered, Lord, I have heard from many of this man, how many evil things he has done to Your saints at Jerusalem.
050914 And here he has authority from the chief priests to bind all who call on Your Name.
050915 But the Lord said to him, Go! For this one is a chosen vessel to Me, to bear My name before nations and kings and the sons of Israel.
050916 For I will show him what great things he must suffer for My name's sake.
050917 And Ananias went and entered into the house. And putting his hands on him, he said, Brother Saul, the Lord, Jesus, who appeared to you in the way in which you came, has sent me to you that you might see and be filled with the Holy Spirit.
050918 And instantly scales as it were fell from his eyes, and he instantly saw again. And rising up, he was baptized.
050919 And taking food, he was strengthened. And Saul was certain days with the disciples in Damascus.
050920 And immediately he proclaimed Christ in the synagogues, that He is the Son of God.
050921 But all who heard him were amazed and said, Is this not he who destroyed those who called on this name in Jerusalem and came here for that reason, that he might bring them bound to the chief priests?
050922 But Saul increased the more in strength and confounded the Jews who lived at Damascus, proving that this One is the Christ.
050923 And after many days had been fulfilled, the Jews took counsel to kill him.
050924 But their plot was known to Saul. And they watched the gates day and night in order to kill him.
050925 Then the disciples took him by night and let him down through the wall in a basket.
050926 And arriving in Jerusalem, Saul attempted to join himself to the disciples. But they were all afraid of him, and did not believe that he was a disciple.
050927 But Barnabas took him and brought him to the apostles and told them how he had seen the Lord in the way, and that He had spoken to him, and how he had spoken boldly in Damascus in the name of Jesus.
050928 And he was with them, coming in and going out in Jerusalem.
050929 And he spoke boldly in the name of the Lord Jesus, and argued with the Hellenists. But they seized him in order to kill him.
050930 But knowing, the brothers brought him down to Caesarea and sent him forth to Tarsus.
050931 Then, indeed, the churches had rest throughout all Judea and Galilee and Samaria, and having been built up. And having gone on in the fear of the Lord and in the comfort of the Holy Spirit, they were increased.
050932 And it happened, passing through all, Peter also came down to the saints who lived at Lydda.
050933 And there he found a certain man named Aeneas, who had lain eight years on a mattress, paralyzed.
050934 And Peter said to him, Aeneas, Jesus the Christ heals you; rise up and spread for yourself! And he arose immediately.
050935 And all who lived at Lydda and Sharon saw him and turned to the Lord.
050936 And in Joppa was a certain disciple named Tabitha (which translated is called Dorcas). She was full of good works and kind deeds which she did.
050937 And it happened in those days, becoming sick, she died. And washing her, they laid her in an upper room.
050938 And, because Lydda was near Joppa, hearing that Peter is in it, the disciples sent two men to him, begging him not to delay to come to them.
050939 And rising up, Peter went with them. When he had come, they brought him into the upper room. And all the widows stood beside him, weeping and showing the coats and garments which Dorcas made while she was with them.
050940 And putting them all out, Peter knelt down and prayed. And turning to the body he said, Tabitha, arise! And she opened her eyes. And when she saw Peter, she sat up.
050941 And he gave her his hand and lifted her up. And when he had called the saints and widows, he presented her alive.
050942 And it was known throughout all Joppa. And many believed in the Lord.
050943 And it was many days that he remained in Joppa, with one Simon, a tanner.
051001 And a certain man named Cornelius was in Caesarea, a centurion of the Italian cohort,
051002 one devout and fearing God, with all his household, both doing many merciful deeds to the people, and praying continually to God.
051003 About the ninth hour of the day he saw plainly in a vision an angel of God coming to him and saying to him, Cornelius!
051004 And he was gazing at him, and becoming terrified, he said, What is it, lord? And he said to him, Your prayers and your merciful deeds have come up for a memorial before God.
051005 And now send men to Joppa and call for Simon, whose last name is Peter.
051006 He is staying with one Simon a tanner, whose house is by the seaside. He will tell you what you must do.
051007 And when the angel who spoke to Cornelius departed, he called two of his servants and a devout soldier from those who waited on him continually.
051008 And explaining all things to them, he sent them to Joppa.
051009 On the next day, as these went on the road, and drawing near the city, Peter went up on the housetop to pray, about the sixth hour.
051010 And he became very hungry and desired to eat. But while they made ready, an ecstasy fell on him.
051011 And he saw the heaven opened and a certain vessel like a sheet coming down to him, being bound at the four corners and let down to the earth;
051012 in which were all the four-footed animals of the earth, and the wild beasts, and the reptiles, and the birds of the heaven.
051013 And a voice came to him, saying, Rise, Peter! Kill and eat!
051014 But Peter said, Not so, Lord, for I have never eaten anything that is common or unclean.
051015 And the voice spoke to him again the second time , What God has made clean, you do not call common.
051016 This happened three times , and the vessel was received up again into the heaven.
051017 And while Peter doubted within himself what the vision which he had seen might be, even behold, the men who were sent from Cornelius had asked for Simon's house and stood on the porch.
051018 And they called and asked if Simon whose last name is Peter was staying there.
051019 And while Peter thought on the vision, the Spirit said to him, Behold, three men are looking for you.
051020 Therefore arise and go down and go with them without doubting, for I have sent them.
051021 And going down to the men, those sent to him from Cornelius, Peter said, Behold, I am the one you are seeking. For what reason have you come?
051022 And they said, Cornelius the centurion, a just man and one who fears God, and one of good report among all the nation of the Jews, was warned from God by a holy angel to send for you to come to his house and to hear words from you.
051023 Then he called them in and lodged them . And on the next day Peter went away with them, and certain brothers from Joppa went with him.
051024 And the next day they entered into Caesarea. And Cornelius was waiting for them, and had called together his kinsmen and near friends.
051025 And as Peter was coming in, Cornelius met him and fell down at his feet and worshiped.
051026 But Peter took him up, saying, Stand up! I also am a man myself.
051027 And as he talked with him, he went in and found many who had come together.
051028 And he said to them, You know that it is an unlawful thing for a man, a Jew to keep company with or to come near to one of another nation. But God has shown me not to call any man common or unclean.
051029 Therefore I came without complaint, being sent for. I ask, then, for what reason have you sent for me.
051030 And Cornelius said, Four days ago I was fasting until this hour. And at the ninth hour I prayed in my house, and behold, a man stood before me in bright clothing.
051031 And he said, Cornelius, your prayer is heard, and your merciful deeds have been remembered before God.
051032 Therefore send to Joppa and call here Simon whose last name is Peter, he is staying in the house of Simon, a tanner by the seaside; who, when he comes, shall speak to you.
051033 Therefore I immediately sent to you, and you have done well to come. Now therefore we are all here present before God to hear all things that are commanded you by God.
051034 Then Peter opened his mouth and said, Truly I see that God is no respecter of persons;
051035 but in every nation he who fears Him and works righteousness is accepted with Him.
051036 You know the word which God sent to the sons of Israel, preaching the gospel of peace by Jesus Christ (He is Lord of all!);
051037 that word which was published throughout all Judea, and began from Galilee, after the baptism which John proclaimed;
051038 how God anointed Jesus of Nazareth with the Holy Spirit and with power, and He went about doing good, and healing all those who were oppressed by the Devil, for God was with Him.
051039 And we are witnesses of all things which He did, both in the land of the Jews and in Jerusalem. They killed Him and hanged Him on a tree;
051040 but God raised Him up the third day and showed Him openly,
051041 not to all the people, but to witnesses hand-picked before by God, even to us who ate and drank with Him after He rose from the dead.
051042 And He commanded us to preach to the people, and to testify that it is He who was ordained of God to be the Judge of the living and the dead.
051043 All the prophets give witness to Him, that through His name whoever believes in Him shall receive remission of sins.
051044 While Peter was still speaking these words, the Holy Spirit fell on all those hearing the Word.
051045 And those of the circumcision, who believed (as many as came with Peter), were astonished because the gift of the Holy Spirit was poured out on the nations also.
051046 For they heard them speak with tongues and magnify God. Then Peter answered,
051047 Can anyone forbid water that these, who have received the Holy Ghost as well as we, should not be baptized?
051048 And he commanded them to be baptized in the name of the Lord. Then they begged him to stay certain days.
051101 And the apostles and brothers who were in Judea heard that the nations had also received the Word of God.
051102 And when Peter had come up to Jerusalem, those of the circumcision contended with him,
051103 saying, You went in to uncircumcised men and ate with them.
051104 But Peter related the matter from the beginning and explained it by order to them, saying,
051105 I was in the city of Joppa praying. And in an ecstasy I saw a vision, a certain vessel like a sheet coming down, let down from the sky by four corners. And it came even to me.
051106 When I had fastened my eyes on it , I looked and saw four-footed animals of the earth, and wild beasts, and reptiles, and birds of the heaven.
051107 And I heard a voice saying to me, Arise, Peter! Kill and eat!
051108 But I said, Not so, Lord, for nothing common or unclean has at any time entered into my mouth.
051109 But the voice answered me again from the heaven, What God has made clean, you do not call common.
051110 And this was done three times , and all were drawn up again into the heaven.
051111 And behold, immediately three men stood at the house in which I was, sent from Caesarea to me.
051112 And the Spirit told me to go with them, not discriminating. And these six brothers went with me, and we entered the man's house.
051113 And he declared to us how he had seen an angel in his house, who stood and said to him, Send men to Joppa and call for Simon whose last name is Peter,
051114 who will tell you words by which you and all your house shall be saved.
051115 And as I began to speak, the Holy Spirit fell on them, as on us at the beginning.
051116 And I remembered the Word of the Lord, how He said, John indeed baptized with water, but you shall be baptized with the Holy Spirit.
051117 If God gave to them the same gift as to us, they having believed on the Lord Jesus Christ, who was I to be able to prevent God?
051118 When they heard these things, they were silent and glorified God, saying, Then God has also granted repentance to life to the nations.
051119 Then, indeed, they who were scattered abroad by the persecution that rose about Stephen traveled as far as Phoenicia and Cyprus and Antioch, preaching the Word to no one except the Jews.
051120 And some of them were men of Cyprus and Cyrene; who, when they had come to Antioch, spoke to the Hellenists, preaching the gospel of the Lord Jesus.
051121 And the hand of the Lord was with them, and a great number believed and turned to the Lord.
051122 And the Word was heard in the ears of the church in Jerusalem. And they sent out Barnabas, that he should go as far as Antioch;
051123 who was glad when he had come and had seen the grace of God. And he exhorted all with purpose of heart to remain near to the Lord.
051124 For he was a good man and full of the Holy Spirit and faith. And many people were added to the Lord.
051125 And Barnabas went out to Tarsus to seek Saul.
051126 And finding him, he brought him to Antioch. And it happened to them a whole year they were assembled in the church. And they taught a considerable crowd. And the disciples were first called Christian in Antioch.
051127 And in these days prophets from Jerusalem came to Antioch.
051128 And one of them named Agabus stood up and signified by the Spirit that there should be great famine over the world (which also happened in the days of Claudius Caesar).
051129 And the disciples, as any were prospered, determined each of them to send for ministry to those brothers who lived in Judea,
051130 which they also did, sending to the elders by the hand of Barnabas and Saul.
051201 And at that time Herod the king threw on his hands to oppress some of those of the church.
051202 And he killed James the brother of John with the sword.
051203 And because he saw it pleased the Jews, he went further to seize Peter also. (And they were days of Unleavened Bread .)
051204 And capturing him , he put him in prison, and delivered him to four sets of four soldiers to keep him; intending to bring him out to the people after the Passover.
051205 Then, indeed, Peter was kept in prison. But earnest prayer was made to God for him by the church.
051206 And when Herod was about to bring him out, the same night Peter was sleeping between two soldiers, bound with two chains. Also guards were keeping the prison before the door.
051207 And behold! An angel of the Lord stood by, and a light shone in the building. And striking Peter's side, he raised him up, saying, Rise up quickly! And his chains fell off his hands.
051208 And the angel said to him, Gird yourself and put on your sandals. And he did so. And he says to him, Throw your robe around you and follow me.
051209 And he went out and followed him. And he did not know that this happening through the angel was true, but thought he saw a vision.
051210 When they were past the first and second guard, they came to the iron gate that leads to the city, which opened to them of its own accord. And they went out and passed on through one street. And immediately the angel departed from him.
051211 And having come to himself, Peter said, Now I know surely that the Lord has sent His angel and has delivered me out of the hand of Herod, and from all the expectation of the people of the Jews.
051212 And thinking about it , he came to the house of Mary the mother of John, whose last name was Mark; where many had gathered together to pray.
051213 And as Peter knocked at the door of the porch, a girl named Rhoda came to listen.
051214 And when she knew Peter's voice, she did not open the porch because of gladness, but running in she reported Peter was standing before the porch.
051215 And they said to her, You are mad. But she kept on saying that it was so. And they said, It is his angel.
051216 But Peter continued knocking, and when they had opened and saw him, they were amazed.
051217 But, waving to them with his hand to be quiet, he declared to them how the Lord had brought him out of the prison. And he said, Go tell these things to James and to the brothers. And he departed and went into another place.
051218 And day coming, there was not a little stir among the soldiers, saying, What, then, became of Peter.
051219 And searching for him, and not finding him , examining the guards, Herod commanded them to be led away to death. And he went down from Judea to Caesarea and stayed.
051220 And Herod was in bitter hostility with the men of Tyre and Sidon. But they came to him with one accord and, having made Blastus (who had charge of the king's bedroom) their friend, desired peace, because their country was fed by the king's country .
051221 And on a certain day, Herod sat on his throne, dressed in royal clothing, and made a speech to them.
051222 And the people gave a shout, saying, It is the voice of a god and not of a man!
051223 And immediately the angel of the Lord struck him, because he did not give God the glory. And he was eaten by worms and gave up the spirit.
051224 But the Word of God grew and increased.
051225 And Barnabas and Saul returned from Jerusalem when they had fulfilled the ministry, having taken with them John, whose last name was Mark.
051301 And in Antioch some among the existing church were prophets and teachers. (such as Barnabas, and Simeon who was called Niger, and Lucius of Cyrene, and Manaen, the foster-brother of Herod the tetrarch) and Saul.
051302 As they ministered to the Lord and fasted, the Holy Spirit said, So, then, separate Barnabas and Saul to Me for the work to which I have called them.
051303 Then having fasted and prayed and laid hands on them, they let them go.
051304 Then these indeed sent out by the Holy Spirit went down to Seleucia. And from there they sailed to Cyprus.
051305 And when they were at Salamis, they announced the Word of God in the synagogues of the Jews. And they also had John as an assistant.
051306 And when they had gone through the island to Paphos, they found a certain conjurer, a false prophet, a Jew whose name was Bar-jesus;
051307 who was with the proconsul of the country, Sergius Paulus, a prudent man. He called for Barnabas and Saul and asked to hear the Word of God.
051308 But Elymas the conjurer (for so his name is, if translated) withstood them, seeking to turn the proconsul away from the faith.
051309 Then Saul (who is also Paul), filled with the Holy Spirit, set his eyes on him
051310 and said, O son of the Devil, full of all deceit and all craftiness, enemy of all righteousness, will you not stop perverting the right ways of the Lord?
051311 And now, behold, the hand of the Lord is on you. And you shall be blind, not seeing the sun for a while. And immediately a mist and a darkness fell on him, and he went about seeking some to lead him by the hand.
051312 Then, seeing the thing happening, the proconsul believed, being astonished at the doctrine of the Lord.
051313 And Paul and those around him sailed from Paphos and came to Perga of Pamphylia. And John left them and returned to Jerusalem.
051314 But going through from Perga, they came to Antioch in Pisidia and went into the synagogue on the sabbath day and sat down.
051315 And after the reading of the Law and the Prophets, the rulers of the synagogue sent to them, saying, Men, brothers, if you have any word of comfort for the people, speak.
051316 And rising up and signaling with his hand, Paul said, Men, Israelites, and those fearing God, listen.
051317 The God of this people Israel chose our fathers and exalted the people in their residency in the land of Egypt, and He brought them out of it with a high arm.
051318 And about the time of forty years He tenderly bore them in the wilderness.
051319 And when He had destroyed seven nations in the land of Canaan, he gave their land to them as an inheritance.
051320 And after that He gave them judges for about four hundred and fifty years, until Samuel the prophet.
051321 And afterward they asked for a king. And God gave them Saul the son of Kish, a man of the tribe of Benjamin, for forty years.
051322 And when He had removed him, He raised up David to them to be their king; to whom He also witnessed and said, I have found David the son of Jesse to be a man after My own heart, who shall fulfill all My will.
051323 Of this man's seed God has raised to Israel, according to His promise, a Savior, Jesus;
051324 John having before proclaimed the baptism of repentance to all the people of Israel, before His coming.
051325 And as John fulfilled his course, he said, Who do you think that I am? I am not He . But behold, One comes after me, the sandals of whose feet I am not worthy to loose.
051326 Men, brothers, sons of the race of Abraham, and whoever among you fears God, the word of this salvation is sent to you.
051327 For those living in Jerusalem, and their rulers, not having known this One, and the voices of the prophets being read throughout every sabbath, condemning Him , they fulfilled the Scriptures .
051328 And finding not one cause of death in Him , they begged Pilate to do away with Him.
051329 And when they had fulfilled all that was written concerning Him, taking Him down from the tree, they laid Him in a tomb.
051330 But God raised Him from the dead,
051331 who appeared for many days by those who came up with Him from Galilee to Jerusalem, who are His witnesses to the people.
051332 And we preach the gospel to you, the promise made to the fathers,
051333 this God has fulfilled to us their children, raising up Jesus, as also it is written in the second Psalm, "You are My Son, this day I have begotten You."
051334 And that He raised Him up from the dead, no more to return to corruption, He spoke in this way: "I will give you the holy promises of David."
051335 Therefore he also says in another psalm , "You shall not allow Your Holy One to see corruption."
051336 For after he had served his own generation by the will of God, David fell asleep and was added to his fathers and saw corruption.
051337 But He whom God raised again saw no corruption.
051338 Therefore be it known to you, men, brothers, that through this One the forgiveness of sins is announced to you.
051339 And by Him all who believe are justified from all things, from which you could not be justified by the law of Moses.
051340 Therefore beware lest that come on you which is spoken of in the prophets:
051341 "Behold, you despisers, and marvel, and perish; for I work a work in your days, a work which you shall in no way believe, though a man declare it to you."
051342 And the Jews having gone out of the synagogue, the nations begged that these words might be preached to them the next sabbath.
051343 And the synagogue being broken up, many of the Jews and of the devout proselytes followed Paul and Barnabas; who, speaking to them, persuaded them to continue in the grace of God.
051344 And on the coming sabbath day almost all the city came together to hear the Word of God.
051345 But when the Jews saw the multitudes, they were filled with envy and contradicted those things which were spoken by Paul, contradicting and blaspheming.
051346 But speaking boldly, Paul and Barnabas said, It was necessary for the word of God to be spoken to you first. But since indeed you put it far from you and judge yourselves unworthy of everlasting life, lo, we turn to the nations.
051347 For so the Lord has commanded us, saying , "I have set You to be a light of the nations, for salvation to the end of the earth."
051348 And hearing, the nations rejoiced and glorified the Word of the Lord. And as many as were ordained to eternal life believed.
051349 And the Word of the Lord was carried throughout all the country.
051350 But the Jews stirred up the devout and honorable women, and the chief ones of the city, and raised a persecution against Paul and Barnabas. And they threw them out of their borders.
051351 But shaking the dust of their feet off on them, they came into Iconium.
051352 And the disciples were filled with joy and with the Holy Spirit.
051401 And it happened in Iconium, they both went together into the synagogue of the Jews, and spoke so as a great multitude both of the Jews and also of the Greeks believed.
051402 But the unbelieving Jews stirred up the nations and made them evil-hearted against the brothers.
051403 Therefore they stayed a long time, speaking boldly in the Lord, who bore witness to the word of His grace, giving miracles and wonders to be done by their hands.
051404 But the multitude of the city was divided. And part held with the Jews, and part with the apostles.
051405 And when there was an assault made by both the nations and the Jews, with their rulers, in order to insult and to stone them,
051406 they were aware of it and fled to Lystra and Derbe, cities of Lycaonia, and to the country around them.
051407 And there they were preaching the gospel.
051408 And a certain man was sitting in Lystra, without strength in the feet, being lame from his mother's womb, who never had walked.
051409 This one heard Paul speaking; and Paul , looking intently at him, and seeing that he had faith to be healed,
051410 said with a loud voice, Stand up on your feet! And he leaped and walked.
051411 And seeing what Paul did, the crowd lifted up their voice, saying in Lycaonian, The gods have come down to us, becoming like men.
051412 And they called Barnabas Jupiter, and Paul Mercury, because he was the chief speaker.
051413 And the priest of Jupiter, being before their city, brought oxen and garlands to the gates, wishing to sacrifice with the crowds.
051414 But hearing this , the apostles Barnabas and Paul tore their clothes and ran in among the people, crying out
051415 and saying, Men, why do you do these things? We also are men of like passions with you, and preaching the gospel to you to turn you from these vanities to the living God, who made the heaven and the earth and the sea, and all things in them;
051416 who in past generations allowed all nations to walk in their own ways.
051417 And yet He did not leave Himself without witness, doing good, giving rain and fruitful season to us from heaven, filling our hearts with food and gladness.
051418 And saying these things, they scarcely stopped the people from sacrificing to them.
051419 And Jews from Antioch and Iconium came there, who, having persuaded the people, and having stoned Paul, they drew him out of the city, supposing him to have died.
051420 But the disciples surrounding him, he rose up and came into the city. And the next day he departed with Barnabas to Derbe.
051421 And preaching the gospel to that city, and having made many disciples, they returned to Lystra and Iconium and Antioch,
051422 confirming the souls of the disciples, calling on them to continue in the faith and that through much tribulation we must enter into the kingdom of God.
051423 And having hand-picked elders for them in every church, and had prayed with fastings, they commended them to the Lord into whom they believed.
051424 And passing through Pisidia, they came to Pamphylia.
051425 And speaking the word in Perga, they went down to Attalia.
051426 And from there they sailed to Antioch, from where they had been recommended to the grace of God for the work which they fulfilled.
051427 And having arrived, and gathering the church they related all that God had done with them, and how He had opened the door of faith to the nations.
051428 And they stayed there not a little time with the disciples.
051501 And certain ones who came down from Judea taught the brothers, saying , Unless you are circumcised according to the custom of Moses, you cannot be saved.
051502 Therefore dissension and not a little disputation occurring by Paul and Barnabas, they appointed Paul and Barnabas and certain others of them to go up to Jerusalem to the apostles and elders about this question.
051503 And indeed being set forward by the church, they passed through Phoenicia and Samaria, declaring the conversion of the nations. And they caused great joy to all the brothers.
051504 And arriving in Jerusalem, they were received by the church, and by the apostles and elders. And they declared all things that God had done with them.
051505 But some of those from the sect of the Pharisees, having believed, rose up, saying, It was necessary to circumcise them and to command them to keep the law of Moses.
051506 And the apostles and elders were assembled to see about this matter.
051507 And after much disputing, Peter rose up and said to them, Men, brothers, you recognize that from ancient days God chose among us that through my mouth the nations should hear the word of the gospel, and believe.
051508 And God, who knows the hearts, bore them witness, giving them the Holy Spirit even as to us.
051509 And He put no difference between us and them, purifying their hearts by faith.
051510 Now therefore why do you tempt God by putting a yoke on the neck of the disciples, a yoke which neither our fathers nor we were able to bear?
051511 But we believe that through the grace of the Lord Jesus Christ we shall be saved, according to which manner they also believed.
051512 And all the multitude kept silent and listened to Barnabas and Paul declaring what miracles and wonders God had worked among the nations through them.
051513 And after they were silent, James answered, saying, Men, brothers, listen to me.
051514 Even as Simon has declared how God at the first visited the nations to take out of them a people for His name.
051515 And the words of the prophets agree to this; as it is written,
051516 "After this I will return and will build again the tabernacle of David which has fallen down; and I will build again its ruins, and I will set it up,
051517 so those men who are left might seek after the Lord, and all the nations on whom My name has been called, says the Lord, who does all these things."
051518 All His works are known to God from eternity.
051519 Therefore my judgment is that we do not trouble those who have turned to God from among the nations,
051520 but that we write to them that they should abstain from pollutions of idols, and from fornication, and from things strangled, and from blood.
051521 For Moses from ages past has those in every city proclaiming him, being read in the synagogues every sabbath day.
051522 Then it pleased the apostles and elders, with the whole church, to send chosen men from them to Antioch with Paul and Barnabas; Judas, whose last name was Barsabas; and Silas, chief men among the brothers.
051523 And they wrote these things by their hand: The apostles and elders and brothers send greeting to the brothers, from the nations in Antioch and Syria and Cilicia.
051524 Because we have heard that certain ones who went out from us have troubled you with words, unsettling your souls, saying, Be circumcised and keep the law! (to whom we gave no such command);
051525 it seemed good to us, being assembled with one accord, to send chosen men to you with our beloved Barnabas and Paul,
051526 men who have given up their lives for the name of our Lord Jesus Christ.
051527 Therefore we have sent Judas and Silas, who will also announce to you the same things by word.
051528 For it seemed good to the Holy Spirit and to us to lay on you no greater burden than these necessary things:
051529 that you abstain from meats offered to idols, and from blood, and from things strangled, and from fornication; from which, if you keep yourselves, you shall do well. Be prospered.
051530 Then indeed they being let go, they came to Antioch. And gathering the multitude, they delivered the letter.
051531 And when they had read it , they rejoiced at the comfort.
051532 And Judas and Silas, also being prophets themselves, exhorted the brothers with many words and confirmed them .
051533 And remaining for a time, they were let go in peace from the brothers to the apostles.
051534 But it pleased Silas to remain there.
051535 Also Paul and Barnabas continued in Antioch, teaching and preaching the gospel, the Word of the Lord, with many others also.
051536 And some days afterward, Paul said to Barnabas, Let us go again and visit our brothers in every city where we have announced the Word of the Lord, to see how they are holding to it.
051537 And Barnabas determined to take with them John, he being called Mark.
051538 But Paul thought it well not to take that one with them , he having withdrawn from them from Pamphylia, and did not go with them to the work.
051539 Then there was sharp feeling, so as to separate them from each other. And taking Mark, Barnabas sailed to Cyprus.
051540 But choosing Silas, Paul went out, being commended by the brothers to the grace of God,
051541 passing through Syria and Cilicia, making the churches strong.
051601 And he came to Derbe and Lystra. And behold, a certain disciple named Timothy was there, the son of a woman who was a Jewess and who believed. But his father was a Greek.
051602 He was well reported of by the brothers at Lystra and Iconium.
051603 Paul wanted him to go with him, and taking him he circumcised him, because of the Jews who were in those places; for they all knew that his father was a Greek.
051604 And as they passed through the cities, they delivered to them the commandments to keep, the ones that were ordained by the apostles and elders in Jerusalem.
051605 Then indeed the churches were established in the faith and increased in number daily.
051606 And coming through the Phrygian and the Galatian region; and by the Holy Spirit being forbidden to speak the Word in Asia;
051607 having come to Mysia, they attempted to go into Bithynia. But the Spirit did not allow them.
051608 Then passing by Mysia, they came down into Troas.
051609 And a vision appeared to Paul in the night. A certain man of Macedonia stood, begging him, saying, Come over into Macedonia and help us!
051610 And after he saw the vision, we immediately tried to go into Macedonia, gathering that the Lord had called us in order to preach the gospel to them.
051611 Then having set sail from Troas, we came with a straight course to Samothracia, and the next day to Neapolis;
051612 and from there to Philippi, which is the chief city of that part of Macedonia, a colony. And we continued spending time in that city some days.
051613 And on the sabbath we went out of the city by a river side, where prayer was usually made. And we sat down and spoke to the women who came together there .
051614 And a certain woman named Lydia heard us, a seller of purple of the city of Thyatira, who worshiped God; whose heart the Lord opened, so that she attended to the things which were spoken by Paul.
051615 And when she was baptized, she and her household, she begged us, saying, If you have judged me to be faithful to the Lord, come into my house and stay. And she constrained us.
051616 And as we went to prayer, it happened that a certain girl possessed with a spirit of divination met us, who brought her masters much gain by divining.
051617 The same followed Paul and us and cried, saying, These men are the servants of the Most High God, who are announcing to us the way of salvation.
051618 And she did this many days. But being distressed, and turning to the demonic spirit, Paul said, I command you in the name of Jesus Christ to come out of her! And it came out in that hour.
051619 And when her masters saw that the hope of their gain went out, having seized Paul and Silas, they dragged them to the market before the rulers.
051620 And bringing them near to the judges, they said, These men, being Jews, are exceedingly troubling our city.
051621 And they teach customs which are not lawful for us to receive nor to do, being Romans.
051622 And the crowd rose up against them. And tearing off their clothes, the judges ordered them to be flogged.
051623 And after laying on them many stripes, they threw them into prison, commanding the jailor to keep them safely;
051624 who, having received such a command, thrust them into the inner prison and made their feet fast in the stocks.
051625 And toward midnight Paul and Silas prayed and praised God in a hymn. And the prisoners listened to them.
051626 And suddenly there was a great earthquake, so that the foundations of the prison were shaken. And immediately all the doors were opened and all the bonds were loosened.
051627 And being awakened, and seeing the doors of the prison being open, drawing a sword, the jailer was about to kill himself, supposing that the prisoners had escaped.
051628 But Paul called out with a loud voice, saying, Do yourself no harm, for we are all here.
051629 Then asking for a light he rushed in and fell trembling before Paul and Silas.
051630 And leading them outside, he said, Sirs, what must I do to be saved?
051631 And they said, Believe on the Lord Jesus Christ and you shall be saved, and your household.
051632 And they spoke the Word of the Lord to him, and to all who were in his household.
051633 And taking them in that hour of the night, he washed from their stripes. And he was baptized, he and all his, immediately.
051634 And bringing them up to the house, he set a table before them and rejoiced, believing in God with all his household.
051635 And day coming, the judges sent the floggers, saying, Let those men go.
051636 And the jailer spoke these words to Paul: The judges have sent to let you go. Now therefore depart, and go in peace.
051637 But Paul said to them, Having beaten us publicly, men who are Romans and uncondemned, they threw us into prison. And now do they put us out secretly? No indeed! But coming themselves, let them bring us out.
051638 And the floggers reported these words to the judges. And hearing that they were Romans, they were afraid.
051639 And coming they begged them . And bringing them out, they asked them to depart out of the city.
051640 And going out from the prison, they entered into the house of Lydia. And seeing the brothers, they comforted them and departed.
051701 And traveling through Amphipolis and Apollonia, they came to Thessalonica, where there was a synagogue of the Jews.
051702 And according to Paul's custom, he went in to them and reasoned with them out of the Scriptures on three sabbaths,
051703 opening and setting forth that Christ must have suffered, and to have risen again from the dead; and that this Jesus whom I preach to you is Christ.
051704 And some of them believed and joined themselves to Paul and Silas, both a great multitude of the worshiping Greeks, and not a few of the chief women.
051705 But the disobeying Jews becoming jealous, and having taken aside some wicked men of the market-loafers, and gathering a crowd, they set all the city in an uproar. And coming on the house of Jason, they sought to bring them out to the mob.
051706 And not finding them, they drew Jason and certain brothers before the city judges, crying, These who have turned the world upside down have come here too,
051707 whom Jason has received. And these all act contrary to the decrees of Caesar, saying that there is another king, Jesus.
051708 And hearing these things, they troubled the crowd and the city judge.
051709 And taking security from Jason and from the rest, they let them go.
051710 And the brothers immediately sent Paul and Silas away by night to Berea. They, when they arrived, went into the synagogue of the Jews.
051711 And these were more noble than those of Thessalonica, in that they received the Word with all readiness of mind and searched the Scriptures daily to see if those things were so .
051712 Therefore many of them believed, and quite a few of honorable Greek women and men.
051713 But when the Jews from Thessalonica knew that the Word of God was preached by Paul at Berea, they came there also and stirred up the people.
051714 And then immediately the brothers sent Paul away to go towards the sea, but both Silas and Timothy stayed there.
051715 And those conducting Paul brought him to Athens. And receiving a command to Silas and Timothy to come to him with all speed, they departed.
051716 But awaiting them in Athens, Paul's spirit was pained within him, seeing the city full of idols.
051717 Then indeed he addressed the Jews in the synagogue, and those worshiping, and daily in the market, to those happening to be there .
051718 And certain philosophers from the Epicureans and from the Stoics met him. And some said, What will this babbler say? And others said, He seems to be an announcer of foreign demons (because he preached Jesus and the resurrection to them).
051719 And taking hold of him, they led him to the Areopagus, saying, Are we able to know what is this new doctrine of which you speak?
051720 For you bring certain strange things to our ears, therefore we are minded to know what these things mean.
051721 (For all the Athenians and strangers who were there spent their time in nothing else except to tell or to hear something newer.)
051722 And standing in the middle of the Areopagus, Paul said, Men, Athenians, I see that you are fearful of gods in everything.
051723 For as I passed by and saw the things you worship, I also found an altar with this inscription: TO THE UNKNOWN GOD. Not knowing then whom you worship, I make Him known to you.
051724 The God who made the world and all things in it, since He is Lord of Heaven and earth, does not dwell in temples made with hands,
051725 nor is served with men's hands, as though He needed anything, since He gives life and breath and all things to all.
051726 And He has made all nations of men of one blood to dwell on all the face of the earth, ordaining fore-appointed seasons and boundaries of their dwelling,
051727 to seek the Lord, if perhaps they might feel after Him and find Him, though indeed He is not far from each one of us.
051728 For in Him we live and move and have our being, as also certain of your own poets have said, For we are also His offspring.
051729 Then being offspring of God, we ought not to think that the Godhead is like gold or silver or stone, engraved by art and man's imagination.
051730 Truly, then, God overlooking the times of ignorance, now He strictly commands all men everywhere to repent,
051731 because He has appointed a day in which He is going to judge the world in righteousness by a Man whom He appointed, having given proof to all by raising Him from the dead.
051732 And hearing of a resurrection of the dead, some indeed mocked; and others said, We will hear you again concerning this.
051733 And so Paul departed from among them.
051734 But certain men joined themselves to him and believed; among whom were Dionysius the Areopagite, and a woman named Damaris, and others with them.
051801 And after these things Paul departed from Athens and came to Corinth.
051802 And finding a certain Jew named Aquila, born in Pontus, lately come from Italy with his wife Priscilla (because Claudius had commanded all Jews to depart from Rome) Paul came to them.
051803 And because he was of the same trade, he stayed and worked with them; for they were tentmakers by occupation.
051804 And he reasoned in the synagogue on every sabbath, persuading both Jews and Greeks.
051805 And when Silas and Timothy had come from Macedonia, Paul was pressed in the spirit and testified to the Jews that Jesus is the Christ.
051806 And they resisting and blaspheming, shaking his garment, he said to them, Your blood is on your own heads. I am pure from it . From now on I will go to the nations.
051807 And he departed from there and entered into the house of one named Justus, one worshiping God, whose house was next to the synagogue.
051808 And Crispus, the chief ruler of the synagogue, believed on the Lord with all his house. And hearing this, many of the Corinthians believed and were baptized.
051809 And the Lord spoke to Paul in the night by a vision, Do not be afraid, but speak, and be not silent.
051810 For I am with you, and no one shall set on you to hurt you, for I have many people in this city.
051811 And he continued there a year and six months, teaching the Word of God among them.
051812 But Gallio being pro-consul of Achaia, the Jews with one accord rushed against Paul and brought him to the judgment seat,
051813 saying, This one persuades men to worship God contrary to the Law.
051814 And Paul being about to open his mouth, Gallio said to the Jews, If indeed then, it was anything wrong or wicked criminality, O Jews, according to reason I would endure you.
051815 But if it is a question of a word and names, and of your law, you look to it . For I do not wish to be a judge of such things.
051816 And he drove them from the judgment seat.
051817 And all the Greeks seized Sosthenes, the chief ruler of the synagogue, and beat him before the judgment seat. And Gallio did not care for any of these things.
051818 And Paul having remained many days more, taking leave of the brothers, he sailed from there into Syria. And Priscilla and Aquila were with him. And Paul had shorn his head in Cenchrea, for he had a vow.
051819 And he came to Ephesus and left them there. But he himself entered into the synagogue and reasoned with the Jews.
051820 And they asking him to stay a longer time with them, he did not consent
051821 but took leave of them, saying, I must by all means keep this feast that is coming in Jerusalem, but I will return again to you, God willing. And he sailed from Ephesus.
051822 And when he had landed at Caesarea and had gone up to greet the church, he went down to Antioch.
051823 And after he had spent some time there , he departed and went over the country of Galatia and Phrygia in order, strengthening all the disciples.
051824 And a certain Jew named Apollos, an Alexandrian by birth, an eloquent man mighty in the Scriptures, came to Ephesus.
051825 This man was instructed in the way of the Lord. And being fervent in the spirit, he spoke and taught the things of the Lord diligently, knowing only the baptism of John.
051826 And he began to speak boldly in the synagogue. And Aquila and Priscilla heard him, and they took him and expounded to him the way of God more perfectly.
051827 And intending to pass into Achaia, being encouraged, the brothers wrote to the disciples to welcome him; who, having arrived, very much helped those who had believed through grace.
051828 For he mightily confuted the Jews publicly, proving by the Scriptures that Jesus was the Christ.
051901 And it happened in the time Apollos was at Corinth, Paul was passing through the higher parts to Ephesus. And finding certain disciples,
051902 he said to them, Have you received the Holy Spirit since you believed? And they said to him, We did not so much as hear whether the Holy Spirit is.
051903 And he said to them, Then to what were you baptized? And they said, To John's baptism.
051904 And Paul said, John truly baptized with the baptism of repentance, saying to the people that they should believe into Him coming after him, that is, into Jesus Christ.
051905 And hearing, they were baptized in the name of the Lord Jesus.
051906 And as Paul laid his hands on them, the Holy Spirit came on them, and they spoke with tongues and prophesied.
051907 And all of the men were about twelve.
051908 And going into the synagogue, he spoke boldly for three months, reasoning and persuading the things concerning the kingdom of God.
051909 But when some were hardened and did not believe, speaking evil of the Way before the multitude, he departed from them and separated the disciples, reasoning daily in the school of one Tyrannus.
051910 And this happened over two years, so that all those living in Asia heard the Word of the Lord Jesus, both Jews and Greeks.
051911 And God did works of power through the hands of Paul,
051912 so that even handkerchiefs or aprons from his skin being brought onto the sick, the diseases were released, and the evil spirits went out of them.
051913 And certain from the strolling Jews, exorcists, undertook to name the name of the Lord Jesus over those having evil spirits, saying, We adjure you by Jesus whom Paul preaches.
051914 And there were seven sons of Sceva, a Jewish chief priest, who did so.
051915 But answering the evil spirit said, Jesus I know, and I comprehend Paul, but who are you?
051916 And the man in whom the evil spirit resided leaped on them, and overcoming them he was strong against them, so that they fled out of the house naked and wounded.
051917 And this was known to all the Jews and Greeks who lived at Ephesus, and fear fell on all of them, and the name of the Lord Jesus was magnified.
051918 And many who believed came and confessed and showed their deeds.
051919 Also many of those practicing the curious arts, bringing together the books, burned them before all. And they counted the prices of them and found it to be fifty thousand pieces of silver.
051920 So the Word of God grew mightily and prevailed.
051921 After these things were ended, passing through Macedonia and Achaia, Paul purposed in the spirit to go to Jerusalem, saying, After I have come there, I must also see Rome.
051922 And sending into Macedonia two who ministered to him, Timothy and Erastus, he stayed in Asia for a time.
051923 And about that time there was not a little a stir about the Way.
051924 For a certain silversmith named Demetrius was making silver temples of Artemis, providing not a little trade for the craftsmen.
051925 And assembling the workmen about such things, he said, Men, you know that from this trade is our wealth.
051926 And you see and hear that, not only at Ephesus, but almost all Asia, this Paul having persuaded, he has perverted a huge crowd, saying that those which are made with hands are no gods.
051927 And not only is this dangerous to us, our share coming into dispute, but also the temple of the great goddess Artemis will be counted for nothing, and her magnificence is also about to be destroyed, whom all Asia and the world worships.
051928 And hearing, and becoming full of anger, they cried out, saying, Great is Artemis of the Ephesians.
051929 And all the city was filled with confusion. And they rushed with one accord to the theater, keeping a firm grip on Gaius and Aristarchus, Macedonians, traveling companions of Paul.
051930 And Paul intending to go in to the mob, the disciples did not allow him.
051931 And some of the chief men of Asia, being his friends, sent to him, begging him not to give himself into the theater.
051932 Then indeed others cried out, some other things; for the assembly was confused, and most of them did not know why they had come together.
051933 And they dragged Alexander forward out of the crowd, the Jews thrusting him forward. And waving his hand Alexander desired to defend himself to the mob.
051934 But when they knew that he was a Jew, all with one voice cried out for two hours' time , Great is Artemis of the Ephesians!
051935 And quieting the crowd, the town clerk said, Men, Ephesians! What one of you does not know that the city of the Ephesians is a worshiper of the great goddess Artemis, and of That Fallen from the Sky?
051936 Since these things cannot be spoken against, you ought to be quiet and to do nothing rashly.
051937 For you have brought these men, who are neither robbers of churches nor blasphemers of your goddess.
051938 Therefore if Demetrius and those craftsmen with him truly have a matter against anyone, the court days are kept , and there are proconsuls. Let them plead against one another.
051939 But if you ask anything concerning other matters, it shall be determined in a lawful assembly.
051940 For we are in danger to be accused of revolt concerning today; there being no cause by which we may give an account of this crowding together.
051941 And saying these things, he dismissed the assembly.
052001 And after the uproar had ceased, calling the disciples and greeting them , Paul left to go into Macedonia.
052002 And passing through those parts, and exhorting them with much speech, he came into Greece.
052003 And spending three months there , there being a plot against him by the Jews, being about to sail into Syria, he proposed to return through Macedonia.
052004 And Sopater of Berea accompanied him into Asia, and Aristarchus and Secundus of the Thessalonians, and Gaius of Derbe, and Timothy, and Tychicus and Trophimus as far as Asia.
052005 Going before, these waited for us at Troas.
052006 And after the days of Unleavened Bread , we sailed away from Philippi and came to them at Troas in five days, where we stayed seven days.
052007 And on the first of the sabbaths, the disciples having been assembled to break bread, being about to depart on the morrow, Paul reasoned to them. And he continued his speech until midnight.
052008 And there were many lights in the upper room where they were assembled.
052009 And a certain young man named Eutychus was sitting on the window sill, Paul reasoning for a longer time, being overborne by sleep, he fell down from the third floor, and was taken up dead.
052010 And Paul went down and fell on him, and embracing him said, Do not be terrified, for his soul is in him.
052011 And going up, and breaking bread, and tasting, and conversing over a long time , until daybreak, he went out thus.
052012 And they brought the young man alive, and were not a little comforted.
052013 And going ahead onto the ship, we sailed to Assos, there intending to take in Paul; for so he had appointed, intending himself to go on foot.
052014 And when he met with us at Assos, we took him in and came to Mitylene.
052015 And we sailed from there and came the next day across from Chios. And the next day we arrived at Samos, and we stayed at Trogyllium. And the next day we came to Miletus.
052016 For Paul had determined to sail past Ephesus, so that he might not lose time in Asia; for, if it were possible for him, he hastened to be at Jerusalem on the day of Pentecost.
052017 And from Miletus he sent to Ephesus and called the elders of the church.
052018 And when they had come to him, he said to them, You know how I was with you at all times, from the first day I arrived in Asia,
052019 serving the Lord with all humility of mind, and many tears and temptations happening to me through the plots of the Jews;
052020 and how I kept back nothing that was profitable, but have shown you and have taught you publicly, and from house to house,
052021 testifying both to the Jews, and also to the Greeks, repentance toward God and faith toward our Lord Jesus Christ.
052022 And now, behold, I am going bound by the Spirit to Jerusalem, not knowing the things that shall happen to me there,
052023 except that the Holy Spirit witnesses in every city, saying that bonds and afflictions await me.
052024 But none of these things move me, neither do I count my life dear to myself, so that I might finish my course with joy, and the ministry which I received from the Lord Jesus Christ , to testify fully the gospel of the grace of God.
052025 And now, behold, I know that you all will see my face no more, among whom I went proclaiming the kingdom of God.
052026 Therefore I testify to you on this day that I am pure from the blood of all.
052027 For I did not keep back from declaring to you all the counsel of God.
052028 Therefore take heed to yourselves, and to all the flock over which the Holy Spirit has made you overseers, to feed the church of God which He has purchased with His own blood.
052029 For I know this, that after my departure grievous wolves shall enter in among you, not sparing the flock.
052030 Also men shall arise from your own selves, speaking perverse things in order to draw disciples away after them.
052031 Therefore watch and remember that for the time of three years I did not cease to warn everyone night and day with tears.
052032 And now, brothers, I commend you to God, and to the word of His grace, which is able to build you up and to give you an inheritance among all those who are sanctified.
052033 I have coveted no man's silver or gold or apparel.
052034 Yea, you yourselves know that these hands have ministered to my needs, and to those who were with me.
052035 I have shown you all things, that working in this way we ought to help the weak, and to remember the words of the Lord Jesus, that He Himself said, It is more blessed to give than to receive.
052036 And saying these things, kneeling, he prayed with them all.
052037 And there was much weeping of all, and falling on the neck of Paul, they ardently kissed him,
052038 grieving most of all over the word which he had spoken, that they should see his face no more. And they went with him to the ship.
052101 And it happened when it was time to sail, we having been torn away from them, running direct we came to Cos; and on the next day to Rhodes, and from there to Patara.
052102 And finding a ship sailing over to Phoenicia, going on board, we set sail.
052103 And sighting Cyprus, and leaving it on the left, we sailed into Syria, and came down to Tyre. For the ship was to unload its cargo there.
052104 And finding disciples, we stayed there seven days; who said to Paul through the Spirit that he should not go up to Jerusalem.
052105 But when it was time to finish the days, going out, we traveled on. And they with all the women and children went with us as far as outside the city. And we kneeled down on the shore and prayed.
052106 And giving parting greetings to one another, we went up into the ship; and they returned to their own things.
052107 And finishing the voyage from Tyre, we came to Ptolemais. And greeting the brothers, we stayed with them one day.
052108 And the next day those around him going out, Paul came to Caesarea. And entering the house of Philip the evangelist, he being of the seven, we stayed with him.
052109 And there were four virgin daughters to this one, who prophesied.
052110 And as we stayed more days, a certain prophet from Judea named Agabus came down.
052111 And coming to us, and taking Paul's belt, and binding his hands and feet, he said, The Holy Spirit says these things : So shall the Jews at Jerusalem bind the man whose belt this is, and will deliver him into the hands of the nations.
052112 And when we heard these things, both we and those of the place begged him not to go up to Jerusalem.
052113 Then Paul answered, What are you doing, weeping and breaking my heart? For I am ready not only to be bound, but also to die at Jerusalem for the name of the Lord Jesus.
052114 And he not being persuaded, we ceased, saying, The will of the Lord be done .
052115 And after those days, making ready, we went up to Jerusalem.
052116 Also some of the disciples from Caesarea went with us, bringing Mnason, a certain Cypriot, an old disciple with whom we were to lodge.
052117 And we being in Jerusalem, the brothers received us gladly.
052118 And on the next day Paul went with us to James. And all the elders were present.
052119 And having greeted them, he related one by one what things God had done among the nations by his ministry.
052120 And hearing, they glorified the Lord, and said to him, You see, brother, how many thousands of Jews there are who believe, and they are all zealous of the law.
052121 And they are informed concerning you, that you teach all the Jews who are among the nations to forsake Moses, saying that they ought not to circumcise their children, nor to walk after the customs.
052122 What is it therefore? At all events a multitude will come together, for they will hear that you have come.
052123 Therefore do this, what we say to you: We have four men who have a vow on themselves;
052124 taking them, be purified with them, and be at expense for them, so that they may shave their heads. And all may know that what they have been told about you is nothing, but you yourself also walk orderly and keep the Law.
052125 And as to the nations who believe, we joined in writing, judging them to observe no such things, except only that they keep themselves from both idol sacrifice, and blood, and a thing strangled, and from fornication.
052126 Then taking the men on the next day, being purified with them, Paul went into the temple, declaring the fulfillment of the days of the purification, until an offering should be offered for each of them.
052127 And when the seven days were about to be completed, the Jews who were from Asia, having seen him in the temple, stirred up all the crowd and laid hands on him,
052128 crying out, Men, Israelites, help! This is the man who teaches all everywhere against the people and the Law and this place. And even he brought Greeks into the temple and has polluted this holy place.
052129 (For they had seen Trophimus the Ephesian with him in the city before, whom they supposed that Paul had brought into the temple.)
052130 And all the city was moved, and the people ran together. And laying hands on Paul, they drew him outside of the temple. And immediately the doors were shut.
052131 And as they were seeking to kill him, the news came to the chiliarch of the cohort, that all Jerusalem was in an uproar.
052132 He immediately took soldiers and centurions, and ran down to them. And seeing the chiliarch and the soldiers, they quit beating Paul.
052133 Then going near, the chiliarch laid hold on him, and commanded him to be bound with two chains. And he demanded who he was and what he had done.
052134 And others cried something else in the crowd, and not being able to know the certainty on account of the uproar, he commanded him to be carried into the fortress.
052135 And when he came on the stairs, it happened that he was carried by the soldiers, because of the violence of the crowd.
052136 For the multitude of the people followed after, crying, Away with him!
052137 And as Paul was about to be led into the fortress, he said to the chiliarch, Is it lawful for me to say a thing to you? And he said, Do you know Greek?
052138 Then are you not the Egyptian who before these days caused a riot, and led four thousand men of the assassins out into the wilderness?
052139 But Paul said, I am a man, a Jew of Tarsus in Cilicia, a citizen of no small city. And I beseech you, allow me to speak to the people.
052140 And he allowing him, standing on the stairs, Paul signaled with his hand to the people. And much silence taking place, he spoke in the Hebrew dialect, saying:
052201 Men, brothers and fathers! Hear my defense now to you.
052202 And hearing that he spoke to them in the Hebrew dialect, they all the more kept silence. And he said,
052203 I am truly a man, a Jew born in Tarsus in Cilicia, yet brought up in this city at the feet of Gamaliel, taught according to the exactness of the law of the fathers, being a zealous one of God, as you all are today.
052204 I persecuted this Way as far as death, binding and delivering both men and women into prisons;
052205 as also the high priest bears witness to me, and all the elderhood. And receiving letters from them to the brothers, I traveled into Damascus indeed to lead those being bound to Jerusalem, in order that they might be punished.
052206 And it happened to me, traveling and drawing near to Damascus: suddenly, about midday, a great light out of the heaven shone around me.
052207 And I fell to the ground and heard a voice saying to me, Saul, Saul, why do you persecute Me?
052208 And I answered, Who are you, lord? And he said to me, I am Jesus of Nazareth, whom you persecute.
052209 And they who were with me indeed saw the light and were afraid. But they did not hear the voice of Him who spoke to me.
052210 And I said, What shall I do, Lord? And the Lord said to me, Arise and go into Damascus. And there it shall be told you all things which are appointed for you to do.
052211 And I did not see, because of the glory of that light; being led by the hand of those who were with me, I came into Damascus.
052212 And one Ananias, a devout man according to the law, testified to by all the Jews who lived there ,
052213 coming to me and standing by, said to me, Brother Saul, look up! And the same hour I looked up on him.
052214 And he said, The God of our fathers has chosen you to know His will and to see the Just One, and to hear a voice out of His mouth.
052215 For you shall be His witness to all men of what you have seen and heard.
052216 And now what do you intend? Arise and be baptized and wash away your sins, calling on the name of the Lord.
052217 And it happened to me, I returning to Jerusalem and praying in the temple, I became in an ecstasy.
052218 And I saw Him say to me, Hurry and go quickly out of Jerusalem, for they will not receive your testimony concerning Me.
052219 And I said, Lord, they know that I was imprisoning and beating those who believed on You throughout the synagogues.
052220 And when the blood of Your martyr Stephen was poured out, I also was standing by and consenting to his death, and holding the garments of those who killed him.
052221 And He said to me, Go, for I will send you far away to the nations.
052222 And they listened to him until this word, and then they lifted up their voice, saying, Take such a one from the earth! For it is not fitting that he should live.
052223 And as they shouted and tore their garments, and threw dust into the air,
052224 the chiliarch commanded him to be brought into the fortress, saying for him to be examined by scourging, so that he might know why they cried out so against him.
052225 And as they stretched him with thongs, Paul said to the centurion who stood by, Is it lawful for you to scourge a man who is a Roman and uncondemned?
052226 And hearing, coming near the centurion reported to the chiliarch, saying, Watch what you are about to do, for this man is a Roman.
052227 And coming up the chiliarch said to him, Tell me, are you a Roman? And He said, Yes.
052228 And the chiliarch answered, With a great sum I bought this citizenship. And Paul said, But I was even born free .
052229 Then immediately, those being about to examine him stood away from him. And the chiliarch also was afraid, fully knowing that he was a Roman, and that he had bound him.
052230 On the next day, he desiring to know with certainty why he was accused by the Jews, he freed him from his bonds, and commanded the chief priests and all their sanhedrin to appear. And bringing Paul down, he set him among them.
052301 And looking earnestly on the sanhedrin, Paul said, Men, brothers, I have lived in all good conscience before God until this day.
052302 And the high priest Ananias commanded those who stood by him to strike him on the mouth.
052303 Then Paul said to him, God shall strike you, whitened wall! For do you sit judging me according to the Law, and against law command me to be stricken?
052304 And they who stood by him said, Do you revile God's high priest?
052305 Then Paul said, I did not know, brothers, that he was the high priest; for it is written, "You shall not speak evil of the ruler of your people."
052306 But when Paul saw that the one part were Sadducees and the other part Pharisees, he cried out in the sanhedrin, Men! Brothers! I am a Pharisee, the son of a Pharisee! I am being judged because of the hope and resurrection of the dead.
052307 And when he had said this, there arose a dissension between the Pharisees and the Sadducees; and the multitude was divided.
052308 For the Sadducees say that there is no resurrection, neither angel, nor spirit; but the Pharisees confess both.
052309 And there arose a great cry. And the scribes who were on the Pharisees' side arose and strove, saying, We find no evil in this man. But if a spirit or an angel has spoken to him, let us not fight against God.
052310 And dissension arising, the chiliarch, fearing lest Paul should have been pulled in pieces by them, commanded the soldiers to go down and to take him from among them by force, and to bring him into the fortress.
052311 And the following night the Lord stood by him and said, Be of good cheer, Paul, for as you have testified of Me in Jerusalem, so you also must bear witness at Rome.
052312 And when it became day, some of the Jews banded together and bound themselves under a curse, saying that they would neither eat nor drink until they had killed Paul.
052313 And they who made this conspiracy were more than forty.
052314 And they came to the chief priests and elders and said, We have bound ourselves under a great curse that we will eat nothing until we have killed Paul.
052315 Now therefore you, with the sanhedrin, inform the chiliarch that he bring him down to you tomorrow, as though you would inquire something more perfectly regarding him. And we are ready to put him to death before he comes near.
052316 And hearing of the ambush, Paul's sister's son, having come near, and entering into the fortress, he reported to Paul.
052317 And calling one of the centurions, Paul said, Bring this young man to the chiliarch, for he has a certain thing to tell him.
052318 So he took him and brought him to the chiliarch and said, Paul the prisoner called me and asked me to bring this young man to you, who has something to say to you.
052319 And laying hold of his hand, and drawing aside privately, the chiliarch asked him , What is it that you have to tell me?
052320 And he said, The Jews have agreed to ask you to bring Paul down to the sanhedrin tomorrow, as though they would inquire something more exactly about him.
052321 But do not yield to them, for there are more than forty men of them lying in wait for him, who have bound themselves with an oath that they will neither eat nor drink until they have killed him. And now they are ready, looking for a promise from you.
052322 So the chiliarch sent away the young man commanding, Tell no one that you have shown these things to me.
052323 And he called two centurions, saying, Make ready two hundred soldiers to go to Caesarea, and seventy horsemen, and two hundred spearmen, at the third hour of the night.
