052324 And provide animals, so that they may set Paul on them and bring him to Felix the governor.
052325 And he wrote a letter in this way:
052326 Claudius Lysias, to the most excellent governor Felix, greetings.
052327 This man was taken by the Jews and would have been killed by them. Then I came with an army and rescued him, having understood that he was a Roman.
052328 And being minded to know the charge for which they accused him, I brought him down to their sanhedrin;
052329 whom I found be accused of questions of their law, and having no charge worthy of death or of bonds.
052330 And it being revealed to me that a plot against the man was about to be executed by the Jews, I immediately sent him to you, commanding his accusers also to say before you what they had against him. Farewell.
052331 Then, indeed, taking up Paul, as it was commanded them, the soldiers brought him by night to Antipatris.
052332 And on the next day they left the horsemen to go with him and returned to the fortress.
052333 And when they had come to Caesarea and had delivered the letter to the governor, they presented Paul before him also.
052334 And when the governor had read the letter , he asked what province he was from. And when he understood that he was from Cilicia,
052335 he said, I will hear you when your accusers have also come. And he commanded him to be kept in Herod's Praetorium.
052401 And after five days Ananias the high priest descended with the elders and with a certain orator, Tertullus, who made a statement to the governor against Paul.
052402 And being called, Tertullus began to accuse, saying,
052403 Since we enjoy great quietness by you, and very worthy deeds are done to this nation due to your forethought, in everything and everywhere, most noble Felix, we accept with all thankfulness.
052404 But that I not hinder you further, I beseech you to hear us briefly in your fairness.
052405 For we have found this man pestilent, and moving rebellion among all the Jews throughout the world, and a ringleader of the sect of the Nazarenes,
052406 who also attempted to profane the temple, whom we took and would have judged according to our law.
052407 But the chiliarch Lysias came with much force, taking him away out of our hands,
052408 commanding his accusers to come to you. By examining him, you yourself may know about all these things of which we accuse him.
052409 And the Jews also assented, saying that these things were so.
052410 But the governor motioning to him to speak, Paul answered; Understanding you as being a judge of this nation many years, I cheerfully defend myself as to the things concerning myself.
052411 You can know that it is not more than twelve days since I went up to Jerusalem to worship.
052412 And they neither found me in the temple disputing with any man, nor making a gathering of a crowd; not even in the synagogues, nor throughout the city.
052413 Nor can they prove the things of which they now accuse me.
052414 But I confess this to you, that after the Way which they call heresy, so I worship the God of my fathers, believing all things that are written in the Law and in the Prophets.
052415 And I have hope toward God, which they themselves also allow, that there shall be a resurrection of the dead, both of the just and unjust.
052416 And in this I exercise myself, always to have a blameless conscience toward God and men.
052417 And after many years I came to bring alms and offerings to my nation.
052418 Among which certain Jews from Asia found me purified in the temple, not with a crowd nor with tumult.
052419 These ought to be present before you and to accuse me, if they have anything against me.
052420 Or else let these themselves say if they have found anything unjust in me while I stood before the sanhedrin,
052421 unless it may be for this one voice that I cried out standing among them, that concerning a resurrection of the dead I am being judged by you today.
052422 And having heard these things, Felix put them off, knowing more accurately of the Way, saying, When Lysias the chiliarch has come down, I will examine the things concerning you.
052423 And he commanded a centurion to keep Paul and to let him have liberty, and not to forbid anyone of his own to minister or come to him.
052424 Then after certain days, when Felix came with his wife Drusilla, who was a Jewess, he sent for Paul and heard him concerning the faith in Christ.
052425 And as he reasoned of righteousness, temperance, and the Judgment to come, Felix trembled and answered, Go for this time, but taking time later, I will call for you.
052426 He also hoped that silver would be given him by Paul, that he might free him. Therefore he also frequently sent for him and talked with him.
052427 But after two years Felix welcomed a successor, Porcius Festus. And wishing to show a favor to the Jews, Felix left Paul bound.
052501 Then entering the province, after three days Festus went from Caesarea to Jerusalem.
052502 And the high priest and the chief of the Jews informed him against Paul, and they begged him
052503 asking a favor against him that he would send for him to Jerusalem, making a plot to kill him on way.
052504 Then indeed Festus answered that Paul should be kept at Caesarea; he himself would depart shortly.
052505 Then he said, those having power among you may go down with me . If there is a thing amiss in this man, let them accuse him.
052506 And staying among them more than ten days, going down to Caesarea, on the next day sitting on the judgment seat, he commanded Paul to be brought.
052507 And he having come, the Jews who came down from Jerusalem stood around and brought many charges against Paul, which they could not prove.
052508 Defending himself, Paul said, Neither against the Law of the Jews, nor against the temple, nor against Caesar have I offended in anything.
052509 But Festus, wanting to please the Jews, answered Paul and said, Will you go up to Jerusalem and be judged there before me about these things?
052510 But Paul said, I stand at Caesar's judgment seat, where I ought to be judged. I have done no wrong to the Jews, as you very well know.
052511 For if I am an offender or have committed anything worthy of death, I do not refuse to die. But if there is nothing of which these accuse me, no one can deliver me to them. I appeal to Caesar.
052512 Then conferring with the sanhedrin, Festus answered, You have appealed to Caesar? To Caesar you shall go.
052513 And after some days king Agrippa and Bernice came to Caesarea to greet Festus.
052514 And when they had been there many days, Festus declared Paul's cause to the king, saying, A certain man has been left in bonds by Felix,
052515 about whom, when I was in Jerusalem, the chief priests and the elders of the Jews informed me , desiring judgment against him.
052516 To them I answered, It is not the custom of the Romans to deliver any man to destruction before he being accused may have the accusers face to face, and have had freedom to answer for himself concerning the accusation.
052517 Therefore, when they had come here, without any delay I sat on the judgment seat the next day and commanded the man to be brought,
052518 about whom, standing up, the accusers brought against him no charge of which I suspected,
052519 but they had certain questions about their own demon-worship, and about a certain Jesus dying, whom Paul affirmed to be alive.
052520 And because I was perplexed about this question, I asked whether he would go to Jerusalem and be judged there about these matters.
052521 But Paul having appealed to be reserved to the hearing of Augustus, I commanded him to be held until I might send him to Caesar.
052522 And Agrippa said to Festus, I also would like to hear the man myself. And he said, Tomorrow you shall hear him.
052523 And on the next day, when Agrippa and Bernice had come with great pomp and had entered into the auditorium with both the chiliarchs and principal men of the city, also Festus commanding, Paul was brought out.
052524 And Festus said, King Agrippa, and all those men present with us, you see this one about whom all the multitude of the Jews pleaded with me, both at Jerusalem and here, crying that he ought not to live any longer.
052525 But I had perceived nothing he had committed worthy of death, and that he himself has appealed to Augustus, I determined to send him,
052526 about whom I have no certain thing to write of him to my lord. Therefore I brought him before you, and especially before you, O king Agrippa, so that, after examination is made, I might have something to write.
052527 For it seems to me unreasonable to send a prisoner, and not to signify the charges against him.
052601 And Agrippa said to Paul, You are permitted to speak for yourself. Then stretching out his hand, Paul made a defense:
052602 Concerning all of which I am accused by Jews, king Agrippa, I think myself happy being about to make defense before you today,
052603 you being especially expert in all customs and questions among the Jews. Therefore I beseech you to hear me patiently.
052604 Truly, then, all the Jews know my manner of life from my youth, which was at first among my own nation at Jerusalem,
052605 who knew me from the first, if they would testify, that according to the strictest sect of our religion I lived a Pharisee.
052606 And now I stand and am judged for the hope of the promise made to our fathers by God,
052607 to which promise our twelve tribes hope to attain, serving God fervently night and day. For the sake of this hope, king Agrippa, I am accused by the Jews.
052608 Why is it thought a thing incredible with you that God raises the dead?
052609 I truly thought within myself that I ought to do many things contrary to the name of Jesus of Nazareth,
052610 which I also did in Jerusalem. And I shut up many of the saints in prisons, having received authority from the chief priests. And they being put to death, I cast a vote.
052611 And I punished them often in every synagogue; I compelled them to blaspheme; and being exceedingly furious against them, I persecuted them even to the outside cities.
052612 In which pursuit also traveling to Damascus with authority and power of decision from the chief priests,
052613 at midday, along the highway, O king, I and those with me saw a light from heaven, brighter than the sun; shining around me.
052614 And all of us falling to the ground, I heard a voice speaking to me and saying in the Hebrew dialect, Saul, Saul, why do you persecute Me? It is hard for you to kick against the goads.
052615 And I said, Who are you, lord? And He said, I am Jesus whom you persecute.
052616 But rise and stand on your feet, for I have appeared to you for this purpose, to make you a minister and a witness both of what you saw, and in what I shall appear to you;
052617 delivering you from the people and the nations, to whom I now send you
052618 in order to open their eyes so that they may turn from darkness to light, and from the authority of Satan to God, so that they may receive remission of sins and an inheritance among those who are sanctified by faith in Me.
052619 After this, king Agrippa, I did not disobey the heavenly vision.
052620 But to those first in Damascus, and Jerusalem, and to all the country of Judea, and to the nations, I made known the command to repent and to turn to God, doing works worthy of repentance
052621 Because of these things, having caught me in the temple, The Jews tried to kill me .
052622 Then having obtained help from God, I stand until this day, witnessing both to small and great, saying no other things than those which the prophets and Moses said was going to happen;
052623 whether the Christ was liable to suffer, whether first by a resurrection of the dead He was going to proclaim light to the people and to the nations.
052624 And he defending himself with these things, Festus said with a loud voice, Paul, you rave! Your many letters turn you to insanity.
052625 But he said, Not to insanity, most noble Festus, but I speak words of truth and sanity.
052626 For the king understands about these things, to whom I speak, even being bold of speech. For I am persuaded that not any of these things are hidden from him, nothing. For the doing of this was not in a corner.
052627 King Agrippa, do you believe the prophets? I know that you believe.
052628 And Agrippa said to Paul, Do you persuade me to be a Christian in but a little?
052629 And Paul said, I would pray to God, both in a little and in much, that not only you, but also all hearing me today to become as I also am, except for these bonds.
052630 And he having spoken this, the king and the governor and Bernice and those who sat with them rose up.
052631 And withdrawing, they spoke with one another, saying, This man does nothing worthy of death or of bonds.
052632 And Agrippa said to Festus, This man might have been set at liberty if he had not appealed to Caesar.
052701 And when it was determined that we should sail to Italy, they delivered Paul and certain other prisoners to one named Julius, a centurion of Augustus' cohort.
052702 And boarding a ship of Adramyttium, which was about to sail alongside Asian places, we set sail, Aristarchus, a Macedonian from Thessalonica, being with us.
052703 And on the next day we were landed at Sidon. And Julius treated Paul courteously and gave him liberty to go to his friends to receive care.
052704 And setting sail from there, we sailed close to Cyprus, because the winds were contrary.
052705 And sailing over the sea against Cilicia and Pamphylia, we came to Myra of Lycia.
052706 And there the centurion found a ship of Alexandria sailing to Italy, and he put us on it.
052707 And sailing slowly many days and with difficulty, coming abreast of Cnidus; the wind not allowing us; we sailed close to Crete, across from Salmone.
052708 And coasting along with difficulty, we came to a place named Fair Havens, near which was a city, Lasea.
052709 And much time having been used up, and the voyage already being dangerous, because the Fast was now already past, Paul warned them ,
052710 saying, Men, I perceive that this voyage is about to be with much harm and loss, and not only much cargo and of the ship, but also of our souls.
052711 But the centurion was rather persuaded by the helmsman and the shipmaster, than by the things spoken by Paul.
052712 And the port not being fit to winter in, the most of them advised to set sail from there, if by any means they might be able to get to Phoenix to winter; which is a port of Crete, looking toward the southwest and northwest.
052713 And a south wind blowing softly, thinking to have obtained their purpose, lifting anchor , they sailed along close beside Crete.
052714 But not long after, a stormy wind called Euroclydon beat down on it.
052715 And the ship being seized, and not being able to beat against the wind, giving way we were borne along.
052716 And running under an islet being called Clauda, we hardly were able to become masters of the boat;
052717 which taking, they used helps, undergirding the ship. And fearing lest they should fall into the sandbanks of Syrtis, lowering the tackle, so they were borne along.
052718 And being exceedingly storm-tossed with a tempest, they made a casting on the next day ;
052719 And on the third day we threw out the ship's tackle with our hands.
052720 And neither sun nor stars appearing in many days, and no small tempest pressing hard, now all hope that we would be saved was taken away.
052721 But there being much fasting, then standing up in their midst, Paul said, O men, being obedient to me you ought not to have set sail from Crete, and to have come by this harm and loss.
052722 And now I exhort you to be of good cheer, for there will be no casting away of life among you, only of the ship.
052723 For tonight an angel of God stood beside me, whose I am and whom I serve,
052724 saying, Fear not, Paul! You must stand before Caesar. And behold! God has given you all those who sail with you.
052725 Therefore, men, be of good cheer, for I believe God, that it will be so, according to the way it was told me.
052726 But we must fall on a certain island.
052727 But when the fourteenth night came, we being carried about in the Adriatic Sea, about midnight the sailors thought that they drew near some country.
052728 And sounding they found it twenty fathoms; and moving a little further, and sounding again, they found it fifteen fathoms.
052729 And fearing that we would fall on rocks, and casting four anchors out of the stern, they wished day to come.
052730 But the sailors seeking to flee out of the ship, and lowering the boat into the sea, pretending to be about to cast out anchors from the prow,
052731 Paul said to the centurion and to the soldiers, Unless these remain in the ship, you cannot be saved.
052732 Then the soldiers cut the ropes of the boat, and let her fall.
052733 And until day was about to come, Paul begged all to take food, saying, This is the fourteenth day that you continued waiting without food, having taken nothing.
052734 Therefore I beg you to take some food, for this is for your deliverance. For not a hair of your head shall perish.
052735 And saying these things, and taking bread, he gave thanks to God before all, and breaking, he began to eat.
052736 And all becoming cheered, they also took food.
052737 And we were, all the souls in the ship, two hundred and seventy-six.
052738 And being filled with food, they lightened the ship, throwing the wheat into the sea.
052739 And when day came, they did not recognize the land. But they discovered a certain bay with a beach, into which they were minded, if they were able, to drive the ship.
052740 And casting off the anchors, they left them in the sea; at the same time they loosened the rudder bands and hoisted up the foresail to the wind and held to the shore.
052741 And coming on a place between two seas, they drove the vessel. And indeed the prow sticking fast, it remained unmovable. But the stern was broken with the violence of the waves.
052742 And the mind of the soldiers was to kill the prisoners, lest any of them should swim out and escape.
052743 But the centurion, desiring to save Paul, kept them from their purpose and commanded those who could swim, to throw themselves overboard, to go out on the land.
052744 And the rest went , some on boards and others on some of the things from the ship. And so it happened that all were saved on the land.
052801 And being saved, then they knew that the island was called Melita.
052802 And the foreigners showed us not the common kindness. For they kindled a fire and welcomed all of us, because of the rain coming on, and because of the cold.
052803 And Paul had gathered a bundle of sticks, and laying them on the fire, a viper came out of the heat and fastened on his hand.
052804 And when the foreigners saw the creature hanging from his hand, they said to one another, No doubt this man is a murderer, whom, being saved from the sea, Justice has not allowed to live.
052805 Then indeed he shook off the creature into the fire, suffering no harm.
052806 But they expected him to be about to become inflamed, or to fall down dead suddenly, But over much time expecting and seeing nothing amiss happening to him, they changed their minds and said that he was a god.
052807 In the quarters about that place were lands to the chief of the island, whose name was Publius. Welcoming us, he lodged us courteously three days.
052808 And it happened the father of Publius was lying down, suffering fevers and dysentery; to whom Paul entered in, and praying and laying on his hands, he healed him.
052809 Then this taking place, the rest who were having infirmities in the island also came, and were healed.
052810 They also honored us with many honors. And on our setting sail, they laid on the things of our needs.
052811 And after three months we sailed in a ship of Alexandria which had wintered in the island, an Alexandrian with an ensign, The Twin Brothers.
052812 And landing at Syracuse, we stayed three days.
052813 Going around from there we arrived at Rhegium. And after one day a south wind coming on, we came to Puteoli on the second,
052814 where finding brothers, we were asked to stay seven days. And so we went toward Rome.
052815 And the brothers from there hearing of us, they came to meet us as far as the market-place of Appius, and Three Taverns. Seeing them, thanking God, Paul took courage.
052816 And when we came into Rome, the centurion delivered the prisoners to the camp commander. But Paul was allowed to dwell by himself, with a soldier guarding him.
052817 And after three days it happened that Paul called together those being chief of the Jews. And they coming together, he said to them, Men, brothers, I did nothing against the people or customs of our fathers. I was delivered a prisoner from Jerusalem into the hands of the Romans
052818 who, examining me, were of a mind to let me go because there was no cause of death in me.
052819 But the Jews speaking against it , I was constrained to appeal to Caesar; not as having anything to accuse my nation.
052820 For this cause, then, I called for you, to see and to speak with you . For I have this chain around me for the hope of Israel.
052821 And they said to him, We neither received letters out of Judea concerning you, nor have any of the brothers who came declared or spoke anything evil of you.
052822 But we think it right to hear from you what you think. For truly as concerning this sect, it is known to us that it is spoken against everywhere.
052823 And they having appointed him a day, many came to him in his lodging; to whom he expounded, testifying the kingdom of God, and persuading them the things concerning Jesus, both out of the law of Moses and out of the prophets, from morning until evening.
052824 And some indeed believed the things that were said, others did not believe.
052825 And disagreeing with one another, they were let go, Paul saying one word: Well did the Holy Spirit speak through Isaiah the prophet to our fathers,
052826 saying, "Go to this people and say: Hearing you shall hear and shall not understand; and seeing you shall see and not perceive.
052827 For the heart of this people was fattened, and they have heard with their ears dully; and they closed their eyes; lest at any time they should see with their eyes, and hear with their ears, and understand with their heart, and should be converted, and I should heal them."
052828 Therefore be it known to you that the salvation of God is sent to the nations, and they will hear.
052829 And he having said these words, the Jews departed, having much discussion amongst themselves.
052830 And Paul remained two years in his own hired house. And he welcomed all who came in to him,
052831 proclaiming the kingdom of God, and teaching those things concerning the Lord Jesus Christ, with all freedom, and without hindrance.
060101 Paul, a servant of Jesus Christ, a called apostle, separated to the gospel of God
060102 (which He had promised beforehand through His prophets in the Holy Scriptures),
060103 about His Son, Jesus Christ our Lord, who was made of the seed of David according to the flesh,
060104 who was marked out the Son of God in power, according to the Spirit of holiness, by the resurrection from the dead;
060105 by whom we have received grace and apostleship, to obedience to the faith among all nations, for His name;
060106 among whom you also are the called-out ones of Jesus Christ:
060107 to all those who are in Rome, beloved of God, called to be saints. Grace to you and peace from God our Father and the Lord Jesus Christ.
060108 First, I thank my God through Jesus Christ for you all, that your faith is spoken of throughout the whole world.
060109 For God is my witness, whom I serve with my spirit in the gospel of His Son, that without ceasing I make mention of you
060110 always in my prayers, making request if by any means now at length I might have a prosperous journey by the will of God to come to you.
060111 For I long to see you, so that I may impart to you some spiritual gift, to you for the establishing of you.
060112 And this is to be comforted together with you by our mutual faith, both yours and mine.
060113 But I would not have you ignorant, brothers, that oftentimes I purposed to come to you, and was kept back until the present; that I might have some fruit among you also, even as among other nations.
060114 I am debtor both to the Greeks and to the foreigners, both to the wise and to the unwise.
060115 So, as much as is in me lies , I am ready to preach the gospel to you who are at Rome also.
060116 For I am not ashamed of the gospel of Christ, for it is the power of God unto salvation to everyone who believes, to the Jew first and also to the Greek.
060117 For in it the righteousness of God is revealed from faith to faith, as it is written, "The just shall live by faith."
060118 For the wrath of God is revealed from Heaven against all ungodliness and unrighteousness of men, who hold the truth in unrighteousness,
060119 because the thing which may be known of God is clearly revealed within them, for God revealed it to them.
060120 For the unseen things of Him from the creation of the world are clearly seen, being realized by the things that are made, even His eternal power and Godhead, for them to be without excuse.
060121 Because, knowing God, they did not glorify Him as God, neither were thankful. But they became vain in their imaginations, and their foolish heart was darkened.
060122 Professing to be wise, they became fools
060123 and changed the glory of the incorruptible God into an image made like corruptible man, and birds, and four-footed animals, and creeping things.
060124 Therefore God also gave them up to uncleanness through the lusts of their hearts, to dishonor their own bodies between themselves.
060125 For they changed the truth of God into a lie, and they worshiped and served the created thing more than the Creator, who is blessed forever. Amen.
060126 For this cause, God gave them up to dishonorable affections. For even their women changed the natural use into that which is against nature.
060127 And likewise also the men, leaving the natural use of the woman, burned in their lust toward one another; males with males working out shamefulness, and receiving in themselves the recompense which was fitting for their error.
060128 And even as they did not think fit to have God in their knowledge, God gave them over to a reprobate mind, to do the things not right,
060129 being filled with all unrighteousness, fornication, wickedness, covetousness, maliciousness; being full of envy, murder, quarrels, deceit, evil habits, becoming whisperers,
060130 backbiters, haters of God, insolent, proud, braggarts, inventors of evil things, disobedient to parents,
060131 undiscerning, perfidious, without natural affection, unforgiving, unmerciful;
060132 who, knowing the righteous order of God, that those practicing such things are worthy of death, not only do them, but have pleasure in those practicing them .
060201 Therefore you are without excuse, O man, everyone who judges; for in that in which you judge another, you condemn yourself, for you who judge do the same things.
060202 But know that the judgment of God is according to truth on those who practice such things.
060203 And, O man, the one judging those who do such things, and practice them, do you think this, that you shall escape the judgment of God?
060204 Or do you despise the riches of His kindness, and the forbearance and long-suffering, not knowing that the kindness of God leads you to repentance?
060205 But according to your hardness and your impenitent heart, do you treasure up wrath for yourself in a day of wrath and revelation of the righteous judgment of God,
060206 who will render to each according to his works;
060207 indeed to those who with patience in good work are seeking for glory, and honor, and incorruptibility, everlasting life.
060208 But to those who indeed disobeying the truth out of self-seeking, and obeying unrighteousness, will be anger and wrath,
060209 tribulation and anguish upon every soul of man who has worked out evil; of the Jew first, and also of the Greek.
060210 But He will give glory, honor and peace to every man who works good, to the Jew first and also to the Greek.
060211 For there is no respect of faces with God.
060212 For as many as sinned without Law will also perish without Law. And as many as have sinned within Law shall be judged through Law.
060213 For it is not the hearers of the Law who are just before God, but the doers of the Law will be justified.
060214 For when the nations, who do not have the Law, do by nature the things of the Law, these, not having the Law, are a law unto themselves;
060215 who show the work of the law written in their hearts, their conscience also bearing witness, and the thoughts between one another accusing or even excusing one another,
060216 in a day when God shall judge the secrets of men by Jesus Christ according to my gospel.
060217 Behold, you are called a Jew, and rest in the Law, and boast in God;
060218 and know His will and approve the things excelling, being instructed out of the Law;
060219 and persuading yourselves to be a guide of the blind, a light to those in darkness;
060220 an instructor of the foolish, a teacher of babes, who have the form of knowledge and of the truth in the Law.
060221 Therefore the one teaching another, do you not teach yourself? The one preaching not to steal, do you steal?
060222 The one saying not to commit adultery, do you commit adultery? The one detesting idols, do you rob temples?
060223 You who boast in Law, do you dishonor God through breaking the Law?
060224 For the name of God is blasphemed among the nations because of you, as it is written.
060225 For circumcision truly profits if you keep the Law, but if you are a transgressor of the Law, circumcision becomes uncircumcision.
060226 If then the uncircumcision keeps the ordinances of the Law, shall not his uncircumcision be counted for circumcision?
060227 And the uncircumcision which is by nature, if it fulfills the Law, shall it not judge you, who through letter and circumcision become transgressors of the Law?
060228 For he is not a Jew who is one outwardly, nor is circumcision that outwardly in flesh;
060229 but he is a Jew who is one inwardly, and circumcision is of the heart; in spirit and not in letter; whose praise is not from men, but from God.
060301 Then what is the superiority of the Jew? Or what is the profit of circumcision?
060302 Much, by every way! Chiefly, indeed, because they were entrusted with the oracles of God.
060303 For what? If some did not believe, will not their unbelief nullify the faith of God?
060304 Let it not be! But let God be true, and every man a liar; as it is written, "That You might be justified in Your sayings, and will overcome when You are judged."
060305 But if our unrighteousness commends the righteousness of God, what shall we say? Is God unrighteous who lays on wrath? (I speak as a man.)
060306 Let it not be! For then how shall God judge the world?
060307 For if in my lie the truth has more abounded to His glory why am I still judged as a sinner?
060308 And not rather , (as we are wrongly accused, and as some affirm that we say), Let us do bad things that good may come? Their condemnation is just.
060309 What then? Do we excel? No, in no way; for we have before charged both Jews and Greeks all with being under sin,
060310 as it is written: "There is none righteous, no not one;
060311 there is none that understands, there is none that seeks after God."
060312 "They are all gone out of the way, they have together become unprofitable, there is none that does good, no, not one."
060313 "Their throat is an open grave, with their tongues they have used deceit, the poison of asps is under their lips;
060314 whose mouth is full of cursing and bitterness;"
060315 "their feet are swift to shed blood;
060316 destruction and misery are in their way,
060317 and the way of peace they did not know."
060318 "There is no fear of God before their eyes."
060319 But we know that whatever things the Law says, it says to those who are under the Law; so that every mouth may be stopped and all the world may be under judgment before God,
060320 because by the works of the Law none of all flesh will be justified in His sight; for through the Law is the knowledge of sin.
060321 But now a righteousness of God has been revealed apart from Law, being witnessed by the Law and the Prophets;
060322 even the righteousness of God through the faith of Jesus Christ, toward all and upon all those who believe. For there is no difference,
060323 for all have sinned and come short of the glory of God,
060324 being justified freely by His grace through the redemption that is in Christ Jesus;
060325 whom God has set forth to be a propitiation through faith in His blood, to declare His righteousness through the passing by of the sins that had taken place before, in the forbearance of God;
060326 for the display of His righteousness at this time, for Him to be just and, forgiving the one being of the faith of Jesus.
060327 Then where is the boasting? It is excluded. Through what law? Of works? No, but through the law of faith.
060328 Therefore we conclude that a man is justified by faith without the works of the law.
060329 Or is He the God of the Jews only, and not also of the nations? Yes, of the nations also,
060330 since it is one God who will justify circumcision by faith, and uncircumcision through faith.
060331 Do we then make the Law void through faith? Let it not be! But we establish the Law.
060401 What then shall we say that our father Abraham has found, according to flesh?
060402 For if Abraham was justified by works, he has a boast; but not before God.
060403 For what does the Scripture say? "Abraham believed God, and it was counted to him for righteousness."
060404 But to him working, the reward is not reckoned according to grace, but according to debt.
060405 But to him not working, but believing on Him justifying the ungodly, his faith is counted for righteousness.
060406 Even as David also says of the blessedness of the man to whom God imputes righteousness without works,
060407 saying , "Blessed are those whose lawlessnesses are forgiven, and whose sins are covered;
060408 blessed is the man to whom the Lord will in no way impute sin."
060409 Is this blessedness then on the circumcision only, or on the uncircumcision also? For we say that faith was reckoned to Abraham for righteousness.
060410 How then was it reckoned? Being in circumcision or in uncircumcision? Not in circumcision, but in uncircumcision.
060411 And he received a sign of circumcision, a seal of the righteousness of the faith while still uncircumcised; so that he might be the father of all those believing through uncircumcision, for righteousness to be imputed to them also;
060412 and a father of circumcision to those not of the circumcision only, but also to those walking by the steps of the faith of our father Abraham during uncircumcision.
060413 For the promise that he should be the heir of the world was not to Abraham or to his seed through the Law, but through the righteousness of faith.
060414 For if they of the Law are heirs, faith is made void and the promise is made of no effect;
060415 because the Law works out wrath, for where no law is, there is no transgression.
060416 Therefore it is of faith so that it might be according to grace; for the promise to be made sure to all the seed, not only to that which is of the Law, but to that also which is of the faith of Abraham, who is the father of us all
060417 (as it has been written, "I have made you a father of many nations") --before God, whom he believed, who makes the dead live, and calls the things which do not exist as though they do exist.
060418 For he who beyond hope believed on hope for him to become the father of many nations (according to that which was spoken, "So your seed shall be").
060419 And not being weak in faith, he did not consider his own body already dead (being about a hundred years old) or the deadening of Sarah's womb.
060420 He did not stagger at the promise of God through unbelief, but was strong in faith, giving glory to God,
060421 and being fully persuaded that what God had promised, He was also able to perform.
060422 And therefore it was imputed to him for righteousness.
060423 Now it was not written for him alone that it was imputed to him,
060424 but for us also to whom it is to be imputed, to the ones believing on Him who has raised up Jesus our Lord from the dead;
060425 who was delivered because of our offenses and was raised for our justification.
060501 Therefore being justified by faith, we have peace with God through our Lord Jesus Christ.
060502 Through Him we also have access by faith into this grace in which we stand, and we rejoice on the hope of the glory of God.
060503 And not only this , but we glory in afflictions also, knowing that afflictions work out patience,
060504 and patience works out experience, and experience works out hope.
060505 And hope does not make us ashamed, because the love of God has been poured out in our hearts through the Holy Spirit given to us.
060506 For we yet being without strength, in due time Christ died for the ungodly.
060507 For one will with difficulty die for a righteous one, yet perhaps one would even dare to die for a good one.
060508 But God commends His love toward us in that while we were yet sinners Christ died for us.
060509 Much more then, being now justified by His blood, we shall be saved from wrath through Him.
060510 For if when we were enemies, we were reconciled to God through the death of His Son, much more, being reconciled, we shall be saved by His life.
060511 And not only so , but we also rejoice in God through our Lord Jesus Christ, by whom we have now received the reconciliation.
060512 Therefore, even as through one man sin entered into the world, and death by sin, and so death passed on all men inasmuch as all sinned:
060513 for until the Law sin was in the world, but sin is not imputed when there is no law.
060514 But death reigned from Adam to Moses, even over those who had not sinned in the likeness of the transgression of Adam, who is the type of Him who was to come;
060515 but the free gift shall not be also like the offense. For if by the offense of the one many died, much more the grace of God, and the gift in grace; which is of the one Man, Jesus Christ, abounded to many.
060516 And the free gift shall not be as by one having sinned; (for indeed the judgment was of one to condemnation, but the free gift is of many offenses to justification.
060517 For if by one man's offense death reigned by one, much more they who receive abundance of grace and the gift of righteousness shall reign in life by One, Jesus Christ.)
060518 Therefore as by one offense sentence came on all men to condemnation, even so by the righteousness of One the free gift came to all men to justification of life.
060519 For as by one man's disobedience many were made sinners, so by the obedience of One shall many be made righteous.
060520 But the Law entered so that the offense might abound. But where sin abounded, grace did much more abound,
060521 so that as sin has reigned to death, even so grace might reign through righteousness to eternal life by Jesus Christ our Lord.
060601 What shall we say then? Shall we continue in sin so that grace may abound?
060602 Let it not be! How shall we who died to sin live any longer in it?
060603 Do you not know that as many of us as were baptized into Jesus Christ were baptized into His death?
060604 Therefore we were buried with Him by baptism into death, so that as Christ was raised up from the dead by the glory of the Father; even so we also should walk in newness of life.
060605 For if we have been joined together in the likeness of His death, we shall also be in the likeness of His resurrection;
060606 knowing this, that our old man is crucified with Him in order that the body of sin might be destroyed, that from now on we should not serve sin.
060607 For he who died has been justified from sin.
060608 But if we died with Christ, we believe that we shall also live with Him,
060609 knowing that when Christ was raised from the dead, He dies no more; death no longer has dominion over Him.
060610 For in that He died, He died to sin once; but in that He lives, He lives to God.
060611 Likewise count yourselves also to be truly dead to sin, but alive to God through Jesus Christ our Lord.
060612 Therefore do not let sin reign in your mortal body, that you should obey it in its lusts.
060613 Do not yield your members as instruments of unrighteousness to sin, but yield yourselves to God, as one alive from the dead, and your members as instruments of righteousness to God.
060614 For sin shall not have dominion over you, for you are not under Law, but under grace.
060615 What then? Shall we sin because we are not under Law, but under grace? Let it not be!
060616 Do you not know that to whom you yield yourselves as slaves for obedience, you are slaves to him whom you obey; whether it is of sin to death, or of obedience to righteousness.
060617 But thanks be to our God that you were the slaves of sin, but you have obeyed from the heart that form of doctrine to which you were delivered.
060618 Then being made free from sin, you became the slaves of righteousness.
060619 I speak in the manner of men because of the weakness of your flesh; for as you have yielded your members as slaves to uncleanness, and to lawless act unto lawless act, even so now yield your members as slaves to righteousness unto holiness.
060620 For when you were the slaves of sin, you were free from righteousness.
060621 What fruit did you have then in those things of which you are now ashamed? For the end of those things is death.
060622 But now, being made free from sin, and having become slaves to God, you have your fruit to holiness, and the end everlasting life.
060623 For the wages of sin is death, but the gift of God is eternal life through Jesus Christ our Lord.
060701 Or are you ignorant, brothers; for I speak to those who know the Law; that the law has dominion over a man as long as he lives?
060702 For the married woman was bound by law to the living husband. But if the husband is dead, she is set free from the law of her husband.
060703 So then if , while her husband lives, she is married to another man, she shall be called an adulteress. But if the husband dies, she is free from the law, so that she is no adulteress by becoming another man's wife.
060704 So, my brothers, you also have become dead to the law by the body of Christ so that you should be married to Another, even to Him raised from the dead, that we should bring forth fruit to God.
060705 For when we were in the flesh, the passions of sin worked in our members through the law to bring forth fruit to death.
060706 But now we having been set free from the Law, having died to that in which we were held, so that we serve in newness of spirit and not in oldness of the letter.
060707 What shall we say then? Is the law sin? Let it not be said! But I did not know sin except through the law. For also I did not know lust except the law said, You shall not lust.
060708 But sin, taking occasion by the commandment, worked in me all kinds of lust. For apart from law sin was dead.
060709 For I was alive without the law once. But when the commandment came, sin revived and I died.
060710 And the commandment, which was to life, was found to be death to me.
060711 For sin, taking occasion by the commandment, deceived me, and by it killed me .
060712 So indeed the Law is holy, and the commandment is holy and just and good.
060713 Then has that which is good become death to me? Let it not be! But sin, that it might appear to be sin, working death in me by that which is good; in order that sin might become exceedingly sinful by the commandment.
060714 For we know that the law is spiritual, but I am carnal, sold under sin.
060715 For that which I do, I know not. For what I desire, that I do not do; but what I hate, that I do.
060716 If then I do that which I do not desire, I consent to the law that it is good.
060717 But now it is no more I that do it, but sin that dwells in me.
060718 For I know that in me (that is, in my flesh) dwells no good thing. For to will is present with me, but how to perform that which is good I do not find.
060719 For I do not do the good that I desire; but the evil which I do not will, that I do.
060720 But if I do what I do not desire, it is no more I working it out, but sin dwelling in me.
060721 I find then a law: when I will to do the right, evil is present with me.
060722 For I delight in the law of God according to the inward man;
060723 but I see another law in my members, warring against the law of my mind, and bringing me into captivity to the law of sin being in my members.
060724 O wretched man that I am ! Who shall deliver me from the body of this death?
060725 I thank God through Jesus Christ our Lord! So then with the mind I myself serve the law of God, but with the flesh the law of sin.
060801 There is therefore now no condemnation to those who are in Christ Jesus, who walk not according to the flesh but according to the Spirit.
060802 But the law of the Spirit of life in Christ Jesus has made me free from the law of sin and death.
060803 For what the law could not do, in that it was weak through the flesh, God sending his own Son in the likeness of sinful flesh, and for sin, condemned sin in the flesh;
060804 so that the righteousness of the Law might be fulfilled in us, who walk not according to the flesh but according to the Spirit.
060805 For they who are according to the flesh mind the things of flesh, but they who are according to the Spirit the things of the Spirit.
060806 For to be carnally minded is death, but to be spiritually minded is life and peace
060807 because the carnal mind is enmity against God, for it is not subject to the law of God, neither indeed can it be .
060808 So then they who are in the flesh cannot please God.
060809 But you are not in the flesh, but in the Spirit, if the Spirit of God dwells in you. But if anyone has not the Spirit of Christ, he is none of His.
060810 And if Christ is in you, indeed the body is dead because of sin, but the Spirit is life because of righteousness.
060811 But if the Spirit of the One who raised up Jesus from the dead dwells in you, the One who raised up Christ from the dead shall also make your mortal bodies alive by His Spirit who dwells in you.
060812 Therefore, brothers, we are not debtors to the flesh, to live according to the flesh.
060813 For if you live according to the flesh, you shall die. But if you through the Spirit mortify the deeds of the body, you shall live.
060814 For as many as are led by the Spirit of God, they are the sons of God.
060815 For you have not received the spirit of bondage again to fear, but you have received the Spirit of adoption by which we cry, Abba, Father!
060816 The Spirit Himself bears witness with our spirit that we are the children of God.
060817 And if we are children, then we are heirs; heirs of God and joint-heirs with Christ; so that if we suffer with Him , we may also be glorified together.
060818 For I reckon that the sufferings of this present time are not worthy to be compared with the coming glory to be revealed in us.
060819 For the earnest expectation of the creation waits for the manifestation of the sons of God.
060820 For the creation was not willingly subjected to vanity, but because of Him who subjected it on hope
060821 that the creation itself also shall be delivered from the bondage of corruption into the glorious liberty of the children of God.
060822 And we know that the whole creation groans and travails in pain together until now.
060823 And not only so , but ourselves also, who have the firstfruit of the Spirit, even we ourselves groan within ourselves, awaiting adoption, the redemption of our body.
060824 For we are saved by hope. But hope that is seen is not hope; for what anyone sees, why does he also hope for it ?
060825 But if we hope for that which we do not see, then we wait for it with patience.
060826 Likewise the Spirit also helps our infirmities. For we do not know what we should pray for as we ought, but the Spirit Himself makes intercession for us with groanings which cannot be uttered.
060827 And He searching the hearts knows what is the mind of the Spirit, because He makes intercession for the saints according to the will of God.
060828 And we know that all things work together for good to those who love God, to those who are called according to His purpose.
060829 For whom He foreknew, He also predestinated to be conformed to the image of His Son, for Him to be the First-born among many brothers.
060830 But whom He predestinated, these He also called; and whom He called, those He also justified. And whom He justified, these He also glorified.
060831 What then shall we say to these things? If God is for us, who can be against us?
060832 Truly He who did not spare His own Son, but delivered Him up for us all, how shall He not with Him also freely give us all things?
060833 Who shall lay anything to the charge of God's elect? It is God who justifies.
060834 Who is he condemning? It is Christ who has died, but rather also who is raised, who is also at the right hand of God, who also intercedes for us.
060835 Who shall separate us from the love of Christ? Shall tribulation, or distress, or persecution, or famine, or nakedness, or peril, or sword?
060836 As it is written, "For Your sake we are killed all the day long. We are counted as sheep of slaughter."
060837 But in all these things we more than conquer through Him who loved us.
060838 For I am persuaded that neither death, nor life, nor angels, nor principalities, nor powers, nor things present, nor things to come,
060839 nor height, nor depth, nor any other creature, shall be able to separate us from the love of God which is in Christ Jesus our Lord.
060901 I tell the truth in Christ, I do not lie, my conscience also bearing me witness in the Holy Spirit,
060902 that I have great heaviness and continual pain in my heart.
060903 For I myself was wishing to be accursed from Christ for my brothers, my kinsmen according to the flesh,
060904 who are Israelites; to whom belong the adoption, and the glory, and the covenants, and the giving of the Law, and the service of God , and the promises;
060905 whose are the fathers, and of whom is the Christ according to flesh, He being God over all, blessed forever. Amen.
060906 Not however that the word of God has failed, for not all those of Israel are Israel;
060907 nor because they are the seed of Abraham are they all children. But, "In Isaac shall your Seed be called."
060908 That is, not the children of the flesh are children of God; but the children of the promise are counted for a seed.
060909 For this is the word of promise: "At this time I will come and Sarah shall have a son."
060910 And not only this , but when Rebekah also had conceived by one, by our father Isaac
060911 (for the children had not yet been born, neither had done any good or evil; but that the purpose of God according to election might stand, not of works but of Him who called,)
060912 it was said to her, "The elder shall serve the younger."
060913 As it is written, "Jacob have I loved, but Esau have I hated."
060914 What shall we say then? Is there not unrighteousness with God? Let it not be!
060915 For He said to Moses, "I will have mercy on whom I will have mercy, and I will have compassion on whom I will have compassion."
060916 So then it is not of the one willing, nor of the one running, but of God, the One showing mercy.
060917 For the Scripture says to Pharaoh, "Even for this same purpose I have raised you up, that I might show My power in you, and that My name might be declared throughout all the earth."
060918 Therefore He has mercy on whom He will have mercy , and whom He will, He hardens.
060919 You will then say to me, Why does He yet find fault? For who has resisted His will?
060920 No, but, O man, who are you who replies against God? Shall the thing formed say to Him who formed it , Why have you made me this way?
060921 Does not the potter have power over the clay, from the same lump to make one vessel to honor and another to dishonor?
060922 What if God, willing to show His wrath and to make His power known, endured with much long-suffering the vessels of wrath fitted to destruction;
060923 and that He might make known the riches of His glory on the vessels of mercy which He had before prepared to glory;
060924 whom He also called, not only us, of Jews, but also of the nations?
060925 As He also says in Hosea, "I will call those not My people, My people; and those not beloved, Beloved."
060926 And it shall be, in the place where it was said to them. "You are not My people; there they shall be called sons of the living God."
060927 Isaiah also cries concerning Israel, "Though the number of the sons of Israel is as the sands of the sea, a remnant shall be saved.
060928 For He is bringing the matter to an end, and cutting short in righteousness, because the Lord will make a short work on the earth."
060929 And as Isaiah said before, "Unless the Lord of hosts had left us a seed, we would have been as Sodom, and would have been like Gomorrah."
060930 What shall we say then? That the nations, who did not follow after righteousness have taken on righteousness, but a righteousness of faith.
060931 But Israel, who followed after a law of righteousness did not arrive at a law of righteousness.
060932 Why? Because it was not of faith, but as it were by the works of the Law. For they stumbled at that Stumbling-stone;
060933 as it is written, "Behold, I lay in Zion a Stumbling-stone and a Rock-of-offense, and everyone believing on Him shall not be put to shame."
061001 Brothers, truly my heart's desire and prayer to God for Israel is for it to be saved.
061002 For I bear record to them that they have a zeal of God, but not according to knowledge.
061003 For they, being ignorant of God's righteousness and going about to establish their own righteousness, have not submitted themselves to the righteousness of God.
061004 For Christ is the end of the law for righteousness for everyone who believes.
061005 For Moses writes of the righteousness which is of the Law, "The man who does those things shall live by them."
061006 But the righteousness of faith says this: "Do not say in your heart, Who shall ascend into Heaven?" that is, to bring Christ down;
061007 or "Who shall descend into the deep?"; that is, to bring up Christ again from the dead.
061008 But what does it say? "The word is near you, even in your mouth and in your heart"; that is, the word of faith which we proclaim;
061009 Because if you confess the Lord Jesus, and believe in your heart that God has raised Him from the dead, you shall be saved.
061010 For with the heart one believes unto righteousness, and with the mouth one confesses unto salvation.
061011 For the Scripture says, "Everyone believing on Him shall not be put to shame."
061012 For there is no difference both of Jew and of Greek, for the same Lord over all is rich to all who call on Him.
061013 For everyone, "whoever shall call on the name of the Lord will be saved."
061014 How then shall they call on Him in whom they have not believed? And how shall they believe in Him of whom they have not heard? And how shall they hear without preaching?
061015 And how shall they preach unless they are sent? As it is written, "How beautiful are the feet of those who preach the gospel of peace and bring glad tidings of good things!"
061016 But they have not all obeyed the gospel. For Isaiah says, "Lord, who has believed our report?"
061017 Then faith is of hearing, and hearing by the Word of God.
061018 But I say, Have they not heard? Yes indeed, their voice went out into all the earth, and their words to the end of the world.
061019 But I say, Did not Israel know? First Moses says, "I will provoke you to jealousy by those who are no people, and by a foolish nation I will anger you."
061020 But Isaiah is very bold and says, "I was found by those who did not seek Me, I became known to those who did not ask after Me."
061021 But to Israel He says, "All day long I have stretched forth My hands to a disobeying and gainsaying people."
061101 I say then, Did not God put away His people? Let it not be said ! For I also am an Israelite, of the seed of Abraham, of the tribe of Benjamin.
061102 God did not thrust out His people whom He foreknew. Or do you not know what the Scripture said in Elijah, how he pleaded with God against Israel, saying,
061103 "Lord, they killed Your prophets and dug down Your altars, and I am left alone, and they seek my life."
061104 But what does the Divine answer say to him? "I have reserved to Myself seven thousand men who have not bowed the knee to Baal."
061105 Even so then, also in this present time a remnant according to the election of grace has come into being.
061106 But if by grace, then it is no more of works; otherwise grace is no more grace. But if it is of works, then it is no more of grace; otherwise work is no more work.
061107 What then? Israel has not obtained that which it seeks, but the election obtained it , and the rest were hardened
061108 even as it is written, "God gave to them a spirit of slumber, eyes not seeing, and ears not hearing" until this day.
061109 And David said, "Let their table become for a snare and a trap and a stumbling block and a recompense to them.
061110 Let their eyes be darkened so that they may not see, and their back always bowing."
061111 I say then, Did they not stumble that they fall? Let it not be! But by their slipping away came salvation to the nations, to provoke them to jealousy.
061112 But if their slipping away is the riches of the world, and their default is the riches of the nations, how much more their fullness?
061113 For I speak to you, the nations; since I am the apostle of the nations, I glorify my ministry;
061114 if by any means I may provoke those who are my flesh to jealousy, and might save some of them.
061115 For if their casting away is the reconciling of the world, what is the reception except life from the dead?
061116 For if the firstfruit is holy, the lump is also holy ; and if the root is holy, also the branches.
061117 And if some of the branches were broken off, and you, being a wild olive tree, were grafted in among them, and became a sharer of the root and the fatness of the olive tree with them,
061118 do not boast against the branches. But if you boast, it is not you that bears the root, but the root bears you.
061119 You will say then, The branches were broken off so that I might be grafted in.
061120 Well, because of unbelief they were broken off, and you stand by faith. Do not be high-minded, but fear.
061121 For if God did not spare the natural branches, fear lest He also may not spare you either!
061122 Behold then the kindness, and the severity of God; on those having fallen, severity; but on you, kindness, if you continue in the kindness. Otherwise you also will be cut off.
061123 And those also, if they do not continue in unbelief, will be grafted in. For God is able to graft them in again.
061124 For if you were cut out of the natural wild olive tree , and were grafted contrary to nature into a good olive tree ; how much more these being according to nature will be grafted into their own olive-tree?
061125 For I do not want you to be ignorant of this mystery, brothers, lest you should be wise within yourselves; that blindness in part has happened to Israel, until the fullness of the nations has comes in.
061126 And so all Israel shall be saved; as it is written, "There shall come out of Zion the Deliverer, and He will turn away ungodliness from Jacob.
061127 For this is My covenant with them, when I have taken away their sins."
061128 Indeed as regards the gospel, they are enemies for your sakes. But as regards the election, they are beloved for the fathers' sakes.
061129 For the free gifts and calling of God are without repentance.
061130 For as you also then disbelieved God, but now have been shown mercy through their disbelief,
061131 even so these also have not believed now, so that through your mercy they may also obtain mercy.
061132 For God has shut up all in unbelief, so that He might show mercy to all.
061133 O the depth of the riches both of the wisdom and knowledge of God! How unsearchable are His judgments, and His ways past finding out!
061134 For who has known the mind of the Lord, or who became His counselor?
061135 Or who first gave to Him, and it will be repaid to him?
061136 For of Him and through Him and to Him are all things; to Him be glory forever! Amen.
061201 I beseech you therefore, brothers, by the mercies of God to present your bodies a living sacrifice, holy, pleasing to God, which is your reasonable service.
061202 And do not be conformed to this world, but be transformed by the renewing of your mind, in order to prove by you what is that good and pleasing and perfect will of God.
061203 For I say, through the grace given to me, to every one who is among you, not to think of himself more highly than he ought to think. But set your mind to be right-minded, even as God has dealt to every man the measure of faith.
061204 For even as we have many members in one body, and all members do not have the same function,
061205 so we the many are one body in Christ, and each one members of one another.
061206 Then having gifts differing according to the grace that is given to us, if prophecy, according to the proportion of faith;
061207 or ministry, in the ministry; or he who teaches, in the teaching;
061208 or he who exhorts, in the encouragement; or he who shares, in simplicity; or he who takes the lead, in diligence; or he who shows mercy, in cheerfulness.
061209 Let love be without hypocrisy, shrinking from evil, cleaving to good;
061210 in brotherly love to one another, loving fervently, having led one another in honor.
061211 As to diligence, not slothful, fervent in spirit, serving the Lord;
061212 rejoicing in hope, patient in affliction, steadfastly continuing in prayer,
061213 distributing to the needs of the saints, pursuing hospitality.
061214 Bless those who persecute you; bless, and do not curse.
061215 Rejoice with rejoicing ones, and weep with weeping ones;
061216 minding the same thing toward one another, not minding high things, but yielding to the lowly. Do not be wise within yourselves.
061217 Repay no one evil for evil. Provide things honest in the sight of all men.
061218 If it is possible, as far as is in you, being in peace with all men.
061219 not avenging yourselves, beloved, but giving place to wrath; for it is written, "Vengeance is Mine, I will repay, says the Lord."
061220 Therefore if your enemy hungers, feed him. If he thirsts, give him drink. For in so doing you shall heap coals of fire on his head.
061221 Do not be overcome by evil, but overcome evil with good.
061301 Let every soul be subject to the higher authorities. For there is no authority but of God; the authorities that exist are ordained by God.
061302 So that the one resisting the authority resists the ordinance of God; and the ones who resist will receive judgment to themselves.
061303 For the rulers are not a terror to good works, but to the bad. And do you desire to be not afraid of the authority? Do the good, and you shall have praise from it.
061304 For it is a servant of God to you for good. For if you practice evil, be afraid, for it does not bear the sword in vain; for it is a servant of God, a revenger for wrath on him who does evil.
061305 Therefore you must be subject, not only for wrath, but also for conscience' sake.
061306 For because of this you also pay taxes. For they are God's servants, always giving attention to this very thing.
061307 Therefore give to all their dues; to the one due tax, the tax; tribute to whom tribute is due , fear to whom fear is due , and honor to whom honor is due .
061308 Owe no one anything, except to love one another; for he who loves another has fulfilled the law.
061309 For: "Do not commit adultery; do not murder; do not steal; do not bear false witness; do not lust;" and if there is any other commandment, it is summed up in this word, "You shall love your neighbor as yourself."
061310 Love works no ill to its neighbor, therefore love is the fulfilling of the law.
061311 This also, knowing the time, that it is already time to awake out of sleep; for now our salvation is nearer than when we believed.
061312 The night is far spent, the day is at hand; therefore let us cast off the works of darkness, and let us put on the armor of light.
061313 Let us walk becomingly, as in the day; not in carousings and drinking; not in co-habitation and lustful acts; not in strife and envy.
061314 But put on the Lord Jesus Christ, and do not take thought beforehand for the lusts of the flesh.
061401 And receive him who is weak in the faith, but not to judgments of your thoughts.
061402 For indeed one believes to eat all things; but being weak, another eats vegetables.
061403 Do not let him who eats despise him who does not eat; and do not let him who does not eat judge him who eats, for God has received him.
061404 Who are you that judges another's servant? To his own master he stands or falls. But he will stand, for God is able to make him stand.
061405 One indeed esteems a day above another day; and another esteems every day alike . Let each one be fully assured in his own mind.
061406 He who regards the day regards it to the Lord; and he not regarding the day, does not regard it to the Lord. He who eats, eats to the Lord, for he gives God thanks; and he who does not eat, does not eat to the Lord, and gives God thanks.
061407 For none of us lives to himself, and no one dies to himself.
061408 For both if we live, we live to the Lord; and if we die, we die to the Lord. Therefore both if we live, and if we die, we are the Lord's.
061409 For this Christ both died and rose and lived again, that He might be Lord both of the dead and living.
061410 But why do you judge your brother? Or also why do you despise your brother? For all shall stand before the judgment seat of Christ.
061411 For it is written, " As I live, says the Lord, every knee shall bow to Me, and every tongue shall confess to God."
061412 So then each one of us will give account concerning himself to God.
061413 Then let us not judge one another any more, but rather judge this, not to put a stumbling-block or an offense toward his brother.
061414 I know and am persuaded in the Lord Jesus, that nothing by itself is common; except to him who esteems anything to be common, it is common.
061415 But if your brother is grieved with your food, you no longer walk according to love. Do not with your food destroy him for whom Christ died.
061416 Then do not let your good be spoken evil of,
061417 for the kingdom of God is not eating and drinking, but righteousness and peace and joy in the Holy Spirit.
061418 For he who serves Christ in these things is well-pleasing to God, and approved by men.
061419 So then let us pursue the things of peace, and the things for building up one another.
061420 Do not undo the work of God for food. Truly, all things indeed are clean, but it is bad to the man eating because of a stumbling-block.
061421 It is good neither to eat flesh, nor to drink wine, nor anything by which your brother stumbles, or is offended, or is made weak.
061422 Do you have faith? Have it to yourself before God. Blessed is he who does not condemn himself in what he approves.
061423 But, the one doubting, if he eats, he has been condemned, because it is not of faith; and all that is not of faith is sin.
061501 Then we who are strong ought to bear the infirmities of the weak, and not to please ourselves.
061502 Let every one of us please his neighbor for his good, to building up.
061503 For even Christ did not please Himself; but as it is written, "The reproaches of those who reproached You fell on Me."
061504 For whatever things were written before were written for our learning, so that we through patience and comfort of the Scriptures might have hope.
061505 And may the God of patience and consolation grant you to be like minded toward one another according to Christ Jesus,
061506 so that with one mind and one mouth you may glorify God, even the Father of our Lord Jesus Christ.
061507 Therefore receive one another as Christ also received us, to the glory of God.
061508 And I say, Jesus Christ has become a minister of the circumcision for the truth of God, to confirm the promises made to the fathers,
061509 and that the nations might glorify God for His mercy, as it is written, "For this cause I will confess to You in the nations, and I will praise Your name."
061510 And again He says, "Rejoice, O nations, with His people."
061511 And again, "Praise the Lord, all the nations, and praise Him, all the peoples."
061512 And again Isaiah says, "There shall be a root of Jesse, and He who shall rise to reign over the nations, in Him shall the nations trust."
061513 And may the God of hope fill you with all joy and peace in believing, that you may abound in hope through the power of the Holy Spirit.
061514 And I myself also am persuaded of you, my brothers, that you also are full of goodness, filled with all knowledge, able also to admonish one another.
061515 But, brothers, I wrote to you boldly, as reminding you in part, because of the grace that is given to me by God,
061516 that I should be the minister of Jesus Christ to the nations, ministering the gospel of God, so that the offering up of the nations might be acceptable, being sanctified by the Holy Spirit.
061517 Therefore I have boasting in Christ Jesus as to the things pertaining to God.
061518 For I will not dare to speak of any of those things which Christ did not work out by me for the obedience of the nations in word and deed,
061519 in power of miracles and wonders, in power of the Spirit of God, so that from Jerusalem, and all around to Illyricum, I have fully preached the gospel of Christ.
061520 Yea, so I have been eager to preach the gospel, not where Christ was named, lest I should build on another man's foundation;
061521 but as it is written, "To whom nothing was said about Him, they shall see. And they who have not heard shall understand."
061522 For this cause I also have been greatly hindered from coming to you.
061523 But now, having no more place in these parts, and having a great desire these many years to come to you,
061524 whenever I may go into Spain, I will come to you. For in traveling through I hope to see you, and to be set forward there by you, if first I may be filled of you in part.
061525 But now I am going to Jerusalem to minister to the saints.
061526 For it has pleased those of Macedonia and Achaia to make a certain contribution for the poor saints in Jerusalem.
061527 Truly it has pleased them, and they are their debtors. For if the nations have been made partakers of their spiritual things, their duty is also to minister to them in fleshly things.
061528 Therefore when I have completed this, and have sealed this fruit to them, I will come by you into Spain.
061529 And I am sure that when I come to you, I shall come in the fullness of the blessing of the gospel of Christ.
061530 But I exhort you, brothers, for the sake of the Lord Jesus Christ and for the love of the Spirit, that you strive together with me in your prayers to God for me,
061531 that I may be delivered from those disbelieving in Judea, and that my service which I have for Jerusalem may be accepted by the saints;
061532 so that I may come to you with joy by the will of God, and may be refreshed with you.
061533 Now may the God of peace be with you all. Amen.
061601 I commend to you Phoebe our sister, who is a servant of the church in Cenchrea,
061602 that you receive her in the Lord, as becomes saints, and that you may assist her in whatever business she has need of you. For she has been a helper of many, and of myself also.
061603 Greet Priscilla and Aquila, my helpers in Christ Jesus,
061604 who have laid down their own necks for my life; to whom not only I give thanks, but also the churches of the nations.
061605 Likewise greet the church that is in their house. Greet my beloved Epenetus, who is the first-fruits of Achaia to Christ.
061606 Greet Mary, who bestowed much labor on us.
061607 Greet Andronicus and Junias, my kinsmen and my fellow prisoners, who are of note among the apostles, who also were in Christ before me.
061608 Greet Amplias my beloved in the Lord.
061609 Greet Urbanus, our helper in Christ, and Stachys my beloved.
061610 Greet Apelles, approved in Christ. Greet those who are of Aristobulus' household .
061611 Greet Herodion my kinsman. Greet those who are of the household of Narcissus, who are in the Lord.
061612 Greet Tryphena and Tryphosa, who labor in the Lord. Greet the beloved Persis, who labored much in the Lord.
061613 Greet Rufus, chosen in the Lord, and his mother and mine.
061614 Greet Asyncritus, Phlegon, Hermas, Patrobas, Hermes, and the brothers with them.
061615 Greet Philologus and Julias, Nereus and his sister, and Olympas, and all the saints with them.
061616 Greet one another with a holy kiss. The churches of Christ greet you.
061617 And I exhort you, brothers, to watch those making divisions and offenses contrary to the doctrine which you have learned, and avoid them.
061618 For they who are such do not serve our Lord Jesus Christ, but their own belly; and by good words and fair speeches they deceive the hearts of the simple.
061619 For your obedience reached to all. Therefore I am glad on your behalf, But I would have you truly wise as to good, and simple toward evil.
061620 And the God of peace shall bruise Satan under your feet shortly. May the grace of our Lord Jesus Christ be with you. Amen.
061621 Timothy my fellow worker, and Lucius, and Jason, and Sosipater my kinsmen, greet you.
061622 I, Tertius, who wrote this epistle, greet you in the Lord.
061623 Gaius my host, and the host of me and the whole church, greets you. Erastus the steward of the city greets you, and Quartus a brother.
061624 May the grace of our Lord Jesus Christ be with you all. Amen.
061625 Now to Him who is able to establish you according to my gospel, and the preaching of Jesus Christ according to the revelation of the mystery, having been unvoiced during eternal times;
061626 but now has been made plain, and by the prophetic Scriptures, according to the commandment of the everlasting God, made known to all nations for the obedience of faith;
061627 to God only wise be glory through Jesus Christ forever. Amen.
070101 Paul, a called apostle of Jesus Christ through the will of God, and Sosthenes our brother,
070102 to the church of God which is in Corinth, to those who are sanctified in Christ Jesus, called out with all those in every place who call on the name of Jesus Christ our Lord, both theirs and ours.
070103 Grace be to you, and peace from God our Father and the Lord Jesus Christ.
070104 I thank my God always on your behalf for the grace of God given you in Jesus Christ,
070105 that in everything you are enriched by Him, in all speech and in all knowledge;
070106 even as the testimony of Christ was confirmed in you;
070107 so that you come behind in no gift, waiting for the revelation of our Lord Jesus Christ.
070108 He shall also confirm you to the end, that you may be blameless in the day of our Lord Jesus Christ.
070109 God is faithful, by whom you were called to the fellowship of His Son, Jesus Christ our Lord.
070110 But I exhort you, brothers, by the name of our Lord Jesus Christ, that you all speak the same thing and that there be no divisions among you; but that you be perfectly joined together in the same mind and in the same judgment.
070111 For it has been declared to me concerning you, my brothers, by those of Chloe, that there are contentions among you.
070112 But I say this, that every one of you says, I am of Paul, and I of Apollos, and I of Cephas, and I of Christ.
070113 Is Christ divided? Was Paul crucified for you, or were you baptized in the name of Paul?
070114 I thank God that I baptized none of you except Crispus and Gaius,
070115 lest any should say that I had baptized in my own name.
070116 And I also baptized the household of Stephanas. Besides these, I do not know if I baptized any other.
070117 For Christ did not send me to baptize, but to preach the gospel; not in wisdom of words, lest the cross of Christ should be made of no effect.
070118 For the preaching of the cross is foolishness to those being lost, but to us being saved, it is the power of God.
070119 For it is written, "I will destroy the wisdom of the wise, and I will set aside the understanding of the perceiving ones."
070120 Where is the wise? Where is the scribe? Where is the lawyer of this world? Has not God made foolish the wisdom of this world?
070121 For since, in the wisdom of God, the world by wisdom did not know God, it pleased God by the foolishness of preaching to save those who believe.
070122 For the Jews ask for a sign, and the Greeks seek after wisdom;
070123 but we preach Christ crucified, to the Jews a stumbling block, and to the Greeks foolishness.
070124 But to them, the called-out ones, both Jews and Greeks, Christ is the power of God and the wisdom of God.
070125 Because the foolish thing of God is wiser than men, and the weak thing of God is stronger than men.
070126 For you see your calling, brothers, that not many wise men according to the flesh are called , not many mighty, not many noble.
070127 But God has chosen the foolish things of the world to confound the wise; and God has chosen the weak things of the world to confound the things which are mighty;
070128 and God has chosen the base things of the world, and things which are despised, and things which are not, in order to bring to nothing things that are;
070129 so that no flesh should glory in His presence.
070130 But of Him you are in Christ Jesus, who of God is made to us wisdom and righteousness and sanctification and redemption;
070131 so that, according as it is written, "He who glories, let him glory in the Lord."
070201 And I, brothers, when I came to you, did not come with excellency of speech or of wisdom, declaring to you the testimony of God.
070202 For I determined not to know anything among you except Jesus Christ and Him crucified.
070203 And I was with you in weakness and in fear, and in much trembling.
070204 And my speech and my preaching was not with enticing words of man's wisdom, but in demonstration of the Spirit and of power,
070205 so that your faith should not stand in the wisdom of men, but in the power of God.
070206 But, we speak wisdom among those who are perfect; yet not the wisdom of this world, nor of the rulers of this world, that come to nothing.
070207 But we speak the wisdom of God in a mystery, which God has hidden, predetermining it before the world for our glory;
070208 which none of the rulers of this world knew (for if they had known, they would not have crucified the Lord of glory).
