070209 But as it is written, "Eye has not seen, nor ear heard," nor has it entered into the heart of man, "the things which God has prepared for those who love Him."
070210 But God has revealed them to us by His Spirit; for the Spirit searches all things, yea, the deep things of God.
070211 For who among men knows the things of a man except the spirit of man within him? So also no one knows the things of God except the Spirit of God.
070212 But we have not received the spirit of the world, but the Spirit from God, so that we might know the things that are freely given to us by God.
070213 These things we also speak, not in words which man's wisdom teaches, but which the Holy Spirit teaches, comparing spiritual things with spiritual.
070214 But the natural man does not receive the things of the Spirit of God, for they are foolishness to him; neither can he know them , because they are spiritually discerned.
070215 But he who is spiritual judges all things, yet he himself is judged by no one.
070216 For who has known the mind of the Lord, that he may instruct Him? But we have the mind of Christ.
070301 And I, brothers, could not speak to you as to spiritual ones, but as to fleshly, as to babes in Christ.
070302 I have fed you with milk and not with solid food, for you were not yet able to bear it ; nor are you able even now.
070303 For you are yet carnal. For in that there is among you envyings and strife and divisions, are you not carnal, and do you not walk according to men?
070304 For while one says, I am of Paul; and another, I am of Apollos; are you not carnal?
070305 Who then is Paul, and who is Apollos, but ministers by whom you believed, even as the Lord gave to each?
070306 I have planted, Apollos watered, but God gave the increase.
070307 So then neither is he who plants anything, nor he who waters, but God who gives the increase.
070308 So he planting, and he watering, are one, and each one shall receive his own reward according to his own labor.
070309 For of God we are fellow-workers, a field of God, and you are a building of God.
070310 According to the grace of God which is given to me, as a wise master builder, I have laid the foundation, and another builds on it . But let every man be careful how he builds on it .
070311 For any other foundation can no one lay than the one being laid, who is Jesus Christ.
070312 And if anyone builds on this foundation gold, silver, precious stones, wood, hay, stubble,
070313 each one's work shall be revealed. For the Day shall declare it , because it shall be revealed by fire; and the fire shall try each one's work as to what kind it is.
070314 If anyone's work which he built remains, he shall receive a reward.
070315 If anyone's work shall be burned up, he shall suffer loss. But he shall be saved, yet so as by fire.
070316 Do you not know that you are a temple of God, and that the Spirit of God dwells in you?
070317 If anyone defiles the temple of God, God shall destroy him. For the temple of God is holy, which you are.
070318 Let no one deceive himself. If anyone among you seems to be wise in this world, let him become a fool so that he may be wise.
070319 For the wisdom of this world is foolishness with God; for it is written, "He takes the wise in their own craftiness."
070320 And again, " The Lord knows the thoughts of the wise, that they are vain."
070321 Therefore let no one glory in men. For all things are yours,
070322 whether it is Paul, or Apollos, or Cephas, or the world, or life, or death, or things present, or things to come; all are yours,
070323 and you are Christ's, and Christ is God's.
070401 So let a man think of us as ministers of Christ and stewards of the mysteries of God.
070402 And the rest, it is sought among stewards that one be found faithful.
070403 But to me it is a very small thing that I should be judged by you, or by a man's day; but I do not judge my own self,
070404 for I know nothing by myself. Yet I have not been justified by this, but He who judges me is the Lord.
070405 Therefore judge nothing before the time, until the Lord comes, who both will bring to light the hidden things of darkness and will make manifest the counsels of the hearts. And then shall each one have praise of God.
070406 And these things, brothers, I have in a figure transferred to myself and Apollos for your sakes, so that you might learn in us not to think of men above that which is written, so that no one of you may be puffed up against one another.
070407 For who makes you to differ from another ? And what do you have that you did not receive? And if you did receive it , why do you boast as if you had not received it?
070408 Already you are full! Already you are rich! You have reigned as kings without us! And oh that indeed you did reign, that we also might reign with you.
070409 For I think that God has set forth us last, the apostles, as it were appointed to death; for we have become a spectacle to the world and to angels and to men.
070410 We are fools for Christ's sake, but you are wise in Christ. We are weak, but you are strong. You are honorable, but we are despised.
070411 Even until this present hour we both hunger and thirst and are naked and are buffeted and have no certain dwelling place.
070412 And we labor, working with our own hands. Being reviled, we bless; being persecuted, we suffer it;
070413 being defamed, we entreat. We are made as the filth of the world, the offscouring of all things until now.
070414 I do not write these things to shame you, but as my beloved children I warn you .
070415 For though you have ten thousand instructors in Christ, yet you do not have many fathers; for I have begotten you in Christ Jesus through the gospel.
070416 Therefore I beseech you, be imitators of me.
070417 For this cause I have sent Timothy to you, who is my beloved son and faithful in the Lord, who shall remind you of my ways which are in Christ, as I teach everywhere in every church.
070418 As to my not coming to you now, some are puffed up.
070419 But I will come to you shortly, if the Lord wills. And I will not know the speech of those who are puffed up, but the power.
070420 For the kingdom of God is not in word, but in power.
070421 What do you desire? Shall I come to you with a rod, or in love and the spirit of meekness?
070501 On the whole it is reported that there is fornication among you, and such fornication as is not even named among the nations, so as one to have his father's wife.
070502 And you are puffed up, and have not rather mourned, so that he who has done this deed may be taken from your midst.
070503 For as being absent in body but present in spirit, I indeed have judged already as though I were present concerning him who worked out this thing;
070504 in the name of our Lord Jesus Christ, when you are gathered together, with my spirit; also, with the power of our Lord Jesus Christ;
070505 to deliver such a one to Satan for the destruction of the flesh, so that the spirit may be saved in the day of the Lord Jesus.
070506 Your boasting is not good. Do you not know that a little leaven leavens the whole lump?
070507 Therefore purge out the old leaven so that you may be a new lump, as you are unleavened. For also Christ our Passover is sacrificed for us.
070508 Therefore let us keep the feast; not with old leaven, nor with the leaven of malice and wickedness, but with the unleavened bread of sincerity and truth.
070509 I wrote to you in the letter not to associate intimately with fornicators;
070510 yet not altogether with the fornicators of this world, or with the covetous, or extortioners, or with idolaters; for then you must go out of the world.
070511 But now I have written to you not to associate intimately, if any man called a brother and is either a fornicator, or covetous, or an idolater, or a reviler, or a drunkard, or an extortioner; with such a one not to eat.
070512 For what is it to me to also judge those who are outside? Do you not judge those who are inside?
070513 But God judges those who are outside. Therefore put out from you the evil one.
070601 Do any of you dare, when you have a matter against another, to go to law before the unjust, and not before the saints?
070602 Do you not know that the saints shall judge the world? And if the world shall be judged by you, are you unworthy to judge the smallest matters?
070603 Do you not know that we shall judge angels, not to mention the things of this life?
070604 If, then, you truly have judgments of the things of this life, set those who are least esteemed in the church to judge .
070605 For I speak to your shame. Is it so that there is not a wise one among you, not even one in your midst who shall be able to judge between his brother?
070606 But brother goes to law with brother, and that before the unbelievers.
070607 Indeed then there is already on the whole a failure among you, that you have lawsuits with yourselves. Why not instead be wronged? Why not instead be defrauded?
070608 But you do wrong and defraud, and these things to brothers.
070609 Do you not know that the unrighteous shall not inherit the kingdom of God? Do not be deceived; neither fornicators, nor idolaters, nor adulterers, nor abusers, nor homosexuals,
070610 nor thieves, nor covetous, nor drunkards, nor revilers, nor extortioners, shall inherit the kingdom of God.
070611 And such were some of you. But you are washed, but you are sanctified, but you are justified in the name of the Lord Jesus, and by the Spirit of our God.
070612 All things are lawful to me, but not all things profit. All things are lawful for me, but I will not be brought under the power of any.
070613 Meats for the belly and the belly for meats, but God shall destroy both it and them. But the body is not for fornication, but for the Lord; and the Lord is for the body.
070614 And God has both raised up the Lord, and also will raise us up by His own power.
070615 Do you not know that your bodies are the members of Christ? Shall I then take the members of Christ and make them the members of a harlot? Let it not be!
070616 Or do you not know that he being joined to a harlot is one body? For He says, The two shall be one flesh.
070617 But he being joined to the Lord is one spirit.
070618 Flee fornication. Every sin that a man does is outside the body, but he who commits fornication sins against his own body.
070619 Or do you not know that your body is a temple of the Holy Spirit in you, whom you have of God? And you are not your own,
070620 for you are bought with a price. Therefore glorify God in your body and in your spirit, which are God's.
070701 Now concerning what you wrote to me: It is good for a man not to touch a woman.
070702 But, because of the fornications, let each have his own wife, and let each have her own husband.
070703 Let the husband give to the wife proper kindness, and likewise the wife also to the husband.
070704 The wife does not have authority over her own body, but the husband. And likewise also the husband does not have authority over his own body, but the wife.
070705 Do not deprive one another, unless it is with consent for a time, so that you may give yourselves to fasting and prayer. And come together again so that Satan does not tempt you for your incontinence.
070706 But I speak this according to permission, not according to commandment.
070707 For I would that all men were even as I myself am. But each has his proper gift from God, one according to this manner and another according to that.
070708 I say therefore to the unmarried and the widows, It is good for them if they remain even as I.
070709 But if they do not have self-control, let them marry; for it is better to marry than to burn.
070710 And to the married I command (not I, but the Lord), a woman not to be separated from her husband.
070711 But if she is indeed separated, let her remain unmarried, or be reconciled to her husband. And a husband is not to leave his wife.
070712 But to the rest I speak, not the Lord, If any brother has a wife who does not believe, and she is pleased to dwell with him, do not let him put her away.
070713 And the woman who has a husband who does not believe, if he is pleased to dwell with her, do not let her leave him.
070714 For the unbelieving husband is sanctified by the wife, and the unbelieving wife is sanctified by the husband; else your children would be unclean, but now they are holy.
070715 But if the unbelieving one separates, let him be separated. A brother or a sister is not in bondage in such cases , but God has called us in peace.
070716 For what do you know, O wife, whether you shall save your husband? Or what do you know, O man, whether you shall save your wife?
070717 But as God has distributed to each one, as the Lord has called each one, so let him walk. And so I ordain in all churches.
070718 Was any called having been circumcised? Do not be uncircumcised. Was anyone called in uncircumcision? Do not be circumcised.
070719 Circumcision is nothing, and uncircumcision is nothing, but the keeping of the commandments of God.
070720 Let each one remain in the calling in which he was called.
070721 Were you called as a slave? It does not matter to you, but if you are able to become free, use it rather.
070722 For he who is called a slave in the Lord is a freed man of the Lord. And likewise, he who is called a free man is a slave of Christ.
070723 You are bought with a price, do not be the slaves of men.
070724 Each in whatever way he was called, brothers, in this remain with God.
070725 But concerning virgins, I have no commandment from the Lord. Yet I give my judgment, as one who has obtained mercy from the Lord to be faithful.
070726 Then I think this is good, because of the present necessity; that it is good for a man to be so.
070727 Are you bound to a wife? Do not seek to be free. Are you loosed from a wife? Do not seek a wife.
070728 But if you do marry, you did not sin; and if a virgin marries, she has not sinned. But such shall have trouble in the flesh, but I spare you.
070729 But this I say, brothers, The time is short. It remains that both those who have wives should be as not having one.
070730 And they who weep are as though they did not weep. And they who rejoice are as though they did not rejoice. And they who buy are as though they did not possess.
070731 And they who use this world are as not abusing it , for the fashion of this world is passing away.
070732 But I desire you to be without anxiety. The one who is unmarried cares for the things that belong to the Lord, how to please the Lord.
070733 But the one who is married cares for the things of the world, how to please his wife.
070734 The wife and the virgin are different. The unmarried woman cares for the things of the Lord, that she may be holy both in body and in spirit. But she who is married cares for the things of the world, how she may please her husband.
070735 And this I speak for your own profit, not that I may cast a snare on you, but for that which is right, and that you may attend on the Lord without distraction.
070736 But if anyone thinks it behaving himself indecently toward his virgin (if she is past her prime, and so it ought to be) let him do what he will; he does not sin; let them marry.
070737 But he who stands steadfast in his heart, having no necessity, but who has authority over his own will (and has so judged in his heart that he will keep his virginity) he does well.
070738 So then he who gives in marriage does well. But he who does not give in marriage does better.
070739 The wife is bound by the law as long as her husband lives, but if her husband sleeps in death, she is at liberty to be remarried to whom she will, only in the Lord.
070740 But she is happier if she so remains, according to my judgment. And I also think that I have the Spirit of God.
070801 But concerning the sacrifices to idols, we know that we all have knowledge. Knowledge puffs up, but love edifies.
070802 And if any man thinks that he knows anything, he knows nothing yet as he ought to know.
070803 But if any one loves God, he has been known of him.
070804 Then concerning the eating of the things sacrificed to idols, we know that an idol is nothing in the world, and that there is no other God except one.
070805 For though there are those who are called gods, whether in Heaven or in earth (as there are many gods and many lords),
070806 but there is to us only one God, the Father, of whom are all things, and we in Him; and one Lord Jesus Christ, through whom are all things, and we by Him.
070807 But this knowledge is not in all. But some being aware of the idol eat as an idolatrous sacrifice until now, and their conscience being weak is defiled.
070808 But food does not commend us to God. For neither if we eat are we the better, nor if we do not eat are we the worse.
070809 But take heed lest by any means this liberty of yours becomes a stumbling block to those who are weak.
070810 For if anyone sees you who have knowledge sitting in an idol temple, will not the weak one's conscience be lifted up so as to eat things sacrificed to idols?
070811 And on your knowledge the weak brother will fall, he for whom Christ died.
070812 And sinning in this way against your brothers, and wounding their conscience, being weak, you sin against Christ.
070813 Therefore, if food offends my brother, I will eat no flesh forever, that I do not offend my brother.
070901 Am I not an apostle? Am I not free? Have I not seen Jesus Christ our Lord? Are you not my work in the Lord?
070902 If I am not an apostle to others, yet doubtless I am to you, for you are the seal of my apostleship in the Lord.
070903 My answer to those who examine me is this:
070904 Do we not have authority to eat and to drink?
070905 Do we not have authority to lead about a sister, a wife, as well as other apostles, and as the brothers of the Lord do, and Cephas?
070906 Or is it only Barnabas and I who have no authority whether not to work?
070907 Who serves as a soldier at his own wages at any time? Who plants a vineyard and does not eat of its fruit? Or who feeds a flock and does not partake of the milk of the flock?
070908 Do I say these things according to man? Or does not the Law say the same also?
070909 For it is written in the law of Moses, "You shall not muzzle an ox threshing grain." Does God take care for oxen?
070910 Or does He say it altogether for our sakes? It was written for us, so that he who plows should plow in hope, and so that he who threshes in hope should be partaker of his hope.
070911 If we have sown to you spiritual things, is it a great thing if we shall reap your carnal things?
070912 If others have a share of this authority over you, rather should not we? But we have not used this authority, but we endured all things lest we should hinder the gospel of Christ.
070913 Do you not know that those who minister about holy things live of the things of the temple? And those attending the altar are partakers with the altar.
070914 Even so, the Lord ordained those announcing the gospel to live from the gospel.
070915 But I have used none of these things, nor have I written these things that it should be done so to me; for it is good for me rather to die than that anyone nullify my glorying.
070916 For though I preach the gospel, no glory is to me. For necessity is laid on me; yea, woe is to me if I do not preach the gospel!
070917 For if I do this thing willingly, I have a reward; but if against my will, I am entrusted with a stewardship.
070918 What then is my reward? That when I preach the gospel I may make the gospel of Christ without charge, that I may not abuse my authority in the gospel.
070919 For though I am free from all, yet I have made myself servant to all, so that I might gain the more.
070920 And to the Jews I became as a Jew, so that I might gain the Jews. To those who are under the Law, I became as under the Law, so that I might gain those who are under the Law.
070921 To those who are outside Law, I became as outside Law (not being outside law to God, but under the law to Christ), so that I might gain those who are outside Law.
070922 To the weak I became as the weak, so that I might gain the weak. I am made all things to all men , so that I might by all means save some.
070923 And this I do for the sake of the gospel, so that I might be partaker of it with you .
070924 Do you not know that those running in a race all run, but one receives the prize? So run, that you may obtain.
070925 And everyone who strives for the mastery is temperate in all things. Then those truly that they may receive a corruptible crown, but we an incorruptible.
070926 So then I run, not as if I were uncertain. And so I fight, not as one who beats the air.
070927 But I buffet my body, and lead it captive, lest proclaiming to others I myself might be rejected.
071001 And, brothers, I do not want you to be ignorant that all our fathers were under the cloud, and all passed through the sea.
071002 And all were baptized to Moses in the cloud and in the sea,
071003 and all ate the same spiritual food,
071004 and all drank the same spiritual drink; for they drank of the spiritual Rock that followed them, and that Rock was Christ.
071005 But with many of them God was not well pleased, for they were scattered in the wilderness.
071006 And these things were our examples, that we should not be lusters after evil, as they also lusted.
071007 Nor should we be idolaters, even as some of them, as it is written: "The people sat down to eat and drink, and rose up to play."
071008 Nor let us commit fornication, as some of them fornicated, and twenty-three thousand fell in one day.
071009 Nor let us tempt Christ, as some of them also tempted Him and were destroyed by serpents.
071010 Nor murmur as some of them also murmured and were destroyed by the destroyer.
071011 And all these things happened to them as examples; and it is written for our warning on whom the ends of the world have come.
071012 So let him who thinks he stands take heed lest he fall.
071013 No temptation has taken you but what is common to man; but God is faithful, who will not allow you to be tempted above what you are able, but with the temptation also will make a way to escape, so that you may be able to bear it .
071014 Therefore, my dearly beloved, flee from idolatry.
071015 I speak as to wise men; you judge what I say.
071016 The cup of blessing which we bless, is it not the communion of the blood of Christ? The bread which we break, is it not the communion of the body of Christ?
071017 For we, the many, are one bread and one body; for we are all partakers of that one bread.
071018 Behold Israel after the flesh. Are not those who eat of the sacrifices also partakers of the altar?
071019 What then do I say? That the idol is anything, or that an idolatrous sacrifice is anything?
071020 But I say that the things which the nations sacrifice, they sacrifice to demons and not to God. And I do not desire that you should have fellowship with demons.
071021 You cannot drink the cup of the Lord and the cup of demons; you cannot be partakers of the Lord's table and of a table of demons.
071022 Or do we provoke the Lord to jealousy? Are we stronger than He?
071023 All things are lawful to me, but not all things profit. All things are lawful to me, but not all things build up.
071024 Let no one seek his own, but each one another's.
071025 Eat whatever is sold in the meat market, asking no question for conscience' sake;
071026 "for the earth is the Lord's, and the fullness of it."
071027 If any of those who do not believe invite you to a feast , and if you are disposed to go, eat whatever is set before you, asking no questions for conscience' sake.
071028 But if anyone says to you, This is slain in sacrifice to idols, do not eat for the sake of him who showed it , and for conscience' sake; "for the earth is the Lord's, and the fullness of it";
071029 conscience, I say, not your own, but the other's. For why is my liberty judged by another's conscience?
071030 For if I by grace am a partaker, why am I evil spoken of for that for which I give thanks?
071031 Therefore whether you eat or drink, or whatever you do, do all to the glory of God.
071032 Give no offense, either to the Jews, or to the Greeks or to the church of God;
071033 even as I please all men in all things , not seeking my own profit, but the profit of the many, so that they may be saved.
071101 Be imitators of me, even as I also am of Christ.
071102 But I praise you, brothers, that you remember me in all things, and you keep the doctrines as I delivered them to you.
071103 But I would have you know that the head of every man is Christ; and the head of the woman is the man; and the head of Christ is God.
071104 Every man praying or prophesying with his head covered dishonors his Head.
071105 But every woman who prays or prophesies with her head unveiled dishonors her head; for that is even the same as if she were shaved.
071106 For if the woman is not veiled, let her also be shorn. But if it is a shame for a woman to be shorn or shaven, let her be veiled.
071107 For a man indeed ought not to have his head covered, because he is the image and glory of God. But the woman is the glory of the man.
071108 For the man is not of the woman, but the woman of the man.
071109 Nor was the man created for the woman, but the woman for the man.
071110 For this reason the woman ought to have authority on her head because of the angels.
071111 But neither is the man without the woman, nor the woman without the man, in the Lord.
071112 For as the woman is of the man, even so the man is also through the woman; but all things of God.
071113 Judge among yourselves: is it right that a woman pray to God unveiled?
071114 Does not even nature itself teach you that if man has long hair, it is a shame to him?
071115 But if a woman should have long hair, it is a glory to her; for her hair is given to her in place of a veil.
071116 But if anyone seems to be contentious, we have no such custom, nor the churches of God.
071117 But in enjoining this, I do not praise you , because you come together not for the better, but for the worse.
071118 For first of all, when you come together in the church, I hear that there are divisions among you, and I partly believe it.
071119 For there must also be heresies among you, that the approved ones may be revealed among you.
071120 Therefore when you come together into one place, this is not to eat the Lord's supper.
071121 For in eating each one takes his own supper first; and one is hungry, and another drunken.
071122 For do you not have houses in which to eat and drink? Or do you despise the church of God, and shame those who do not have? What shall I say to you? Shall I praise you for this? I do not praise you !
071123 For I received from the Lord what I also delivered to you, that the Lord Jesus in the night in which he was betrayed took bread;
071124 And giving thanks, He broke it and said, "Take, eat; this is My body, which is broken for you; this do in remembrance of Me."
071125 In the same way He took the cup also, after supping, saying, "This cup is the New Covenant in My blood; as often as you drink it, do this in remembrance of Me."
071126 For "as often as you eat this bread and drink this cup, you show" the Lord's death until He shall come.
071127 So that whoever shall eat this bread and drink this cup of the Lord unworthily, he will be guilty of the body and blood of the Lord.
071128 But let a man examine himself, and so let him eat of that bread and drink of that cup.
071129 For he who eats and drinks unworthily eats and drinks condemnation to himself, not discerning the Lord's body.
071130 For this cause many among you are weak and sickly, and many sleep.
071131 For if we would judge ourselves, we would not be judged.
071132 But when we are judged, we are chastened by the Lord, that we should not be condemned with the world.
071133 So that, my brothers, when you come together to eat, wait for one another.
071134 But if anyone hungers, let him eat at home, so that you do not come together to condemnation. And the rest I will set in order when I come.
071201 Now concerning spiritual gifts , brothers, I would not have you ignorant.
071202 You know that being led away, you nations were led to dumb idols.
071203 Therefore I make known to you that no one speaking by the Spirit of God says Jesus is a curse, and that no one can say that Jesus is Lord, but by the Holy Spirit.
071204 But there are differences of gifts, but the same Spirit.
071205 And there are differences of ministries, but the same Lord.
071206 And there are differences of workings, but it is the same God working all things in all.
071207 But to each one is given the showing forth of the Spirit to our profit.
071208 For through the Spirit is given to one a word of wisdom; and to another a word of knowledge, according to the same Spirit;
071209 and to another faith by the same Spirit; and to another the gifts of healing by the same Spirit;
071210 and to another workings of powers, to another prophecy; and to another discerning of spirits; and to another kinds of tongues; and to another the interpretation of tongues.
071211 But the one and the same Spirit works all these things, distributing separately to each one as He desires.
071212 For as the body is one and has many members, and all the members of that one body, being many, are one body; so also is Christ.
071213 For also by one Spirit we are all baptized into one body, whether Jews or Greeks, whether bond or free, even all were made to drink into one Spirit.
071214 For the body is not one member, but many.
071215 If the foot shall say, Because I am not the hand, I am not of the body; is it therefore not of the body?
071216 And if the ear shall say, Because I am not the eye, I am not of the body; is it therefore not of the body?
071217 If all the body were an eye, where would be the hearing? If all hearing, where would be the smelling?
071218 But now God has set the members, each one of them, in the body as it has pleased Him.
071219 And if they were all one member, where would be the body?
071220 But now indeed many are the members, yet only one body.
071221 And the eye cannot say to the hand, I have no need of you; nor again the head to the feet, I have no need of you.
071222 But much rather the members of the body seeming to be weaker are necessary.
071223 And those members of the body which we think to be less honorable, on these we put more abundant honor around them . And our unpresentable members have more abundant propriety.
071224 For our presentable members have no need, but God tempered the body together, giving more abundant honor to the member having need;
071225 that there not be division in the body, but that the members should have the same care for one another.
071226 And if one member suffers, all the members suffer with it ; if one member is glorified, all the members rejoice with it .
071227 And you are the body of Christ, and members in part.
071228 And God set some in the church, firstly, apostles; secondly, prophets; thirdly, teachers, then works of power, then gifts of healings, helps, governments, kinds of languages.
071229 Are all apostles? Are all prophets? Are all teachers? Are all workers of power?
071230 Do all have gifts of healings? Do all speak languages? Do all interpret?
071231 But zealously strive after the better gifts. And yet I show to you a more excellent way.
071301 Though I speak with the tongues of men and of angels, and have not charity, I have become as sounding brass or a tinkling cymbal.
071302 And though I have prophecies, and understand all mysteries and all knowledge; and though I have all faith, so as to move mountains, and do not have charity, I am nothing.
071303 And though I give out all my goods to feed the poor , and though I deliver my body to be burned, and have not charity, I am profited nothing.
071304 Charity has patience, is kind; charity is not envious, is not vain, is not puffed up;
071305 does not behave indecently, does not seek her own, is not easily provoked, thinks no evil.
071306 Charity does not rejoice in unrighteousness, but rejoices in the truth,
071307 quietly covers all things, believes all things, hopes all things, endures all things.
071308 Charity never fails. But if there are prophecies, they will be abolished; if tongues, they shall cease; if knowledge, it will be abolished.
071309 For we know in part, and we prophesy in part.
071310 But when the perfect thing comes, then that which is in part will be caused to cease.
071311 When I was an infant, I spoke as an infant, I thought as an infant, I reasoned as an infant. But when I became a man, I did away with the things of an infant.
071312 For now we see in a mirror dimly, but then face to face. Now I know in part, but then I shall fully know even as I also am fully known.
071313 And now faith, hope, charity, these three remain; but the greatest of these is charity.
071401 Follow after charity and desire spiritual things , but rather that you may prophesy.
071402 For he who speaks in a tongue does not speak to men but to God. For no one hears, but in spirit he speaks mysteries.
071403 But he who prophesies speaks to men for building up, and exhortation, and comfort.
071404 The one speaking in a tongue builds himself up, but he prophesying builds up a church.
071405 I wish all of you to speak in languages, but rather that you may prophesy; for greater is he prophesying than he speaking in tongues, unless he interpret so that the church may receive building up.
071406 But now, brothers, if I come to you speaking in tongues, what will I profit you, except I speak to you either in revelation, or in knowledge, or in prophecy, or in teaching?
071407 Yet lifeless things giving a sound, whether flute or harp, if they do not give a distinction in the sound, how will it be known what is being piped or harped?
071408 For also if a trumpet gives an uncertain sound, who shall prepare himself for the battle?
071409 So also you, if you do not give a clear word through the language, how will it be known what is being said? For you will be speaking into the air.
071410 So it may be many kinds of sounds are in the world, and not one is without a distinct sound.
071411 Therefore if I do not know the power of the sound, I will be a foreigner to him speaking, and he speaking will be a foreigner to me.
071412 Even so you, since you are zealots of spiritual things , seek to build up the church, in order that you may abound
071413 So then he speaking in a language, let him pray that he may interpret.
071414 For if I pray in a tongue, my spirit prays, but my mind is unfruitful.
071415 What is it then? I will pray with the spirit, and I will also pray with the mind; I will sing with the spirit, and I will also sing with the mind.
071416 Else, if you bless in the spirit, he occupying the place of the unlearned, how will he say the amen at your giving of thanks, since he does not know what you say?
071417 For you truly give thanks well, but the other is not built up.
071418 I thank my God that I speak more languages than all of you;
071419 yet in a church I desire to speak five words with my mind, so that I might also teach others, than ten thousand words in a tongue.
071420 Brothers, do not be children in your minds, but in malice be like infants, and in your minds be mature.
071421 In the law it is written, "By other tongues and other lips I will speak to this people, and even so they will not hear Me, says the Lord."
071422 So that tongues are not a sign to those who believe, but to those who do not believe. But prophesying is not to those who do not believe, but to those who believe.
071423 Therefore if the whole church has come together, and all speak in languages, and if uninstructed ones or unbelievers come in, will they not say that you rave?
071424 But if all prophesy, and some unbeliever or one not instructed comes, he is convicted by all, he is judged by all.
071425 And so the secrets of his heart become revealed. And so, falling down on his face, he will worship God and report that God is truly among you.
071426 Then how is it, brothers? When you come together, each one of you has a psalm, has a teaching, has a tongue, has a revelation, has an interpretation. Let all things be for building up.
071427 If one speaks in a language, let it be by two, or at the most three, and in succession. And let one interpret.
071428 But if there is no interpreter, let him be silent in a church; and let him speak to himself and to God.
071429 And if there are two or three prophets, let them speak, and let the others judge.
071430 If a revelation is revealed to another sitting by, let the first be silent.
071431 For you may all prophesy one by one, so that all may learn and all may be comforted.
071432 And the spirits of the prophets are subject to the prophets.
071433 For God is not the author of confusion, but of peace, as in all churches of the saints.
071434 Let your women be silent in the churches; for it is not permitted to them to speak, but to be in subjection, as the Law also says.
071435 And if they desire to learn anything, let them ask their husbands at home; for it is a shame for a woman to speak in a church.
071436 Or did the Word of God go out from you? Or did it reach only to you?
071437 If anyone thinks to be a prophet, or a spiritual one, let him recognize the things I write to you, that they are a commandment of the Lord.
071438 But if any is ignorant, let him be ignorant.
071439 So then, brothers, seek to prophesy, and do not forbid to speak in languages.
071440 Let all things be done decently and in order.
071501 And, brothers, I declare to you the gospel which I preached to you, which also you have received, and in which you stand;
071502 by which you also are being kept safe, if you hold fast the word which I preached to you, unless you believed in vain.
071503 For I delivered to you first of all that which I also received, that Christ died for our sins, according to the Scriptures,
071504 and that He was buried, and that He rose again the third day according to the Scriptures;
071505 and that He was seen by Cephas, then by the Twelve.
071506 Afterward He was seen by over five hundred brothers at once, of whom the greater part remain until this present day, but also some fell asleep.
071507 Afterward He was seen by James, then by all the apostles.
071508 And last of all He was seen by me also, as one born out of time.
071509 For I am the least of the apostles and am not sufficient to be called an apostle, because I persecuted the church of God.
071510 But by the grace of God I am what I am, and His grace which was toward me has not been without fruit, but I labored more abundantly than all of them; yet not I, but the grace of God with me.
071511 Therefore whether it was I or they, so we preach, and so you believed.
071512 But if Christ is proclaimed, that He was raised from the dead, how do some among you say that there is no resurrection of the dead?
071513 But if there is no resurrection of the dead, neither has Christ been raised.
071514 And if Christ has not been raised, then our proclamation is worthless, and your faith is also worthless.
071515 And we are also found to be false witnesses of God, because we testified of God that He raised Christ; whom He did not raise if the dead are not raised.
071516 For if the dead are not raised, then Christ is not raised.
071517 And if Christ is not raised, your faith is foolish; you are yet in your sins.
071518 Then also those that fell asleep in Christ were lost.
071519 If in this life only we have hope in Christ, we are of all men most miserable.
071520 But now Christ has risen from the dead, and has become the firstfruit of those who slept.
071521 For since death is through man, the resurrection of the dead also is through a Man.
071522 For as in Adam all die, even so in Christ all will be made alive.
071523 But each in his own order: Christ the first-fruit, and afterward they who are Christ's at His coming;
071524 then is the end, when He delivers the kingdom to God, even the Father; when He makes to cease all rule and all authority and power.
071525 for it is right for Him to reign until He has put all the enemies under His feet.
071526 The last enemy made to cease is death.
071527 For He put all things under His feet. But when He says that all things have been put under His feet , it is plain that it excepts Him who has put all things under Him.
071528 But when all things are subjected to Him, then the Son Himself also will be subject to Him who has subjected all things to Him, so that God may be all things in all.
071529 Otherwise, what will they do, those being baptized on behalf of the dead? If the dead are not at all raised, why indeed are they baptized on behalf of the dead?
071530 And why are we also in danger every hour?
071531 Day by day I die, by your rejoicing, which I have in Christ Jesus our Lord.
071532 If according to man I fought with beasts in Ephesus, what advantage is to me if the dead are not raised? "Let us eat and drink, for tomorrow we die!"
071533 Do not be deceived; evil companionships corrupt good habits.
071534 Be righteously awake, and sin not; for some have ignorance of God. I speak this to your shame.
071535 But someone will say, How are the dead raised up, and with what body do they come?
071536 Foolish one! What you sow is not made alive unless it dies.
071537 And what you sow, you do not sow the body that is going to be, but a bare grain (perhaps of wheat or of some of the rest).
071538 And God gives it a body as it has pleased Him, and to each of the seeds its own body.
071539 All flesh is not the same flesh; but one kind of flesh of men, and another flesh of beasts, and another of fish, and another of birds.
071540 There are also heavenly bodies and earthly bodies. But the glory of the heavenly is truly different, and that of the earthly different;
071541 one glory of the sun, and another glory of the moon, and another glory of the stars; for one star differs from another star in glory.
071542 So also the resurrection of the dead. It is sown in corruption, it is raised in incorruption;
071543 it is sown in dishonor, it is raised in glory; it is sown in weakness, it is raised in power;
071544 it is sown a natural body, it is raised a spiritual body. There is a natural body, and there is a spiritual body.
071545 And so it is written, "The first man, Adam, became a living soul," the last Adam was a life-giving Spirit.
071546 But not the spiritual first, but the natural; afterward the spiritual.
071547 The first man was out of earth, earthy; the second Man was the Lord from Heaven.
071548 Such the earthy man , such also the earthy ones. And such the heavenly Man , such also the heavenly ones.
071549 And according as we bore the image of the earthy man , we shall also bear the image of the heavenly Man .
071550 And I say this, brothers, that flesh and blood cannot inherit the kingdom of God, nor does corruption inherit incorruption.
071551 Behold, I speak a mystery to you; we shall not all fall asleep, but we shall all be changed;
071552 in a moment, in a glance of an eye, at the last trumpet. For a trumpet shall sound, and the dead shall be raised incorruptible, and we shall all be changed.
071553 For this corruptible must put on incorruption, and this mortal must put on immortality.
071554 But when this corruptible shall put on incorruption, and when this mortal shall put on immortality, then will take place the word that is written, "Death is swallowed up in victory.
071555 O death, where is your sting? O grave, where is your victory?"
071556 The sting of death is sin, and the strength of sin is the law.
071557 But thanks be to God who gives us the victory through our Lord Jesus Christ.
071558 So that, my beloved brothers, be steadfast, immovable, always abounding in the work of the Lord, knowing that your labor is not without fruit in the Lord.
071601 And concerning the collection for the saints, as I charged the churches of Galatia, so also you do.
071602 On the first of the sabbaths let each of you put by himself, storing up what ever he is prospered, so that there may be no collections when I come.
071603 And when I come, whomever you shall approve by your letters, I will send them to bring your gift to Jerusalem.
071604 And if it is suitable for me to go also, they shall go with me.
071605 But I will come to you when I pass through Macedonia; for I am going through Macedonia.
071606 And it may be that I will stay with you, and even spend the winter with you, so that you may set me forward wherever I go.
071607 For I do not desire to see you now in passage, but I am hoping to stay some time with you, if the Lord permits.
071608 But I will stay in Ephesus until Pentecost.
071609 For a great and effective door opened to me, and many are opposing.
071610 But if Timothy comes, see that he is with you without fear, for he works the work of the Lord, even as I do .
071611 Therefore let not any despise him, but set him forward in peace, so that he may come to me; for I am waiting for him with the brothers.
071612 As regards our brother Apollos, I greatly desired him to come to you with the brothers, but it was not altogether his will that he come now. But he will come when he has opportunity.
071613 Watch! Stand fast in the faith! Be men! Be strong!
071614 Let all your things be done in charity.
071615 But I exhort you, brothers. You know the house of Stephanas, that it is the firstfruit of Achaia, and they appointed themselves to ministry to the saints.
071616 See that you also submit to such ones, and to everyone working and laboring with me .
071617 I am glad at the coming of Stephanas and Fortunatus and Achaicus; for these supplied your lack.
071618 For they have refreshed my spirit and yours; then acknowledge such ones.
071619 The churches of Asia greet you. Aquila and Priscilla greet you much in the Lord, with the church that is in their house.
071620 All the brothers greet you. Greet one another with a holy kiss.
071621 The salutation of Paul with my own hand.
071622 If anyone does not love the Lord Jesus Christ, let him be accursed. The Lord comes!
071623 May the grace of the Lord Jesus Christ be with you.
071624 Let my love be with you all in Christ Jesus. Amen.
080101 Paul, an apostle of Jesus Christ by the will of God, and Timothy our brother, to the church of God which is at Corinth, with all the saints who are in all Achaia.
080102 Grace be unto you, and peace from God our Father and from the Lord Jesus Christ.
080103 Blessed be God, even the Father of our Lord Jesus Christ, the Father of mercies and the God of all comfort,
080104 He comforting us in all our trouble, so that we may be able to comfort those who are in every trouble, through the comfort with which we ourselves are comforted by God.
080105 For as the sufferings of Christ abound in us, so our consolation also abounds by Christ.
080106 And if we are troubled, it is for your consolation and salvation, being worked out in the endurance of the same sufferings which we also suffer; if we are comforted, it is for your consolation and salvation.
080107 And our hope of you is certain, knowing that as you are partakers of the sufferings, so also of the consolation.
080108 For, brothers, we would not have you ignorant of our trouble which came to us in Asia, that we were pressed out of measure, above strength; so much so that we despaired even of life.
080109 But we had the sentence of death in ourselves, so that we should not trust in ourselves, but in God who raises the dead;
080110 who delivered us from so great a death, and does deliver; in whom we trust that He will yet deliver us ,
080111 with you also helping together by prayer for us, so that the gracious gift by many persons be the cause of thanksgiving through many for us.
080112 For our rejoicing is this, the testimony of our conscience, that in simplicity and godly sincerity; not with fleshly wisdom, but by the grace of God; we have had our conduct in the world, and more abundantly toward you.
080113 For we write no other things to you than what you read or recognize, and I trust you shall recognize them even to the end,
080114 even as you have recognized us in part, that we are your rejoicing, even as you also are ours in the day of the Lord Jesus.
080115 And in this confidence I intended to come to you before, so that you might have a second benefit,
080116 and to pass by you into Macedonia, and to come again out of Macedonia to you, and to be brought on my way toward Judea by you.
080117 Then purposing this, did I indeed use lightness? Or the things that I purpose, do I purpose them according to the flesh, so that with me there should be yes, yes, and no, no?
080118 But as God is true, our word toward you was not yes and no.
080119 For the Son of God, Jesus Christ, who was preached among you by us; by me and Silas and Timothy; was not yes and no, but in Him was, yes!
080120 For all the promises of God in Him are yes, and in Him Amen, to the glory of God by us.
080121 But He confirming us and anointing us with you in Christ is God.
080122 And He has sealed us and having given the earnest of the Spirit in our hearts.
080123 And I call God as witness to my soul that in order to spare you I have not yet come to Corinth.
080124 Not that we have dominion over your faith, but we are helpers of your joy; for by faith you stand.
080201 But I determined this within myself, that I would not come to you again in grief.
080202 For if I make you sorry, who then is he who makes me glad, but the same who has been made sorry by me?
080203 And I wrote this to you, lest when I came I should have sorrow from the ones of whom I ought to rejoice; having confidence in you all, that my joy is the joy of you all.
080204 For out of much trouble and anguish of heart I wrote to you with many tears, not that you should be grieved, but that you might know the love which I have more abundantly to you.
080205 But if anyone has caused grief, he has not grieved me, except in part; so that I not overbear all of you.
080206 This punishment by the majority is enough for such a one;
080207 so that, on the contrary, you should rather forgive and comfort him , lest perhaps such a one should be swallowed up with overwhelming sorrow.
080208 So I beseech you to confirm your love toward him.
080209 For to this end I also wrote, that I might know the proof of you, whether you are obedient in all things.
080210 But to whom you forgive anything, I also forgive . For if I forgave anything, for your sakes I forgave it to him in the person of Christ;
080211 so that we should not be overreached by Satan, for we are not ignorant of his devices.
080212 And, when I came to Troas to preach Christ's gospel, and a door was opened to me by the Lord,
080213 I had no rest in my spirit because I did not find Titus my brother. But taking my leave of them, I went from there into Macedonia.
080214 Now thanks be to God, who always causes us to triumph in Christ, and He revealing through us the odor of the knowledge of Him in every place.
080215 For we are to God a sweet savor of Christ, in those being saved, and in those being lost;
080216 to the one we are the savor of death to death, and to the other we are the savor of life to life. And who is sufficient for these things?
080217 For we are not as many, hawking the Word of God; but as of sincerity, but as of God, we speak in Christ in the sight of God.
080301 Do we begin again to commend ourselves? Or do we need, like some, epistles of commendation to you, or letters of commendation from you?
080302 You are our epistle written in our hearts, known and read by all men,
080303 it having been made plain that you are the epistle of Christ, ministered by us, not having been written with ink, but with the Spirit of the living God; not on tablets of stone, but in fleshly tablets of the heart.
080304 And we have such trust through Christ toward God,
080305 not that we are sufficient of ourselves to think anything as of ourselves, but our sufficiency is of God;
080306 who also has made us able ministers of the new covenant; not of the letter, but of the spirit; for the letter kills, but the Spirit makes alive.
080307 But if the ministry of death, having been engraved in letters in stone was with glory (so that the sons of Israel could not steadfastly behold the face of Moses because of the glory of his face), which was being done away;
080308 shall not the ministry of the Spirit be with more glory?
080309 For if the ministry of condemnation is glorious, much more does the ministry of righteousness exceed in glory.
080310 For even that which was made glorious had no glory in this respect, because of the glory that excels.
080311 For if that which has been done away was glorious, much more that which remains is glorious.
080312 Then since we have such hope, we use great plainness of speech.
080313 And we are not like Moses, who put a veil over his face so that the sons of Israel could not steadfastly look to the end of the thing being done away.
080314 (But their thoughts were blinded; for until the present the same veil remains on the reading of the old covenant, not taken away.) But this veil has been done away in Christ.
080315 But until this day, when Moses is read, the veil is on their heart.
080316 But whenever it turns to the Lord, the veil shall be taken away.
080317 And the Lord is that Spirit; and where the Spirit of the Lord is , there is liberty.
080318 But we all, with our face having been unveiled, having beheld the glory of the Lord as in a mirror, are being changed into the same image from glory to glory, even as by the Lord Spirit.
080401 Therefore since we have this ministry, as we have received mercy, we do not faint.
080402 But we have renounced the hidden things of shame, not walking in craftiness, nor adulterating the Word of God, but by the revelation of the truth commending ourselves to every man's conscience in the sight of God.
080403 But also if our gospel is hidden, it is hidden to those being lost,
080404 in whom the god of this world has blinded the minds of the unbelieving ones, so that the light of the glorious gospel of Christ (who is the image of God) should not dawn on them.
080405 For we do not preach ourselves, but Christ Jesus as Lord, and ourselves your servants for Jesus' sake.
080406 For it is God who said, "Out of darkness Light shall shine;" who shone in our hearts to give the brightness of the knowledge of the glory of God in the face of Jesus Christ.
080407 But we have this treasure in earthen vessels, so that the excellence of the power may be of God and not of us;
080408 in every way having been troubled, but not having been hemmed in; having been perplexed, but not utterly at a loss;
080409 having been persecuted, but not having been forsaken; having been thrown down, but not having been destroyed;
080410 always bearing about the dying of the Lord Jesus in the body, so that the life of Jesus also might be revealed in our body.
080411 For we who live are always being delivered to death for Jesus' sake, so that the life of Jesus might also be revealed in our body.
080412 So then death works in us, but life in you.
080413 For we, having the same spirit of faith (according as it is written, "I believed, and therefore I have spoken"); we also believed and therefore speak,
080414 knowing that He who raised up the Lord Jesus shall also raise us up by Jesus, and shall present us with you.
080415 For all things are for your sake, so that the superabounding grace might be made to abound through the thanksgiving of the greater number, to the glory of God.
080416 For this cause we do not faint; but though our outward man perishes, yet the inward man is being renewed day by day.
080417 For the lightness of our present affliction works out for us a far more excellent eternal weight of glory,
080418 we not considering the things which are seen, but the things which are not seen; for the things which are seen are not lasting, but the things which are not seen are everlasting.
080501 For we know that if our earthly house of this tabernacle were dissolved, we have a building from God, a house not made with hands, eternal in the heavens.
080502 For indeed in this we groan, earnestly desiring to be clothed with our dwelling-place out of Heaven;
080503 if indeed in being clothed, we shall not be found naked.
080504 For we who are in this tabernacle groan, being burdened; inasmuch as we do not wish to be unclothed, but to be clothed, so that the mortal might be swallowed up by the life.
080505 And He who has worked in us for this same thing is God, who also is giving to us the earnest of the Spirit.
080506 Then being always confident, knowing that while we are at home in the body, we are away from home from the Lord;
080507 for we walk by faith, not by sight;
080508 then we are confident and we are pleased rather to go away from home out of the body, and to come home to the Lord.
080509 Therefore we are also laboring to be well-pleasing to Him, whether at home or away from home.
080510 For we must all appear before the judgment seat of Christ, so that each one may receive the things done through the body, according to that which he has done, whether good or bad.
080511 Therefore, knowing the fear of the Lord, we persuade men. But we are revealed to God, and I trust also that we are revealed in your consciences.
080512 For we do not commend ourselves again to you, but are giving you occasion to glory on our behalf, so that you may have it to answer those boasting in appearance, and not in heart.
080513 For if we are out of our mind, it is to God; or if we are in our senses, it is for you.
080514 For the love of Christ constrains us, judging this, that if one died for all, then all died;
080515 and He died for all, that the living ones may live no more to themselves, but to Him who died for them and having been raised.
080516 So as we now know no one according to flesh, but even if we have known Christ according to flesh, yet now we no longer know Him so.
080517 So that if any one is in Christ, that one is a new creature; old things have passed away; behold, all things have become new.
080518 And all things are of God, who has reconciled us to Himself through Jesus Christ, and has given to us the ministry of reconciliation;
080519 whereas God was in Christ reconciling the world to Himself, not imputing their trespasses to them, and putting the word of reconciliation in us.
080520 Then we are ambassadors on behalf of Christ, as God exhorting through us, we beseech you on behalf of Christ, be reconciled to God.
080521 For He has made Him who knew no sin, to be sin for us, that we might become the righteousness of God in Him.
080601 But working together, we also call on you not to receive the grace of God in vain.
080602 (For He says, "In an acceptable time I heard you, and in a day of salvation, I helped you;" Behold, now is the accepted time. Behold, now is the day of salvation.)
080603 We are in nothing giving cause of stumbling, in no way, so that the ministry may not be blamed,
080604 but in everything commending ourselves as God's servants, in much patience, in troubles, in emergencies, in distresses,
080605 in stripes, in imprisonments, in riots, in labors, in watchings, in fastings;
080606 in pureness, in knowledge, in long-suffering, in kindness, in the Holy Spirit, in love unfeigned,
080607 in the word of truth, in the power of God, through the weapons of righteousness on the right hand and on the left,
080608 through glory and dishonor, through evil report and good report; as deceivers and yet true;
080609 as unknown and yet well known; as dying and, behold, we live; as chastened and not killed;
080610 as sorrowful, yet always rejoicing; as poor, yet making many rich; as having nothing, yet possessing all things.
080611 O Corinthians, our mouth is opened to you, our heart has been enlarged.
080612 You are not restrained in us, but you are restrained in your own affections.
080613 But for the same reward, (I speak as to children), you also be enlarged.
080614 Do not be unequally yoked together with unbelievers; for what fellowship does righteousness have with lawlessness? And what partnership does light have with darkness?
080615 And what agreement does Christ have with Belial? Or what part does a believer have with an unbeliever?
080616 And what agreement does a temple of God have with idols? For you are the temple of the living God, as God has said, "I will dwell in them and walk among them ; and I will be their God, and they shall be My people."
080617 Therefore come out from among them and be separated, says the Lord, and do not touch the unclean thing . And I will receive you
080618 and I will be a Father to you, and you shall be My sons and daughters, says the Lord Almighty.
080701 Then having these promises, dearly beloved, let us cleanse ourselves from all defilements of flesh and spirit, perfecting holiness in the fear of God.
080702 Make room for us. We wronged no one, we corrupted no one, we overreached no one.
080703 I do not speak this to condemn you, for I have said before that you are in our hearts for us to die together, and to live together.
080704 My boldness of speech is great toward you; my glorying on your behalf is much. I have been filled with comfort, I am overflowing with joy on all our trouble.
080705 For, indeed, coming into Macedonia, our flesh had no rest, but being troubled in every way, with fightings on the outside, and fears on the inside.
080706 But He who comforts the lowly comforted us by the coming of Titus.
080707 And not only by his coming, but by the comfort with which he was comforted over you, telling us your longing, your mourning, your zeal for me; so that I rejoiced the more.
080708 For even if I grieved you in the letter, I do not regret; if indeed I did regret; for I see that that letter grieved you for an hour.
080709 Now I rejoice, not that you were grieved, but that you grieved to repentance. For you were grieved according to God, so that you might suffer loss by nothing in us.
080710 For the grief according to God works repentance to salvation, not to be regretted, but the grief of the world works out death.
080711 For behold this same thing (you being grieved according to God); how much it worked out earnestness in you; but also defense; but also indignation; but also fear; but also desire; but also zeal; but also vengeance! In everything you approved yourselves to be clear in the matter.
080712 Then, though I wrote to you, it was not on account of the one who did wrong, nor on account of the one who suffered wrong, but for the sake of revealing our earnestness on your behalf, for you before God.
080713 Therefore we have been comforted in your comfort, and we rather rejoiced more abundantly over the joy of Titus, because his spirit was refreshed by you all.
080714 For if I have boasted anything about you to him, I was not ashamed. But as we spoke all things to you in truth, even so our boasting as to Titus became truth.
080715 And his tender feelings are more abundant toward you, remembering the obedience of you all, as you received him with fear and trembling.
080716 Therefore I rejoice that I have confidence in you in everything.
080801 And, brothers, we make known to you the grace of God which has been given among the churches of Macedonia;
080802 that in much testing of trouble, the overflowing of their joy, and the depth of their poverty, abounded to the riches of their generosity.
080803 For I testify that according to their ability, and beyond their ability; they gave willingly;
080804 with much beseeching, begging us that they might receive of us the grace and the fellowship of the ministry to the saints.
080805 And not as we hoped, but first they gave themselves to the Lord, and to us through the will of God,
080806 for us to call on Titus, that even as he began before, so he would also complete this grace to you also.
080807 But even as you abound in everything, in faith, and in word, and in knowledge, and in all earnestness, and in your love to us; you should abound in this grace also.
080808 I do not speak according to command, but through the eagerness of others, and testing the trueness of your love.
080809 For you know the grace of our Lord Jesus Christ, that, though He was rich, for your sakes He became poor, in order that you might be made rich through His poverty.
080810 And in this I give my judgment; for this is profitable for you, who began before, not only to do, but also to be willing a year ago.
080811 But now also finish the doing of it , so that, as there was a readiness to will, so also the finishing, giving out of what you have.
080812 For if the eagerness is present, it is acceptable according to what one has, and not according to what one does not have.
080813 For it is not that others may have ease, but you trouble;
080814 but by equality in the present time; your abundance for their need, that their abundance also may be for your need; so that there may be equality;
080815 as it is written, "He gathering much, he had nothing left over; and he gathering little did not have less."
080816 But thanks be to God, who put the same earnest care into the heart of Titus for you.
080817 For indeed he accepted the entreaty. But being more earnest, of his own accord he went to you.
080818 And we have sent with him the brothers whose praise is in the gospel throughout all the churches;
080819 and not only so , but also he having been chosen by the churches to travel with us with this gift, which is administered by us to the glory of the Lord Himself, and as a witness of your eager mind;
080820 avoiding this, that no man should blame us in this abundance which is administered by us;
080821 providing for honest things, not only before the Lord, but also before men.
080822 And we have sent with them our brother whom we have often proved earnest in many things, but now much more earnest by the great confidence which I have in you.
080823 If anyone inquires of Titus, he is my partner and fellow-worker for you, or of our brothers, they are the messengers of the churches, the glory of Christ.
080824 Therefore show them a proof of your love and of our boasting toward you in the presence of the churches.
080901 For indeed regarding the ministry to the saints, it is not necessary for me to write to you.
080902 For I know your eagerness, of which I boast to Macedonia on your behalf, that Achaia was ready a year ago; and your zeal has aroused the greater number.
080903 Yet I sent the brothers, lest our boasting (which is on your behalf) should not be in vain, that, as I said, you may be ready.
080904 I say this lest perhaps Macedonians should come with me and find you unprepared. We (not to say you) would then be put to shame in this confident boasting.
080905 Therefore I thought it necessary to exhort the brothers that they would go forward to you, and make up beforehand your blessing, it having been promised that this would be ready, thus as a matter of blessing, and not as of covetousness.
080906 But I say this, He who sows sparingly shall also reap sparingly, and he who sows bountifully shall also reap bountifully.
080907 Each one, as he purposes in his heart, let him give ; not of grief, or of necessity, for God loves a cheerful giver.
080908 And God is able to make all grace abound toward you, that in everything, always having all self-sufficiency, you may abound to every good work;
080909 As it is written, "He scattered; he has given to the poor; his righteousness remains forever."
080910 Now He who supplies seed to the sower, and bread for eating, may He supply and multiply your seed, and increase the fruits of your righteousness
080911 you being enriched in everything to all generosity, which works out thanksgiving to God through us.
080912 For the ministry of this service not only supplies the things lacking of the saints, but also multiplying through many thanksgivings to God,
080913 through the proof of this ministry they glorify God for your freely expressed submission to the gospel of Christ, and the generosity of the fellowship toward them and toward all,
080914 and in their prayer for you, who long after you, because of the exceeding grace of God on you.
080915 Thanks be to God for His unspeakable free gift.
081001 And I myself, Paul, beseech you by the meekness and gentleness of Christ; I, who indeed to look upon am lowly among you, but being absent am bold toward you.
081002 But I ask, not being present, that I may be bold with the confidence which I think to be daring against some, who thought of us as walking according to flesh.
081003 For though walking about in flesh, we do not war according to flesh.
081004 For the weapons of our warfare are not fleshly, but mighty through God to the pulling down of strongholds,
081005 pulling down imaginations and every high thing that exalts itself against the knowledge of God, and bringing into captivity every thought into the obedience of Christ;
081006 and having readiness to avenge all disobedience, when your obedience is fulfilled.
081007 Do you look at things according to appearance? If anyone has persuaded himself that he is Christ's, let him think this again as to himself, that as he is Christ's, even so we are Christ's.
081008 For even if I also should boast somewhat more fully of our authority (which the Lord has given us for building up, and not for pulling you down) I will not be put to shame;
081009 so that I might not seem to terrify you by letters.
081010 For indeed they say, the letters are weighty and powerful, but the bodily presence is weak, and his speech is contemptible.
081011 Let such a one think this, that, such as we are in word by letters, being absent, such we will be also in deed when we are present.
081012 For we do not dare to rank or compare ourselves with some of the ones commending themselves. But they, measuring themselves among themselves, and comparing themselves to themselves, are not perceptive.
081013 But we will not boast beyond measure, but according to the measure of the rule which the God of measure distributed to us, to reach even to you.
081014 For we do not overstretch ourselves as though not reaching to you. For we also came to you in the gospel of Christ;
081015 not boasting beyond measure in the labors of others, but having hope that the growing faith among you will be increased according to our rule, to overflowing;
081016 to preach the gospel in that beyond you, and not to boast in another's rule in things made ready.
081017 But he who glories, let him glory in the Lord.
081018 For not he who commends himself is approved, but he whom the Lord commends.
081101 I would that you were bearing with me a little in foolishness; but indeed bear with me.
081102 For I am jealous over you with godly jealousy. For I have espoused you to one Man, to present you as a pure virgin to Christ.
081103 But I fear lest by any means, as the serpent beguiled Eve in his craftiness, so your thoughts should be corrupted from the simplicity due to Christ.
081104 For if, indeed, the one coming proclaims another Jesus, whom we have not proclaimed, or if you receive another spirit, which you did not receive, or another gospel, which you never accepted, you might well endure these .
081105 For I judge myself to have come behind the highest apostles in nothing.
081106 But even if I am unskilled in speech, yet not in knowledge; but in every way I have been clearly revealed to you in all things.
081107 Or did I commit sin in humbling myself that you might be exalted, because I preached the gospel of God to you without charge?
081108 I stripped other churches, taking wages for the serving of you.
081109 And being present with you, and in need, I was not a burden to anyone. For the brothers from Macedonia made up completely my need. And in every way I have kept myself from being burdensome to you , and I will keep myself.
081110 The truth of Christ is in me that this boasting shall not be silenced in me in the regions of Achaia.
081111 Why? Because I do not love you? God knows.
081112 But what I do, that I will do, so that I may cut off occasion from those who desire occasion; so that in the thing in which they boast, they may be found even as we.
081113 For such ones are false apostles, deceitful workers, transforming themselves into the apostles of Christ.
081114 Did not even Satan marvelously transform himself into an angel of light?
081115 Therefore it is no great thing if his ministers also transform themselves as ministers of righteousness, whose end shall be according to their works.
081116 Again I say, Let no one think me foolish. If otherwise, yet receive me as foolish, so that I may also boast a little.
081117 What I speak, I do not speak according to the Lord, but as in foolishness, in this boldness of boasting.
081118 Since many glory according to the flesh, I also will boast.
081119 For you gladly bear with fools, being wise.
081120 For you endure if anyone enslaves you, if anyone devours, if anyone takes from you , if anyone exalts himself, if anyone strikes you in the face.
081121 I speak according to dishonor, as though we have been weak. But in whatever anyone dares (I speak foolishly), I also dare.
081122 Are they Hebrews? I also! Are they Israelites? I also! Are they the seed of Abraham? I also!
081123 Are they ministers of Christ? (I speak as beside myself,) I am more! I have been in labors more abundantly, in stripes above measure, in prisons more, in deaths many times.
081124 Five times from the Jews I received forty stripes minus one.
081125 Three times I was beaten with rods, once I was stoned, three times I was shipwrecked. I have spent a night and a day in the deep.
081126 I have been in travels often; in dangers from waters; in dangers from robbers; in dangers from my race; in dangers from the heathen; in dangers in the city; in dangers in the wilderness; in dangers on the sea; in dangers among false brothers.
081127 I have been in hardship and toil; often in watchings; in hunger and thirst; often in fastings; in cold and nakedness;
081128 besides the things outside conspiring against me daily, the care of all the churches.
081129 Who is weak, and I am not weak? Who is caused to stumble, and I do not burn?
081130 If it is right to boast, I will boast of the things of my weakness.
081131 The God and Father of our Lord Jesus Christ, who is blessed forever, knows that I do not lie.
081132 In Damascus the governor under Aretas the king guarded the city of the Damascenes, desiring to lay hold of me.
081133 And I was let down in a basket through a window through the wall, and escaped their hands.
081201 Indeed, it is not profitable for me to boast. For I will come to visions and revelations of the Lord.
081202 I know a man in Christ fourteen years before (whether in the body, I do not know; or outside of the body, I do not know; God knows) such a one was caught up to the third Heaven.
081203 And I know such a man (whether in the body, or outside of the body, I do not know; God knows),
081204 that he was caught up into Paradise and heard unspeakable words, which it is not allowed for a man to utter.
081205 I will glory of such a one, yet I will not boast on my behalf, except in my weaknesses.
081206 For if I desire to boast, I shall not be foolish. For I will speak the truth. But I spare, lest anyone should think of me as being beyond what he sees me, or hears of me;
081207 and by the surpassing revelations, lest I be made haughty, a thorn in the flesh was given to me, a messenger of Satan to buffet me, lest I be made haughty.
081208 For this thing I besought the Lord three times, that it might depart from me.
081209 And He said to me, My grace is sufficient for you, for My power is made perfect in weakness. Most gladly therefore I will rather glory in my weaknesses, that the power of Christ may overshadow me.
081210 Therefore I am pleased in weaknesses, in insults, in necessities, in persecutions, in distresses for Christ's sake; for when I am weak, then I am powerful.
081211 I have become foolish boasting. You compelled me. For I ought to be commended by you. For I lacked nothing of the highest apostles, if even I am nothing.
081212 Truly the signs of the apostle were worked out among you in all patience, in miracles and in wonders, and by works of power.
081213 For what is it in which you were inferior to the rest of the churches, except that I myself did not burden you? Forgive me this wrong.
081214 Behold, a third time I am ready to come to you. And I will not burden you, for I do not seek your things, but you. For the children ought not to lay up treasure for the parents, but the parents for the children.
081215 And I will very gladly spend and be spent for your souls, even if loving you more and more, I am loved the less.
081216 But let it be so, I did not burden you. But being crafty, I caught you with bait.
081217 By any whom I have sent to you, did I overreach you by him?
081218 I begged Titus and sent with him the brother. Did Titus overreach you? Did we not walk in the same spirit? Did we not walk in the same steps?
081219 Again, do you think we are defending ourselves to you? We speak before God in Christ, but we do all things, dearly beloved, for your building up.
081220 For I fear, lest somehow coming I might not find you as I wish, and that I shall be found by you such as you might not wish; lest somehow there be strifes, envyings, angers, contentions, backbitings, whisperings, proud thoughts, tumults;
081221 lest in my coming again my God will humble me with you; and I shall mourn many who have already sinned, and not repenting over the uncleanness, and fornication, and lustfulness which they have practiced.
081301 I am coming to you this third time . In the mouth of two or three witnesses every word shall be established.
081302 I told you before, and I say beforehand, as being present the second time and being absent now. I write to those who sinned before, and to all the rest, that if I come again, I will not spare.
081303 Since you seek a proof of Christ speaking in me (who is not weak toward you, but is powerful in you;
081304 for even if He was crucified out of weakness, yet He lives by the power of God. For indeed even we are weak in Him, but we shall live with Him by the power of God toward you),
081305 examine yourselves, whether you are in the faith, prove your own selves. Do you not know your own selves, that Jesus Christ is in you, unless you are reprobates?
081306 But I trust that you will know that we are not reprobates.
081307 But I pray to God for you not to do evil, none. And not that we may appear approved, but that you should do the good things, though we are deemed to be reprobates.
081308 For we have no power against the truth, but for the truth.
081309 For we are glad when we are weak, and you are powerful. But we pray also for this, your perfection.
081310 Therefore I write these things while absent, lest being present I may not deal sharply with you according to the authority which the Lord gave me for building up, and not for pulling down.
081311 Finally, brothers, rejoice. Perfect yourselves; encourage yourselves; mind the same thing; be at peace. And the God of love and peace will be with you.
081312 Greet one another with a holy kiss.
081313 All the saints greet you.
081314 May the grace of the Lord Jesus Christ, and the love of God, and the fellowship of the Holy Spirit be with you all. Amen.
