090101 Paul, an apostle (not from men, nor through man, but through Jesus Christ and God the Father, who raised Him from the dead),
090102 and all the brothers with me, to the churches of Galatia.
090103 Grace be to you, and peace from God the Father and from our Lord Jesus Christ,
090104 who gave Himself for our sins, that He might deliver us from this present evil world according to the will of God and our Father,
090105 to whom be glory forever and ever. Amen.
090106 I marvel that you so soon are being moved away from Him who called you into the grace of Christ, to another gospel,
090107 which is not another, but some are troubling you, and desiring to pervert the gospel of Christ.
090108 But even if we or an angel from Heaven preach a gospel to you beside what we preached to you, let him be accursed.
090109 As we said before, and now I say again, If anyone preaches a gospel to you beside what you have received, let him be accursed.
090110 For now do I persuade men, or God? Or do I seek to please men? For if I yet pleased men, I would not be a servant of Christ.
090111 And, brothers, I make known to you the gospel which was preached by me, that it is not according to man.
090112 For I did not receive it from man, nor was I taught it except by a revelation of Jesus Christ.
090113 For you heard my manner of life when I was in Judaism, that I persecuted the church of God with surpassing zeal , and ravaged it.
090114 And I progressed in Judaism beyond many contemporaries in my race, being much more a zealot of the traditions of my fathers.
090115 But when it pleased God, who separated me from my mother's womb, and having called me by His grace,
090116 to reveal His Son in me so that I might preach Him among the nations, immediately I did not confer with flesh and blood;
090117 Nor did I go up to Jerusalem to those apostles before me, but I went into Arabia and returned again to Damascus.
090118 Then after three years I went up to Jerusalem to see Peter, and stayed with him fifteen days.
090119 But I saw no other of the apostles, except James the Lord's brother.
090120 And what I write to you, behold, before God, I do not lie.
090121 Then I went into the regions of Syria and of Cilicia,
090122 and was unknown by face to the churches of Judea in Christ.
090123 But only they were hearing that he who then persecuted us, now preaches the faith which he once ravaged.
090124 And they glorified God in me.
090201 Then through fourteen years, I went up again to Jerusalem with Barnabas, and took Titus with me also.
090202 And I went up by revelation. And I put before them the gospel which I proclaim in the nations, but privately to those seeming to be pillars, lest I run, or I ran, into vanity.
090203 (But not even Titus, the one with me, a Greek, was compelled to be circumcised.)
090204 But because of those false brothers stealing in, who stole in to spy out our liberty which we have in Christ Jesus; they desiring to enslave us;
090205 to whom not even for an hour did we yield in subjection, that the truth of the gospel might continue with you.
090206 But from those who seemed to be something (what kind they were then does not matter to me; God does not accept the face of man), for those seeming important conferred nothing to me.
090207 But on the contrary, seeing that I have been entrusted with the gospel of the uncircumcision, as Peter to the circumcision;
090208 for He working in Peter to the apostleship of the circumcision also worked in me to the nations.
090209 and knowing the grace given to me, James, and Cephas, and John, who seemed to be pillars, gave right hands of fellowship to Barnabas and me, that we go to the nations, but they to the circumcision.
090210 Only they asked that we remember the poor, which very thing I was eager to do.
090211 But when Peter came to Antioch, I opposed him to his face, because he was to be blamed.
090212 For before some came from James, he ate with the nations. But when they came, he withdrew and separated himself, fearing those of the circumcision.
090213 And the rest of the Jews also dissembled with him, so as even Barnabas was led away with their dissembling.
090214 But when I saw that they did not walk uprightly with the truth of the gospel, I said to Peter before all, If you, being a Jew, live as a Gentile, and not as the Jews, why do you compel the nations to judaize?
090215 We Jews by nature, and not sinners of the nations,
090216 knowing that a man is not justified by works of the Law, but through faith in Jesus Christ; even we believed in Jesus Christ, that we might be justified by the faith in Christ, and not by works of the Law. For all flesh will not be justified by works of law.
090217 But if, while we seek to be justified in Christ, we also were found to be sinners, is Christ therefore a minister of sin? Let it not be said !
090218 For if I build again the things which I destroyed, I confirm myself as a transgressor.
090219 For through the Law I died to the law, that I might live to God.
090220 I have been crucified with Christ, and I live; yet no longer I, but Christ lives in me. And that life I now live in the flesh, I live by faith toward the Son of God, who loved me and gave Himself on my behalf.
090221 I do not set aside the grace of God, for if righteousness is through law, then Christ died without cause.
090301 O foolish Galatians, who bewitched you not to obey the truth, to whom before your eyes Jesus Christ was written among you crucified?
090302 This only I would learn from you: Did you receive the Spirit by works of the law, or by hearing of faith?
090303 Are you so foolish? Having begun in the Spirit, do you now perfect yourself in the flesh?
090304 Did you suffer so many things in vain, if indeed it is even in vain?
090305 Then He supplying the Spirit to you and working powerful works in you, is it by works of the law, or by hearing of faith?
090306 Even as Abraham believed God, and it was counted to him for righteousness.
090307 Therefore know that those of faith, these are the sons of Abraham.
090308 And the Scripture, foreseeing that God would justify the nations through faith, preached the gospel before to Abraham, saying , "In you shall all nations be blessed."
090309 So then those of faith are blessed with faithful Abraham.
090310 For as many as are out of works of the Law, these are under a curse; for it is written, "Cursed is everyone who does not continue in all things which are written in the Book of the Law, to do them."
090311 But that no one is justified by the Law in the sight of God is clear, for, "The just shall live by faith."
090312 But the Law is not of faith; but, "The man who does these things shall live in them."
090313 Christ redeemed us from the curse of the Law, being made a curse for us (for it is written, "Cursed is everyone having been hanged on a tree");
090314 so that the blessing of Abraham might be to the nations in Jesus Christ, and that we might receive the promise of the Spirit through faith.
090315 Brothers, I speak according to man, a covenant having been ratified, even among mankind, no one sets aside or adds to it .
090316 And to Abraham and to his Seed the promises were spoken. It does not say, And to seeds, as of many; but as of one, "And to your Seed," which is Christ.
090317 And I say this, A covenant having been ratified by God in Christ, the Law (coming into being four hundred and thirty years after) does not annul the promise, so as to abolish it.
090318 For if the inheritance is of Law, it is no more of promise; but God gave it to Abraham by way of promise.
090319 Why then the Law? It was added because of transgressions, until the Seed should come to those to whom it had been promised, being ordained through angels in the Mediator's hand.
090320 But the Mediator is not a mediator of one, but God is one.
090321 Is the Law then against the promises of God? Let it not be said ! For if a law had been given which could have given life, indeed righteousness would have been out of Law.
090322 But the Scripture shut up all under sin, so that the promise by faith of Jesus Christ might be given to those who believe.
090323 But before faith came, we were kept under Law, having been shut up to the faith about to be revealed.
090324 So that the Law has become a trainer of us until Christ, that we might be justified by faith.
090325 But faith coming, we are no longer under a trainer.
090326 For you are all sons of God through faith in Christ Jesus.
090327 For as many as were baptized into Christ, you put on Christ.
090328 There cannot be Jew nor Greek, there is neither bond nor free, there is no male nor female; for you are all one in Christ Jesus.
090329 And if you are Christ's, then you are Abraham's seed and heirs according to the promise.
090401 But I say, Over so long a time the heir is an infant, he does not differ from a slave, though being lord of all;
090402 but he is under guardians and housemasters until the term appointed before by the father.
090403 Even so we, when we were infants, were in bondage under the elements of the world.
090404 But when the fullness of the time came, God sent forth His Son, coming into being out of a woman, having come under Law,
090405 that He might redeem those under Law, so that we might receive the adoption of sons.
090406 And because you are sons, God has sent forth the Spirit of His Son into your hearts, crying, Abba, Father.
090407 So that you are no longer a slave, but a son; and if a son, also an heir of God through Christ.
090408 But then, indeed, not knowing God, you served as slaves to those not by nature being gods.
090409 But now, knowing God, but rather are known by God, how do you turn again to the weak and beggarly elements to which you again desire to slave anew?
090410 You observe days and months and times and years.
090411 I fear for you, lest somehow I have labored among you in vain.
090412 Brothers, I beseech you, be as I am ; for I am as you. You have not injured me at all.
090413 But you know that through infirmity of the flesh I preached the gospel to you before,
090414 and you did not despise my temptation in my flesh, nor did you spurn it . But you received me as an angel of God, as Christ Jesus.
090415 What then was your blessedness? For I bear you record that, if you were able, plucking out your eyes, you would have given them to me.
090416 So then did I become your enemy speaking to you the truth?
090417 They are zealous for you, but not well. But they only desire to shut you out, that you be zealous to them.
090418 But it is good to be zealous always in a good thing , and not only in my being present with you.
090419 My children, for whom I again travail until Christ should be formed in you,
090420 even now I desired to be present with you, and to change my voice; for I am in doubt as to you.
090421 Tell me, those desiring to be under Law, do you not hear the Law?
090422 For it is written: Abraham had two sons, the one out of the slave-woman, and one out of the free woman.
090423 But, indeed, he out of the slave-woman has been born according to flesh, and he out of the free woman through the promise;
090424 which things are being allegorized; for these are the two covenants, one indeed from Mount Sinai bringing forth to slavery, which is Hagar.
090425 For Hagar is Mount Sinai in Arabia, and answers to Jerusalem which now is, and is in slavery with her children.
090426 But the Jerusalem from above is free, who is the mother of us all.
090427 For it is written, "Rejoice, barren one not bearing; break forth and shout, you not travailing; for more are the children of the desolate than she having the husband."
090428 But brothers, we, like Isaac, are children of promise.
090429 But then even as he born according to flesh persecuted him born according to the Spirit, so it is also now.
090430 But what does the Scripture say? "Cast out the slave-woman and her son; for in no way shall the son of the slave-woman inherit with the son of the free woman."
090431 Then, brothers, we are not children of a slave-woman, but of the free woman.
090501 Stand fast therefore in the liberty with which Christ has made us free, and do not again be held with the yoke of bondage.
090502 Behold, I, Paul, say to you that if you are circumcised, Christ shall profit you nothing.
090503 For I testify again to every man that is circumcised, that he is a debtor to do all the Law,
090504 you who are justified by Law are deprived of all effect from Christ; you fell from grace.
090505 For we through the Spirit wait for the hope of righteousness out of faith.
090506 For in Christ Jesus neither circumcision nor uncircumcision has any strength, but faith working through love.
090507 You were running well. Who hindered you that you do not obey the truth?
090508 This persuasion is not from Him who calls you.
090509 A little leaven leavens all the lump.
090510 I have confidence in you in the Lord, that you will think nothing else, but that he troubling you shall bear the judgment, whoever he may be.
090511 And I, brothers, if I yet proclaim circumcision, why am I still persecuted? Then the offense of the Cross has ceased.
090512 I wish that those causing you to doubt will cut themselves off.
090513 For, brothers, you were called to liberty. Only do not use the liberty for an opening to the flesh, but by love serve one another.
090514 For all the Law is fulfilled in one word, even in this, "You shall love your neighbor as yourself."
090515 But if you bite and devour one another, take heed that you are not consumed by one another.
090516 I say, then, Walk in the Spirit and you shall not fulfill the lusts of the flesh.
090517 For the flesh lusts against the Spirit, and the Spirit against the flesh. And these are contrary to one another; lest whatever you may will, these things you do.
090518 But if you are led by the Spirit, you are not under law.
090519 Now the works of the flesh are clearly revealed, which are: adultery, fornication, uncleanness, lustfulness,
090520 idolatry, sorcery, hatreds, fightings, jealousies, angers, rivalries, divisions, heresies,
090521 envyings, murders, drunkennesses, revelings, and things like these; of which I tell you before, as I also said before, that they who do such things shall not inherit the kingdom of God.
090522 But the fruit of the Spirit is: love, joy, peace, long-suffering, kindness, goodness, faith,
090523 meekness, self-control; against such things there is no law.
090524 But those belonging to Christ have crucified the flesh with its passions and lusts.
090525 If we live in the Spirit, let us also walk in the Spirit.
090526 Let us not become glory-seeking, provoking one another, envying one another.
090601 Brothers, if a man is overtaken in a fault, you the spiritual ones restore such a one in the spirit of meekness, considering yourself, lest you also be tempted.
090602 Bear one another's burdens, and so you will fulfill the law of Christ.
090603 For if anyone thinks himself to be something, being nothing, he deceives himself.
090604 But let each one prove his own work, and then he alone will have a boast in himself, and not in another.
090605 For each one will bear his own load.
090606 But let him who is taught in the Word share with the one teaching in all good things.
090607 Do not be deceived, God is not mocked. For whatever a man sows, that he also will reap.
090608 For he sowing to his flesh will reap corruption from the flesh. But he sowing to the Spirit will reap life everlasting from the Spirit.
090609 But we should not lose heart in well-doing, for in due season we shall reap, if we do not faint.
090610 So then as we have time, let us work good toward all, especially toward those of the household of faith.
090611 See in what large letters I write to you with my hand.
090612 As many as desire to look well in the flesh, these compel you to be circumcised; only lest they should suffer persecution for the cross of Christ.
090613 For they themselves, having been circumcised, do not even keep the Law, but they desire you to be circumcised so that they may boast in your flesh.
090614 But may it never be for me to boast, except in the cross of our Lord Jesus Christ, by whom the world is crucified to me, and I to the world.
090615 For in Christ Jesus neither circumcision has any strength, nor uncircumcision, but a new creation.
090616 And as many as walk according to this rule, peace and mercy be upon them and upon the Israel of God.
090617 For the rest, let no one give troubles to me, for I bear in my body the brands of the Lord Jesus.
090618 Brothers, the grace of our Lord Jesus Christ be with your spirit. Amen.
100101 Paul, an apostle of Jesus Christ by the will of God, to the saints who are in Ephesus, and faithful in Christ Jesus.
100102 Grace be to you, and peace from God our Father and from the Lord Jesus Christ.
100103 Blessed be the God and Father of our Lord Jesus Christ, who blessed us with every spiritual blessing in the heavenlies in Christ;
100104 according as He chose us in Him before the foundation of the world, that we should be holy and without blame before Him in love,
100105 having predestined us to the adoption of children by Jesus Christ to Himself, according to the good pleasure of His will,
100106 to the praise of the glory of His grace, in which He has made us accepted in the One having been loved.
100107 In Him we have redemption through His blood, the forgiveness of sins, according to the riches of His grace,
100108 which He caused to abound toward us in all wisdom and understanding;
100109 having made known to us the mystery of His will, according to His good pleasure which He purposed in Himself,
100110 for an administration of the fullness of times, to head up all things in Christ, both the things in Heaven, and the things on earth, even in Him,
100111 in whom also we have been chosen to an inheritance, being predestinated according to the purpose of Him who works all things according to the counsel of His own will,
100112 for us to be to the praise of His glory, who previously had trusted in Christ;
100113 in whom also you, hearing the word of truth, the gospel of our salvation, in whom also believing, you were sealed with the Holy Spirit of promise,
100114 who is the earnest of our inheritance, to the redemption of the purchased possession, to the praise of His glory.
100115 Therefore I also, hearing of your faith in the Lord Jesus and love to all the saints,
100116 do not cease giving thanks for you, making mention of you in my prayers,
100117 that the God of our Lord Jesus Christ, the Father of glory, may give to you the spirit of wisdom and revelation in the knowledge of Him,
100118 the eyes of your understanding being enlightened, that you may know what is the hope of His calling, and what is the riches of the glory of His inheritance in the saints,
100119 and what is the surpassing greatness of His power toward us, the ones believing according to the working of His mighty strength
100120 which He worked in Christ in raising Him from the dead, and He seated Him at His right hand in the heavenlies,
100121 far above all principality and authority and power and dominion, and every name being named, not only in this world, but also in the coming age.
100122 And He has put all things under His feet and gave Him to be Head over all things to the church,
100123 which is His body, the fullness of Him who fills all in all.
100201 And He has made you alive , who were once dead in trespasses and sins,
100202 in which you once walked according to the course of this world, according to the prince of the power of the air, the spirit that now works in the children of disobedience;
100203 among whom we also had our way of life in times past, in the lusts of our flesh, fulfilling the desires of the flesh and of the thoughts, and were by nature the children of wrath, even as others.
100204 But God, who is rich in mercy, for His great love with which He loved us
100205 (even when we were dead in sins) has made us alive together with Christ (by grace you are saved),
100206 and has raised us up together and made us sit together in the heavenlies in Christ Jesus,
100207 so that in the ages to come He might show the exceeding riches of His grace in His kindness toward us through Christ Jesus.
100208 For by grace you are saved through faith, and that not of yourselves, it is the gift of God,
100209 not of works, lest anyone should boast.
100210 For we are His workmanship, created in Christ Jesus to good works, which God has before ordained that we should walk in them.
100211 Therefore remember that you, the nations, in time past were in the flesh, who are called Uncircumcision by that which is called the Circumcision in the flesh made by hands;
100212 and that at that time you were without Christ, being aliens from the commonwealth of Israel, and strangers from the covenants of promise, having no hope, and without God in the world.
100213 But now in Christ Jesus you who were once afar off are made near by the blood of Christ.
100214 For He is our peace, He making us both one, and He has broken down the middle wall of partition between us ,
100215 having abolished in His flesh the enmity (the Law of commandments contained in ordinances) so that in Himself He might make the two into one new man, making peace between them ;
100216 and so that He might reconcile both to God in one body by the cross, having slain the enmity in Himself.
100217 And He came and preached peace to you who were afar off, and to those who were near.
100218 For through Him we both have access by one Spirit to the Father.
100219 Now therefore you are no longer strangers and foreigners, but fellow citizens with the saints, and of the household of God,
100220 and are built upon the foundation of the apostles and prophets, Jesus Christ Himself being the chief cornerstone,
100221 in whom every building having been fitly framed together, grows into a holy sanctuary in the Lord;
100222 in whom you also are built together for a dwelling place of God through the Spirit.
100301 For this cause, I, Paul, am the prisoner of Jesus Christ for you nations,
100302 if you have heard of the dispensation of the grace of God which is given to me toward you,
100303 that by revelation He made known to me the mystery (as I wrote before in few words,
100304 by which, when you read, you may understand my knowledge in the mystery of Christ)
100305 which in other ages was not made known to the sons of men, as it is now revealed to His holy apostles and prophets by the Spirit,
100306 that the nations should be fellow heirs, and of the same body, and partaker of His promise in Christ through the gospel.
100307 Of this gospel I was made a minister, according to the gift of the grace of God given to me by the effectual working of His power.
100308 This grace is given to me ( who am less than the least of all saints) to preach the gospel of the unsearchable riches of Christ among the nations,
100309 and to bring to light what is the fellowship of the mystery which from eternity has been hidden in God, who created all things by Jesus Christ;
100310 so that now to the rulers and powers in the heavenlies might be known by the church the manifold wisdom of God,
100311 according to the eternal purpose which He purposed in Christ Jesus our Lord;
100312 in whom we have boldness and access with confidence through His faith.
100313 For this reason I desire that you faint not at my tribulations for you, which is your glory.
100314 For this cause I bow my knees to the Father of our Lord Jesus Christ,
100315 of whom the whole family in Heaven and earth is named,
100316 that He would grant you, according to the riches of His glory, to be strengthened with might by His Spirit in the inner man;
100317 that Christ may dwell in your hearts by faith; that you, being rooted and grounded in love,
100318 may be able to comprehend with all saints what is the breadth and length and depth and height,
100319 and to know the love of Christ which passes knowledge, that you might be filled with all the fullness of God.
100320 Now to Him who is able to do exceeding abundantly above all that we ask or think, according to the power that works in us,
100321 to Him be glory in the church by Christ Jesus throughout all ages, forever. Amen.
100401 I therefore, the prisoner in the Lord, beseech you that you walk worthy of the calling with which you are called,
100402 with all lowliness and meekness, with long-suffering, forbearing one another in love,
100403 endeavoring to keep the unity of the Spirit in the bond of peace.
100404 There is one body and one Spirit, even as you are called in one hope of your calling,
100405 one Lord, one faith, one baptism,
100406 one God and Father of all, who is above all and through all and in you all.
100407 But to every one of us is given grace according to the measure of the gift of Christ.
100408 Therefore He says, "When He ascended up on high, He led captivity captive and gave gifts to men."
100409 (Now that He ascended, what is it but that He also descended first into the lower parts of the earth?
100410 He who descended is the same also as He who ascended up far above all heavens, that He might fill all things.)
100411 And truly He gave some to be apostles, and some to be prophets, and some to be evangelists, and some to be pastors and teachers,
100412 for the perfecting of the saints, for the work of the ministry, for the edifying of the body of Christ.
100413 And this until we all come into the unity of the faith and of the knowledge of the Son of God, to a full-grown man, to the measure of the stature of the fullness of Christ;
100414 so that we no longer may be infants, tossed to and fro and carried about by every wind of doctrine, in the dishonesty of men, in cunning craftiness, to the wiles of deceit.
100415 But that you, speaking the truth in love, may in all things grow up to Him who is the Head, even Christ;
100416 from whom the whole body, fitted together and compacted by that which every joint supplies, according to the effectual working in the measure of each part, producing the growth of the body to the edifying of itself in love.
100417 This I say therefore, and testify in the Lord, that you should not walk from now on as other nations walk, in the vanity of their mind,
100418 having the understanding darkened, being alienated from the life of God through the ignorance that is in them, because of the blindness of their heart.
100419 For they, being past feeling, have given themselves up to lust, to work all uncleanness with greediness.
100420 But you have not so learned Christ,
100421 if indeed you have heard Him and were taught by Him, as the truth is in Jesus.
100422 For you ought to put off the old man (according to your way of living before) who is corrupt according to the deceitful lusts,
100423 and be renewed in the spirit of your mind.
100424 And you should put on the new man, who according to God was created in righteousness and true holiness.
100425 Therefore putting away lying, let each man speak truth with his neighbor, for we are members of one another.
100426 Be angry, and do not sin. Do not let the sun go down upon your wrath,
100427 neither give place to the Devil.
100428 Let him who stole steal no more, but rather let him labor, working with his hands the thing which is good, so that he may have something to give to him who needs.
100429 Let not any filthy word go out of your mouth, but if any is good to building up in respect of need, that it may give grace to the ones hearing.
100430 And do not grieve the Holy Spirit of God, by whom you are sealed until the day of redemption.
100431 Let all bitterness and wrath and anger and tumult and evil speaking be put away from you, with all malice.
100432 And be kind to one another, tenderhearted, forgiving one another, even as God for Christ's sake has forgiven you.
100501 Therefore be followers of God, as dear children.
100502 And walk in love, as Christ also has loved us, and has given Himself for us as an offering and a sacrifice to God for a sweet smelling savor.
100503 For let fornication and all uncleanness or covetousness not be once named among you, as becomes saints,
100504 neither baseness, foolish talking, jesting, which are not becoming, but rather giving of thanks.
100505 For you know this, that no fornicator, or unclean person, or covetous one (who is an idolater), has any inheritance in the kingdom of Christ and of God.
100506 Let no man deceive you with vain words, for because of these things the wrath of God comes upon the children of disobedience.
100507 Therefore do not be partakers with them.
100508 For you were once darkness, but now you are light in the Lord; walk as children of light
100509 (for the fruit of the Spirit is in all goodness and righteousness and truth),
100510 proving what is acceptable to the Lord.
100511 And have no fellowship with the unfruitful works of darkness, but rather reprove them .
100512 For it is a shame even to speak of those things which are done by them in secret.
100513 But all things that are reproved are made manifest by the light, for whatever makes manifest is light.
100514 Therefore he says, "Awake, sleeping ones! And arise from the dead, and Christ shall give you light."
100515 See then that you walk circumspectly, not as fools, but as wise,
100516 redeeming the time, because the days are evil.
100517 Therefore do not be unwise, but understand what the will of the Lord is .
100518 And do not be drunk with wine, in which is excess, but be filled with the Spirit,
100519 speaking to yourselves in psalms and hymns and spiritual songs, singing and making melody in your heart to the Lord;
100520 always giving thanks for all things to God the Father in the name of our Lord Jesus Christ,
100521 submitting yourselves to one another in the fear of God.
100522 Wives, submit yourselves to your own husbands, as to the Lord.
100523 For the husband is the head of the wife, even as Christ is the head of the church; and He is the Savior of the body.
100524 Therefore as the church is subject to Christ, so let the wives be to their own husbands in everything.
100525 Husbands, love your wives, even as Christ also loved the church and gave Himself for it,
100526 that He might sanctify and cleanse it with the washing of water by the Word,
100527 that He might present it to Himself as the glorious church, without spot or wrinkle or any such things, but that it should be holy and without blemish.
100528 So men ought to love their wives as their own bodies. He who loves his wife loves himself.
100529 For no man ever yet hated his own flesh, but nourishes and cherishes it, even as the Lord loves the church.
100530 For we are members of His body, of His flesh, and of His bones.
100531 "For this cause a man shall leave his father and mother and shall be joined to his wife, and the two of them shall be one flesh."
100532 This is a great mystery, but I speak concerning Christ and the church.
100533 But also let everyone of you in particular so love his wife even as himself, and the wife that she defers to her husband.
100601 Children, obey your parents in the Lord, for this is right.
100602 Honor your father and mother (which is the first commandment with a promise),
100603 so that it may be well with you, and that you may live long on the earth.
100604 And fathers, do not provoke your children to wrath, but bring them up in the nurture and admonition of the Lord.
100605 Slaves, obey your masters according to the flesh, with fear and trembling, in singleness of your heart, as to Christ;
100606 not with eye-service, as men-pleasers, but as the servants of Christ, doing the will of God from the heart,
100607 with good will doing service as to the Lord and not to men
100608 (knowing that whatever good thing he does, he shall receive the same from the Lord, whether he is a slave or a freeman).
100609 And masters, do the same things to them, forbearing threatening, knowing that your Master also is in Heaven. There is no respect of persons with Him.
100610 Finally, my brothers, be strong in the Lord and in the power of His might.
100611 Put on the whole armor of God so that you may be able to stand against the wiles of the devil.
100612 For we do not wrestle against flesh and blood, but against principalities, against powers, against the world's rulers, of the darkness of this age, against spiritual wickedness in high places .
100613 Therefore take to yourselves the whole armor of God, that you may be able to withstand in the evil day, and having done all, to stand.
100614 Therefore stand, having your loins girded about with truth, and having on the breastplate of righteousness
100615 and your feet shod with the preparation of the gospel of peace.
100616 Above all, take the shield of faith, with which you shall be able to quench all the fiery darts of the wicked.
100617 And take the helmet of salvation, and the sword of the Spirit, which is the Word of God,
100618 praying always with all prayer and supplication in the Spirit, and watching to this very thing with all perseverance and supplication for all saints.
100619 And pray for me, that utterance may be given to me, that I may open my mouth boldly to make known the mystery of the gospel,
100620 for which I am an ambassador in bonds; so that in it I may speak boldly, as I ought to speak.
100621 But, so that you also may know my affairs and how I do, Tychicus, a beloved brother and faithful minister in the Lord, shall make known to you all things,
100622 whom I have sent to you for the same purpose, that you might know our affairs and that he might comfort your hearts.
100623 Peace to the brothers, and love with faith, from God the Father and the Lord Jesus Christ.
100624 Grace be with all those who love our Lord Jesus Christ in sincerity. Amen.
110101 Paul and Timothy, the servants of Jesus Christ, to all the saints in Christ Jesus who are at Philippi, with the overseers and deacons.
110102 Grace to you, and peace from God our Father and from the Lord Jesus Christ.
110103 I thank my God upon every remembrance of you,
110104 always in every prayer of mine making my request for you all with joy
110105 for your fellowship in the gospel from the first day until now;
110106 being confident of this very thing, that He who has begun a good work in you will perform it until the day of Jesus Christ,
110107 even as it is righteous for me to think this of you all, because you have me in your heart, inasmuch as both in my bonds, and in the defense and confirmation of the gospel, you are all partakers of my grace.
110108 For God is my witness how greatly I long after you all in the bowels of Jesus Christ.
110109 And this I pray, that your love may abound yet more and more in full knowledge and in all perception;
110110 that you may distinguish between things that differ, that you may be sincere and without offense until the day of Jesus Christ,
110111 being filled with the fruits of righteousness through Jesus Christ, to the glory and praise of God.
110112 But I desire that you should understand, brothers, that the things which happened to me have fallen out rather to the furtherance of the gospel;
110113 so that my bonds in Christ are manifest in all the palace, and in all other places .
110114 And most of the brothers in the Lord, becoming confident by my bonds, are much more bold to speak the word without fear.
110115 Some indeed even preach Christ because of envy and strife, and some also of good will.
110116 Those, indeed, preach Christ out of contention, not sincerely, supposing to add affliction to my bonds.
110117 But these others preach in love, knowing that I am set for the defense of the gospel.
110118 What then? Nevertheless, in every way, whether in pretense or in truth, Christ is preached. And I rejoice in this. Yet, also I will rejoice.
110119 For I know that this shall turn to my salvation through your prayer and the supply of the Spirit of Jesus Christ,
110120 according to my earnest expectation and hope that I shall be ashamed in nothing, but as always now Christ shall be magnified in my body with all boldness, whether it is by life or by death.
110121 For to me to live is Christ, and to die is gain.
110122 But if I live in the flesh, this is the fruit of my labor. Yet I do not know what I shall choose.
110123 For I am pressed together by the two: having a desire to depart and to be with Christ, which is far better.
110124 But to remain in the flesh is more needful for you.
110125 And having this confidence, I know that I shall remain and continue with you all, for your advancement and joy of faith,
110126 so that your rejoicing may be more abundant in Jesus Christ for me by my coming to you again.
110127 Only let your conduct be as becomes the gospel of Christ, so that whether I come and see you, or else am absent, I may hear of your affairs , that you stand fast in one spirit, striving together with one mind for the faith of the gospel,
110128 and terrified in nothing by your adversaries. For this is to them an evident token of perdition, but to you of salvation, and that of God.
110129 For to you it is given on behalf of Christ not only to believe on Him, but also to suffer for His sake,
110130 having the same conflict which you saw in me, and now hear to be in me.
110201 If there is therefore any encouragement in Christ, if any comfort of love, if any fellowship of the Spirit, if any tendernesses and mercies,
110202 then fulfill my joy, that you may be like-minded, having the same love, being of one accord and of one mind.
110203 Let nothing be done through strife or vainglory, but in lowliness of mind let each esteem others better than themselves.
110204 Do not let each man look upon his own things, but each man also on the things of others.
110205 For let this mind be in you which was also in Christ Jesus,
110206 who, being in the form of God, thought it not robbery to be equal with God,
110207 but made Himself of no reputation, and took upon Himself the form of a servant, and was made in the likeness of men.
110208 And being found in fashion as a man, He humbled Himself and became obedient unto death, even the death of the cross.
110209 Therefore God has highly exalted Him, and has given Him a name which is above every name,
110210 that at the name of Jesus every knee should bow, of heavenly ones, and of earthly ones, and of ones under the earth;
110211 and that every tongue should confess that Jesus Christ is Lord, to the glory of God the Father.
110212 Therefore, my beloved, as you have always obeyed, not as in my presence only, but now much more in my absence, cultivate your own salvation with fear and trembling.
110213 For it is God who works in you both to will and to do of His good pleasure.
110214 Do all things without murmurings and disputings,
110215 so that you may be blameless and harmless, the sons of God, without rebuke, in the midst of a crooked and perverse nation. Among these you shine as lights in the world,
110216 holding forth the word of life, so that I may rejoice with you in the day of Christ, that I have not run in vain nor labored in vain.
110217 Yea, and if I am offered upon the sacrifice and service of your faith, I joy and rejoice with you all.
110218 And you also rejoice in the same, and rejoice with me.
110219 But I trust in the Lord Jesus to send Timothy shortly to you, so that I also may be of good comfort when I know your state .
110220 For I have no one who is like-minded, who will naturally care for your state .
110221 For all seek their own, not the things which are of Jesus Christ.
110222 But you know the proof of him, that, as a son with the father, he has served with me in the gospel.
110223 Therefore I hope to send him presently, as soon as I shall see the things about me.
110224 But I trust in the Lord that I myself shall also come shortly.
110225 Yet I thought it necessary to send to you Epaphroditus, my brother and fellow-worker, and fellow-soldier, but your messenger and he who ministered to my wants.
110226 For he longed after you all and was full of heaviness, because you had heard that he had been sick.
110227 For indeed he was sick, coming near death, but God had mercy on him, and not on him only, but on me also, lest I should have sorrow upon sorrow.
110228 Therefore I sent him the more eagerly, so that you may rejoice when you see him again, and that I may be the less sorrowful.
110229 Therefore receive him in the Lord with all gladness, and hold such in honor,
110230 because for the work of Christ he was near death, not regarding his life, to supply your lack of service toward me.
110301 Finally, my brothers, rejoice in the Lord. To write the same things to you is indeed not grievous to me, but for you it is safe.
110302 Beware of dogs, beware of evil workers, beware of the concision party.
110303 For we are the circumcision who worship God in the spirit and rejoice in Christ Jesus and have no confidence in the flesh;
110304 though I might also have confidence in the flesh. If any other thinks that he has reason to trust in the flesh, I more.
110305 I was circumcised the eighth day, of the stock of Israel, of the tribe of Benjamin, a Hebrew of the Hebrews. As regards the Law, I was a Pharisee;
110306 concerning zeal, persecuting the church; regarding the righteousness in the Law, blameless.
110307 But whatever things were gain to me, those I counted loss for Christ.
110308 But no, rather, I also count all things to be loss for the excellency of the knowledge of Christ Jesus my Lord, for whose sake I have suffered the loss of all things, and count them to be dung, so that I may win Christ
110309 and be found in Him; not having my own righteousness, which is of the Law, but through the faith of Christ, the righteousness of God by faith,
110310 that I may know Him and the power of His resurrection and the fellowship of His sufferings, being made conformable to His death;
110311 if by any means I might attain to the resurrection of the dead.
110312 Not as though I had already attained, either were already perfect, but I am pressing on, if I may lay hold of that for which I also was taken hold of by Christ Jesus.
110313 My brothers, I do not count myself to have taken possession, but one thing I do , forgetting the things behind and reaching forward to the things before,
110314 I press toward the mark for the prize of the high calling of God in Christ Jesus.
110315 Let us therefore, as many as are perfect, be of this mind. And if in anything you are otherwise minded, God shall reveal even this to you.
110316 Yet, as to what we have already attained, let us walk in the same rule, let us mind the same thing.
110317 Brothers, be imitators together of me, and mark those who walk this way, for you have us for a pattern.
110318 (For many are walking, of whom I have told you often and now tell you even weeping, as the enemies of the cross of Christ;
110319 whose end is destruction, whose god is their belly, and whose glory is in their shame, those who mind earthly things.)
110320 For our citizenship is in Heaven, from which also we are looking for the Savior, the Lord Jesus Christ,
110321 who shall change our body of humiliation so that it may be fashioned like His glorious body, according to the working of His power, even to subdue all things to Himself.
110401 Therefore, my brothers, ones loved and longed for, my joy and crown, stand fast in this way in the Lord, beloved ones.
110402 I beg Euodia and Syntyche that they be of the same mind in the Lord.
110403 And I also beg you, true yoke-fellow, help those women who labored in the gospel with me and with Clement, and others of my fellow-laborers, whose names are in the Book of Life.
110404 Rejoice in the Lord always. Again I say, Rejoice!
110405 Let your moderation be known to all men. The Lord is at hand.
110406 Do not be anxious about anything, but in everything by prayer and supplication, with thanksgiving, let your requests be made known to God.
110407 And the peace of God which passes all understanding shall keep your hearts and minds through Christ Jesus.
110408 Finally, my brothers, whatever things are true, whatever things are honest, whatever things are right, whatever things are pure, whatever things are lovely, whatever things are of good report; if there is any virtue and if there is any praise, think on these things.
110409 Do those things which you have also learned and received and heard and seen in me. And the God of peace shall be with you.
110410 But I rejoiced in the Lord greatly, that now at the last your care of me has flourished again. Although you indeed did think, but you lacked opportunity.
110411 Not that I speak according to need, for I have learned to be content in whatever state I am.
110412 I know both how to be abased, and I know how to abound. In everything and in all things I am instructed both to be full and to be hungry, both to abound and to suffer need.
110413 I can do all things through Christ who strengthens me.
110414 Yet you did well in sharing my troubles.
110415 Now you Philippians know also that in the beginning of the gospel, when I departed from Macedonia, no church communicated with me as regards giving and receiving, except you alone.
110416 For even in Thessalonica you sent once and again to my necessity.
110417 I do not say this because I desire a gift, but I desire fruit that may abound to your account.
110418 But I have all, and abound. I have been filled, having received from Epaphroditus the things which you sent , an odor of a sweet smell, a sacrifice acceptable and well-pleasing to God.
110419 But my God shall supply all your need according to His riches in glory by Christ Jesus.
110420 Now unto God and our Father be glory forever and ever. Amen.
110421 Greet every saint in Christ Jesus. The brothers who are with me greet you.
110422 All the saints greet you, most of all those who are of Caesar's household.
110423 May the grace of our Lord Jesus Christ be with you all. Amen.
120101 Paul, an apostle of Jesus Christ by the will of God, and Timothy our brother,
120102 to the saints and faithful brothers in Christ at Colosse. Grace to you, and peace from God our Father and from the Lord Jesus Christ.
120103 We give thanks to God and the Father of our Lord Jesus Christ, praying always for you,
120104 since we heard of your faith in Christ Jesus, and of the love you have to all the saints,
120105 for the hope which is laid up for you in Heaven, of which you heard before in the Word of the truth of the gospel,
120106 which has come to you as it has also in all the world, and it is bearing fruit, even also among you, since the day you heard and fully knew the grace of God in truth,
120107 even as you learned from Epaphras our beloved fellow-servant, who is a faithful minister of Christ for you,
120108 he also having shown your love in the Spirit to us.
120109 For this cause we also, since the day we heard, do not cease to pray for you, and to desire that you might be filled with the knowledge of His will in all wisdom and spiritual understanding,
120110 that you might walk worthy of the Lord to all pleasing, being fruitful in every work and increasing in the knowledge of God,
120111 being empowered with all power, according to the might of His glory, to all patience and long-suffering with joyfulness,
120112 giving thanks to the Father, who has made us meet to be partakers of the inheritance of the saints in light.
120113 For He has delivered us from the power of darkness and has translated us into the kingdom of His dear Son;
120114 in whom we have redemption through His blood, the remission of sins.
120115 who is the image of the invisible God, the First-born of all creation.
120116 For all things were created in Him, the things in the heavens, and the things on the earth, the visible and the invisible, whether thrones or dominions or principalities or powers, all things were created through Him and for Him.
120117 And He is before all things, and by Him all things consist.
120118 And He is the Head of the body, the church, who is the Beginning, the First-born from the dead, that He may be pre-eminent in all things.
120119 For it pleased the Father that in Him all fullness should dwell.
120120 And through Him having made peace through the blood of His cross, it pleased the Father to reconcile all things to Himself through Him, whether the things on earth or the things in Heaven.
120121 And you, who were once alienated and enemies in your mind by wicked works, yet now He has reconciled
120122 in the body of His flesh through death, to present you holy and without blemish, and without charge in His sight,
120123 if indeed you continue in the faith grounded and settled, and are not moved away from the hope of the gospel, which you have heard and which was proclaimed in all the creation under Heaven, of which I, Paul, became a minister,
120124 who now rejoice in my sufferings on your behalf, and I fill up the things lacking of the afflictions of Christ in my flesh, on behalf of His body, which is the church;
120125 of which I became a minister, according to the administration of God given to me for you, to fulfill the word of God;
120126 the mystery which has been hidden from ages and from generations, but now has been revealed to His saints.
120127 For to them God would make known what are the riches of the glory of this mystery among the nations, which is Christ in you, the hope of glory,
120128 whom we preach, warning every man and teaching every man in all wisdom, so that we may present every man perfect in Christ Jesus.
120129 For which I also labor, striving according to the working of Him who works in me in power.
120201 For I want you to know what a great conflict I have for you and those at Laodicea, and for as many as have not seen my face in the flesh,
120202 that their hearts might be comforted, being knit together in love, and to all riches of the full assurance of the understanding, to the full knowledge of the mystery of God, and of the Father, and of Christ;
120203 in whom are hidden all the treasures of wisdom and knowledge.
120204 And I say this that not anyone should beguile you with enticing words.
120205 For though I am absent in the flesh, yet I am with you in the spirit, rejoicing and beholding your order and the steadfastness of your faith in Christ.
120206 Therefore as you have received Christ Jesus the Lord, so walk in Him,
120207 rooted and built up in Him, and established in the faith, as you have been taught, abounding in it with thanksgiving.
120208 Beware lest anyone rob you through philosophy and vain deceit, according to the tradition of men, according to the elements of the world, and not according to Christ.
120209 For in Him dwells all the fullness of the Godhead bodily.
120210 And you are complete in Him, who is the Head of all principality and power,
120211 in whom also you are circumcised with the circumcision made without hands, in putting off the body of the sins of the flesh by the circumcision of Christ,
120212 buried with Him in baptism, in whom also you were raised through the faith of the working of God, raising Him from the dead.
120213 And you, being dead in your sins and the uncircumcision of your flesh, He has made alive together with Him, having forgiven you all trespasses,
120214 blotting out the handwriting of ordinances that was against us, which was contrary to us, and has taken it out of the way, nailing it to the cross.
120215 Having stripped rulers and authorities, He made a show of them publicly, triumphing over them in it.
120216 Therefore let no one judge you in food or in drink, or in respect of a feast, or of the new moon, or of the sabbaths.
120217 For these are a shadow of things to come, but the body is of Christ.
120218 Let no one defraud you, delighting in humility and worship of the angels, intruding into things which he has not seen, without a cause being vainly puffed up by his fleshly mind,
120219 and not holding the Head, from whom all the body, having been supplied through the joints and bands, and having been joined together, will grow with the growth of God.
120220 If then you died with Christ from the elements of the world, why, as though living in the world, are you subject to its ordinances:
120221 touch not, taste not, handle not;
120222 which things are all for corruption in the using, according to the commands and doctrines of men?
120223 These things indeed have a reputation of wisdom in self-imposed worship and humility, and unsparing severity of the body, not in any honor for the satisfying of the flesh.
120301 If then you were raised with Christ, seek those things which are above, where Christ is sitting at the right hand of God.
120302 Be mindful of things above, not on things on the earth.
120303 For you died, and your life has been hidden with Christ in God.
120304 When Christ our Life is revealed, then you also will be revealed with Him in glory.
120305 Therefore put to death your members which are on the earth: fornication, uncleanness, passion, evil desire, and covetousness (which is idolatry),
120306 on account of which things' sake the wrath of God is coming on the sons of disobedience,
120307 among whom you also once walked, when you lived in these.
120308 But now also put off all these things: anger, wrath, malice, blasphemy, shameful speech out of your mouth.
120309 Do not lie to one another, having put off the old man with his deeds
120310 and having put on the new, having been renewed in knowledge according to the image of Him who created him,
120311 where there is neither Greek nor Jew, circumcision and uncircumcision, foreigner, Scythian, slave or freeman, but Christ is all things in all.
120312 Therefore, as the elect of God, holy and beloved, put on tender feelings of mercy, kindness, humbleness of mind, meekness, long-suffering,
120313 forbearing one another and forgiving yourselves, if anyone has a complaint against any. As Christ forgave you, so also you do .
120314 And above all these things put on love, which is the bond of perfectness.
120315 And let the peace of God rule in your hearts, to which you also are called in one body, and be thankful.
120316 Let the word of Christ dwell in you richly in all wisdom, teaching and admonishing one another in psalms and hymns and spiritual songs, singing with grace in your hearts to the Lord.
120317 And everything, whatever you do in word or deed, do all in the name of the Lord Jesus, giving thanks to God and the Father by Him.
120318 Wives, be subject to your own husbands, as is becoming in the Lord.
120319 Husbands, love your wives, and do not be bitter against them.
120320 Children, obey your parents in all things, for this is well-pleasing to the Lord.
120321 Fathers, do not provoke your children, lest they be discouraged.
120322 Slaves, obey your masters according to the flesh in all things; not with eye-service, as men-pleasers, but in singleness of heart, fearing God.
120323 And whatever you do, do it heartily, as to the Lord and not to men;
120324 knowing that from the Lord you shall receive the reward of the inheritance. For you serve the Lord Christ.
120325 But he who does wrong shall receive justice for the wrong which he did, and there is no respect of persons.
120401 Masters, give to your slaves what is just and equal, knowing that you also have a Master in Heaven.
120402 Continue in prayer and watch in it with thanksgiving,
120403 praying together about us also, that God may open to us a door of the Word, to speak the mystery of Christ, for which I also have been bound,
120404 that I may make it clear, as I ought to speak.
120405 Walk in wisdom toward those on the outside, redeeming the time.
120406 Let your speech be always with grace, having been seasoned with salt, that you may know how you ought to answer each one.
120407 Tychicus, the beloved brother and faithful minister and fellow-servant in the Lord, will make known to you all things about me.
120408 I sent him to you for this very purpose, that he might know the things about you, and that he might comfort your hearts,
120409 along with Onesimus, a faithful and beloved brother, who is one of you. They shall make known to you all things here.
120410 Aristarchus my fellow prisoner greets you, and Mark, the cousin of Barnabas (regarding whom you received commandments; if he comes to you, receive him),
120411 and greetings from Jesus, who is called Justus, those being of the circumcision. These alone are my fellow-workers for the kingdom of God, who became a comfort to me.
120412 Epaphras greets you, he being of you, a servant of Christ, always laboring fervently for you in prayers, that you may stand perfect and complete in all the will of God.
120413 For I bear him record that he has a great zeal for you and for those who are in Laodicea and those in Hierapolis.
120414 Luke, the beloved physician, and Demas, greet you.
120415 Greet the brothers who are in Laodicea, and Nymphas, and the church in his house.
120416 And when this letter is read before you, cause that it be read also in the church of the Laodiceans, and that you also read the letter of Laodicea.
120417 And say to Archippus, Take heed to the ministry which you have received in the Lord, that you fulfill it.
120418 The salutation of Paul, by my own hand. Remember my bonds. Grace be with you. Amen.
130101 Paul and Silvanus and Timothy to the church of the Thessalonians, in God the Father and in the Lord Jesus Christ. Grace to you, and peace from God our Father and the Lord Jesus Christ.
130102 We give thanks to God for you always, making mention of you in our prayers,
130103 remembering without ceasing your work of faith and labor of love and patience of hope in our Lord Jesus Christ, in the sight of God and our Father,
130104 knowing, beloved brothers, your election of God.
130105 For our gospel did not come to you in word only, but also in power and in the Holy Spirit, and in much assurance, as you know what kind of men we were among you for your sake.
130106 And you became imitators of us and of the Lord, welcoming the word in much affliction, with joy of the Holy Spirit,
130107 so that you were examples to all who believe in Macedonia and Achaia.
130108 For from you the Word of the Lord sounded out, not only in Macedonia and Achaia, but also in every place your faith toward God has gone out, so that we do not need to speak anything.
130109 For they themselves witness what kind of entrance we had to you, even how you turned from idols to God in order to serve the living and true God,
130110 and to wait for His Son from Heaven (whom He raised from the dead), Jesus, who delivered us from the wrath to come.
130201 For, my brothers, you yourselves know our coming in to you, that it was not in vain.
130202 But also suffering before, being insulted in Philippi, as you know, we were bold in our God to speak to you the gospel of God in much agony.
130203 For our exhortation to you was not of error, nor of uncleanness, nor in guile,
130204 but as we have been approved by God to be entrusted with the gospel, even so we speak, not as pleasing men, but God, who tries our hearts.
130205 For neither at any time did we use flattering words, as you know, nor with pretense of covetousness; God is witness.
130206 Nor did we seek glory from men, neither from you nor from others, being able to be so with heaviness, as apostles of Christ.
130207 But we were gentle among you, even as a nurse warmly cherishes her children.
130208 So affectionately longing for you, we were willing to have imparted to you, not only the gospel of God, but also our own souls, because you have become beloved to us.
130209 For, brothers, you remember our labor and toil. For laboring night and day in order not to put a burden on any one of you, we preached the gospel of God to you.
130210 You and God are witnesses how holily and justly and blamelessly we were to you who believe,
130211 even as you know how we exhorted and comforted and testified to each one of you, as a father to his children,
130212 that you should walk worthy of God, who has called you to His kingdom and glory.
130213 And for this cause we thank God without ceasing, that when you received the Word of hearing, of God, you welcomed it as the Word of God, not as a word of men, but as it is, truly the Word of God, which also effectually works in you who believe.
130214 For you, brothers, became imitators of the churches of God which are in Judea in Christ Jesus. For you also have suffered these things by your own countrymen, even as they also by the Jews;
130215 who both killed the Lord Jesus and their own prophets, also driving us out and they do not please God and being contrary to all men,
130216 forbidding us to speak to the nations that they might be saved, to fill up their sins always; but the wrath has come upon them to the uttermost.
130217 But, my brothers, when we were taken away from you for an hour's time (in presence, not in heart), more abundantly we were eager with much desire to see your face.
130218 Therefore we desired to come to you, truly I, Paul, both once and twice; but Satan hindered us.
130219 For what is our hope or joy, or crown of rejoicing? Are you not even to be in the presence of our Lord Jesus Christ at His coming?
130220 For you are our glory and joy.
130301 Therefore when we could no longer endure, we were pleased to be left at Athens alone.
130302 And we sent Timothy, our brother and minister of God, and our fellow laborer in the gospel of Christ, to establish you and to comfort you concerning your faith,
130303 so that no one should be drawn aside by these afflictions. For you yourselves know that we are appointed to them.
130304 For truly, when we were with you, we told you before that we were going to suffer affliction, as it also happened, even you know.
130305 For this cause, when I could no longer endure, I also sent to know your faith, lest by some means the tempter may have tempted you and our labor may have been in vain.
130306 But now when Timothy came from you to us and brought us good news of your faith and love, and that you have good remembrance of us always, desiring to see us (as we also you),
130307 then, my brothers, we were comforted over you, through your faith, even in all our affliction and needs;
130308 for now we live, if you stand fast in the Lord.
130309 For what thanks can we render to God again for you, for all the joy with which we rejoice for your sakes before our God,
130310 night and day praying exceedingly for me to see your face and to perfect the things lacking in your faith?
130311 And may God Himself and our Father and our Lord Jesus Christ direct our way to you.
130312 And may the Lord make you to increase and abound in love toward one another and toward all, even as we also toward you,
130313 in order to establish your hearts blameless in holiness before God, even our Father, at the coming of our Lord Jesus Christ with all His saints.
130401 For the rest, then, my brothers, we beseech you and exhort you in the Lord Jesus, that, as you have received from us how you ought to walk and to please God, so you would abound more and more .
130402 For we know what commands we gave you by the Lord Jesus.
130403 For this is the will of God, your sanctification, for you to abstain from fornication,
130404 each one of you to know how to possess his vessel in sanctification and honor
130405 (not in the passion of lust, even as the nations who do not know God),
130406 not to go beyond and defraud his brother in this matter (because the Lord is the avenger concerning all these, as we also have forewarned you and testified).
130407 For God has not called us to uncleanness, but in sanctification.
130408 Therefore he who despises does not despise man, but God, who also has given us His Holy Spirit.
130409 But regarding brotherly love, you do not need that I write to you, for you yourselves are taught by God to love one another.
130410 And indeed you do it toward all the brothers who are in all Macedonia. But we beseech you, brothers, that you abound more and more ,
130411 and that you try earnestly to be quiet and to do your own business, and to work with your own hands, as we commanded you,
130412 so that you may walk becomingly toward those outside, and that you may lack nothing.
130413 But I would not have you ignorant, brothers, concerning those who are asleep, that you be not grieved, even as others who have no hope.
130414 For if we believe that Jesus died and rose again, even so God will also bring with Him all those who have fallen asleep through Jesus.
130415 For we say this to you by the Word of the Lord, that we who are alive and remain until the coming of the Lord shall not go before those who are asleep.
130416 For the Lord Himself shall descend from Heaven with a shout, with the voice of the archangel and with the trumpet of God. And the dead in Christ shall rise first.
130417 Then we who are alive and remain shall be caught up together with them in the clouds, to meet the Lord in the air. And so we shall ever be with the Lord.
130418 Therefore comfort one another with these words.
130501 But of the times and the seasons, brothers, you have no need that I write to you.
130502 For you yourselves know accurately that the day of the Lord comes like a thief in the night.
130503 For when they shall say, Peace and safety! Then sudden destruction comes on them, as travail upon a woman with child. And they shall not escape.
130504 But you, brothers, are not in darkness, that the Day should overtake you like a thief.
130505 You are all the sons of light and the sons of the day. We are not of the night, or of darkness.
130506 Therefore let us not sleep as the rest do , but let us watch and be calm.
130507 For those sleeping sleep in the night, and those being drunken are drunken in the night.
130508 But let us, who are of the day, be calm, having put on the breastplate of faith and love and the hope of salvation for a helmet.
130509 For God has not appointed us to wrath, but to obtain salvation by our Lord Jesus Christ,
130510 who died for us, so that whether we watch or sleep we should live together with Him.
130511 Therefore comfort one another, and edify one another, even as you also do.
130512 And, brothers, we beseech you to know those who labor among you, and are over you in the Lord, and who admonish you,
130513 and to esteem them very highly in love for their work's sake. Be at peace among yourselves.
130514 Now we exhort you, brothers, warn those who are unruly, comfort the faint-hearted, support the weak, be patient toward all.
130515 See that none gives evil for evil to anyone, but always pursue the good, both towards one another and towards all.
130516 Rejoice evermore.
130517 Pray without ceasing.
130518 In everything give thanks, for this is the will of God in Christ Jesus concerning you.
130519 Do not quench the Spirit.
130520 Do not despise prophesying.
130521 Prove all things, hold fast to the good.
130522 Abstain from every appearance of evil.
130523 And may the God of peace Himself sanctify you, and may your whole spirit and soul and body be preserved blamelessly at the coming of our Lord Jesus Christ.
130524 Faithful is He who called you, who also will do it .
130525 Brothers, pray for us.
130526 Greet all the brothers with a holy kiss.
130527 I charge you by the Lord that this letter be read to all the holy brothers.
130528 May the grace of our Lord Jesus Christ be with you. Amen.
140101 Paul and Silvanus and Timothy to the church of the Thessalonians in God our Father and the Lord Jesus Christ.
140102 Grace to you, and peace from God our Father and the Lord Jesus Christ.
140103 We are bound to thank God always for you, my brothers, as it is right, because your faith grows exceedingly, and the love of each one of you abounds toward one another;
140104 so much so that we ourselves glory in you in the churches of God, for your patience and faith in all your persecutions and tribulations which you endure.
140105 For this is a manifest token of the righteous judgment of God, that you may be counted worthy of the kingdom of God for which you also suffer,
140106 since it is a righteous thing with God to repay tribulation to those who trouble you,
140107 and to give rest with us to you who are troubled, at the revealing of the Lord Jesus from Heaven with the angels of His power,
140108 in flaming fire taking vengeance on those who do not know God and who do not obey the gospel of our Lord Jesus Christ,
140109 who shall be punished with everlasting destruction from the presence of the Lord and from the glory of His power,
140110 when He shall come to be glorified in His saints and to be admired in all those who believe (because our testimony among you was believed) in that Day.
140111 Therefore we also pray always for you that our God would count you worthy of the calling and fulfill all the good pleasure of His goodness and the work of faith with power,
140112 that the name of our Lord Jesus Christ may be glorified in you, and you in Him, according to the grace of our God and the Lord Jesus Christ.
140201 Now we beseech you, my brothers, with regard to the coming of our Lord Jesus Christ and our gathering together to Him,
140202 that you should not be soon shaken in mind or troubled, neither by spirit, nor by word or letter, as through us, as if the Day of Christ is at hand.
140203 Let not anyone deceive you by any means. For that Day shall not come unless there first comes a falling away, and the man of sin shall be revealed, the son of perdition,
140204 who opposes and exalts himself above all that is called God, or that is worshiped, so that he sits as God in the temple of God, setting himself forth, that he is God.
140205 Do you not remember that I told you these things when I was still with you?
140206 And now you know what holds back, for him to be revealed in his own time.
140207 For the mystery of lawlessness is already working, only he is now holding back until it comes out of the midst.
140208 And then the lawless one will be revealed, whom the Lord shall consume with the breath of His mouth and shall destroy with the brightness of His coming,
140209 whose coming is according to the working of Satan with all power and signs and lying wonders,
140210 and with all deceit of unrighteousness in those who perish, because they did not receive the love of the truth, so that they might be saved.
140211 And for this cause God shall send them strong delusion, that they should believe a lie,
140212 so that all those who do not believe the truth, but delight in unrighteousness, might be condemned.
140213 But we are bound to give thanks always to God for you, brothers beloved of the Lord, because God has from the beginning chosen you to salvation through sanctification of the Spirit and belief of the truth,
140214 to which He called you by our gospel, to the obtaining of the glory of our Lord Jesus Christ.
140215 Therefore, my brothers, stand fast and hold the teachings which you have been taught, whether by word or by our letter.
140216 Now may our Lord Jesus Christ Himself, and God, even our Father, who has loved us and has given us everlasting consolation and good hope through grace,
140217 comfort your hearts and establish you in every good word and work.
140301 Finally, my brothers, pray for us, that the word of the Lord may have free course and be glorified, even as it also is with you.
140302 And pray that we may be delivered from unreasonable and wicked men; for all do not have the faith.
140303 But the Lord is faithful, who shall establish you and guard you from the evil.
140304 And we have confidence in the Lord regarding you, that you both do and will do the things which we command you.
140305 And may the Lord direct your hearts into the love of God, and into the patience of Christ.
140306 Now we command you, brothers, in the name of our Lord Jesus Christ, that you withdraw yourselves from every brother who walks disorderly, and not after the teaching which he received from us.
140307 For you yourselves know how you ought to follow us. For we did not behave ourselves disorderly among you,
140308 neither did we eat any man's bread freely, but we worked with labor and travail night and day, so that we might not be heavy on any of you
140309 (not because we do not have authority, but to make ourselves an example to you, to imitate us).
140310 For even when we were with you, we commanded you this, that if anyone would not work, neither should he eat.
140311 For we hear that there are some who walk disorderly among you, not working at all, but being busybodies.
140312 Now we command and exhort those who are such, by our Lord Jesus Christ, that they work with quietness and eat their own bread.
140313 But you, brothers, do not be weary in well doing.
140314 And if anyone does not obey our word by this letter, mark that one and have no company with him, that he may be ashamed.
140315 Yet do not count him as an enemy, but admonish him as a brother.
140316 And may the Lord of peace Himself give you peace always in every way. The Lord be with you all.
140317 The greeting of Paul by my own hand which is the sign in every letter, so I write.
140318 The grace of our Lord Jesus Christ be with you all. Amen.
150101 Paul, an apostle of Jesus Christ according to the command of God our Savior, and of the Lord Jesus Christ, our hope,
150102 to Timothy, my own son in the faith. Grace, mercy and peace from God our Father and Jesus Christ our Lord.
150103 Even as I begged you to remain at Ephesus, when I was going to Macedonia, that you might charge some that they teach no other doctrine,
150104 nor to give heed to fables and endless genealogies (which provide doubts rather than the nurture of God in faith).
150105 But the end of the commandment is love out of a pure heart, and a good conscience, and faith unfeigned,
150106 from which some, having swerved, have turned aside to foolish talking,
150107 desiring to be teachers of the law, neither understanding what they say nor that which they affirm.
150108 But we know that the law is good if a man uses it lawfully,
150109 knowing this, that the law is not made for a righteous one, but for the lawless and disobedient, for the ungodly and for sinners, for unholy and profane, for murderers of fathers and murderers of mothers, for manslayers,
150110 for fornicators, for homosexuals, for slave-traders, for liars, for perjurers, and anything else that is contrary to sound doctrine,
150111 according to the glorious gospel of the blessed God, which was committed to my trust.
150112 And I thank Christ Jesus our Lord, who strengthened me, because He counted me faithful, putting me into the ministry--
150113 the one who before was a blasphemer and a persecutor and insolent. But I obtained mercy, because being ignorant, I did it in unbelief.
150114 And the grace of our Lord was exceedingly abundant, with faith and love in Christ Jesus.
150115 Faithful is the Word and worthy of all acceptance, that Christ Jesus came into the world to save sinners, of whom I am chief.
150116 But for this cause I obtained mercy, that in me first Jesus Christ might show forth all long-suffering, as a pattern to those being about to believe on Him to life everlasting.
150117 Now to the King eternal, immortal, invisible, the only wise God, be honor and glory forever and ever. Amen.
150118 This charge I commit to you, my son Timothy, according to the prophecies which went before about you, in order that you might war a good warfare by them,
150119 holding faith and a good conscience, which some have put away and made shipwreck as to faith.
150120 Among these are Hymeneus and Alexander, whom I have delivered to Satan so that they may learn not to blaspheme.
150201 First of all, then, I exhort that supplications, prayers, intercessions, and giving of thanks be made for all men,
150202 for kings and all who are in authority, so that we may lead a quiet and peaceable life in all godliness and reverence.
150203 For this is good and acceptable in the sight of God our Savior,
150204 who will have all men to be saved and to come to the knowledge of the truth.
150205 For God is one, and there is one Mediator of God and of man, the Man Christ Jesus,
150206 who gave Himself a ransom for all, to be testified in due time.
150207 To this I am ordained a preacher and an apostle (I speak the truth in Christ, I do not lie), a teacher of the nations, in faith and truth.
150208 Therefore, I desire that men pray everywhere, lifting up holy hands, without wrath and doubting.
150209 In the same way also, I desire that women adorn themselves in decent clothing, with modesty and sensibleness, not adorned with braiding, or gold, or pearls, or costly clothing,
150210 but with good works, which becomes women professing godliness.
150211 Let the woman learn in silence with all subjection.
150212 But I do not allow a woman to teach, or to exercise authority over a man, but to be in silence.
150213 For Adam was first formed, then Eve.
150214 And Adam was not deceived, but the woman being deceived was in the transgression.
150215 But she will be kept safe through childbearing, if they continue in faith and love and holiness with sensibleness.
150301 Faithful is the word: If anyone reaches out to overseership, he desires a good work.
150302 Then it behooves the overseer to be without reproach, husband of one wife, temperate, sensible, well-ordered, hospitable, apt at teaching,
150303 not a drunkard, not contentious, not greedy of ill gain, but gentle, not quarrelsome, not covetous,
150304 ruling his own house well, having children in subjection with all honor.
150305 (For if a man does not know to rule his own house, how shall he take care of the church of God?)
150306 not a novice, lest being puffed up he may fall into the condemnation of the Devil.
150307 But he must also have a good report from those on the outside, lest he fall into reproach and the snare of the Devil.
150308 Likewise the deacons are to be reverent, not double-tongued, not given to much wine, not greedy of ill gain,
150309 having the mystery of the faith in a pure conscience.
150310 And let these also first be tested, then let them minister without reproach.
150311 Even so their wives are to be reverent, not slanderers, temperate, faithful in all things.
150312 Let the deacons be the husbands of one wife, ruling their children and households well.
150313 For they having served well gain a good grade for themselves, and much boldness in the faith, those in Christ Jesus.
150314 I write these things to you, hoping to come to you shortly.
150315 But if I should delay, that you may know how you ought to behave in the house of God, which is the church of the living God, the pillar and foundation of the truth.
150316 And without controversy great is the mystery of godliness: God was manifested in the flesh, justified in the Spirit, seen by angels, preached among nations, believed on in the world, and received up into glory.
150401 But the Spirit expressly says that in the latter times some shall depart from the faith, giving heed to seducing spirits and teachings of demons,
150402 speaking lies in hypocrisy, being seared in their own conscience,
150403 forbidding to marry, saying to abstain from foods which God has created to be received with thanksgiving by those who believe and know the truth.
150404 For every creation of God is good, and nothing to be refused if it is received with thanksgiving.
150405 For it is sanctified through the Word of God and prayer.
