150406 Having suggested these things to the brothers, you shall be a good minister of Jesus Christ, nourished up in the words of faith and by the good doctrine which you have followed.
150407 But refuse profane and old-womanish tales, and exercise yourself to godliness.
150408 For bodily exercise profits a little, but godliness is profitable to all things, having promise of the present life, and of that which is to come.
150409 Faithful is the Word, and worthy of all acceptance.
150410 For to this we both labor and suffer reproach, because we trust in the living God, who is the preserver of all men, especially of those who believe.
150411 Command and teach these things.
150412 Let no one despise your youth, but be an example of the believers, in word, in conduct, in love, in spirit, in faith, in purity.
150413 Until I come, attend to reading, to exhortation, to teaching.
150414 Do not neglect the gift in you, which was given you by prophecy, with the laying on of the hands of the body of elders.
150415 Meditate on these things; be in these things in order that your improvement may appear to all.
150416 Hold on to yourself and to the doctrine; continue in them, for doing this you shall both save yourself and those who hear you.
150501 Do not sharply rebuke an elder, but exhort as a father, and the younger ones as brothers,
150502 older women as mothers, the younger as sisters in all purity.
150503 Honor widows who are widows indeed.
150504 But if any widow has children or grandchildren, let them first learn to be godly to their own house, and give back to their forebears what is due them; for that is good and pleasing before God.
150505 But she being really a widow, and having been left alone, has set her hope on God and continues in supplications and prayers night and day.
150506 But she who lives in self-pleasure has died while living.
150507 And command these things so that they may be blameless.
150508 But if anyone does not provide for his own, and especially his family, he has denied the faith and is worse than an infidel.
150509 Do not let a widow be enrolled having become less than sixty years old, the wife of one man,
150510 well reported of for good works: if she brought up children, if she lodged strangers, if she washed the feet of saints, if she relieved the afflicted, if she followed after every good work.
150511 But refuse younger widows, for whenever they grow lustful against Christ, they desire to marry;
150512 having guilt because they have cast off the first faith.
150513 And with it all they also learn to be idle, going around the houses; and not only idle, but tattlers also and busybodies, speaking things they ought not.
150514 Therefore I want the younger ones to marry, bear children, guide the house, giving no occasion to the adversary because of reproach.
150515 For some have already turned aside after Satan.
150516 If any believing man or believing woman has widows, let them relieve them, and do not let the church be charged, so that it may relieve those who are widows indeed.
150517 Let the elders who rule well be counted worthy of double honor, especially those who labor in word and doctrine.
150518 For the Scripture says, "You shall not muzzle the ox treading out grain," and, "The laborer is worthy of his reward."
150519 Do not receive an accusation against an elder except before two or three witnesses.
150520 Those who sin, rebuke before all, so that the rest also may fear.
150521 I charge you before God and the Lord Jesus Christ, and the elect angels, that you guard these things without prejudice, doing nothing by partiality.
150522 Do not lay hands quickly on anyone, neither be partaker of the sins of others. Keep yourself pure.
150523 Drink water no longer, but use a little wine for your stomach's sake, and for your frequent infirmities.
150524 Some men's sins are open beforehand, going before to judgment. And some they also follow after.
150525 Likewise also the good works of some are manifest beforehand, and those who are otherwise cannot be hidden.
150601 Let as many slaves as are under the yoke count their own masters worthy of all honor, so that the name and doctrine of God may not be blasphemed.
150602 And those who have believing masters, let them not despise them because they are brothers. But rather let them serve, because they are faithful and beloved, those of the good service receiving in return. Teach and exhort these things.
150603 If anyone teaches otherwise, and does not consent to wholesome words (those of our Lord Jesus Christ), and to the doctrine according to godliness,
150604 he is proud, knowing nothing. He is sick concerning doubts and arguments, from which comes envy, strife, evil speakings, evil suspicions,
150605 meddling, of men whose minds have been corrupted and deprived of the truth, supposing that gain is godliness. Withdraw from such.
150606 But godliness with contentment is great gain.
150607 For we brought nothing into the world, and it is clear that we can carry nothing out.
150608 But having food and clothing, we will be content.
150609 But they who will be rich fall into temptation and a snare, and into many foolish and hurtful lusts which plunge men into destruction and perdition.
150610 For the love of money is a root of all evils, of which some having lusted after, they were seduced from the faith and pierced themselves through with many sorrows.
150611 But you, O man of God, flee these things and follow after righteousness, godliness, faith, love, patience, and meekness.
150612 Fight the good fight of faith. Lay hold on eternal life, to which you are also called and have professed a good profession before many witnesses.
150613 I charge you before God (who makes all things alive) and in the sight of Christ Jesus (who witnessed the good confession to Pontius Pilate),
150614 that you keep the commandment without spot and without blame until the appearing of our Lord Jesus Christ.
150615 For He in His own time will reveal who is the blessed and only Potentate, the King of kings and Lord of lords,
150616 who alone has immortality, dwelling in light which cannot be approached, whom no one of men have seen, nor can see; to whom be honor and power everlasting. Amen.
150617 Charge the rich in this world that they be not high-minded, nor trust in uncertain riches, but in the living God, He offering to us richly all things to enjoy,
150618 that they do good, that they be rich in good works, ready to share, to be generous,
150619 laying up in store for themselves a good foundation against the time to come, that they may lay hold on eternal life.
150620 O Timothy, guard the Deposit, avoiding profane and vain babblings, and oppositions of falsely-named science,
150621 which some professing have erred concerning the faith. Grace be with you. Amen.
160101 Paul, an apostle of Jesus Christ by the will of God, according to the promise of life which is in Christ Jesus,
160102 to Timothy, my dearly beloved child. Grace, mercy, peace from God the Father and Christ Jesus our Lord.
160103 I thank God, whom I serve from my forefathers with pure conscience, that without ceasing I remember you in my prayers night and day,
160104 greatly desiring to see you, being mindful of your tears, so that I may be filled with joy,
160105 taking recollection of the unfeigned faith that is in you, which first dwelt in your grandmother Lois, and in your mother Eunice. And I am persuaded that it is in you also.
160106 Therefore I remind you to inflame anew the gift of God, which is in you by the putting on of my hands.
160107 For God has not given us the spirit of fear, but of power and of love and of a sound mind.
160108 Therefore you should not be ashamed of the testimony of our Lord, nor of me His prisoner. But be partaker of the afflictions of the gospel according to the power of God,
160109 who has saved us and called us with a holy calling, not according to our works, but according to His own purpose and grace which was given us in Christ Jesus before the eternal times.
160110 But it is now having been manifested by the appearing of our Savior Jesus Christ, who has made death of no effect, bringing life and immortality to light through the gospel;
160111 to which I am appointed a preacher and an apostle and a teacher of the nations.
160112 For this cause I also suffer these things; but I am not ashamed, for I know whom I have believed, and I am persuaded that He is able to guard My deposit unto that Day.
160113 Hold fast the pattern of sound words which you have heard from me, in faith and love which is in Christ Jesus.
160114 Guard the good Deposit given through the Holy Spirit indwelling in us.
160115 This you know, that all those in Asia have turned away from me, of whom are Phygellus and Hermogenes.
160116 May the Lord give mercy to the house of Onesiphorus, for he often refreshed me and was not ashamed of my chain.
160117 But when he was in Rome, he sought me out very diligently and found me .
160118 May the Lord grant to him that he may find mercy from the Lord in that Day. And in what things he ministered to me at Ephesus, you know very well.
160201 Therefore, my son, be strong in the grace that is in Christ Jesus.
160202 And the things that you have heard from me among many witnesses, commit the same to faithful men who will be able to teach others also.
160203 Therefore endure hardness, as a good soldier of Jesus Christ.
160204 No one who wars tangles with the affairs of this life, that he may please him who chose him to be a soldier.
160205 And also if anyone competes, he is not crowned unless he competes lawfully.
160206 It is right for the laboring farmer to partake first of the fruits.
160207 Consider what I say, and the Lord will give you understanding in all things.
160208 Remember that Jesus Christ of the seed of David was raised from the dead according to my gospel,
160209 in which I suffer ill as an evildoer, even to bonds. But the Word of God is not chained.
160210 Therefore I endure all things for the sake of the elect, that they may also obtain the salvation which is in Christ Jesus with eternal glory.
160211 For faithful is the Word, for if we died with Him , we shall also live with Him.
160212 If we suffer, we shall also reign with Him . If we deny Him , He also will deny us.
160213 If we do not believe Him , yet He remains faithful; He cannot deny Himself.
160214 Put them in memory of these things, charging them before the Lord not to dispute about words to no profit, to the subverting of the hearers.
160215 Study earnestly to present yourself approved to God, a workman that does not need to be ashamed, rightly dividing the Word of Truth.
160216 But shun profane, vain babblings, for they will increase to more ungodliness.
160217 And their word will eat like a gangrene; among whom are Hymeneus and Philetus,
160218 who have erred concerning the truth, saying that the resurrection is already past, and who overthrow the faith of some.
160219 Nevertheless the foundation of God stands sure, having this seal: " The Lord knew those who are His." And, "Let everyone who names the name of Christ depart from iniquity!"
160220 But in a great house there are not only vessels of gold and of silver, but also of wood and of earth; and some to honor, and some to dishonor.
160221 Therefore if anyone purges himself from these, he shall be a vessel to honor, sanctified and useful to the Master, prepared for every good work.
160222 But flee youthful lusts, and follow righteousness, faith, love, peace, with those who call on the Lord out of a pure heart.
160223 But avoid foolish and unlearned questions, knowing that they give birth to strifes.
160224 But the servant of the Lord must not strive, but to be gentle to all, apt to teach, patient,
160225 in meekness instructing those who oppose, if perhaps God will give them repentance to the acknowledging of the truth,
160226 and that they awake out of the snare of the Devil, having been taken captive by him, so as to do the will of that one.
160301 Know this also, that in the last days grievous times will be at hand.
160302 For men will be self-lovers, money-lovers, boasters, proud, blasphemers, disobedient to parents, unthankful, unholy,
160303 without natural affection, unyielding, false accusers, without self-control, savage, despisers of good,
160304 traitors, reckless, puffed up, lovers of pleasure rather than lovers of God,
160305 having a form of godliness, but denying the power of it; even turn away from these.
160306 For of these are those who creep into houses and lead captive silly women loaded with sins, led away with different kinds of lusts,
160307 ever learning and never able to come to the full knowledge of the truth.
160308 But as Jannes and Jambres withstood Moses, so these also resist the truth, men of corrupt mind, reprobate concerning the faith.
160309 But they shall proceed no further. For their foolishness shall be plain to all, as theirs also became.
160310 But you have fully known my doctrine, manner of life, purpose, faith, long-suffering, love, patience,
160311 persecutions, afflictions, such as happened to me at Antioch, at Iconium, at Lystra. What persecutions I endured! But the Lord delivered me out of all.
160312 Yea, and all who desire to live godly in Christ Jesus will be persecuted.
160313 But evil men and seducers will go forward to worse, deceiving and being deceived.
160314 But continue in the things that you have learned and have been assured of, knowing from whom you have learned them ,
160315 and that from a babe you have known the Holy Scriptures, which are able to make you wise to salvation through faith in Christ Jesus.
160316 All Scripture is God-breathed, and is profitable for doctrine, for reproof, for correction, for instruction in righteousness,
160317 that the man of God may be perfected, thoroughly furnished to every good work.
160401 Therefore I solemnly witness before God and the Lord Jesus Christ, who is going to judge the living and the dead according to His appearance and His kingdom,
160402 preach the Word, be instant in season and out of season, reprove, rebuke, exhort with all long-suffering and doctrine.
160403 For a time will be when they will not endure sound doctrine, but they will heap up teachers to themselves according to their own lusts, tickling the ear.
160404 And they will turn away their ears from the truth and will be turned to myths.
160405 But you watch in all things, endure afflictions, do the work of an evangelist, fully carry out your ministry.
160406 For I am already being poured out, and the time of my release is here.
160407 I have fought the good fight, I have finished the course, I have kept the faith.
160408 Now there is laid up for me the crown of righteousness, which the Lord, the righteous Judge, shall give me at that Day; and not to me only, but also to all those who love His appearing.
160409 Make haste to come to me quickly.
160410 For Demas has forsaken me, having loved this present world, and he has departed to Thessalonica. Crescens went to Galatia, Titus to Dalmatia.
160411 Only Luke is with me. Take Mark and bring him with you, for he is profitable to me for the ministry.
160412 And I sent Tychicus to Ephesus.
160413 When you come, bring the cloak that I left at Troas with Carpus, and the books, especially the parchments.
160414 Alexander the coppersmith showed many evil things to me. The Lord will give back to him according to his works.
160415 You also should beware of him , for he has greatly withstood our words.
160416 At my first answer no one was beside me, but all deserted me. May it not be laid to their charge.
160417 But the Lord stood with me and strengthened me, that through me the preaching might be fulfilled, and that all the nations might hear. And I was delivered out of the mouth of the lion.
160418 And the Lord shall deliver me from every evil work and will preserve me to His heavenly kingdom, to whom be glory forever and ever. Amen.
160419 Greet Priscilla and Aquila and the household of Onesiphorus.
160420 Erastus stayed at Corinth, but Trophimus I left sick at Miletus.
160421 Try to come before winter. Eubulus greets you, and Pudens, and Linus, and Claudia, and all the brothers.
160422 May the Lord Jesus Christ be with your spirit. Grace be with you. Amen.
170101 Paul, a servant of God and an apostle of Jesus Christ (according to the faith of God's elect, in the acknowledging of the truth which is according to godliness
170102 on hope of eternal life, which God, who cannot lie, promised before the eternal times,
170103 but revealed His word in its own times in a proclamation, with which I was entrusted by the command of God our Savior,)
170104 to Titus, a true child according to our common faith. Grace mercy and peace from God the Father and the Lord Jesus Christ our Savior.
170105 For this cause I left you in Crete, that you should set in order the things that are lacking and ordain elders in every city, as I had appointed you,
170106 if anyone is blameless, husband of one wife, having believing children, not accused of loose behavior, or disobedient.
170107 For an overseer must be blameless, as a steward of God, not self-willed, not full of passion, not given to wine, not quarrelsome, not greedy for ill gain;
170108 but hospitable, a lover of good, discreet, just, holy, temperate,
170109 holding fast the faithful word according to the doctrine, that he may be able, by sound doctrine, both to exhort and to convict the gainsayers.
170110 For there are indeed many unruly men, vain talkers and deceivers, especially those of the circumcision,
170111 whose mouth you must stop, who subvert whole houses, teaching things not right for the sake of ill gain.
170112 One of them, a prophet of their own, said, Cretans are always liars, evil beasts, lazy gluttons.
170113 This witness is true; for which cause convict them sharply, so that they may be sound in the faith,
170114 not giving heed to Jewish myths and commandments of men, turning away from the truth.
170115 To the pure all things are pure. But to those who are defiled and unbelieving nothing is pure, but even their mind and conscience is defiled.
170116 They profess that they know God, but in their works they deny Him , being abominable and disobedient and reprobate to every good work.
170201 But you speak the things which become sound doctrine:
170202 aged men to be temperate, sensible, discreet, sound in faith, in love, in patience.
170203 Let the aged women likewise be in reverent behavior, not slanderers, not enslaved by much wine, teachers of good;
170204 that they may train the young women to love their husbands, to love their children,
170205 to be discreet, chaste, keepers at home, good, subject to their own husbands, that the Word of God may not be blasphemed.
170206 Likewise exhort the young men to be discreet;
170207 In all things having shown yourself a pattern of good works: in the doctrine, purity, sensibleness, without corruption,
170208 in sound speech that cannot be condemned, that he who is opposed may be ashamed, having no evil thing to say of you.
170209 Slaves are to be obedient to their masters, to please them well in all things , not talking against,
170210 not stealing, but showing all good faith, so that they may adorn the doctrine of God our Savior in all things.
170211 For the grace of God that brings salvation has appeared to all men,
170212 teaching us that having denied ungodliness and worldly lusts, we should live discreetly, righteously and godly, in this present world,
170213 looking for the blessed hope, and the appearance of the glory of our great God and Savior Jesus Christ,
170214 who gave Himself for us that He might redeem us from all iniquity and purify to Himself a special people, zealous of good works.
170215 Speak these things, and exhort, and rebuke with all authority. Let no one despise you.
170301 Put them in mind to be subject to rulers and authorities, to be obedient, to be ready to every good work,
170302 to speak evil of no one, not being quarrelsome, but forbearing, showing all meekness to all men.
170303 For we ourselves also were once foolish, disobedient, deceived, slaving for various lusts and pleasures, living in malice and envy, hateful, hating one another.
170304 But when the kindness and love of God our Savior toward man appeared,
170305 not by works of righteousness which we have done, but according to His mercy He saved us, through the washing of regeneration and renewal of the Holy Spirit,
170306 whom He poured out on us abundantly through Jesus Christ our Savior,
170307 that being justified by His grace, we should become heirs according to the hope of eternal life.
170308 Faithful is the Word, and as to these things, I desire that you strongly affirm that those believing God might be careful to maintain good works. These things are good and profitable to men.
170309 But avoid foolish questions and genealogies and contentions, and strivings about the Law, for they are unprofitable and vain.
170310 After the first and second warning, reject a man of heresy,
170311 knowing that he who is such has been perverted, and sins, being self-condemned.
170312 When I send Artemas to you, or Tychicus, hasten to come to me at Nicopolis, for I have determined to winter there.
170313 Diligently set forward Zenas the lawyer, and Apollos, that nothing may be lacking to them.
170314 And let ours also learn to maintain good works for necessary uses, so that they may not be unfruitful.
170315 All those with me greet you. Greet those who love us in the faith. May grace be with you all. Amen.
180101 Paul, a prisoner of Jesus Christ, and Timothy our brother, to Philemon the beloved and fellow laborer,
180102 and to Apphia the beloved, and to Archippus our fellow soldier, and to the church in your house.
180103 Grace to you and peace from God our Father and the Lord Jesus Christ.
180104 I thank my God, making mention of you always in my prayers,
180105 hearing of your love and faith which you have toward the Lord Jesus and toward all the saints,
180106 that the fellowship of your faith may operate in a full knowledge of every good thing in you in Christ Jesus.
180107 For we have great joy and consolation over your love, because the hearts of the saints have been refreshed by you, brother.
180108 Therefore, having much boldness in Christ to enjoin you to do the fitting thing;
180109 rather through love I entreat, being such a one as Paul the aged, and now also a prisoner of Jesus Christ.
180110 I entreat you for my child Onesimus, whom I have fathered in my bonds,
180111 he who was once worthless to you, but now useful to you and to me; whom I sent back to you.
180112 Even receive him, that is, my own heart,
180113 whom I resolved to retain with myself, so that for you he might have ministered to me in the bonds of the gospel.
180114 But without your consent I was willing to do nothing, that your good should not be of necessity, but willingly.
180115 For perhaps because of this he was separated from you for an hour, that you should receive him eternally,
180116 not now as a slave, but beyond a slave, a beloved brother, especially to me, but how much more to you, both in the flesh and in the Lord.
180117 If then you have me as a partner, receive him as me.
180118 If he has wronged you or owes you in anything, put that on my account.
180119 I, Paul, wrote it with my own hand; I will repay, that I do not say to you that you owe even yourself to me also.
180120 Yes, brother, that I may have your help in the Lord, refresh my heart in the Lord.
180121 Trusting to your obedience, I wrote to you, knowing that you will do even beyond what I say.
180122 But at once prepare lodging for me, for I hope that through your prayers I shall be given to you.
180123 Epaphras, my fellow prisoner in Christ Jesus, greets you,
180124 and also Mark, Aristarchus, Demas, Luke, my fellow-laborers.
180125 May the grace of our Lord Jesus Christ be with your spirit. Amen.
190101 God, who at many times and in many ways spoke in time past to the fathers by the prophets,
190102 has in these last days spoken to us by His Son, whom He has appointed heir of all things, by whom also He made the worlds,
190103 who being the shining splendor of His glory, and the express image of His essence, and upholding all things by the word of His power, through Himself cleansing of our sins, He sat down on the right of the Majesty on high,
190104 being made so much better than the angels, as He has by inheritance obtained a more excellent name than they.
190105 For to which of the angels did He say at any time, "You are My Son, this day I have begotten You?" And again, "I will be to Him a Father, and He shall be to Me a Son?"
190106 And again, when He brings in the First-born into the world, He says, "And let all the angels of God worship Him."
190107 And of the angels He says, "Who makes His angels spirits and His ministers a flame of fire."
190108 But to the Son He says , "Your throne, O God, is forever and ever. A scepter of righteousness is the scepter of Your kingdom.
190109 You have loved righteousness and hated iniquity, therefore God, Your God, has anointed You with the oil of gladness above Your fellows."
190110 And, "You, Lord, have laid the foundation of the earth in the beginning, and the heavens are the works of Your hands.
190111 They shall perish, but You will remain. And they shall all become old as a garment,
190112 and as a covering You shall fold them up, and they shall be changed. But You are the same, and Your years shall not fail."
190113 But to which of the angels, did He say at any time, "Sit on My right hand until I make Your enemies Your footstool?"
190114 Are they not all ministering spirits, sent forth to minister for those who shall be heirs of salvation?
190201 Therefore we ought to give the more earnest heed to the things which we have heard, lest at any time we should let them slip.
190202 For if the word spoken by angels was steadfast, and if every transgression and disobedience received a just recompense of reward,
190203 how shall we escape if we neglect so great a salvation, which at the first began to be spoken by the Lord, and was confirmed unto us by those who heard Him ;
190204 God also bearing them witness, both with signs and wonders, and with different kinds of miracles and gifts of the Holy Spirit, according to His own will?
190205 For He has not put in subjection to the angels the world to come, of which we speak.
190206 But one testified in a certain place, saying, "What is man, that You are mindful of him; or the son of man, that You visit him?
190207 You have made him a little lower than the angels. You crowned him with glory and honor and set him over the works of Your hands.
190208 You subjected all things under his feet." For in subjecting all things to Him, He did not leave anything not subjected to Him. But now we do not see all things having been subjected to him.
190209 But we see Jesus, who was made a little lower than the angels for the suffering of death, crowned with glory and honor, that He by the grace of God should taste death for every son .
190210 For it became Him, for whom are all things and by whom are all things, in bringing many sons into glory, to perfect the Captain of their salvation through sufferings.
190211 For both He who sanctifies and they who are sanctified are all of One, for which cause He is not ashamed to call them brothers,
190212 saying, "I will declare Your name to My brothers; in the midst of the assembly I will sing praise to You."
190213 And again, "I will put My trust in Him." And again, "Behold Me and the children whom God has given Me."
190214 Since then the children have partaken of flesh and blood, He also Himself likewise partook of the same; that through death He might destroy him who had the power of death (that is, the Devil),
190215 and deliver those who through fear of death were all their lifetime subject to bondage.
190216 For truly He did not take the nature of angels, but He took hold of the seed of Abraham.
190217 Therefore in all things it behoved him to be made like His brothers, that He might be a merciful and faithful high priest in things pertaining to God, to make propitiation for the sins of His people.
190218 For in that He Himself has suffered, having been tempted, He is able to rescue those who are being tempted.
190301 Therefore, holy brothers, called to be partakers of the heavenly calling , consider the Apostle and High Priest of our profession, Christ Jesus,
190302 who was faithful to Him who appointed Him, as Moses also was faithful in all his house.
190303 For He was counted worthy of more glory than Moses, because he who has built the house has more honor than the house.
190304 For every house is built by someone, but He who built all things is God.
190305 And Moses truly was faithful in all his house, as a servant, for a testimony of those things which were to be spoken afterward.
190306 But Christ was faithful as a Son over his own house; whose house we are, if we hold fast the confidence and the rejoicing of the hope firm to the end.
190307 Therefore, as the Holy Spirit says, "Today if you will hear His voice,
190308 do not harden your hearts, as in the provocation, in the day of temptation in the wilderness,
190309 when your fathers tempted Me, proved Me, and saw My works forty years.
190310 Therefore I was grieved with that generation and said, They always err in their heart, and they have not known My ways.
190311 So I swore in My wrath, They shall not enter into My rest."
190312 Take heed, brothers, lest there be in any of you an evil heart of unbelief, in departing from the living God.
190313 But exhort one another daily, while it is called today, lest any of you be hardened through the deceitfulness of sin.
190314 For we are made partakers of Christ, if we hold the beginning of our confidence steadfast to the end,
190315 while it is said, "Today if you will hear His voice, harden not your hearts, as in the provocation."
190316 For some, when they had heard, did provoke; however, not all who came out of Egypt by Moses.
190317 But with whom was He grieved forty years? Was it not with those who had sinned, whose carcasses fell in the wilderness?
190318 And to whom did He swear that they should not enter into His rest, but to those who did not believe?
190319 So we see that they could not enter in because of unbelief.
190401 Therefore, a promise being left to enter into His rest, let us fear lest any of you should seem to come short of it.
190402 For also we have had the gospel preached, as well as them. But the word preached did not profit them, not being mixed with faith in those who heard it .
190403 For we who have believed do enter into the rest, as He said, "I have sworn in My wrath that they should not enter into My rest;" although the works were finished from the foundation of the world.
190404 For He spoke in a certain place of the seventh day in this way: "And God rested the seventh day from all His works."
190405 And in this place again, "They shall not enter into My rest."
190406 Since then it remains that some must enter into it, and since they to whom it was first preached did not enter in because of unbelief,
190407 He again marks out a certain day, saying in David, "Today," (after so long a time). Even as it is said, "Today, if you will hear His voice, harden not your hearts."
190408 For if Joshua had given them rest, then He would not afterward have spoken of another day.
190409 So then there remains a rest to the people of God.
190410 For he who has entered into his rest, he also has ceased from his own works, as God did from His.
190411 Therefore let us labor to enter into that rest, lest anyone fall after the same example of unbelief.
190412 For the word of God is living and powerful and sharper than any two-edged sword, piercing even to the dividing apart of soul and spirit, and of the joints and marrow, and is a discerner of the thoughts and intents of the heart.
190413 Neither is there any creature that is not manifest in His sight, but all things are naked and opened to the eyes of Him with whom we have to do.
190414 Since then we have a great High Priest who has passed into the heavens, Jesus the Son of God, let us hold fast our profession.
190415 For we do not have a high priest who cannot be touched with the feelings of our infirmities, but was in all points tempted just as we are, yet without sin.
190416 Therefore let us come boldly to the throne of grace, that we may obtain mercy and find grace to help in time of need.
190501 For every high priest taken from among men is ordained for men in the things pertaining to God, so that he may offer both gifts and sacrifices for sins,
190502 who can have compassion on the ignorant and on those who are out of the way. For he himself also is compassed with weakness.
190503 And because of this he should, as for the people, so also for himself, offer for sins.
190504 And no man takes this honor to himself, but he who is called of God, as Aaron was .
190505 So also Christ did not glorify Himself to be made a high priest, but He who said to Him, "You are My Son, today I have begotten You."
190506 As He says also in another place , "You are a priest forever after the order of Melchizedek."
190507 For Jesus , in the days of His flesh, when He had offered up prayers and supplications with strong cryings and tears to Him who was able to save Him from death, and was heard in that He feared,
190508 though being a Son, yet He learned obedience by the things which He suffered.
190509 And being perfected, He became the Author of eternal salvation to all those who obey Him,
190510 being called by God a high priest after the order of Melchizedek;
190511 of whom we have much to say, and hard to be explained since you are dull of hearing.
190512 For indeed because of the time, you ought to be teachers, you have need that one teach you again what are the first principles of the oracles of God. And you have become in need of milk, and not of solid food.
190513 For everyone partaking of milk is unskillful in the word of righteousness, for he is an infant.
190514 But solid food belongs to those who are of full age, even those who because of use have their senses exercised to discern both good and evil.
190601 Therefore, having left the discourse of the beginning of Christ, let us go on to full growth, not laying again the foundation of repentance from dead works, and of faith toward God,
190602 of the baptisms, of doctrine, and of laying on of hands, and of resurrection of the dead, and of eternal judgment.
190603 And this we will do, if God permits.
190604 For it is impossible for those who were once enlightened, and have tasted of the heavenly gift, and were made partakers of the Holy Spirit,
190605 and have tasted the good Word of God and the powers of the world to come,
190606 and who have fallen away; it is impossible, I say, to renew them again to repentance, since they crucify the Son of God afresh to themselves and put Him to an open shame.
190607 (For the earth which drinks in the rain that comes often upon it, and brings forth plants fit for those by whom it is dressed, receives blessing from God.
190608 But that which bears thorns and briers is rejected and is a curse, whose end is to be burned.)
190609 But, beloved, we are persuaded better things of you and things that accompany salvation, though we speak in this way.
190610 For God is not unrighteous to forget your work and labor of love which you have shown toward His name, in that you have ministered to the saints, and do minister.
190611 And we desire that each one of you show the same eagerness to the full assurance of hope to the end,
190612 that you be not slothful, but imitators of those who through faith and patience inherit the promises.
190613 For when God made promise to Abraham, because He could swear by no greater, He swore by Himself,
190614 saying, "Surely in blessing I will bless you, and in multiplying I will multiply you."
190615 And so, after he had patiently endured, he obtained the promise.
190616 For men truly swear by the greater, and an oath for confirmation is to them an end of all strife.
190617 In this way desiring to declare more fully to the heirs of promise the immutability of His counsel, God interposed by an oath,
190618 so that by two immutable things, in which it was impossible for God to lie, we might have a strong consolation, who have fled for refuge to lay hold upon the hope set before us ,
190619 which hope we have as an anchor of the soul, both sure and steadfast, and which enters into that within the veil,
190620 where the Forerunner has entered for us, even Jesus, having become a high priest forever after the order of Melchizedek.
190701 For this Melchizedek, king of Salem and priest of the Most High God, met Abraham returning from the slaughter of the kings and blessed him.
190702 To him Abraham also gave a tenth of all. He was first by interpretation king of righteousness, and after that also king of Salem, which is king of peace,
190703 without father, without mother, without descent, having neither beginning of days nor end of life, but made like the Son of God, he remains a priest continually.
190704 Now consider how great this man was , to whom even the patriarch Abraham gave the tenth of the spoils.
190705 And truly they who are of the sons of Levi, who receive the office of the priest, have a commandment to take tithes of the people according to the Law, that is, from their brothers, though they come out of the loins of Abraham.
190706 But he whose descent is not counted from them received tithes from Abraham and blessed him who had the promises.
190707 And without all contradiction the lesser is blessed by the better.
190708 And here men who die receive tithes; but there he receives them , of whom it is witnessed that he lives.
190709 And if I may say so, Levi, also, who receives tithes, paid tithes in Abraham.
190710 For he was still in the loins of his father when Melchizedek met him.
190711 Therefore if perfection were by the Levitical priesthood (for under it the people received the Law), what further need was there that another priest should rise after the order of Melchizedek, and not be called after the order of Aaron?
190712 For the priesthood being changed, there is of necessity a change made in the law also.
190713 For He of whom these things are spoken belongs to another tribe, from which no man gave attendance at the altar.
190714 For it is evident that our Lord sprang out of Judah, of which tribe Moses spoke nothing concerning priesthood.
190715 And it is still far more evident, since there arises another priest after the likeness of Melchizedek,
190716 who is made, not according to the law of a fleshly commandment, but according to the power of an endless life.
190717 For He testifies, "You are a priest forever after the order of Melchizedek."
190718 For truly there is a putting away of the commandment which went before, because of the weakness and unprofitableness of it.
190719 For the Law made nothing perfect, but the bringing in of a better hope did , by which we draw near to God.
190720 And inasmuch as He was not made priest without an oath
190721 (for those priests were made without an oath, but this one was made with an oath by Him who said to Him, "The Lord swore and will not repent, You are a priest forever after the order of Melchizedek,")
190722 by so much was Jesus made a surety of a better covenant.
190723 And they truly were many priests, because they were not allowed to continue because of death;
190724 but He, because He continues forever, has an unchangeable priesthood.
190725 Therefore He is able also to save to the uttermost those who come unto God by Him, since He ever lives to make intercession for them.
190726 For such a high priest became us, who is holy, harmless, undefiled, separate from sinners and made higher than the heavens,
190727 who does not need, as those high priests, to offer up sacrifice daily, first for his own sins and then for the people's sins. For He did this once for all, when He offered up Himself.
190728 For the Law appoints men high priests who have infirmity, but the word of the swearing of an oath, after the Law, has consecrated the Son forever, having been perfected.
190801 Now the sum of the things which we have spoken is this : We have such a High Priest, who has sat down on the right of the throne of the Majesty in Heaven,
190802 a Minister of the sanctuary and of the true tabernacle, which the Lord pitched, and not man.
190803 For every high priest is appointed to offer gifts and sacrifices. Therefore it is necessary that this One have something to offer also.
190804 For if indeed He were on earth, He would not be a priest, since there are priests who offer gifts according to the Law,
190805 who serve the example and shadow of heavenly things, as Moses was warned of God when he was about to make the tabernacle. For, He says "See that you make all things according to the pattern shown to you in the mountain."
190806 But now He has obtained a more excellent ministry, by so much He is also the Mediator of a better covenant, which was built upon better promises.
190807 For if that first covenant had been without fault, then no place would have been sought for the second.
190808 For finding fault with them, He said to them, "Behold, days are coming, says the Lord, and I will make an end on the house of Israel and on the house of Judah; a new covenant shall be,
190809 not according to the covenant that I made with their fathers in the day I took hold of their hand to lead them out of the land of Egypt," because they did not continue in My covenant, and I did not regard them, says the Lord.
190810 "For this is the covenant that I will make with the house of Israel after those days, says the Lord: I will put My laws into their mind and write them in their hearts, and I will be their God, and they shall be My people.
190811 And they shall not each man teach his neighbor, and each man his brother, saying, Know the Lord, for all shall know Me, from the least to the greatest.
190812 For I will be merciful to their unrighteousness, and their sins and their iniquities I will remember no more."
190813 In that He says, A new covenant , He has made the first one old. Now that which decays and becomes old is ready to vanish away.
190901 Then truly the first tabernacle had also ordinances of divine service and an earthly sanctuary.
190902 For the first tabernacle was prepared, in which was both the lampstand, and the table, and the setting out of the loaves, which is called Holies.
190903 And after the second veil was a tabernacle which is called the Holy of Holies,
190904 having a golden altar of incense, and the ark of the covenant overlaid all around with gold, in which was the golden pot that had manna, and Aaron's rod that budded, and the tablets of the covenant.
190905 And over it were the cherubs of glory overshadowing the mercy-seat (about which we cannot now speak piece by piece.
190906 Now when these things were ordained in this way, the priests always went into the first tabernacle, accomplishing the service of God .
190907 But once in the year into the second the high priest goes alone, not without blood, which he offered for himself and for the errors of the people)
190908 the Holy Spirit signifying by this that the way into the Holiest of all was not yet made manifest while the first tabernacle was still standing.
190909 For it was a figure for the time then present, in which were offered both gifts and sacrifices that could not make him who did the service perfect as regards the conscience,
190910 which stood only in meats and drinks, and different kinds of washings and fleshly ordinances, imposed on them until the time of reformation.
190911 But when Christ had become a high priest of good things to come, by a greater and more perfect tabernacle, not made with hands, that is to say, not of this building
190912 nor by the blood of goats and calves, but by His own blood He entered once for all into the Holies, having obtained eternal redemption for us .
190913 For if the blood of bulls and of goats and the ashes of a heifer sprinkling the unclean sanctifies to the purifying of the flesh,
190914 how much more shall the blood of Christ (who through the eternal Spirit offered Himself without spot to God) purge your conscience from dead works to serve the living God?
190915 And for this cause He is the Mediator of the new covenant, so that by means of death, for the redemption of the transgressions that were under the first covenant, those who are called might receive the promise of eternal inheritance.
190916 For where a covenant is , the death of him covenanting must be offered.
190917 For a covenant is affirmed over those dead, since it never has force when The one covenanting is living.
190918 From which we see that neither was the first covenant dedicated without blood.
190919 For when Moses had spoken every precept to all the people according to the Law, he took the blood of calves and of goats, with water and scarlet wool and hyssop, and sprinkled both the book, and all the people,
190920 saying, "This is the blood of the covenant which God has enjoined to you."
190921 And likewise he sprinkled with blood both the tabernacle and all the vessels of the ministry.
190922 And almost all things are by the law purged with blood, and without shedding of blood is no remission.
190923 Therefore it was necessary that the patterns of things in the heavens should be purified with these, but the heavenly things themselves were purified with better sacrifices than these.
190924 For Christ has not entered into the Holy of Holies made with hands, which are the figures of the true, but into Heaven itself, now to appear in the presence of God for us.
190925 Nor yet that He should offer Himself often, even as the high priest enters into the Holy of Holies every year with the blood of others
190926 (for then He must have suffered often since the foundation of the world), but now once in the end of the world He has appeared to put away sin by the sacrifice of Himself.
190927 And as it is appointed to men once to die, but after this the judgment,
190928 so Christ was once offered to bear the sins of many. And to those who look for Him He shall appear the second time without sin to salvation.
191001 For the Law which has a shadow of good things to come, not the very image of the things, appearing year by year with the same sacrifices, which they offer continually, they are never able to perfect those drawing near.
191002 For then would they not have ceased to be offered? Because the worshipers, when they had been once for all purged, would have had no more conscience of sin.
191003 But in those sacrifices there is a remembrance again of sins every year.
191004 For it is not possible that the blood of bulls and of goats should take away sins.
191005 Therefore when He comes into the world, He says, "Sacrifice and offering You did not desire, but You have prepared a body for Me.
191006 In burnt offerings and sacrifices for sin You have had no pleasure.
191007 Then I said, Lo, I come ( in the volume of the Book it is written of Me) to do Your will, O God."
191008 Above, when He said, "Sacrifice and offering, and burnt offerings and offering for sin You did not desire, neither did You have pleasure in them" (which are offered according to the Law),
191009 then He said, "Lo, I come to do Your will, O God." He takes away the first so that He may establish the second.
191010 By this will we are sanctified through the offering of the body of Jesus Christ once for all.
191011 And indeed every priest stands daily ministering and offering often the same sacrifices, which can never take away sins.
191012 But this Man, after He had offered one sacrifice for sins forever, sat down on the right of God,
191013 from then on expecting until His enemies are made His footstool.
191014 For by one offering He has perfected forever those who are sanctified.
191015 The Holy Spirit also is a witness to us; for after He had said before,
191016 "This is the covenant that I will make with them after those days, says the Lord; I will put My laws into their hearts, and in their minds I will write them,"
191017 also He adds, "their sins and their iniquities I will remember no more."
191018 Now where remission of these is, there is no more offering for sin.
191019 Therefore, brothers, having boldness to enter into the Holy of Holies by the blood of Jesus,
191020 by a new and living way which He has consecrated for us through the veil, that is to say, His flesh;
191021 and having a High Priest over the house of God,
191022 let us draw near with a true heart in full assurance of faith, having our hearts sprinkled from an evil conscience and our bodies having been washed with pure water.
191023 Let us hold fast the profession of our faith without wavering (for He is faithful who promised),
191024 and let us consider one another to provoke to love and to good works,
191025 not forsaking the assembling of ourselves together, as the manner of some is , but exhorting one another , and so much the more as you see the Day approaching.
191026 For if we sin willfully after we have received the knowledge of the truth, there remains no more sacrifice for sins,
191027 but a certain fearful looking for judgment and fiery indignation, which shall devour the adversaries.
191028 He who despised Moses' law died without mercy on the word of two or three witnesses.
191029 Of how much worse punishment, do you suppose, will he be thought worthy of punishment, the one who has trampled the Son of God, and who has counted the blood of the covenant with which he was sanctified an unholy thing, and has insulted the Spirit of grace?
191030 For we know Him who has said, "Vengeance belongs to Me, I will repay, says the Lord." And again, "The Lord shall judge His people."
191031 It is a fearful thing to fall into the hands of the living God.
191032 But call to memory the former days, in which (after you were illuminated) you endured a great fight of afflictions,
191033 indeed being exposed both by reproaches and afflictions, and while you became companions of those who lived so.
191034 For you both sympathized with my bonds and took joyfully the spoiling of your goods, knowing in yourselves that you have in Heaven a better and an enduring substance.
191035 Therefore do not cast away your confidence, which has great recompense of reward.
191036 For you have need of patience, so that after you have done the will of God you might receive the promise.
191037 For "yet a little while, and He who shall come will come and will not delay."
191038 Now, "the Just shall live by faith. But if he draws back, My soul shall have no pleasure in him."
191039 But we are not of those withdrawing to destruction, but of those who believe to the preserving of the soul.
191101 Now faith is the substance of things hoped for, the evidence of things not seen.
191102 For by it the elders obtained a good report.
191103 By faith we understand that the ages were framed by a word of God, so that the things being seen not to have come into being out of the things that appear.
191104 By faith Abel offered to God a more excellent sacrifice than Cain, by which he obtained witness that he was righteous, God testifying of his gifts. And by it he, being dead, yet speaks.
191105 By faith Enoch was translated so as not to see death, and he was not found, because God had translated him; for before his translation he had this testimony, that he pleased God.
191106 But without faith it is impossible to please Him , for he who comes to God must believe that He is and that He is a rewarder of those who diligently seek Him.
191107 By faith Noah, having been warned by God of things not yet seen, moved with fear, prepared an ark to the saving of his house, by which he condemned the world and became heir of the righteousness which is according to faith.
191108 By faith Abraham obeyed when he was called to go out into a place which he was afterward going to receive for an inheritance. And he went out, not knowing where he went.
191109 By faith he lived in the land of promise as a stranger, dwelling in tents with Isaac and Jacob, the heirs of the same promise with him.
191110 For he looked for a city which has foundations, whose builder and maker is God.
191111 By faith also Sarah herself received strength to conceive seed and was delivered of a child when she was past age, because she judged Him who had promised to be faithful.
191112 Because of this came into being from one, and that of one having died, even as the stars of the sky in multitude, and as innumerable as the sand which is by the seashore.
191113 These all died by way of faith, not having received the promises, but having seen them afar off. And they were persuaded of them and embraced them and confessed that they were strangers and pilgrims on the earth.
191114 For they who say such things declare plainly that they seek a fatherland.
191115 And truly, if they had been mindful of that country from which they came out, they might have had opportunity to have returned.
191116 But now they stretch forth to a better fatherland , that is, a heavenly one. Therefore God is not ashamed to be called their God, for He has prepared a city for them.
191117 By faith Abraham, being tested, offered up Isaac. And he who had received the promises offered up his only-begotten son ,
191118 of whom it was said that in Isaac your Seed shall be called,
191119 concluding that God was able to raise him up, even from the dead, from where he even received him, in a figure.
191120 By faith Isaac blessed Jacob and Esau concerning things to come.
191121 By faith Jacob, when he was dying, blessed each of the sons of Joseph and worshiped, leaning upon the top of his staff.
191122 By faith, Joseph dying remembered concerning the Exodus of the sons of Israel and gave orders concerning his bones.
191123 By faith Moses, having been born, was hidden three months by his parents, because they saw he was a beautiful child. And they were not afraid of the king's commandments.
191124 Having become great, Moses by faith refused to be called the son of Pharaoh's daughter,
191125 choosing rather to suffer affliction with the people of God than to enjoy the pleasures of sin for a time,
191126 esteeming the reproach of Christ greater riches than the treasures in Egypt, for he was looking to the reward.
191127 By faith he left Egypt, not fearing the wrath of the king, for he endured as seeing Him who is invisible.
191128 Through faith he kept the Passover and the sprinkling of blood, lest He who destroyed the first-born should touch them.
191129 By faith they passed through the Red Sea as by dry land , which the Egyptians attempting to do were drowned.
191130 By faith the walls of Jericho fell down, after they had been compassed seven days.
191131 By faith the harlot Rahab did not perish with those who did not believe, when she had received the spies with peace.
191132 And what more shall I say? For the time would fail me to tell of Gideon and Barak and Samson and Jephthah; also David, and Samuel and the prophets,
191133 who through faith subdued kingdoms, wrought righteousness, obtained promises, stopped the mouths of lions,
191134 quenched the violence of fire, escaped the edge of the sword, out of weakness were made strong, became valiant in fight, turned to flight the armies of the strangers.
191135 Women received their dead raised to life again, and others were tortured, not accepting deliverance, that they might obtain a better resurrection.
191136 And others had trial of cruel mockings and scourgings; yes, more, of bonds and imprisonments.
191137 They were stoned, they were sawed in two, were tempted, were slain with the sword. They wandered about in sheepskins and goatskins, being destitute, afflicted, tormented.
191138 The world was not worthy of them. They wandered in deserts and mountains and dens and caves of the earth.
191139 And these all, having obtained a good report through faith, did not receive the promise,
191140 for God had provided some better thing for us, that they should not be made perfect without us.
191201 Therefore since we also are surrounded with so great a cloud of witnesses, let us lay aside every weight and the sin which so easily besets us , and let us run with patience the race that is set before us,
191202 looking to Jesus the Author and Finisher of our faith, who for the joy that was set before Him endured the cross, despising the shame, and sat down at the right of the throne of God.
191203 For consider Him who endured such contradiction of sinners against Himself, lest you be weary and faint in your minds.
191204 You have not yet resisted unto blood, striving against sin.
191205 And you have forgotten the exhortation which speaks to you as to sons, "My son, despise not the chastening of the Lord, nor faint when you are rebuked by Him;
191206 for whom the Lord loves He chastens, and He scourges every son whom He receives."
191207 If you endure chastening, God deals with you as with sons, for what son is he whom the father does not chasten?
191208 But if you are without chastisement, of which all are partakers, then you are bastards and not sons.
191209 Furthermore we have had fathers of our flesh who corrected us , and we gave them reverence. Shall we not much rather be in subjection to the Father of spirits and live?
191210 For truly they chastened us for a few days according to their own pleasure, but He for our profit, that we might be partakers of His holiness.
191211 Now chastening for the present does not seem to be joyous, but grievous. Nevertheless afterward it yields the peaceable fruit of righteousness to those who are exercised by it.
191212 Because of this, straighten up the hands which hang down and the enfeebled knees.
191213 And make straight paths for your feet, lest that which is lame be turned out of the way, but let it rather be healed.
191214 Follow peace with all, and holiness, without which no one shall see the Lord;
191215 looking diligently lest any fail of the grace of God, or lest any root of bitterness springing up disturb you , and by it many are defiled,
191216 (lest there be any fornicator, or profane person like Esau, who for one morsel of food sold his birthright.
191217 For you know that afterward, when he desired to inherit the blessing, he was rejected; for he did not find any place of repentance, though he sought it carefully with tears).
191218 For you have not come to the mountain that might be touched and that burned with fire, nor to blackness and darkness and tempest,
191219 and the sound of a trumpet, and the voice of words (which voice they who heard begged that a word should not be spoken to them any more,
191220 for they could not endure the thing commanded, "And if so much as a beast should touch the mountain, it shall be stoned or thrust through with a dart,"
191221 and so fearful was the sight that Moses said, I exceedingly fear and quake).
191222 But you have come to Mount Zion and to the city of the living God, the heavenly Jerusalem, and to an innumerable company of angels,
191223 to the general assembly and church of the first-born who are written in Heaven, and to God the judge of all, and to the spirits of just men made perfect,
191224 and to Jesus the Mediator of the new covenant, and to blood of sprinkling that speaks better things than that of Abel.
191225 See that you do not refuse Him who speaks. For if they did not escape, those who refused him that spoke on earth, much more we shall not escape if we turn away from Him who speaks from Heaven,
191226 whose voice then shook the earth; but now He has promised, saying, "Yet once more I will not only shake the earth, but also the heavens."
191227 And this word , "Yet once more," signifies the removing of those things that are shaken, as of things that have been made, so that the things which cannot be shaken may remain.
191228 Therefore, since we are receiving a kingdom that cannot be shaken, let us have grace, by which we may serve God acceptably with reverence and godly fear,
191229 for also, "Our God is a consuming fire."
191301 Let brotherly love continue.
191302 Do not be forgetful of hospitality, for by this some have entertained angels without knowing it.
191303 Remember those who are in bonds, as bound with them , those who suffer adversity, as being yourselves also in the body.
191304 Marriage is honorable in all, and the bed undefiled, but fornicators and adulterers God will judge.
191305 Let your way of life be without the love of money, and be content with such things as you have, for He has said, "Not at all will I leave you, not at all will I forsake you, never!"
191306 so that we may boldly say, " The Lord is my helper, and I will not fear what man shall do to me."
191307 Remember those leading you, who have spoken to you the Word of God, whose faith follow, considering the end of their conduct:
191308 Jesus Christ the same yesterday and today and forever.
191309 Do not be carried about with different and strange doctrines, for it is good for the heart to be established with grace, not with foods, in which those who have walked in them were not helped.
191310 We have an altar of which they have no right to eat, those who serve the tabernacle.
191311 For the bodies of those animals, whose blood is brought into the Holy of Holies by the high priest for sin, are burned outside the camp.
191312 Therefore Jesus also, so that He might sanctify the people through His own blood, suffered outside the gate.
191313 Therefore let us go forth to Him outside the camp, bearing His reproach.
191314 For here we have no continuing city, but we seek one to come.
191315 By Him, then, let us offer the sacrifice of praise to God continually, that is, the fruit of our lips, confessing His name.
191316 But do not forget to do good and to share, for with such sacrifices God is well pleased.
191317 Yield to those leading you, and be submissive, for they watch for your souls, as those who must give account, that they may do it with joy and not with grief; for that is unprofitable for you.
191318 Pray for us; for we trust we have a good conscience, in all things willing to live honestly.
191319 But I beseech you the rather to do this, so that I may be more quickly restored to you.
191320 Now may the God of peace (who brought again our Lord Jesus from the dead, that great Shepherd of the sheep, through the blood of the everlasting covenant)
191321 make you perfect in every good work to do His will, working in you that which is well pleasing in His sight through Jesus Christ, to whom be glory forever and ever. Amen.
191322 And I beseech you, brothers, allow the word of exhortation. For I have written a letter to you in few words.
191323 Know that our brother Timothy has been set at liberty, with whom, if he comes shortly, I will see you.
191324 Greet all those leading you, and all the saints. Those from Italy greet you.
191325 Grace be with you all. Amen.
200101 James, a servant of God and of the Lord Jesus Christ, to the twelve tribes in the Dispersion, greeting:
200102 My brothers, count it all joy when you fall into different kinds of temptations,
200103 knowing that the trying of your faith works patience.
200104 But let patience have its perfect work, so that you may be perfect and entire, lacking nothing.
200105 But if any of you lacks wisdom, let him ask of God, who gives to all liberally and with no reproach, and it shall be given to him.
200106 But let him ask in faith, doubting nothing. For he who doubts is like a wave of the sea, driven by the wind and tossed.
200107 For do not let that man think that he shall receive anything from the Lord;
200108 he is a double-minded man, not dependable in all his ways.
200109 But let the humble brother rejoice in his exaltation;
200110 and the rich one rejoice in his humiliation, because he shall pass away as the flower of the grass.
200111 For the sun rose with the hot wind and dried up the grass, and its flower fell out, and the beauty of its appearance perished; so also the rich one will fade away in his ways.
200112 Blessed is the man who endures temptation, because having been approved, he will receive the crown of life which the Lord has promised to those who love Him.
200113 Let no one being tempted say, I am tempted from God. For God is not tempted by evils, and He tempts no one.
200114 But each one is tempted by his lusts, being drawn away and seduced by them .
200115 Then when lust has conceived, it brings forth sin. And sin, when it is fully formed, brings forth death.
200116 Do not err, my beloved brothers.
200117 Every good gift and every perfect gift is from above and comes down from the Father of lights, with whom is no variableness nor shadow of turning.
200118 Of His own will He brought us forth with the Word of truth, for us to be a certain firstfruit of His creatures.
200119 Therefore, my beloved brothers, let every man be swift to hear, slow to speak, slow to wrath.
200120 For the wrath of man does not work out the righteousness of God.
200121 Therefore putting aside all filthiness and overflowing of evil, receive in meekness the implanted Word, which is able to save your souls.
200122 But become doers of the Word, and not hearers only, deceiving your own selves.
200123 For if anyone is a hearer of the Word and not a doer, he is like a man studying his natural face in a mirror.
200124 For he studied himself and went his way, and immediately he forgot what he was like.
200125 But whoever looks into the perfect law of liberty and continues in it , he is not a forgetful hearer, but a doer of the work. This one shall be blessed in his doing.
200126 If anyone thinks to be religious among you, yet does not bridle his tongue, but deceives his own heart, this one's religion is vain.
200127 Pure religion and undefiled before God and the Father is this, to visit orphans and widows in their afflictions, and to keep oneself unspotted from the world.
200201 My brothers, do not have the faith of our Lord Christ, the Lord of glory, with respecter of faces.
200202 For if there comes a gold-fingered man in fancy clothing into your assembly, and if there also comes in a poor man in shabby clothing,
200203 and if you have respect to him who has the fancy clothing and say to him, You sit here in a good place, and say to the poor, You stand there, or sit here under my footstool;
200204 Did you not make a difference among yourselves and became judges with evil thoughts?
200205 Listen, my beloved brothers, has not God chosen the poor of this world rich in faith and heirs of the kingdom which He has promised to those who love Him?
200206 But you dishonored the poor one. Do not rich men oppress you and draw you before the judgment seats?
200207 Do they not blaspheme that worthy Name by which you are called?
200208 If you fulfill the royal law according to the Scripture, "You shall love your neighbor as yourself," you do well.
200209 But if you have respect to persons, you commit sin and are convicted by the law as transgressors.
200210 For whoever shall keep the whole law and yet offend in one point , he is guilty of all.
200211 For He who said, "Do not commit adultery," also said, "Do not murder." But if you do not commit adultery, yet if you murder, you have become a transgressor of the law.
200212 So speak and do as those who shall be judged by the law of liberty.
200213 For he who has shown no mercy shall have judgment without mercy, and mercy exults over judgment.
200214 My brothers, what profit is it if a man says he has faith and does not have works? Can faith save him?
200215 If a brother or sister is naked and destitute of daily food,
200216 and if one of you says to them, Go in peace, be warmed and filled, but you do not give them those things which are needful to the body, what good is it ?
200217 Even so, if it does not have works, faith is dead, being by itself.
200218 But someone will say, You have faith, and I have works. Show me your faith without your works, and I will show you my faith from my works.
200219 You believe that there is one God, you do well; even the demons believe and tremble.
200220 But will you know, O vain man, that faith without works is dead?
200221 Was not Abraham our father justified by works when he had offered Isaac his son upon the altar?
200222 Do you see how faith worked with his works, and from the works faith was made complete?
200223 And the Scripture was fulfilled which says, "Abraham believed God, and it was imputed to him for righteousness, and he was called the friend of God."
200224 You see then how a man is justified by works, and not by faith only.
200225 And in the same way, was not Rahab the harlot also justified by works when she had received the messengers and had sent them out another way?
200226 For as the body without the spirit is dead, so faith without works is dead also.
200301 My brothers, do not be many teachers, knowing that we shall receive the greater condemnation.
200302 For in many things we all offend. If anyone does not offend in word, the same is a full-grown man, able also to bridle the whole body.
200303 Behold, we put bits in the horses' mouths, so that they may obey us, and we turn about their whole body.
200304 Behold also the ships being so great, and driven by fierce winds, yet they are turned about with a very small rudder, where the impulse of him steering desires.
200305 Even so the tongue is a little member and boasts great things. Behold how little a fire kindles how large a forest!
200306 And the tongue is a fire, a world of iniquity. So the tongue is set among our members, spotting all the body and inflaming the course of nature, and being inflamed by hell.
200307 For every kind of animals, and of birds, and of reptiles, and of sea-animals, is tamed, and has been tamed by mankind.
200308 But no one can tame the tongue, it is an unruly evil, full of deadly poison.
200309 By this we bless God, even the Father. And by this we curse men, who have come into being according to the image of God.
200310 Out of the same mouth proceeds blessing and cursing. My brothers, these things ought not to be so.
200311 Does a fountain send forth at the same hole the sweet and the bitter?
200312 Can the fig tree, my brothers, bear olive berries; or a vine, figs? So no fountain can yield both salt water and fresh.
200313 Who is wise and knowing among you? Let him show his works by his good conduct with meekness of wisdom.
200314 But if you have bitter jealousy and strife in your hearts, do not glory and lie against the truth.
200315 This is not the wisdom coming down from above, but is earthly, sensual, devilish.
200316 For where envying and strife are , there is confusion and every foul deed.
200317 But the wisdom that is from above is first truly pure, then peaceable, gentle, easy to be entreated, full of mercy and good fruits, without partiality and without hypocrisy.
200318 And the fruit of righteousness is sown in peace by those who make peace.
200401 From where do wars and fightings among you come ? Is it not from this, from your lusts which war in your members?
200402 You desire, and do not have. You murder, and are jealous, and cannot obtain. You fight and war, yet you have not because you ask not.
200403 You ask and receive not, because you ask amiss, that you may spend it upon your lusts.
200404 Adulterers and adulteresses! Do you not know that the friendship of the world is enmity with God? Therefore whoever desires to be a friend of the world is the enemy of God.
200405 Do you think that the Scripture says in vain, The spirit that dwells in us yearns to envy?
200406 But He gives more grace. Therefore He says, God resists the proud, but He gives grace to the humble.
200407 Therefore submit yourselves to God. Resist the devil, and he will flee from you.
200408 Draw near to God, and He will draw near to you. Cleanse your hands, sinners; and purify your hearts, double-minded ones.
200409 Be afflicted, and mourn and weep. Let your laughter be turned to mourning and your joy to heaviness.
200410 Be humbled before the Lord, and He will lift you up.
200411 Do not speak against one another, brothers. He who speaks against his brother, and who judges his brother, speaks against the Law and judges the Law. But if you judge the Law, you are not a doer of the Law, but a judge.
200412 There is one Lawgiver, who is able to save and to destroy. Who are you who judges another?
200413 Come now, those saying, Today or tomorrow we will go into such a city and spend a year there, and we will trade and will make a profit,
200414 who do not know of the morrow. For what is your life? For it is a vapor, which appears for a little time, and then disappears.
200415 Instead of you saying, If the Lord wills, we shall live and do this or that.
200416 But now you boast in your presumptions. All such boasting is evil.
200417 Therefore to him who knows to do good, and does not do it , to him it is sin.
200501 Come now, rich ones, weep and howl for your hardships coming on.
200502 Your riches have rotted, and your clothes have become moth-eaten.
200503 Your gold and silver have corroded, and their poison will be a witness against you, and will eat your flesh as fire. You heaped treasure in the last days.
200504 Behold, the hire of the laborers reaping your fields cry out, being kept back by you. And the cries of those who have reaped have entered into the ears of the Lord of hosts.
200505 You have lived luxuriously on the earth, and lived wantonly. You have nourished your hearts, as in a day of slaughter.
200506 You have condemned and murdered the just; he does not resist you.
200507 Therefore be patient, brothers, until the coming of the Lord. Behold, the farmer waits for the precious fruit of the earth and has long patience for it, until he receives the early and the latter rain.
200508 You also be patient, establish your hearts, for the coming of your Lord draws near.
200509 Do not grudge against one another, brothers, lest you be condemned. Behold, the Judge stands before the door.
200510 My brothers, take the prophets who have spoken in the name of the Lord, for an example of suffering ill, and of patience.
200511 Behold, we count blessed those who endure. You have heard of the patience of Job, and you have seen the end of the Lord, that the Lord is full of pity and of tender mercy.
200512 But before all things, my brothers, do not swear; neither by the heaven nor by the earth, nor any other oath. But let your yes be yes, and your no, no, lest you fall into condemnation.
200513 Is any among you afflicted? Let him pray. Is any cheerful? Let him sing psalms.
200514 Is any sick among you? Let him call for the elders of the church, and let them pray over him, anointing him with oil in the name of the Lord.
200515 And the prayer of faith will cure the sick, and the Lord shall raise him up. And if he has committed sins, it will be forgiven him.
200516 Confess faults to one another, and pray for one another, that you may be healed. The effectual fervent prayer of a righteous one avails much.
200517 Elijah was a man of like passion as we are. And he prayed earnestly that it might not rain, and it did not rain on the earth for the time of three years and six months.
200518 And he prayed again, and the heaven gave rain, and the earth caused its fruit to sprout.
200519 Brothers, if anyone among you err from the truth, and if anyone turns him back,
200520 know that he who turns back the sinner from the error of his way shall save a soul from death, and shall hide a multitude of sins.
210101 Peter, an apostle of Jesus Christ, to the elect sojourners of the Dispersion of Pontus, of Galatia, of Cappadocia, of Asia, and of Bithynia,
210102 according to the foreknowledge of God the Father, in sanctification of the Spirit, to obedience and sprinkling of the blood of Jesus Christ. May grace and peace be multiplied to you.
210103 Blessed be the God and Father of our Lord Jesus Christ, who according to His great mercy has regenerated us again to a living hope through the resurrection of Jesus Christ from the dead,
210104 to an inheritance incorruptible and undefiled, and unfading, reserved in Heaven for you
210105 by the power of God, having been kept through faith to a salvation ready to be revealed in the last time;
210106 in which you greatly rejoice, yet a little while , if need be, grieving in manifold temptations;
210107 so that the trial of your faith (being much more precious than that of gold that perishes, but being proven through fire) might be found to praise and honor and glory at the revelation of Jesus Christ,
210108 whom having not seen, you love; in whom not yet seeing, but believing in Him you exult with unspeakable joy, and having been glorified,
210109 obtaining the end of your faith, the salvation of your souls.
210110 About which salvation the prophets sought out and searched out, prophesying concerning the grace for you;
210111 searching for what, or what manner of time, the Spirit of Christ made clear within them, testifying beforehand of the sufferings of Christ, and the glories that should follow.
210112 To them it was revealed that not to themselves, but to us, they ministered the things which are now reported to you by those who have preached the gospel to you in the Holy Spirit sent from Heaven; which things the angels desire to look into.
210113 Therefore girding up the loins of your mind, being sober, perfectly hope for the grace being brought to you at the revelation of Jesus Christ,
210114 as obedient children, not fashioning yourselves according to the former lusts in your ignorance,
210115 but according to the Holy One who has called you, you also become holy in all conduct,
210116 because it is written, "Be holy, for I am holy."
210117 And if you call on the Father, who without respect of persons judges according to the work of each one, pass the time of your earthly residence in fear,
210118 knowing that you were not redeemed with corruptible things, silver or gold, from your vain manner of life handed down from your fathers,
210119 but with the precious blood of Christ, as of a lamb without blemish and without spot;
210120 indeed having been foreknown before the foundation of the world, but revealed in the last times for you,
210121 those believing in God through Him, He who raised Him up from the dead and gave Him glory, so that your faith and hope might be in God.
210122 Purifying your souls in the obedience of the truth through the Spirit to unfeigned love of the brothers, love one another fervently out of a pure heart,
210123 having been born again, not of corruptible seed, but of incorruptible, through the living word of God, and abiding forever.
210124 For all flesh is as grass, and all the glory of men as the flower of the grass. The grass withers, and its flower falls out,
210125 but the Word of the Lord endures forever. And this is the Word preached as gospel to you.
210201 Therefore laying aside all malice and all guile and hypocrisies and envyings, and all evil speakings,
210202 desire the sincere milk of the word, as newborn babes, so that you may grow by it;
210203 if truly you have tasted that the Lord is gracious.
210204 For having been drawn to Him, a living Stone, indeed rejected by men, but elect, precious with God;
