210205 you also as living stones are built up a spiritual house, a holy priesthood, to offer up spiritual sacrifices acceptable to God through Jesus Christ.
210206 Therefore also it is contained in the Scripture: "Behold, I lay in Zion a chief corner Stone, elect, precious, and he who believes on Him shall never be ashamed."
210207 Therefore to you who believe is the honor. But to those who are disobedient, He is the Stone which the builders rejected; this One came to be the Head of the corner,
210208 and a Stone-of-stumbling and a Rock-of-offense to those disobeying, who stumble at the word, to which they also were appointed.
210209 But you are a chosen generation, a royal priesthood, a holy nation, a people for possession, so that you might speak of the praises of Him who has called you out of darkness into His marvelous light;
210210 you who then were not a people, but now the people of God, those not pitied then , but now pitied.
210211 Dearly beloved, I exhort you as temporary residents and pilgrims to abstain from fleshly lusts which war against the soul,
210212 having your conduct honest among the nations, in that which they speak against you as evildoers, they may glorify God in a day of His visitation, seeing your good works.
210213 Then be in obedience to every ordinance of men, because of the Lord, whether to a king as supreme,
210214 or to governors as sent by Him for vengeance on evildoers, but for praise on well-doers.
210215 For such is the will of God, doing good to silence the ignorance of foolish men;
210216 as free, and not having freedom as a cover of evil, but as servants of God.
210217 Honor all. Love the brotherhood. Fear God. Honor the king.
210218 Servants, be subject to your masters with all fear, not only to those good and forbearing, but also to the perverse ones.
210219 For this is a grace, if for conscience toward God anyone endures grief, suffering wrongfully.
210220 For what glory is it if you patiently endure while sinning and being buffeted? But if you suffer while doing good, and patiently endure, this is a grace from God.
210221 For you were not called to this? For Christ also suffered on our behalf, leaving us an example, that you should follow His steps,
210222 He who did no sin, nor was guile found in His mouth,
210223 who when He was reviled did not revile in return. When He suffered, He did not threaten, but gave Himself up to Him who judges righteously.
210224 He Himself bore our sins in His own body on the tree, that dying to sins, we might live to righteousness; by whose stripes you were healed.
210225 For you were as sheep going astray, but now you are turned to the Shepherd and Overseer of your souls.
210301 Likewise, wives, be in subjection to your own husbands, so that if any do not obey the word, they may also be won without the word by the conduct of the wives,
210302 having witnessed your chaste behavior in the fear of God .
210303 Of whom let not be the adorning of garments, or outward braiding of hair and wearing of gold, or of putting on clothing,
210304 but let it be the hidden man of the heart, in that which is not corruptible, the meek and quiet spirit, which is of great price in the sight of God.
210305 For so once indeed the holy women hoping in God adorned themselves, being in subjection to their own husbands;
210306 as Sarah obeyed Abraham, calling him lord; whose children you became, doing good and fearing no terror.
210307 Likewise, husbands, live together according to knowledge, giving honor to the wife as to the weaker vessel, the female, as truly being co-heirs together of the grace of life, not cutting off your prayers.
210308 And finally, all be of one mind, having compassion on one another, loving the brothers, tenderhearted, friendly.
210309 Never give back evil for evil, or reviling for reviling, but on the contrary, giving blessing, knowing that you are called to this so that you might inherit blessing.
210310 For he that wants to love life and to see good days, let him restrain his tongue from evil, and his lips from speaking guile.
210311 Let him turn aside from evil and do good. Let him seek peace and pursue it.
210312 For the eyes of the Lord are on the righteous, and His ears open to their prayers. But the Lord's face is against those who do evil.
210313 And who is the one who will harm you if you become imitators of the good?
210314 But if you also suffer for righteousness' sake, you are blessed. And do not fear their fear, nor be troubled,
210315 but sanctify the Lord God in your hearts, and be ready always to give an answer to everyone who asks you a reason of the hope in you, with meekness and fear;
210316 having a good conscience, that while they speak against you as evildoers they may be shamed, those falsely accusing your good behavior in Christ.
210317 For it is better, if the will of God wills it , to suffer for well-doing than for evil-doing.
210318 For Christ also once suffered for sins, the just for the unjust, that He might bring us to God, indeed being put to death in the flesh, but made alive in the Spirit;
210319 in which also He went and preached to the spirits in prison,
210320 to disobeying ones, when once the long-suffering of God waited in the days of Noah, while the ark was being prepared (in which a few, that is, eight souls were saved through water);
210321 which figure now also saves us, baptism; not a putting away of the filth of the flesh, but the answer of a good conscience toward God, by the resurrection of Jesus Christ;
210322 who is at the right hand of God, having gone into Heaven, where the angels and authorities and powers are being subjected to Him.
210401 Therefore, Christ having suffered for us in the flesh, also you arm yourselves with the same thought, that he suffering in the flesh has been made to rest from sin,
210402 in order no longer to live in the lusts of men, but in the will of God the remaining time in the flesh.
210403 For the time of life which is past is enough for us to have worked out the will of the nations, having gone on in lasciviousness, lusts, excess of wine, parties, carousings, and abominable idolatries.
210404 In these things they are surprised, that you are not running with them into the same excess of riot, blaspheming.
210405 But they shall give account to Him who is ready to judge the living and the dead.
210406 For to this end the gospel was preached also to the dead, that they might be judged according to men in the flesh, but live according to God in the Spirit.
210407 But the end of all things has drawn near. Therefore be of sound mind, and be sensible to prayers.
210408 And above all things have fervent love to yourselves, for love will cover a multitude of sins.
210409 Be hospitable to one another, without grudging;
210410 each one as he received a gift, ministering it to yourselves as good stewards of the manifold grace of God.
210411 If anyone speaks, let it be as the words of God. If anyone ministers, let him do it as of the ability which God gives, so that God may be glorified in all things through Jesus Christ, to whom is the glory, and the might forever and ever. Amen.
210412 Beloved, do not be astonished at the fiery trial which is to try you, as though a strange thing happened to you,
210413 but rejoice according as you are partakers of Christ's suffering, so that when His glory shall be revealed, you may be glad also with exceeding joy.
210414 If you are reviled for the name of Christ, you are blessed, because the Spirit of God and of glory rests on you. Truly according to them, He is blasphemed, but according to you He is glorified.
210415 But let none of you suffer as a murderer, or a thief, or an evildoer, or a meddler in the affairs of others.
210416 But if one suffers as a Christian, let him not be ashamed, but let him glorify God because of this.
210417 For the time has come for the judgment to begin from the house of God. And if it first begins from us, what will be the end of those disobeying the gospel of God?
210418 And if the righteous one is scarcely saved, where shall the ungodly and the sinner appear?
210419 Therefore let those who suffer according to the will of God commit their souls in well-doing, as to a faithful Creator.
210501 I exhort the elders who are among you, I being also an elder and a witness of the sufferings of Christ, and also a partaker of the glory that shall be revealed.
210502 Feed the flock of God among you, taking the oversight, not by compulsion, but willingly; nor for base gain, but readily;
210503 nor as lording it over those allotted to you by God , but becoming examples to the flock.
210504 And when the Chief Shepherd shall appear, you shall receive a never-fading crown of glory.
210505 Likewise, younger ones, be subject to older ones, and all being subject to one another. Put on humility. For God resists proud ones, but He gives grace to the humble.
210506 Therefore be humbled under the mighty hand of God, so that He may exalt you in due time,
210507 casting all your anxiety onto Him, for He cares for you.
210508 Be sensible and vigilant, because your adversary the Devil walks about like a roaring lion, seeking someone he may devour;
210509 whom firmly resist in the faith, knowing that the same afflictions in the world are being completed in your brotherhood.
210510 But the God of all grace, He calling us to His eternal glory by Christ Jesus, after you have suffered a little, He will perfect, confirm, strengthen, and establish you .
210511 To Him be the glory and the might forever and ever. Amen.
210512 I wrote to you through a few words , by Silvanus, a faithful brother to you, as I suppose, exhorting and testifying this to be the true grace of God in which you stand.
210513 The fellow-elected in Babylon greet you; also Mark my son.
210514 Greet one another with a kiss of holy love. Peace be to you, all those in Christ Jesus. Amen.
220101 Simon Peter, a servant and an apostle of Jesus Christ, to those who have obtained like precious faith with us through the righteousness of our God and our Savior Jesus Christ,
220102 Grace and peace be multiplied to you through the knowledge of God and of Jesus our Lord,
220103 according as His divine power has given to us all things that pertain to life and godliness, through the knowledge of Him who has called us to glory and virtue,
220104 through which He has given to us exceedingly great and precious promises, so that by these you might be partakers of the divine nature, having escaped the corruption that is in the world through lust.
220105 But also in this very thing, bringing in all diligence, filling out your faith with virtue, and with virtue, knowledge;
220106 and with knowledge self-control, and with self-control, patience, and with patience, godliness,
220107 and with godliness, brotherly kindness, and with brotherly kindness, love.
220108 For if these things are in you and abound, they make you to be neither idle nor unfruitful in the knowledge of our Lord Jesus Christ.
220109 For he in whom these things are not present is blind and cannot see afar off and has forgotten that he was purged from his sins in the past.
220110 Therefore, brothers, rather be diligent to make your calling and election sure, for if you do these things, you shall never fall.
220111 For so an entrance shall be ministered to you abundantly into the everlasting kingdom of our Lord and Savior Jesus Christ.
220112 Therefore I will not neglect to put you always in remembrance of these things, though you know them and are established in the present truth.
220113 But I think it right, as long as I am in this tabernacle, to stir you up by a reminder,
220114 knowing that the putting off of my tabernacle is soon, as indeed our Lord Jesus Christ made clear to me.
220115 And I will also be diligent to cause you to always have memory of these things after my departure.
220116 For not having followed fables having been cunningly devised, but becoming eyewitnesses of the majesty of Jesus Christ, we made known to you the power and coming of our Lord.
220117 For He received honor and glory from God the Father, when was borne to Him a voice from the excellent glory, "This is My beloved Son, in whom I am well pleased."
220118 And we heard this voice being borne from Heaven, being with Him in the holy mountain.
220119 We also have a more sure word of prophecy, to which you do well to take heed, as to a light that shines in a dark place, until the day dawns and the Daystar arises in your hearts,
220120 knowing this first, that no prophecy of the Scripture came into being of its own private interpretation.
220121 For prophecy was not borne at any time by the will of man, but holy men of God spoke being borne along by the Holy Spirit.
220201 But there were also false prophets among the people, even as there will be false teachers among you, who secretly will bring in destructive heresies, even denying the Master who bought them, bringing on themselves swift destruction.
220202 And many will follow their pernicious ways, and because of them the way of truth will be evil spoken of.
220203 And through covetousness they will use you for gain with well-turned words; for whom judgment from of old does not linger, and their destruction does not sleep.
220204 For if God did not spare sinning angels, but thrust them down into Tartarus, and delivered them into chains of darkness, being reserved to judgment.
220205 And He did not spare the old world, but saved Noah the eighth one, a preacher of righteousness, bringing in the flood upon the world of the ungodly.
220206 And turning the cities of Sodom and Gomorrah into ashes, He condemned them with an overthrow, setting an example to men intending to live ungodly.
220207 And He delivered righteous Lot, oppressed with the lustful behavior of the lawless.
220208 For that righteous one living among them, in seeing and hearing, his righteous soul was tormented from day to day with their unlawful deeds.
220209 The Lord knows how to deliver the godly out of temptation, and to reserve the unjust for a day of judgment, to be punished,
220210 and especially those who walk after the flesh in the lust of uncleanness, and despise dominion. They are darers, self-pleasing; not trembling at glories, speaking evil.
220211 Where angels, who are greater in power and might, do not bring a reproaching accusation against them before the Lord.
220212 But these, as unreasoning natural brute animals having been born for capture and corruption, speak evil of the things that they do not understand. And they will utterly perish in their own corruption,
220213 being about to receive the wages of unrighteousness, deeming indulgence as pleasure in the daytime, and reveling in spots and blemishes, feasting along with you in their deceits,
220214 having eyes full of adultery and never ceasing from sin, alluring unstable souls, having a heart exercised with covetousness. They are cursed children
220215 who have forsaken the right way and have gone astray, following the way of Balaam the son of Beor, who loved the wages of unrighteousness,
220216 but had reproof of his lawbreaking, a dumb ass speaking in a man's voice, held back the madness of the prophet.
220217 These are wells without water, clouds driven with a tempest, for whom the blackness of darkness is reserved forever.
220218 For when they speak great swelling words of vanity, they lure through the lusts of the flesh, by unbridled lust, the ones who were escaping from those who live in error;
220219 promising them liberty, they themselves are the slaves of corruption. For by whom anyone has been overcome, even to this one he has been enslaved.
220220 For if they have escaped the pollutions of the world through the full knowledge of the Lord and Savior Jesus Christ, and are again entangled, they have been overcome by these, their last things are worse than the first.
220221 For it would have been better for them not to have fully known the way of righteousness, than fully knowing it , to turn from the holy commandment delivered to them.
220222 But the word of the true proverb has happened to them: The dog turning to his own vomit; and, The washed sow to wallowing in the mire.
220301 Beloved, I now write this second letter to you, in which I stir up your pure mind by reminder
220302 to remember the words which were spoken before by the holy prophets, and of the commandment of the Lord and Savior by us, the apostles.
220303 First, knowing this, that there will come in the last days scoffers walking according to their own lusts
220304 and saying, Where is the promise of His coming? For since the fathers fell asleep, all things continue as they were from the beginning of creation.
220305 For this is hidden from them by their willing it, that the heavens were of old, and the earth out of the water, and through water, being held together by the word of God,
220306 through which the world that then was, being flooded by water, perished.
220307 But the present heavens and the earth being kept in store by the same word, are being kept for fire until the day of judgment and destruction of ungodly men.
220308 But, beloved, let not this one thing be hidden from you , that one day is with the Lord as a thousand years, and a thousand years as one day.
220309 The Lord is not slow concerning His promise, as some count slowness, but is long-suffering toward us, not purposing that any of us should perish, but that all should come to repentance.
220310 But the day of the Lord will come as a thief in the night, in which the heavens will pass away with a rushing noise, and the elements will melt with fervent heat. And the earth and the works in it will be burned up.
220311 Then, all these things being about to be dissolved, what sort ought you to be in holy behavior and godliness,
220312 looking for and rushing the coming of the Day of God, on account of which the heavens, being on fire, will melt away, and the elements will melt, burning with heat?
220313 But according to His promise, we look for new heavens and a new earth in which righteousness dwells.
220314 Therefore, beloved, looking for these things, be diligent, spotless, and without blemish, to be found by Him in peace.
220315 And think of the long-suffering of our Lord as salvation (as our beloved brother Paul also has written to you according to the wisdom given to him
220316 as also in all his letters, speaking in them of these things; in which are some things hard to be understood, which the unlearned and unstable pervert, as also they do the rest of the Scriptures, to their own destruction).
220317 Therefore, beloved, knowing beforehand, beware lest being led away with the error of the lawless, you fall from your own steadfastness.
220318 But grow in grace and in knowledge of our Lord and Savior Jesus Christ. To Him be the glory, both now and to the day of eternity. Amen.
230101 That which was from the beginning, which we have heard, which we have seen with our eyes, which we have looked upon, and our hands have handled, concerning the Word of life,
230102 (for the Life was revealed, and we have seen it and bear witness, and show to you the everlasting Life, who was with the Father and was revealed to us),
230103 that which we have seen and heard we declare unto you, so that you also may have fellowship with us. And truly our fellowship is with the Father and with His Son Jesus Christ.
230104 And we write these things to you so that your joy may be full.
230105 And this is the message which we have heard from Him and declare to you, that God is light, and in Him is no darkness at all.
230106 If we say that we have fellowship with Him and walk in darkness, we lie and do not practice the truth.
230107 But if we walk in the light, as He is in the light, we have fellowship with one another, and the blood of Jesus Christ His Son cleanses us from all sin.
230108 If we say that we have no sin, we deceive ourselves, and the truth is not in us.
230109 If we confess our sins, He is faithful and just to forgive us our sins, and to cleanse us from all unrighteousness.
230110 If we say that we have not sinned, we make Him a liar, and His Word is not in us.
230201 My little children, I write these things to you so that you may not sin. And if anyone sins, we have an Advocate with the Father, Jesus Christ the righteous.
230202 And He is the propitiation concerning our sins, and not concerning ours only, but also concerning the sins of all the world.
230203 And by this we know that we have known Him, if we keep His commandments.
230204 He who says, I have known Him, and does not keep His commandments, is a liar, and the truth is not in him.
230205 But whoever keeps His Word, truly in this one the love of God is perfected. By this we know that we are in Him.
230206 He who says he abides in Him ought himself also to walk even as He walked.
230207 Brothers, I do not write a new commandment to you, but an old commandment which you had from the beginning. The old commandment is the word which you have heard from the beginning.
230208 Again, I write a new commandment to you, which thing is true in Him and in you, because the darkness is passing away, and the true Light now shines.
230209 He who says he is in the light and hates his brother is in darkness until now.
230210 He who loves his brother abides in the light, and there is no offense in him.
230211 But he who hates his brother is in darkness, and walks in darkness, and does not know where he is going, because darkness has blinded his eyes.
230212 I write to you, little children, because your sins are forgiven you for His name's sake.
230213 I write to you, fathers, because you have known Him who is from the beginning. I write to you, young men, because you have overcome the evil one. I write to you, little children, because you have known the Father.
230214 I write to you, fathers, because you have known Him who is from the beginning. I have written to you, young men, because you are strong, and the word of God abides in you, and you have overcome the evil one.
230215 Do not love the world, nor the things in the world. If anyone loves the world, the love of the Father is not in him,
230216 because all that is in the world, the lust of the flesh, and the lust of the eyes, and the pride of life, is not of the Father, but is of the world.
230217 And the world passes away, and the lust of it, but he who does the will of God abides forever.
230218 Little children, it is the last time. And just as you have heard that antichrist is coming, even now many antichrists have risen up, from which we know that it is the last hour.
230219 They went out from us, but they were not of us; for if they were of us, they would have continued with us. But they went out so that it might be revealed that they were not all of us.
230220 But you have an anointing from the Holy One, and you know all things.
230221 I have not written to you because you do not know the truth, but because you know it, and know that no lie is of the truth.
230222 Who is a liar but he who denies that Jesus is the Christ? He who denies the Father and the Son is antichrist.
230223 Everyone who denies the Son neither has the Father. The one confessing the Son also has the Father.
230224 Therefore what you heard from the beginning, let it abide in you. If what you heard from the beginning remains in you, you will abide in both the Son and in the Father.
230225 And this is the promise that He has promised us: everlasting life.
230226 These things I have written to you concerning those leading you astray.
230227 But the anointing which you received from Him abides in you, and you do not need anyone to teach you. But as His anointing teaches you concerning all things, and is true and no lie, and as He has taught you, abide in Him.
230228 And now, little children, abide in Him, so that when He is revealed, we may have confidence and not be ashamed before Him in His coming.
230229 If you know that He is righteous, you know that everyone who does righteousness has been born of Him.
230301 Behold what manner of love the Father has given us, that we should be called children of God. Therefore the world does not know us, because it did not know Him.
230302 Beloved, now we are children of God, and it has not yet been revealed what we shall be. But we know that when He shall be revealed, we shall be like Him, for we shall see Him as He is.
230303 And everyone who has this hope on him purifies himself, even as that One is pure.
230304 Everyone who practices sin also practices lawlessness, for sin is lawlessness.
230305 And you know that He was revealed that He might take away our sins, and in Him is no sin.
230306 Everyone who abides in Him does not sin. Everyone who sins has not seen Him nor known Him.
230307 Little children, let no one deceive you. He who does righteousness is righteous, even as that One is righteous.
230308 He who practices sin is of the Devil, for the Devil sins from the beginning. For this purpose the Son of God was revealed, that He might undo the works of the Devil.
230309 Everyone who has been born of God does not commit sin, because His seed remains in him, and he cannot sin, because he has been born of God.
230310 In this the children of God are revealed, and the children of the Devil: everyone not practicing righteousness is not of God, also he who does not love his brother.
230311 For this is the message that you have heard from the beginning, that we should love one another;
230312 not as Cain who was of the evil one, and killed his brother. And for what did he kill him? Because his own works were evil, and his brother's things were righteous.
230313 Do not marvel, my brothers, if the world hates you.
230314 We know that we have passed from death to life, because we love the brothers. He who does not love his brother abides in death.
230315 Everyone hating his brother is a murderer. And you know that no murderer has everlasting life abiding in him.
230316 By this we have known the love of God , because He laid down His life for us. And we ought to lay down our lives for the brothers.
230317 But whoever has this world's goods and sees his brother having need, and shuts up his bowels from him, how does the love of God dwell in him?
230318 My children, let us not love in word or in tongue, but in deed and in truth.
230319 And in this we shall know that we are of the truth, and shall assure our hearts before Him,
230320 that if our heart accuses us, God is greater than our heart and knows all things.
230321 Beloved, if our heart does not accuse us, we have confidence toward God.
230322 And whatever we ask, we receive from Him, because we keep His commandments and do those things that are pleasing in His sight.
230323 And this is His commandment, that we should believe on the name of His Son Jesus Christ, and love one another, as He gave us commandment.
230324 And he who keeps His commandment dwells in Him, and He in him. And by this we know that He abides in us, by the Spirit which He gave to us.
230401 Beloved, do not believe every spirit, but try the spirits to see if they are of God, because many false prophets have gone out into the world.
230402 By this you know the Spirit of God: every spirit that confesses that Jesus Christ has come in the flesh is of God;
230403 and every spirit that does not confess that Jesus Christ has come in the flesh is not of God. And this is the antichrist you heard is coming, and even now is already in the world.
230404 You are of God, little children, and you have overcome them, because He who is in you is greater than he who is in the world.
230405 They are of the world, therefore they speak of the world, and the world hears them.
230406 We are of God. He who knows God hears us. The one who is not of God does not hear us. From this we know the spirit of truth and the spirit of error.
230407 Beloved, let us love one another, for love is of God, and everyone who loves has been born of God, and knows God.
230408 The one who does not love has not known God. For God is love.
230409 In this the love of God was revealed in us, because God sent His only begotten Son into the world that we might live through Him.
230410 In this is love, not that we loved God, but that He loved us and sent His Son to be the propitiation concerning our sins.
230411 Beloved, if God so loved us, we ought also to love one another.
230412 No one has seen God at any time. If we love one another, God dwells in us, and His love is perfected in us.
230413 By this we know that we dwell in Him, and He in us, because He has given us of His Spirit.
230414 And we have seen and testify that the Father sent the Son to be the Savior of the world.
230415 Whoever shall confess that Jesus is the Son of God, God dwells in him and he in God.
230416 And we have known and believed the love that God has in us. God is love, and he who abides in love abides in God, and God in him.
230417 In this is our love made perfect, that we may have boldness in the day of judgment, that as He is, so also we are in this world.
230418 There is no fear in love, but perfect love casts out fear, because fear has torment. He who fears has not been perfected in love.
230419 We love Him because He first loved us.
230420 If anyone says, I love God, and hates his brother, he is a liar. For if he does not love his brother whom he has seen, how can he love God whom he has not seen?
230421 And we have this commandment from Him, that he who loves God should love his brother also.
230501 Everyone who believes that Jesus is the Christ has been born of God. And everyone who loves Him who begets also loves him who has been born of Him.
230502 By this we know that we love the children of God, whenever we love God and keep His commandments.
230503 For this is the love of God, that we keep His commandments, and His commandments are not burdensome.
230504 For everything that has been born of God overcomes the world. And this is the victory that overcomes the world, our faith.
230505 Who is he who overcomes the world, but he who believes that Jesus is the Son of God?
230506 This is He who came through water and blood, Jesus Christ, not by water only, but by the water and blood. And the Spirit is He who bears witness, because the Spirit is the truth.
230507 For there are three that bear witness in heaven: the Father, the Word, and the Holy Spirit, and these three are one.
230508 And there are three that bear witness on the earth: the Spirit, and the water, and the blood; and the three are into the one.
230509 If we receive the witness of men, the witness of God is greater. For this is the witness of God which He has testified about His Son.
230510 He who believes on the Son of God has the witness in himself. He who does not believe God has made Him a liar, because he does not believe the record that God gave of His Son.
230511 And this is the record, that God has given to us everlasting life, and this life is in His Son.
230512 He who has the Son has life; he who does not have the Son of God does not have life.
230513 I have written these things to you who believe on the name of the Son of God, that you may know that you have everlasting life, and that you may believe on the name of the Son of God.
230514 And this is the confidence that we have toward Him, that if we ask anything according to His will, He hears us.
230515 And if we know that He hears us, whatever we ask, we know that we have the petitions that we desired of Him.
230516 If anyone sees his brother sin a sin not to death, he shall ask, and He shall give him life for those that do not sin to death. There is a sin to death, I do not say that he shall pray for it.
230517 All unrighteousness is sin, and there is a sin not to death.
230518 We know that everyone who has been born of God does not continue to sin, but the one born of God guards himself, and the evil one does not touch him.
230519 We know that we are of God, and all the world lies in evil.
230520 And we know that the Son of God has come, and He has given us an understanding so that we may know Him who is true. And we are in Him that is true, in His Son Jesus Christ. This is the true God, and the everlasting life.
230521 Little children, guard yourselves from idols. Amen.
240101 The elder to the elect lady and her children, whom I love in the truth and not only I, but also all those who have known the truth,
240102 for the sake of the truth dwelling in us, and which shall be with us forever.
240103 Grace will be with you, mercy and peace from God the Father and from the Lord Jesus Christ, the Son of the Father, in truth and love.
240104 I rejoiced greatly that I found your children walking in truth, as we have received command from the Father.
240105 And now I beseech you, lady, not as though I wrote a new commandment to you, but that which we had from the beginning, that we love one another.
240106 And this is love, that we walk according to His commandments. This is the commandment, as you heard from the beginning, that you should walk in it.
240107 For many deceivers have entered into the world, who do not confess Jesus Christ coming in the flesh. This is the deceiver and the anti-christ.
240108 Look to yourselves, so that we may not lose those things which we worked out, but that we may receive a full reward.
240109 Everyone transgressing and not abiding in the doctrine of Christ does not have God. He who abides in the doctrine of Christ, he has both the Father and the Son.
240110 If anyone comes to you and does not bring this doctrine, do not receive him into your house, nor speak a greeting to him.
240111 For he who speaks a greeting to him is partaker of his evil deeds.
240112 Having many things to write to you, I do not want to say with paper and ink. But I trust to come to you and speak face to face, so that our joy may be full.
240113 The children of your elect sister greet you. Amen.
250101 The elder to Gaius the beloved, whom I love in the truth.
250102 Beloved, in regard to all things I pray that you prosper and be in health, even as your soul prospers.
250103 For I rejoiced greatly when the brothers came and testified of the truth that is in you, even as you walk in the truth.
250104 I have no greater joy than these things, to hear that my children walk in the truth.
250105 Beloved, you do faithfully whatever you work for the brothers and for strangers,
250106 who in love bore witness of you before the church, whom you will do well to send forward worthily of God;
250107 because they went forth for His name's sake, taking nothing from the nations.
250108 Therefore we ought to entertain such, so that we might be co-workers in the truth.
250109 I wrote to the church, but Diotrephes, who loves to have the preeminence among them, did not receive us.
250110 Therefore if I come, I will remember his deeds which he does, ranting against us with evil words. And not content with these, neither does he himself receive the brothers. And he forbids those who would, and casts them out of the church.
250111 Beloved, do not imitate the bad, but the good. He who does good is from God, but he who does evil has not seen God.
250112 Demetrius has good report by all, and by the truth itself. And we also bear witness, and you know that our witness is true.
250113 I had many things to write, but I will not write to you with pen and ink,
250114 but I trust I shall shortly see you, and we shall speak face to face. Peace be to you. The friends greet you. Greet the friends by name.
260101 Jude, a servant of Jesus Christ, and brother of James, to the ones called in God the Father, having been set apart, and having been kept by Jesus Christ:
260102 Mercy and peace and love be multiplied to you.
260103 Having made all haste to write to you about the common salvation, beloved, I had need to write to you to exhort you to contend earnestly for the faith once delivered to the saints.
260104 For certain men crept in secretly, those having been of old previously written into this condemnation, ungodly ones perverting the grace of our God for unbridled lust, and denying the only Master, God, even our Lord Jesus Christ.
260105 But I intend to remind you, you once knowing these things, that the Lord having delivered a people out of the land of Egypt, in the second place destroyed the ones not believing.
260106 And those angels not having kept their first place, but having deserted their dwelling-place, He has kept in everlasting chains under darkness for the judgment of a great Day;
260107 as Sodom and Gomorrah, and the cities around them, in like manner to these, committing fornication, and going away after other flesh, laid down an example before-times, undergoing vengeance of everlasting fire.
260108 Likewise, indeed, also these dreaming ones even defile flesh, and despise rulership, and speak evil of glories.
260109 But Michael, the archangel, when contending with the Devil, he argued about the body of Moses, he dared not bring a judgment of blasphemy, but said, Let the Lord rebuke you!
260110 But what things they do not know, they speak evil of. And what things they understand naturally, like the animals without reason, they are corrupted by these.
260111 Woe to them! For they went the way of Cain, and gave themselves up to the error of Balaam for reward, and perished in the gainsaying of Korah.
260112 These are sunken rocks in your love feasts, feasting together with you; feeding themselves without fear; waterless clouds being carried about by winds; fruitless autumn trees, having died twice, having been plucked up by the roots;
260113 wild waves of the sea foaming up their shames; wandering stars for whom blackness of darkness has been kept forever.
260114 And Enoch, the seventh from Adam, also prophesied to these, saying, Behold, the Lord came with myriads of His saints,
260115 to do judgment against all, and to rebuke all the ungodly of them concerning all their ungodly works which they ungodly did, and concerning all the hard things ungodly sinners spoke against Him.
260116 These are murmurers, complainers, leading lives according to their lusts. And their mouth speaks proud things, admiring faces for the sake of gain.
260117 But you, beloved, remember the words spoken before by the apostles of our Lord Jesus Christ,
260118 because they told you that at the last time there will be mockers according to their lusts, leading ungodly lives.
260119 These are those setting themselves apart, animal-like ones, not having the Spirit.
260120 But you, beloved, building yourselves up in your most holy faith, praying in the Holy Spirit,
260121 keep yourselves in the love of God, eagerly awaiting the mercy of our Lord Jesus Christ to everlasting life.
260122 But pity some, making distinction.
260123 But save others with fear, snatching them out of the fire; hating even the garment having been stained from the flesh.
260124 Now to Him being able to keep you without stumbling, and to set you before His glory without blemish, with unspeakable joy;
260125 to the only wise God, our Savior, be glory and majesty and might and authority, even now and forever. Amen.
270101 A Revelation of Jesus Christ, which God gave to Him to declare to His servants things which must shortly come to pass. And He signified it by sending His angel to His servant John,
270102 who bore record of the Word of God and of the testimony of Jesus Christ and of all the things that he saw.
270103 Blessed is the one who reads and hears the words of this prophecy, and the ones keeping the things written in it, for the time is near.
270104 John to the seven churches which are in Asia. Grace to you and peace from Him who is and who was and who is coming; and from the seven spirits which are before His throne;
270105 even from Jesus Christ the faithful Witness, the First-born from the dead and the Ruler of the kings of the earth. To Him who loved us and washed us from our sins in His own blood,
270106 and made us kings and priests to God and His Father, to Him be glory and dominion forever and ever. Amen.
270107 Behold, He comes with the clouds, and every eye will see Him, and those who pierced Him will see Him, and all the kindreds of the earth will wail because of Him. Even so, Amen.
270108 I am the Alpha and Omega, the Beginning and the Ending, says the Lord, who is and who was and who is to come, the Almighty.
270109 I, John, who also am your brother and companion in the affliction, and in the kingdom and patience of Jesus Christ, was in the island that is called Patmos, for the Word of God and for the testimony of Jesus Christ.
270110 I came to be in the Spirit in the Lord's day and heard behind me a great voice, as of a trumpet,
270111 saying, I am the Alpha and Omega, the First and the Last. Also, What you see, write in a book and send it to the seven churches which are in Asia: to Ephesus, and to Smyrna, and to Pergamos, and to Thyatira, and to Sardis, and to Philadelphia, and to Laodicea.
270112 And I turned to see the voice that spoke with me.
270113 And having turned, I saw seven golden lampstands. And in the midst of the seven lampstands I saw One like the Son of man, clothed with a garment down to the feet, and tied around the breast with a golden band.
270114 His head and hair were white like wool, as white as snow. And His eyes were like a flame of fire.
270115 And His feet were like burnished brass having been fired in a furnace. And His voice was like the sound of many waters.
270116 And He had seven stars in His right hand, and out of His mouth went a sharp two-edged sword. And His face was like the sun shining in its strength.
270117 And when I saw Him, I fell at His feet as dead. And He laid His right hand upon me, saying to me, Do not fear, I am the First and the Last,
270118 and the Living One, and I became dead, and behold, I am alive for ever and ever, Amen. And I have the keys of hell and of death.
270119 Write the things which you have seen, and the things which are, and the things which shall be after this,
270120 the mystery of the seven stars which you saw in My right hand and the seven golden lampstands. The seven stars are the angels of the seven churches, and the seven lampstands which you saw are the seven churches.
270201 To the angel of the church of Ephesus write: He who holds the seven stars in His right hand, who walks in the midst of the seven golden lampstands, says these things.
270202 I know your works and your labor and your patience, and how you cannot bear those who are evil. And you tried those pretending to be apostles, and are not, and have found them liars.
270203 And you have borne, and have patience, and for My name's sake you have labored and have not fainted.
270204 But I have against you that you left your first love.
270205 Therefore remember from where you have fallen, and repent, and do the first works, or else I will come to you quickly and will remove your lampstand out of its place unless you repent.
270206 But you have this, that you hate the deeds of the Nicolaitans, which I also hate.
270207 He who has an ear, let him hear what the Spirit says to the churches. To him who overcomes I will give to eat of the Tree of Life, which is in the midst of the paradise of God.
270208 And to the angel of the church in Smyrna write: The First and the Last, who became dead and lived, says these things:
270209 I know your works and tribulation and poverty (but you are rich), and I know the blasphemy of those saying themselves to be Jews, and are not, but are the synagogue of Satan.
270210 Do not at all fear what you are about to suffer. Behold, the Devil will cast some of you into prison, so that you may be tried. And you will have tribulation ten days. Be faithful to death, and I will give you the crown of life.
270211 He who has an ear, let him hear what the Spirit says to the churches. He who overcomes will not be hurt by the second death.
270212 And to the angel of the church in Pergamos write: He who has the sharp sword with two edges says these things.
270213 I know your works, and where you live, even where Satan's seat is . And you hold fast My name and have not denied My faith, even in those days in which Antipas was My faithful martyr, who was slain among you, where Satan dwells.
270214 But I have a few things against you, because you have there those who hold the teachings of Balaam, who taught Balak to cast a stumbling-block before the sons of Israel, to eat things sacrificed to idols and to commit fornication.
270215 So you also have those who hold the teaching of the Nicolaitans, which thing I hate.
270216 Repent! But if not I will come to you quickly, and will fight with them by the sword of My mouth.
270217 He who has an ear, let him hear what the Spirit says to the churches. To him who overcomes I will give to eat of the hidden manna, and will give to him a white stone, and in the stone a new name written, which no man knows except he who receives it .
270218 And to the angel of the church in Thyatira write: The Son of God, He who has His eyes like a flame of fire and His feet like burnished metal, says these things:
270219 I know your works and love and service and faith and your patience, and your works; and the last to be more than the first.
270220 But I have a few things against you because you allow that woman Jezebel to teach, she saying herself to be a prophetess, and to cause My servants to go astray, and to commit fornication, and to eat idol-sacrifices.
270221 And I gave her time that she might repent of her fornication, and she did not repent.
270222 Behold, I am throwing her into a bed, and those who commit adultery with her into great affliction, unless they repent of their deeds.
270223 And I will kill her children with death. And all the churches will know that I am He who searches the reins and hearts, and I will give to every one of you according to your works.
270224 But to you I say, and to the rest in Thyatira, as many as do not have this doctrine, and who have not known the depths of Satan, as they speak, I will put on you no other burden.
270225 But that which you have, hold fast until I come.
270226 And he who overcomes and keeps My works to the end, to him I will give power over the nations.
270227 And he will rule them with a rod of iron, as the vessels of a potter they will be broken to pieces, even as I received from My Father.
270228 And I will give him the Morning Star.
270229 He who has an ear, let him hear what the Spirit says to the churches.
270301 And to the angel of the church in Sardis write: He who has the seven Spirits of God and the seven stars says these things. I know your works, that you have a name that you live, and are dead.
270302 Be watchful and strengthen the things which remain, that are ready to die. For I have not found your works being fulfilled before God.
270303 Remember then how you have received and heard, and hold fast, and repent. Therefore if you will not watch, I will come upon you as a thief, and you will not know what hour I will come upon you.
270304 You have a few names even in Sardis who have not defiled their garments. And they will walk with Me in white, for they are worthy.
270305 The one who overcomes, this one will be clothed in white clothing. And I will not blot out his name out of the Book of Life, but I will confess his name before My Father and before His angels.
270306 He who has an ear, let him hear what the Spirit says to the churches.
270307 And to the angel of the church in Philadelphia write: He who is holy, He who is true, He who has the key of David, He who opens and no one shuts; and shuts and no one opens, says these things:
270308 I know your works. Behold, I have given before you an open door, and no one can shut it. For you have a little strength and have kept My word and have not denied My name.
270309 Behold, I give out of those of the synagogue of Satan, those saying themselves to be Jews and are not, but lie; behold, I will make them to come and worship before your feet, and to know that I have loved you.
270310 Because you have kept the word of My patience, I also will keep you from the hour of temptation which will come upon all the habitable world, to try those who dwell upon the earth.
270311 Behold, I come quickly. Hold fast to that which you have, so that no one may take your crown.
270312 Him who overcomes I will make him a pillar in the temple of My God, and he will go out no more. And I will write upon him the name of My God, and the name of the city of My God, the New Jerusalem, which comes down out of Heaven from My God, and My new name.
270313 He who has an ear, let him hear what the Spirit says to the churches.
270314 And to the angel of the church of the Laodicea write: The Amen, the faithful and true Witness, the Head of the creation of God, says these things:
270315 I know your works, that you are neither cold nor hot. I would that you were cold or hot.
270316 So because you are lukewarm, and neither cold nor hot, I will vomit you out of My mouth.
270317 Because you say, I am rich and increased with goods and have need of nothing, and do not know that you are wretched and miserable and poor and blind and naked,
270318 I counsel you to buy from Me gold purified by fire, so that you may be rich; and white clothing, so that you may be clothed, and so that the shame of your nakedness does not appear. And anoint your eyes with eye salve, so that you may see.
270319 As many as I love, I rebuke and chasten; therefore be zealous and repent.
270320 Behold, I stand at the door and knock. If anyone hears My voice and opens the door, I will come in to him and will dine with him and he with Me.
270321 To him who overcomes I will grant to sit with Me in My throne, even as I also overcame and have sat down with My Father in His throne.
270322 He who has an ear, let him hear what the Spirit says to the churches.
270401 After these things I looked, and behold, a door was opened in Heaven. And the first voice which I heard was as it were of a trumpet talking with me, saying, Come up here, and I will show you what must occur after these things.
270402 And immediately I became in spirit. And behold, a throne was set in Heaven, and One sat upon the throne.
270403 And He who sat there looked like a jasper stone and a sardius. And a rainbow was around the throne, looking like an emerald.
270404 And around the throne I saw twenty-four thrones. And on the thrones I saw twenty-four elders sitting, clothed in white clothing. And they had crowns of gold on their heads.
270405 And out of the throne came lightnings and thunderings and voices. And seven lamps of fire were burning in front of the throne, which are the seven spirits of God.
270406 And a sea of glass was in front of the throne, like crystal. And in the midst of the throne, and around the throne, were four living creatures, full of eyes in front and behind.
270407 And the first living creature was like a lion, and the second living creature like a calf, and the third living creature had the face of a man, and the fourth living creature like a flying eagle.
270408 And each one of the four living creatures had six wings about him , and within being full of eyes. And they had no rest day and night, saying, Holy, holy, holy, Lord God, the Almighty, who was and is and is to come.
270409 And whenever the living creatures gave glory and honor and thanks to Him who sat on the throne, who lives forever and ever,
270410 the twenty-four elders fell down before the One sitting on the throne. And they worshiped Him who lives for ever and ever, and threw their crowns before the throne, saying,
270411 O Lord, You are worthy to receive glory and honor and power, because You created all things, and for Your will they are and were created.
270501 And I saw a book on the right of Him sitting on the throne, written inside and on the back, sealed with seven seals.
270502 And I saw a mighty angel proclaiming with a loud voice, Who is worthy to open the book and to loosen its seals?
270503 And no one in Heaven, nor on the earth, nor under the earth, was able to open the book or to look at it.
270504 And I wept very much, because no one was found worthy to open and to read the book, nor to look at it.
270505 And one of the elders said to me, Do not weep. Behold, the Lion of the tribe of Judah, the Root of David, has prevailed to open the book and to loose the seven seals of it.
270506 And I looked, and lo, in the midst of the throne and of the four living creatures, amidst the elders, a Lamb stood, as if it had been slain, having seven horns and seven eyes, which are the seven Spirits of God sent forth into all the earth.
270507 And He came and took the book out of the right hand of Him sitting on the throne.
270508 And when He had taken the book, the four living creatures and the twenty-four elders fell down before the Lamb, each one having harps and golden vials full of incense, which are the prayers of the saints.
270509 And they sang a new song, saying, You are worthy to take the book and to open its seals, for You were slain and have redeemed us to God by Your blood out of every kindred and tongue and people and nation.
270510 And You made us kings and priests to our God, and we will reign over the earth.
270511 And I looked, and I heard the voice of many angels around the throne, and the living creatures and the elders. And the number of them was myriads and myriads, and thousands of thousands,
270512 saying with a great voice, Worthy is the Lamb who was slain, to receive power and riches and wisdom and strength and honor and glory and blessing.
270513 And I heard every creature which is in the Heaven and on the earth, and under the earth, and those that are in the sea, and all who are in them, saying, Blessing and honor and glory and power be to Him sitting on the throne, and to the Lamb forever and ever.
270514 And the four living creatures said, Amen. And the twenty-four elders fell down and worshiped the One living forever and ever.
270601 And I saw when the Lamb opened one of the seals, and I heard one of the four living creatures like a sound of thunder, saying, Come and see.
270602 And I saw. And behold a white horse! And he sitting on it had a bow. And a crown was given to him, and he went forth conquering and to conquer.
270603 And when He had opened the second seal, I heard the second living creature say, Come and see.
270604 And another, a red horse, went out. And power was given to him sitting on it, to take peace from the earth, and that they should kill one another. And there was given to him a great sword.
270605 And when He had opened the third seal, I heard the third living creature say, Come and see. And I looked, and lo, a black horse. And he sitting on it had a balance in his hand.
270606 And I heard a voice in the midst of the four living creatures say, A choenix of wheat for a denarius, and three choenixes of barley for a denarius. And do not hurt the oil and the wine.
270607 And when He had opened the fourth seal, I heard the voice of the fourth living creature say, Come and see.
270608 And I looked, and behold, a pale horse. And the name of him sitting on it was Death, and Hell followed with him. And authority was given to them over the fourth part of the earth, to kill with the sword and with hunger and with death and by the beasts of the earth.
270609 And when He had opened the fifth seal, I saw under the altar the souls of those who had been slain for the word of God, and for the testimony which they held.
270610 And they cried with a loud voice, saying, Until when, Master, holy and true, do You not judge and avenge our blood on those who dwell on the earth?
270611 And white robes were given to each one of them. And it was said to them that they should rest yet for a little time, until both their fellow servants and their brothers (those about to be killed as they were ) should have their number made complete.
270612 And when He had opened the sixth seal, I looked, and behold, there was a great earthquake. And the sun became black as sackcloth of hair, and the moon became like blood.
270613 And the stars of heaven fell to the earth, even as a fig tree casts her untimely figs when she is shaken by a mighty wind.
270614 And the heaven departed like a scroll when it is rolled together. And every mountain and island were moved out of their places.
270615 And the kings of the earth, and the great men, and the rich, and the chief captains, and the mighty men, and every bondman, and every freeman, hid themselves in the dens and in the rocks of the mountains.
270616 And they said to the mountains and rocks, Fall on us and hide us from the face of Him sitting on the throne, and from the wrath of the Lamb;
270617 for the great day of His wrath has come, and who will be able to stand?
270701 And after these things I saw four angels standing on the four corners of the earth, holding the four winds of the earth so that the wind should not blow on the earth, nor on the sea, nor on any tree.
270702 And I saw another angel ascending from the east, having the seal of the living God. And he cried with a loud voice to the four angels, to whom it was given to hurt the earth and the sea,
270703 saying, Do not hurt the earth or the sea or the trees until we have sealed the servants of our God in their foreheads.
270704 And I heard the number of those who were sealed, one hundred and forty-four thousands, having been sealed out of every tribe of the sons of Israel.
270705 Out of the tribe of Judah, twelve thousand had been sealed. Out of the tribe of Reuben, twelve thousand had been sealed. Out of the tribe of Gad, twelve thousand had been sealed.
270706 Out of the tribe of Asher, twelve thousand had been sealed. Out of the tribe of Naphtali, twelve thousand had been sealed. Out of the tribe of Manasseh, twelve thousand had been sealed.
270707 Out of the tribe of Simeon, twelve thousand had been sealed. Out of the tribe of Levi, twelve thousand had been sealed. Out of the tribe of Issachar, twelve thousand had been sealed.
270708 Out of the tribe of Zebulun, twelve thousand had been sealed. Out of the tribe of Joseph, twelve thousand had been sealed. Out of the tribe of Benjamin, twelve thousand had been sealed.
270709 After these things I looked, and lo, a great multitude, which no man could number, out of all nations and kindreds and people and tongues, stood before the throne and before the Lamb, clothed with white robes, with palms in their hands.
270710 And they cried with a loud voice, saying, Salvation to our God sitting on the throne, and to the Lamb.
270711 And all the angels stood around the throne, and the elders, and the four living creatures, and they fell before the throne on their faces and worshiped God,
270712 saying, Amen! Blessing and glory and wisdom and thanksgiving and honor and power and might be to our God forever and ever. Amen.
270713 And one of the elders answered, saying to me, Who are these who are arrayed in white robes, and from where do they come?
270714 And I said to him, Sir, you know. And he said to me, These are the ones who came out of the great tribulation and have washed their robes, and have whitened them in the blood of the Lamb.
270715 Therefore they are before the throne of God, and they serve Him day and night in His temple. And He sitting on the throne will dwell among them.
270716 They will not hunger any more, nor thirst any more, nor will the sun light on them, nor any heat.
270717 For the Lamb who is in the midst of the throne will feed them and will lead them to the fountains of living waters. And God will wipe away all tears from their eyes.
270801 And when He opened the seventh seal, there was silence in Heaven for about half an hour.
270802 And I saw the seven angels who stood before God, and seven trumpets were given to them.
270803 And another angel came and stood at the altar, having a golden censer. And many incenses were given to him, so that he should offer it with the prayers of all saints on the golden altar before the throne.
270804 And the smoke of the incense which came with the prayers of the saints, ascended up before God from the angel's hand.
270805 And the angel took the censer and filled it with fire from the altar, and cast it into the earth. And voices and thunderings and lightnings and an earthquake occurred.
270806 And the seven angels which had the seven trumpets prepared themselves to sound.
270807 The first angel sounded, and there followed hail and fire mixed with blood, and they were cast on the earth. And the third part of trees was burned up, and all green grass was burned up.
270808 And the second angel sounded, and as it were a great mountain burning with fire was cast into the sea. And the third part of the sea became blood.
270809 And the third part of the creatures in the sea, those having souls, died; and the third part of the ships was destroyed.
270810 And the third angel sounded, and a great star burning like a lamp fell from the heaven, and it fell on the third part of the rivers and on the fountains of waters.
270811 And the name of the star is called Wormwood, and a third part of the waters became wormwood. And many men died from the waters, because they were made bitter.
270812 And the fourth angel sounded, and the third part of the sun was stricken, and the third part of the moon, and the third part of the stars, so that the third part of them was darkened, and the day did not appear for a third part of it, and the night also.
270813 And I saw and I heard one angel flying in mid-heaven, saying with a loud voice, Woe! Woe! Woe to the inhabitants of the earth, from the rest of the voices of the trumpet of the three angels being about to sound!
270901 And the fifth angel sounded. And I saw a star fall from the heaven to the earth, and it was given the key of the abyss.
270902 And it opened the bottomless pit. And there arose a smoke out of the pit, like the smoke of a great furnace. And the sun and air were darkened because of the smoke of the pit.
270903 And out of the smoke came forth locusts onto the earth. And authority was given to them, as the scorpions of the earth have authority.
270904 And they were commanded not to hurt the grass of the earth, or any green thing, or any tree, but only those men who do not have the seal of God in their foreheads.
270905 And to them it was given that they should not kill them, but that they should be tormented five months. And their torment was like a scorpion's torment when he stings a man.
270906 And in those days men will seek death and will not find it. And they will long to die, and death will flee from them.
270907 And the shapes of the locusts were like horses prepared for battle. And on their heads were as it were crowns like gold, and their faces were like the faces of men.
270908 And they had hairs like the hairs of women, and their teeth were like the teeth of lions.
270909 And they had breastplates like breastplates of iron. And the sound of their wings was like the sound of chariots of many horses running to battle.
270910 And they had tails like scorpions, and there were stings in their tails. And their authority was to hurt men five months.
270911 And they had a king over them, the angel of the bottomless pit, whose name in the Hebrew tongue is Abaddon, but in Greek his name is Apollyon.
270912 The first woe is past. Behold, after these things yet come two woes.
270913 And the sixth angel sounded his trumpet. And I heard a voice from the four horns of the golden altar before God,
270914 saying to the sixth angel who had the trumpet, Loose the four angels who are bound at the great river Euphrates.
270915 And the four angels were loosed, who were prepared for an hour, and a day, and a month, and a year, in order to slay the third part of men.
270916 And the number of the armies of the horsemen was two myriads of myriads. And I heard their number.
270917 And so I saw the horses in the vision, and those sitting on them, having breastplates of fire, even dusky red and brimstone. And the heads of the horses were like the heads of lions. And out of their mouths issued fire and smoke and brimstone.
270918 By these three the third part of men was killed, by the fire, and by the smoke, and by the brimstone which issued out of their mouths.
270919 For their authority is in their mouth and in their tails. For their tails were like serpents with heads, and with them they do harm.
270920 And the rest of the men who were not killed by these plagues still did not repent of the works of their hands, that they should not worship demons, and golden, and silver, and bronze, and stone, and wooden idols (which neither can see, nor hear, nor walk).
270921 And they did not repent of their murders, nor of their sorceries, nor of their fornication, nor of their thefts.
271001 And I saw another mighty angel coming down out of the heaven, clothed with a cloud. And a rainbow was on his head, and his face was as the sun, and his feet like pillars of fire.
271002 And he had a little book open in his hand. And he set his right foot on the sea and his left foot on the earth.
271003 And he cried with a loud voice, like a lion roaring. And when he had cried, seven thunders spoke their sounds.
271004 And when the seven thunders spoke their sounds, I was about to write. And I heard a voice from Heaven saying to me, Seal up what things the seven thunders spoke, and do not write these things.
271005 And the angel whom I saw standing on the sea and on the earth lifted his hand to the heaven,
271006 and swore by Him who lives forever and ever, who created the heaven and the things in it, and the earth and the things in it, and the sea and the things in it, that there should no longer be time.
271007 But in the days of the voice of the seventh angel, when he will begin to sound, the mystery of God should be finished, as He has declared to His servants the prophets.
271008 And the voice which I heard from Heaven spoke to me again, and said, Go, take the little book which is open in the hand of the angel who stands on the sea and on the earth.
271009 And I went to the angel and said to him, Give me the little book. And he said to me, Take it and eat it up, and it will make your belly bitter, but it will be sweet as honey in your mouth.
271010 And I took the little book out of the angel's hand and ate it up. And it was sweet as honey in my mouth, and as soon as I had eaten it, my belly was made bitter.
271011 And he said to me, You must prophesy again before many peoples and nations and tongues and kings.
271101 And a reed like a rod was given to me. And the angel stood, saying, Rise up and measure the temple of God, and the altar, and those who worship in it.
271102 But leave out the court which is outside the temple, and do not measure it, for it was given to the nations. And they will trample the holy city forty-two months.
271103 And I will give power to My two witnesses, and they will prophesy a thousand, two hundred and sixty days, clothed in sackcloth.
271104 These are the two olive trees and the two lampstands standing before the God of the earth.
271105 And if anyone will hurt them, fire proceeds out of their mouth and devours their enemies. And if anyone will hurt them, so it is right for him to be killed.
271106 These have authority to shut up the heaven, that it may not rain in the days of their prophecy. And they have authority over waters to turn them to blood, and to strike the earth with every plague, as often as they desire.
271107 And when they complete their testimony, the beast coming up out of the abyss will make war against them and will overcome them and kill them.
271108 And their bodies will lie in the street of the great city, which spiritually is called Sodom and Egypt, where also our Lord was crucified.
271109 And many of the peoples and tribes and tongues and nations will see their dead bodies three days and a half, and they will not allow their dead bodies to be put in tombs.
271110 And the ones who dwell on the earth will rejoice over them, and will make merry, and will send one another gifts, because these two prophets tormented those living on the earth.
271111 And after three days and a half, a spirit of life from God entered into them, and they stood on their feet. And great fear fell on those seeing them.
271112 And they heard a great voice from Heaven saying to them, Come up here. And they went up to Heaven in a cloud, and their enemies watched them.
271113 And in that hour a great earthquake occurred, and the tenth part of the city fell. And seven thousand names of men were slain in the earthquake. And the rest were frightened and gave glory to the God of Heaven.
271114 The second woe passed away. Behold, the third woe comes quickly.
271115 And the seventh angel sounded. And there were great voices in Heaven, saying, The kingdoms of this world have become the kingdoms of our Lord, and of His Christ. And He will reign forever and ever.
271116 And the twenty-four elders sitting before God on their thrones, fell on their faces and worshiped God,
271117 saying, We thank You, O Lord God Almighty, who are, and who was, and who is coming, because You took Your great power and reigned.
271118 And the nations were full of wrath, and Your wrath came, and the time of the judging of the dead, and to give the reward to Your servants the prophets, and to the saints, and to the ones fearing Your name, to the small and to the great, and to destroy those destroying the earth.
271119 And the temple of God was opened in Heaven, and there was seen in His temple the ark of His covenant, and there occurred lightnings and voices, and thunders and an earthquake, and a great hail.
271201 And there appeared a great sign in the heavens, a woman clothed with the sun, and the moon was under her feet, and a crown of twelve stars on her head,
271202 and having a babe in womb, she cries, being in travail, having been distressed to bear.
271203 And another sign was seen in the heavens. And behold a great red dragon, having seven heads and ten horns and seven crowns on his heads!
271204 And his tail drew the third part of the stars of heaven, and cast them onto the earth. And the dragon stood before the woman being about to bear, so that when she bears he might devour her child.
271205 And she bore a son, a male, who is going to rule all nations with a rod of iron. And her child was caught up to God and to His throne.
271206 And the woman fled into the wilderness, where she had a place prepared by God, so that they might nourish her there a thousand, two hundred and sixty days.
271207 And there was war in Heaven. Michael and his angels warring against the dragon. And the dragon and his angels warred,
271208 but did not prevail. Nor was place found for them in Heaven any more.
271209 And the great dragon was cast out, the old serpent called Devil, and Satan, who deceives the whole world. He was cast out into the earth, and his angels were cast out with him.
271210 And I heard a great voice saying in Heaven, Now has come the salvation and power and the kingdom of our God, and the authority of His Christ. For the accuser of our brothers is cast down, who accused them before our God day and night.
271211 And they overcame him because of the blood of the Lamb, and because of the word of their testimony. And they did not love their soul until death.
271212 Therefore rejoice, O heavens, and those tabernacling in them. Woe to the inhabitants of the earth and in the sea! For the Devil came down to you, having great wrath, knowing that he has but a little time.
271213 And when the dragon saw that he was cast to the earth, he persecuted the woman who bore the man child .
271214 And two wings of a great eagle were given to the woman, so that she might fly into the wilderness, into her place, where she is nourished for a time and times and half a time, from the serpent's face.
271215 And the serpent cast out of his mouth water like a flood after the woman, so that he might cause her to be carried away by the river.
271216 And the earth helped the woman. And the earth opened its mouth and swallowed up the river which the dragon cast out of his mouth.
271217 And the dragon was enraged over the woman, and went to make war with the rest of her seed, who keep the commandments of God and have the testimony of Jesus Christ.
271301 And I stood on the sand of the sea, and I saw a beast coming up out of the sea, having seven heads and ten horns. And on its horns were ten crowns, and on its heads was the name of blasphemy.
271302 And the beast which I saw was like a leopard, and its feet like those of a bear, and its mouth like the mouth of a lion. And the dragon gave him its power and its seat and great authority.
271303 And I saw one of its heads as having been slain to death, and its deadly wound was healed. And all the earth marveled after the beast.
271304 And they worshiped the dragon who gave authority to the beast. And they worshiped the beast, saying, Who is like the beast? Who is able to make war with it?
271305 And a mouth speaking great things was given to it, and blasphemies. And authority was given to it to continue forty-two months.
271306 And it opened its mouth in blasphemy toward God, to blaspheme His name and His tabernacle, and those dwelling in Heaven.
271307 And it was given to it to war with the saints and to overcome them. And authority was given to it over every tribe and tongue and nation.
271308 And all dwelling on the earth will worship it, those whose names have not been written in the Book of Life of the Lamb slain, from the foundation of the world.
271309 If anyone has an ear, let him hear.
271310 He who leads into captivity will go into captivity. If anyone will kill with the sword, he must be killed by a sword. Here is the patience and the faith of the saints.
271311 And I saw another beast coming up out of the earth. And it had two horns like a lamb, and he spoke like a dragon.
271312 And it exercises all the authority of the first beast before him, and causes the earth and those dwelling in it to worship the first beast, whose deadly wound was healed.
271313 And it does great wonders, so that it makes fire come down from the heaven onto the earth in the sight of men.
271314 And it deceives those dwelling on the earth, because of the miracles which were given to it to do before the beast, saying to those dwelling on the earth that they should make an image to the beast who had the wound by a sword and lived.
271315 And there was given to it to give a spirit to the image of the beast, so that the image of the beast might both speak, and might cause as many as would not worship the image of the beast to be killed.
271316 And it causes all, both small and great, rich and poor, free and bond, to receive a mark on their right hand, or in their foreheads,
271317 even that not any might buy or sell except those having the mark, or the name of the beast, or the number of its name.
271318 Here is the wisdom. Let him having reason count the number of the beast, for it is the number of a man. And its number is six hundred and sixty-six.
271401 And I looked, and lo, the Lamb stood on Mount Zion. And with Him were a hundred and forty-four thousands, having His Father's name written in their foreheads.
271402 And I heard a voice from Heaven, like the voice of many waters and like the voice of a great thunder. And I heard the voice of harpers harping with their harps.
271403 And they sang as it were a new song before the throne and before the four living creatures and the elders. And no one could learn that song except the hundred and forty-four thousands who were redeemed from the earth.
271404 These are those who were not defiled with women; for they are virgins. These are those who follow the Lamb wherever He goes. These were redeemed from among men, as a firstfruit to God and to the Lamb.
271405 And in their mouth was found no guile, for they were without blemish before the throne of God.
271406 And I saw another angel flying in mid-heaven, having the everlasting gospel to preach to those dwelling on the earth, even to every nation and kindred and tongue and people,
271407 saying with a great voice, Fear God and give glory to Him! For the hour of His judgment has come. And worship Him who made the heaven and the earth, and the sea, and the fountains of waters.
271408 And another angel followed, saying, The great city, Babylon, has fallen, has fallen; because of the wine of the anger of her fornication; she has made all nations to drink.
271409 And a third angel followed them, saying with a great voice, If anyone worships the beast and its image, and receives a mark in his forehead or in his hand,
271410 he also will drink of the wine of the anger of God, having been mixed undiluted in the cup of His wrath. And he will be tormented by fire and brimstone before the holy angels, and in the presence of the Lamb.
271411 And the smoke of their torment goes up forever and ever. And they have no rest day or night, those who worship the beast and its image, and whoever receives the mark of its name.
271412 Here is the patience of the saints. Here are the ones who keep the commandments of God and the faith of Jesus.
271413 And I heard a voice from Heaven saying to me, Write, Blessed are the dead who die in the Lord from now on. Yes, says the Spirit, they shall rest from their labors, and their works follow them.
271414 And I looked, and behold, a white cloud. And on the cloud sat one like the Son of man, having a golden crown on His head, and a sharp sickle in His hand.
271415 And another angel came out of the temple, crying in a great voice to Him sitting on the cloud, Thrust in Your sickle and reap, for the time has come for You to reap, for the harvest of the earth was dried.
271416 And He sitting on the cloud thrust in His sickle on the earth, and the earth was reaped.
271417 And another angel came out of the temple in Heaven, also having a sharp sickle.
271418 And another angel came out from the altar, who had authority over fire. And he spoke with a great cry to him who had the sharp sickle, saying, Thrust in your sharp sickle, and gather the clusters of the vine of the earth, for her grapes are fully ripe.
271419 And the angel thrust in his sickle into the earth and gathered the vine of the earth, and cast it into the great winepress of the anger of God.
271420 And the winepress was trodden outside the city, and blood came out of the winepress, even to the bridles of the horses, for the space of a thousand, six hundred stadia.
271501 And I saw another sign in Heaven, great and marvelous: seven angels with the seven last plagues; for in them is filled up the wrath of God.
271502 And I saw as it were a sea of glass mingled with fire. And those who had gotten the victory over the beast, and over his image, and over his mark, and over the number of his name, stand on the sea of glass, having the harps of God.
271503 And they sing the song of Moses the servant of God, and the song of the Lamb, saying, Great and marvelous are Your works, Lord God Almighty, just and true are Your ways, O King of saints.
271504 Who shall not fear You, O Lord, and glorify Your name? For You only are holy. For all nations shall come and worship before You, for Your righteousnesses were made known.
271505 And after these things I looked, and behold, the temple of the tabernacle of the testimony was opened in Heaven.
271506 And the seven angels came out of the temple, having the seven plagues, clothed in pure and white linen, and were tied at the breasts with golden bands.
